[1,i]	yaḥ san jāta mahā kṛpaḥ vyasaninam trātum samagram janam puṇya jñāna mayam pracitya vipulam hetum vidhūta śramaḥ kṛtsna jñeya visarpi nirmalatara prajñā udaya adrim śritaḥ loke hārddatama upahaḥ jina ravirmūrdhnā namasyāmi tam 
[1,ii]	varam hi dhārma kīrteṣu carviteṣu api carvaṇam niṣpīḍitā api mṛdvīkā nanu svādam jahāti kim 
[1,iii]	nyāya mārga tulā ārūḍham jagat ekatra yat matiḥ jayet tasya kva gambhīrāḥ giraḥ aham jaḍa dhīḥ kva ca tathā api manda matayaḥ santi mattaḥ api kecana teṣām kṛte mayā api eṣa hetu binduḥ vibhajyate 
[1,iv_1,v]	parokṣa ityādinā prakaraṇa ārambhe prayojanam āha tat ca śrotṛ jana pravṛtti artham iti kecid tat uktam sarvasya eva hi śāstrasya karmaṇaḥ vā api kasyacid yāvat prayojanam na uktam tāvat tat kena gṛhyatām iti tat ayuktam yatas asya prakaraṇasya idam prayojanam iti pradarśane prayojana viśeṣam prati upāyatām prakaraṇasya niścitya anupāye pravṛtti asambhavāt prekṣāvatām tad arthitayā prakaraṇa śravaṇa ādau pravṛttiḥ syāt iti tad abhidhānasya arthavat tā varṇyate na ca etat yuktam yatas prekṣāvatām pravṛttiḥ prayojana arthinām tad upāye tad bhāva niścayāt yathā kṛṣīvala ādīnām sasya ādi upāye bīja ādāva bīja ādi vivekena avadhṛta bīja ādi bhāvānām anyathā hi aniścita upāyānām upeya arthinām pravṛttau prekṣāvat tā eva hīyeta upeye tu pramāṇa vyāpāra asambhavāt a niścaye api vivecita upāyāḥ pratibandha vaikalyayoḥ asambhave yogyam etat vivakṣitam kāryam niṣpādayitum iti saṃbhāvanayā pravṛttau prekṣāvat tātaḥ na hīyeran 
[2,i]	niścayaḥ ca pramāṇāt eva na ca prayojana vākyasya prāmāṇyam asti śābdānām bahis arthe pratibandha abhāvāt vivakṣāyām tasya prāmāṇye api yathā vastu pravṛtti niyama abhāvāt na tatas prakaraṇasya prayojana viśeṣam prati upāya tā niścayaḥ samasti na hi ye yathā yam artham vivakṣanti te tathā eva tam anutiṣṭhanti visaṃvādana abhiprāyāṇām anyathā abhidhāyānyathā pravṛtti darśanāt loke sarva tra anāśvāsāt 
[2,ii]	prayojana viśeṣa upanyāsāt prakaraṇasya tad upāya tā viṣaye saṃśayaḥ janyate tatas tad bhāva nirdhāraṇāya kṛṣīvala ādeḥ iva bīja ādi avadhṛtaye pravṛttiḥ yuktā iti ced na prayojana viśeṣa upāya tā saṃśayasya tad abhidhānāt prāk api bhāvāt tad sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāve tasya nyāya prāpta tvāt anumāna ādi vyutpatti arthānām ca prakaraṇānām darśanāt kim asya anumāna vyutpādanam prayojanam anyaddhā na vā kiñcid api iti evaṃrūpaḥ ca saṃśayaḥ prāk pravartamānaḥ kena nivāryeta api ca kim idam niṣprayojanam uta prayojana vat atha asmad abhimatena vā prayojanena tadvat iti jijñāsoḥ pravṛtti sambhave vyarthaḥ eva prayojana vākya upanyāsaḥ 
[2,iii]	tasmāt yat prayojana rahitam vākyam tad arthaḥ vā na tat prekṣāvatārabhyate kartum pratipādayitum vā tat yathā daśa dāḍima ādi vākyam kāka danta parīkṣā ca niṣprayojanam ca idam prakaraṇam tad arthaḥ vā iti vyāpaka anupalabdhyā pratyavatiṣṭhamānasya tad asiddha tā udbhāvanā artham ādau prayojana vākya upanyāsaḥ 
[3,i^1]	tatra tad yutpādana artham iti vākyena svayam asya prakaraṇasya prayojanam āha yathāsvam abhidheya pratītiḥ hi vākyasya prayojanam tat ca iha asti padānām avāntara vākyānām ca paraspara saṃsargāt samāsa artha pratīteḥ tathā hi anumānam atra prakaraṇe vyutpādyate iti tat abhidheyam tasya eva tad śabdena sambandhāt yadi api parokṣa artha pratipattau guṇa bhūtam anumānam tathā api vaktuḥ abhiprāya anuvidhāyitayā śabda vṛtteḥ tad śabdena parāmṛśyate anyathā pradhāna saṃsparśa upi katham syāt śabdānām svabhāvataḥ sambandha ayogāt pakṣa dharmaḥ ityādinā ca anumānasya eva vyutpādanāt 
[3,i^2]	tasya vyutpatti ravi parīta svarūpa pratītiḥ asya prakaraṇasya prayojanam tad sādhya tvāt atas eva ca anumāna vyutpatti viṣayam prakaraṇa vyāpāram pratipādayitum ṇicā nirdiśati tadvayutpādana artham iti tatas ca prakaraṇa prayojanayoḥ sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ api uktaḥ bhavati yadi api śabda vṛttena anumāna vyutpatti viṣayasya prakaraṇa vyāpārasya prādhānyam tathā api vastu vṛttena vyutpatteḥ eva pradhāna tā tasyāḥ tad sādhya tvāt itarasya ca tad upāya tvena apradhāna tvāt tasmāt anumāna vyutpatti reva prayojana tayā pratīyate na prakaraṇa vyāpāraḥ iti 
[3,ii]	parokṣa artha pratipatteḥ amumān āśraya tvāt iti anena tu prakaraṇa arthasya anumāna lakṣaṇasya prayojanam āha na hi vākyasya sva artha pratīti lakṣaṇam phalam asti iti etāvatā eva prekṣāvān pravartate api tu tad abhidheya arthasya puruṣa artha upayogi tve sati tat ca iha asti yatas parokṣa arthasya yā pratipattiḥ niścayaḥ tasyāḥ anumānam trirūpa liṅgam kāraṇe kārya upacārāt ananya upāya sādhya tām darśayitum para mata nirāsa artham āśrayaḥ kāraṇam anumānam āśrayaḥ yasya iti sāmānyena vigṛhya tadanu ca kasya anumāna āśraya tvāt iti viśeṣa apekṣāyām yadi api parokṣa artha pratipatti śabda sambandhe strī tvam gamyate tathā api tat pada saṃskāra velāyām buddhi asaṃnihita tvāt bahis aṅgam iti na strī pratyaya nimittam yathā bhūtam iyam brāhmaṇī āvapanam iyam uṣṭrikā iti 
[4,i_4,ii]	anena ca sarvā parokṣa artha pratipattiḥ pramāṇa bhūtā anyasmāt tad pratipatti ayogāt trirūpa liṅga āśraya eva iti uktam bhavati anumāna āśraya tvāt eva iti avadhāraṇāt tatas ca śabda ādīnām sati prāmāṇye anumāna tā anyathā teṣām api vyutpādyatā prasaṅgaḥ nimittasya samāna tvāt tathā hi sarvā parokṣa artha pratipattiḥ pramāṇa bhūtā na svatantrā bhavati tasyāḥ sva artha pratibandha abhāvena niyamena tad saṃvāda ayogāt avisaṃvāda lakṣaṇa tvāt ca pramāṇasya anyatas api yadi syāt sarvatas sarva pratipatti prasaṅgāt dharmya sambandhe api sarvatra pratītim janayet pratyāsatti vipra karṣa abhāvāt evambhūtaḥ ca trirūpa liṅgam eva arthaḥ bhavati iti sarvā parokṣa artha pratipattiḥ trirūpa liṅga ja tvena anumānāt na bhidyate iti eṣa ca arthaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ kasya parokṣa artha pratipatteḥ iti prakṛtena saṃbandhāt darśitaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ eva tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ eva ca parokṣa artha pratipatteḥ hetuḥ iti avadhāraṇāt 
[4,iii_5,i]	artha grahaṇam tu parokṣa artha pratipatteḥ iti anumānasya api sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam prāmāṇyam darśayitum artha kriyā samarthaḥ hi arthaḥ sva lakṣaṇam ca evam ātmakam atas eva vastu adhiṣṭhāna tvāt pramāṇa vyavasthāyāḥ iti vakṣyati anyathā anumānāt tatra pravṛttiḥ na syāt artha kriyā arthinaḥ sāmānyasya avastu tve api jñāna mātra lakṣaṇa tvāt tad artha kriyāyāḥ tasyāḥ ca tad utpādya tvena siddha tvāt na hi jātiḥ dāha pāka ādau upayujyate sva lakṣaṇasya eva tatra upayogāt tad sambandhāt tatra pravṛttiḥ iti ced na nityasya anupakāraka tvena kenacid sambandha abhāvāt sati api ca sambandhe katham anya pratipattau anyatra pravṛttiḥ atiprasaṅgāt samavāyasya sūkṣma tvena anavasita vivekasya avasāyāt bhrāntyā tatra pravṛttiḥ iti ced evam tarhi bhrānti mātram eva astu kim antar gaḍunā sāmānyena nirbbīja bhrānti ayogāt iti ced tāḥ eva vyaktayaḥ tad eka kārya kāriṇyaḥ bhrānteḥ bījam varṇa ākṛti samāna ākāram hi sāmānya jñānam na ca sāmānyam tad rūpam tat katham tat bhrānteḥ bbījam sādṛśya nibandhanā hi bhrāntiḥ iṣyate paraiḥ vyaktayaḥ eva ca asamāna jātīya vyāvṛttāḥ sāmānya ākāra jñāna svarūpāḥ tatas tāḥ eva bhrānti bījam atad rūpa vyāvṛtteḥ tāsu bhāvāt vastu bhūtasya tu sāmānyasya sambandhaā saṃbhavena tāsu bhāva ayogāt ca 
[5,ii]	yaiḥ tu vyakti ātmakam eva sāmānyam kalpitam taiḥ sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam anumānasya prāmāṇyam abhyupagatam eva bhavati sva lakṣaṇa ātmakam tu sāmānyam katham anumāne pratibhāsate iti cintyam na ca vyakti rūpam apāsya aparam sāmānyasya rūpam iṣyate vaiśeṣika darśana upagama prasaṅgāt 
[6,i]	 hi kathitam tatra kārya svabhāvayoḥ vidhi sādhana tvāt na pratiṣedhe sādhye vyāpāraḥ anupalabdhitaḥ api na hetu antara abhāva niścayaḥ yatas sā caturddha avasthitā svabhāva kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhayaḥ viruddha vidhiḥ ca iti tulya yogya tārūpasya eka jñāna saṃsargiṇaḥ svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ anyā upalabdhi rūpā abhāva vyavahāra hetuḥ iṣyate na ca hetu antaram atyantā bhāva tayā upagatam anukrānta rūpam yadi hi syāt deśa ādi niṣedhaḥ eva asya syāt na atyanta abhāvaḥ kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhī tu siddhe kārya kāraṇa vyāpya vyāpaka bhāve bhavataḥ na ca hetu antarā iti antā sattayā aṅgīkṛte prakāraḥ ayam sambhavati tat katham te tad abhāvam gamayiṣyataḥ virodhaḥ api avikala kāraṇasya bhavataḥ anya bhāve abhāvāt avagamyate iti viruddha upalabdhiḥ api asambhavinī sambhave vā kāraṇa anupalabdhi ādīnām katham atyanta niṣedhaḥ iti āśaṅkayā āha hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare iti tatas trividhāt hetoḥ apare anye hetvābhāsāḥ yatas tatas tridhā eva saḥ iti 
[6,ii^1]	evam manyate iha yat yatra niyamyate tat hi paryayeṇa tad vipakṣasya vyāptau sa niyamaḥ siddhyati yathā yat sat tat kṣaṇikam eva iti sattvasya kṣaṇikeṣu niyamaḥ ucyamānaḥ sattva viparyayeṇa asattvena kṣaṇika vipakṣasya akṣaṇikasya vyāptau siddhyati evam iha api tri tve hetuḥ niyamyamānaḥ hetu viparyayeṇa hetvābhāsa tvena tri saṃkhyā bāhyasya arthasya vyāptau trisaṃkhyāyām eva niyataḥ bhavati tatas trividha hetu vyatiriktānām arthānām hetvābhāsa tām darśayati tena svabhāva viruddha upalabdhyā kārya svabhāva anupalambha vyatiriktānām arthānām hetu tva abhāva niścayaḥ iti 
[6,ii^2]	hetu tad ābhāsayoḥ ca paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tayā eva virodhaḥ hetu lakṣaṇa pratīti kāle eva pratipannaḥ tad ātma niyata pratibhāsa jñānāt eva tad viparītasya anyatayā tad ābhāsatā pratīteḥ parasparam itaretara rūpa abhāva niścayāt tatra trividha hetu vyatirikteṣu artheṣu hetvābhāsa tvam upalabhyamānam sva viruddham hetu tvam nirākaroti te ca hetu traya bāhyāḥ arthāḥ na atyanta asattayā upagatā na api hetu tvam teṣu niṣidhyamānam kevalam vyāmohāt hetu tvam anyatra prasiddham eva tatra āropitam āśaṅkitam vā tad viruddha upalambhāt apasāryate 
[6,ii^3]	tat kim ucyate atyanta asaṃbhavinaḥ katham virodhaḥ iti na ca saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ eva virodhaḥ yena tat nyāyaḥ sarvatra upavarṇyeta na api yat yatra pratiṣidhyate tasya tatra eva virodhaḥ pratipattavyaḥ yena katham asataḥ kenacid virodha gatiḥ iti ca udyeta na hi na atra śīta sparśaḥ agneḥ iti sādhya dharmiṇī eva śīta sparśasya agninā virodha saṃbandhaḥ yathā tu asya anyatra pratīta virodhasya agninā sādhya dharmiṇi niṣedhaḥ tathā hetvābhāsa tva upalambhāt hetu traya bāhyeṣu artheṣu hetu tva nirāsaḥ atyanta asataḥ api ca lākṣaṇikaḥ virodhaḥ pratīyate yathā kṣaṇika tvena akṣaṇika tvasya tasya vastuni kvacid api asambhavāt bhāvena vā yadvat abhāvasya sarva śakti virahala lakṣaṇasya iti alam durmati viṣpanditeṣu atyādareṇa iti sthitam etat tri tve hetu tvam niyamyamānam tad viparyayasyāḥ api ca vyāptau satyām tatra niyatam bhavati iti abhiprāyavatā viparyaya vyāptim pradarśayitum idam uktam hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare iti 
[7,i]	tatra etat syāt kṣaṇika vipakṣasya sattva viparyayeṇa vyāptiḥ bādhaka pramāṇa vaśāt avasitāḥ iha tu tri saṅkhyā bāhyānām arthānām hetvābhāsa tvena vyāptiḥ katareṇa pramāṇena avasitā itya trāha avinā abhauva niyamāt iti trividha hetu vyatirikte liṅga tayā upagate śaṅkayamāne vā vastuni pakṣa dharma tā sadbhāve api avinā abhāva abhāvāt iti arthaḥ tathā ca vakṣyati na sa trividhāt hetoḥ anyatra asti iti atra eva niyataḥ ucyate iti avinā abhāva vaikalyam ca hetvābhāsa tvena asiddha viruddha anaikāntika sāmānya dharmeṇa vyāptam prameya tva ādau niścitam iti hetvābhāsa tve sādhye avinā abhāva vaikalyam svabhāva hetuḥ 
[8,i]	avinā abhāva vaikalyam ca trividha hetu vyatirikta tvāt eva tad anyeṣām vyāpaka anupalabdhitaḥ siddham tathā hi tādātmya tad utpattibhyām avinā abhāvaḥ vyāptaḥ tayoḥ tatra avaśyaṃbhāvāt tasya ca tayoḥ eva bhāvāt atad svabhāvasya atad utpatteḥ ca tad anāyatta tayā tad avyabhicāra niyama abhāvāt tat uktam kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā svabhāvāt vā niyāmakāt avinā abhau a niyamaḥ adarśanāt na na darśanāt avaśyaṃbhāva niyamaḥ kaḥ parasya anyathā paraiḥ anartha antara nimitte vā dharme vāsasi rāga vat iti 
[8,ii^1]	rūpa ādinā api hi rasa ādeḥ avinā abhāvaḥ na svatas kintu sva kāraṇa avyabhicāra dvārakaḥ iti tad kāraṇa utpattiḥ eva avinābhāva nibandhanam anyathā tad anāyat tasya tad kāraṇān āyattasya vā tena avinābhāva kalpanāyām sarvasya sarva arthaiḥ avinābhāvaḥ syāt aviśeṣāt eka artha samavāya nimittaḥ rūpa rasa ādeḥ avinā abhāvaḥ iti ced nanu samavāyaḥ api ādhārya ādhāra bhūtānām upavarṇyate sa ca ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ tad ā ātmā anupakāra iti prasaṅgataḥ na sidhyati iti eka sāmagrī a dhīna tā eva eka artha samavāyaḥ avaseyaḥ anyaḥ vā vastu bhūtaḥ saṃbandhaḥ asambhavī tathā sambandha parīkṣāyām vistarataḥ śāstra kṛtā pratipādim eva iti tatas eva avadhāryam asa 
[8,ii^2]	nanu asati api janya janaka bhāve tādātmye vā tena eva avinābhāvaḥ na anyena iti atra vastu svabhāvaiḥ eva uttaram vācyam ye evam bhavanti na asmābhiḥ kevalam vayam draṣṭāraḥ iti ced ākasmikaḥ tarhi sa vastūnām svabhāvaḥ iti na kasyacid na syāt na hi aheta uḥ ddeśa kāla dravya niyamaḥ yuktaḥ tat hi kiñcid kvacid upanīyeta na vā yasya yatra kiñcid āyattam anāyattam vā anyathā viśeṣa abhāva ādiṣṭa deśa kāla dravya vat anya deśa ādi bhāvaḥ kena vāryeta viśeṣa abhāvāt tatas yadi ena avinābhūtam dṛśyate tasya tena avyabhicāra kāraṇam tattva cintakaiḥ abhidhānīyam na tu pāda prasārikā avalambanīyā tat ca avyabhicāra kāraṇam yathā uktāt anyat na yujyate iti tad vikalā na hetu lakṣaṇa bhājaḥ iti tathā ca āha saṃyogi ādiṣu yeṣu asti pratibandhaḥ na tādṛśaḥ na te hetavaḥ iti uktam vyabhicārasya saṃbhavāt iti 
[9,i_9,iii]	atra prayogaḥ yasya yena saha tādātmya tad utpattī na staḥ na sa tad avinā bhāvī yathā prameya tvādiḥ a nitya tva ādinā na staḥ ca kenacid tādātmya tad utpatti svabhāva kārya vyatirekiṇām arthānām iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ tu svabhāva hetau antar bhāvitā iti tasyāḥ tādātmya lakṣaṇaḥ eva pratibandhaḥ vyāpaka kāraṇa anupalabdhī tu tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇa pratibandha vaśāt eva vyāpya kāryayoḥ nivṛtti sādhayataḥ tat uktam tasmāt tanmātra saṃbaddhaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhāvam eva vā nivartayet kāraṇam vā kāryam avyabhicārataḥ iti tat evam hetu lakṣaṇam saṃkhyā niyamaḥ tad upadarśakam ca pramāṇam atra śloke nirdiṣṭam iti 
[9,iv]	athavā tridhā eva saḥ iti sa pakṣa dharmaḥ tri prakāraḥ eva svabhāva kārya anupalambha ākhyaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ na anyaḥ sa tri prakāraḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ eva iti sambandhaḥ kim kāraṇam avinā abhau a niyamāt avinābhā asya vyāpteḥ trividhaḥ eva pakṣa dharme niyamāt trividhasya ca pakṣa dharmasya avinābhāva niyamāt tena ca svabhāva kārya anupalambha ātmaka trividha pakṣa dharma vyatiriktā na tad aṃśena vyāptāḥ iti trividhaḥ ca kārya svabhāva anupalabdhi rūpaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ eva iti na tasya ahetu tvam iti uktam bhavati tatas trividha hetu bāhyeṣu avinābhā bāt hetu vyavahāram kurvantaḥ trividhe ca hetau avinābhāvasya avaśyambhāva abhāvāt ahetu tvam ācakṣāṇāḥ nirastāḥ bhavanti 
[10,i^1]	tatra etat syāt hetvābhāsānam api lakṣaṇambhidhānīyam tatra śiṣyāṇām hetu vyavahāra nivṛttayaḥ iti āha hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare iti tatas pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ iti hetu lakṣaṇāt apare anye talakṣaṇa vikalāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ gamyante eva iti na tad lakṣaṇam ucyate tathā hi pakṣa dharmaḥ iti ukte yatra pakṣa dharma tā na asti na sa hetuḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ iti vacane yatra tad aṃśa vyāpti virahaḥ viparyaya vyāpteḥ vyāpakasya vā tatra avaśi ambhāva abhāvāt te hetu rūpa vikala tayā hetvābhāsāḥ asiddha viruddha anaikāntikāḥ gamyante eva tathā hi yat lakṣaṇaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ śiṣyasya vyutpāditaḥ tad lakṣaṇa virahite na tad vayava hāram svayam eva pravartayiṣyati atadrūpa parihāreṇa eva tad rūpa pratipatteḥ iti na tatra yatnaḥ phalavān bhavati 
[10,i^2]	yat tu anyatra hetvābhāsa vyutpādanam tat manda buddhīn adhikṛtya idam tu prakaraṇam vipulam atīnut diśya praṇītam saṃkṣepataḥ iti vacanāt te eva hi saṃkṣepa uktam yathāvat avagantum kṣamāḥ na manda matayaḥ teṣām vistara abhidhānam antareṇa yathāvat artha pratipatteḥ abhāvāt atas eva artha ākṣipta upanyāsa pūrvakam eva hetvābhāsa lakṣaṇam tatra upavarṇitam iti tat atra vyākhyāne hetu lakṣaṇam hetu saṃkhyā niyamaḥ tasya ca trividhasya hetu tva avadhāraṇam tad ubhaya kāraṇam śliṣṭa nirddeśa ākhyānam hetvābhāsa lakṣaṇa anabhidhāna kāraṇam ca iti ṣaṣ arthāḥ śloke atra nirdiṣṭāḥ iti 
[11,i]	kiñca idam api sādhu dṛśyate tridhā eva kārya svabhāva anupalabdhi bheda bhinnaḥ sa hetuḥ tathā tridhā eva pakṣa dharma anvaya vyatireka rūpa bhedāt tri prakāraḥ eva trirūpaḥ eva tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanena anvaya vyatirekayoḥ abhidhānāt na ābādhita viṣaya tva ādi rūpa antara yogī api sa hetuḥ kutas yatas hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare tatas trividhāt svabhāva ādeḥ pakṣa dharma ādi rūpa traya yoginaḥ vai apare anye saṃyogi ādayaḥ abādhita viṣaya tva ādi vyatirikta rūpavantaḥ vā kasmāt avinā abhā asya atra eva trividhaḥ eva trirūpaḥ eva ca hetau niyamāt anyatra svabhāva ādi vyatirikte rūpa antara sambhavini vā avinā abhāva abhāvāt iti arthaḥ na hi svabhāva ādi vyatirikte pratibandha nibandhanasya avinā bhāvasya saṃbhavaḥ tadvati vā rūpa antarasya yathā ca sati eva avinā abhāve rūpa antarasya na sambhavaḥ tathā ṣaṣ lakṣaṇaḥ ityādinā vakṣyati 
[11,ii]	pakṣa dharmaḥ iti atra hetu lakṣaṇe api kriyamāṇe yadi samudāyaḥ pakṣaḥ gṛhyate yaḥ anumāna viṣayaḥ tadā sarvaḥ hetuḥ asiddhaḥ siddhau vā anumāna vaiyarthyam iti āha pakṣaḥ dharmī iti katham punar samudāya vacanaḥ pakṣa śabdaḥ dharmi mātre vartate iti ced avayave samudāya upacārāt pakṣa ākhyasya hi samudāyasya dvau avayavau dharmī dharmaḥ ca tat atra dharmi mātre samudāya upacārāt pakṣa śabdaḥ vartate tat eka deśa tvam ca samudāya upacāra nimittam iti na sādhya dharmiṇaḥ anyatra tad prasaṅgaḥ tat uktam samudāyasya sādhya tvāt dharma mātre cadharmiṇi amukhye api ekadeśa tvāt sādhya tvam upacaryate iti 
[12,i_12,iii]	tat etat ācāryīyam vyākhyānam īśvarasenena ākṣiptam parihartum pūrva pakṣayan āha prayojana ityādinā na ṛte prayojana āt iṣṭam mukhya śabda artha laṅghanam iti asati prayojane na upacāraḥ yuktaḥ tatas dharmi dharmaḥ iti eva astu iti paraḥ na prayojana abhāvaḥ kutas sarvaḥ ca asau vivāda āśrayaḥ anyaḥ vā dharmī yaḥ tasya pratiṣedhaḥ arthaḥ prayojanam yasya upacārasya tad bhāvaḥ tasmāt sarva dharmi dharma pratiṣedha artha tvāt upacārasya iti prayojana abhāva āditya siddhaḥ hetuḥ kaḥ evam sati guṇaḥ iti ced āha evam hi upacāre sati cākṣuṣa tva ādi ādi grahaṇāt kākasya kārṣṇyāt ityādi vyadhikaraṇa asiddham parihṛtam hetu tvena nirastam bhavati dharmi dharmaḥ iti tu sāmānye na abhidhānāt teṣām api hetu tā syāt iti 
[12,iv^1]	asati upacāre dharmi grahaṇāt api etat sidhyati tatas anarthakaḥ eva upacāraḥ iti āha paraḥ dharma vacanena api na kevalam dharmi vacanena dharmya āśraya siddhau dharmiṇaḥ āśrayaṇam āśrayaḥ parigrahaḥ tasya siddhiḥ tasyām satyām kim punar ddharmasya dharmyākṣepa nimittam iti ced para āśraya tvāt dharmi paratantra tvāt dharmasya avaśyam asau dharmiṇam ākṣipati tatas dharmivacanam atiricyamānam viśiṣṭam sādhya dharmiṇam eva pratipādayati na dharmi mātram syāt matam dharmi grahaṇāt viśiṣṭaḥ atra dharmī kaścid abhipretaḥ iti gamyeta sa tu sādhya dharmī iti kutas iti āha pratyāsatteḥ nyāyāt pratyāsattiḥ ca atra dharmi vacana sāmarthyāt abhipretā iti gamyate vyāptau tu nyāye dharma vacanena api dharmi mātra ākṣepat dharmi grahaṇa vaiyarthyam pratyāsanna tā ca sādhya dharmiṇaḥ eva tatra prathamam hetu upadarśanāt na pratyāsatteḥ sādhya dharmi parigrahaḥ kutas dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇaḥ api na kevalam sādhya dharmiṇaḥ pratyāsatteḥ kadācid vyāpti darśana pūrvake prayoge dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇī api prathamam hetu sadbhāva upadarśanāt 
[13,i]	yadi na pratyāsatteḥ sādhya dharmi siddhiḥ pāriśeṣyāt tarhi bhaviṣyati yatas tad aṃśa vyāptyā hetu bhūtayā dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi dharmasya sattva siddheḥ na hi dṛṣṭāntam antareṇa hetoḥ sādhyena vyāptiḥ pradarśayitum śakyate iti manyate tatas dharmi grahaṇā dvaya tiḥ icyamānāt sādhya dharmiṇaḥ eva parigrahaḥ tad aṃśena iti ca tad śabdena dharma vacana ākṣiptaḥ dharmī sambhantsyate iti tad sambandhana artham api dharmi grahaṇam na aśaṅkanīyam yatra prayojana antaram na sambhavati sa pāriśeṣya viṣayaḥ dharmi vacanasya tu anyat api prayojanam sambhāvyate tat kutas pāriśeṣyāt dharmi vacanāt sādhya dharmi parigrahaḥ iti manyamānaḥ siddhāntavādi āha siddhe tad aṃśa vyāptyā dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sattve punar ddharmiṇaḥ vacanam dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇaḥ eva yaḥ dharmaḥ sa hetuḥ iti niyama artham āśaṅkayeta tatas ca cākṣuṣa tva ādayaḥ eva hetavaḥ syuḥ na kṛtaka tva ādayaḥ iti aniṣṭam eva syāt tasmāt upacāraḥ kartavyaḥ iti 
[13,ii^1]	kim punar tarka śāstra dṛṣṭam kvacid niyama artha vacanam ityaḥ āha dṛṣṭam sajātīyaḥ eva ityādi tatra yaḥ san sajātīye iti atra ācāryīye hetu lakṣaṇe sajātīyaḥ eva sattvam iti avadhāraṇena siddhe api hetoḥ vyatireke kutra sādhya abhāve yat etat asan tad atyaye iti asattva vacanam tat niyama artham ācāryeṇa vyākhyātam asati eva na astitāḥ yathā syāt na anyatra na viruddhaḥ iti tathā iha api dharmi vacanam tatra eva bhāva niyama artham āśaṅkayeta kadā siddhe api dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sattve kutas tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanāt kva bhāva niyama artham tatra eva dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sati ca āśaṅkā sambhave kutas pāriśeṣyāt sādhya dharmi parigrahaḥ nanu apakṣa dharmasya ahetu tvāt na niyama artha tā āśaṅkā 
[13,ii^2_14,i]	tathā hi sādhya dharmeṇa vyāptaḥ api dharmaḥ yadi kvacid dharmiṇī upalabhyeta tadā tatra eva sva vyāpaka pratītim janayet na anyatra pratyāsatti viprakarṣābhyām yathākramam anupalabdhaḥ tu kvacid dharmiṇi katham gamakaḥ tathā abhāve vā sarvatra sva vyāpakam gamayet pratyāsatti vipra karṣa abhāvāt eva iti atas āha tasmāt sāmarthyāt ityādi yat idam anantaram sāmarthyam samupavarṇitam āsmāt sāmarthyāt arthasya sādhya dharmi parigraha lakṣaṇasya bhavati pratītiḥ paṭu dhiyām śrotṛṇām kintva śabdakam artham svayam anusara tām pratipatti gauravam syāt tad upacāra mātrāt svayam aśabdaka artha abhyūha rahitāt dharmi dharmaḥ iti ane na pakṣa dharmaḥ iti samāna nirddeśāt pratipatti gauravam ca parihṛtam bhavati pratipatti gauravam ca iti caśabdena etat āha ye para upadeśam ākāṅkṣanti taiḥ ayam arthaḥ lakṣaṇa vacanāt boddhavyaḥ iti yathālakṣaṇam pratīteḥ apakṣa dharmaḥ na hetuḥ iti kutas iyam āśaṅkā tatas teṣām lakṣaṇa anusāriṇām niyama āśaṅkā parihāra artham ca upacāra karaṇam iti 
[14,ii]	iha vyavaccheda phala tvāt śabda prayogasya avaśyam eva avadhārayitavyam ṣaṣṭhī samāsāt ca pakṣa dharmaḥ iti atra na anyaḥ samāsaḥ sambhavati tathā ca pakṣasya eva dharmaḥ iti evam avadhāraṇāt tad aṃśa vyāptiḥ virudhyate iti viruddha lakṣaṇa tām udbhāvayan āha pakṣasya dharma tve tam pakṣam viśeṣaṇam anyatas vyavacchedakam apekṣate iti tad viśeṣaṇa apekṣasya dharmasya anyatra pakṣīkṛtāt anyasmin sa pakṣe ananuvṛttiḥ tathā hi yaḥ pakṣeṇa viśeṣyate sa pakṣasya eva bhavati na anyasya yathā yaḥ devadattasya putraḥ sa tasya eva putraḥ na yajñadattasya api tatas anyatra ananuvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā sādhāraṇa tā na syāt tadam śavya āpti virodhaḥ iti yāvat sādhāraṇa tāyāḥ ca tad aṃśa vyāptyā pratipādanāt tatas yadi pakṣa dharmaḥ na tad aṃśena vyāptiḥ atha tad aṃśa vyāptiḥ na pakṣa dharmaḥ iti vyāhatam lakṣaṇam iti 
[15,i^1]	nanu ca tad aṃśavyāptiḥ nāma sādhya dharmasya vyāpakasya tatra hetau sati tad ādhāra dharmiṇi bhāva eva vyāpyasya vā hetoḥ tatra eva vyāpake sādhya dharme sati eva bhāvaḥ iti sva sādhya avinābhāva lakṣaṇā vakṣyate na ca anayā avaśyam pakṣīkṛtāt anyatra vṛttiḥ ākṣipyate yatas lakṣaṇa vyāghātaḥ āśaṅkyeta tathā hi tatra eva pakṣīkṛte sati eva sādhya dharme hetuḥ vartamānaḥ tad aṃśa vyāptim pratipadyate eva yā eva ca asya sādhya dharmiṇi svasādhya avinā bhāvitā sā eva gamaka tve nibandhanam na anya dharmiṇi sa ca svasādhya avinābhāvaḥ pratibandha sādhaka pramāṇa nibandhanaḥ na sa pakṣe kvacid bahulam vā saha bhāva mātra darśana nibandhanaḥ na hi loha lekhyam vajram pārthiva tvāt kāṣṭha ādi vat iti tat anyatra pārthiva tvasya loha lekhya tā vinābhāvaḥ api tathā abhāvaḥ bhavati 
[15,i^2]	yadi ca pakṣīkṛtāt anyatra eva vyāptiḥ ādarśayitavyā iti niyamaḥ tadā sattvam katham kṣaṇika tām bhāveṣu pratipādayet yaḥ hi sakala padārtha vyāpinīm kṣaṇīka tām icchati tam prati kasyacid sa pakṣasya eva abhāvāt yat api kaiścid jvālā ādeḥ kṣaṇika tvam abhyupagamyate tat api na pratyakṣataḥ kṣaṇa vivekasya ati sūkṣma tayā anupalakṣaṇāt anyatra eva ca vyāptiḥ ādarśanīyāḥ na sādhya dharmiṇī api iti kaḥ ayam nyāyaḥ evam hi kālpanika tvam hetu lakṣaṇasya pratipannam syāt na vastu bala pravṛtta tvam tasmāt sva sādhya pratibandhāt hetuḥ tena vyāptaḥ sidhyati sa ca viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā sādhya dharmiṇī api sidhyati iti na kiñcid anyatra anuvṛtti apekṣayā atas eva anyatra uktam yat kvacid dṛṣṭam tasya yatra pratibandhaḥ tad vidaḥ tasya tat gamakam tatra iti vastu gatiḥ iti 
[16,i^1]	yat api anumeye atha tad talye sadbhāvaḥ ityādi lakṣaṇam tatra api sādhya dharmavān eva sa pakṣaḥ ucyate tatas sati eva sādhya dharme vā asti iti evaṃparam etat tatas ca tad dharmaṇaḥ sādhya dharmiṇaḥ api vāstavam sa pakṣa tvam na vyāvartate sādhya tvena iṣṭatayā icchā vi avasthita lakṣaṇena pakṣa tvena tasya nirākartum aśakyatvāt tasmāt tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanena svasādhya avinābhāvi tvasya pratibandha nibandhanasya anyathā tad ayogāt abhidhānāt na avaśya manyatra vṛttiḥ ākṣiptā iti katham idam āśaṅkitam satyam na eva idam āśaṅkanīyam yadi sarvasya hetoḥ pakṣīkṛte eva dharmiṇi sva sādhya pratibandhaḥ pramāṇataḥ niścetum śakyeta yathā sattva lakṣaṇasya svabhāva hetoḥ kṣaṇikatāyām sādhyāyām tādātmyam viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā 
[16,i^2]	kārya hetoḥ tu pakṣīkṛta dharmiṇā kasyacid svabhāva hetoḥ pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhanaḥ pratibandhaḥ katham parokṣe sādhya dharme gṛhyeta tasmāt tasya anyatra eva prasiddhiḥ iti tad viśeṣaṇa apekṣasya tatra apekṣaṇāt anyatra ananuvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā sambhava mātreṇa āśaṅkitā tadā hi anyatra āvartamānaḥ sādhya viparīta vyatireka tad ubhaya bahis bhāva ayogāt tad dharmiṇaḥ sādhya vṛtti vyavacchedābhyām sarva saṃgrahāt tatra saṃśaya hetuḥ bhavati syāt matam kvacid āśraye sattāyāḥ prāc pravṛtta pūrva gṛhīta vismṛta pratibandha sādhaka pramāṇa smṛtaye anyatra vṛttiḥ apekṣaṇīyā etat pariharati na ityādi 
[16,i^3]	na anyatra ananubhavattiḥ kutas ayogaḥ asambandhaḥ tad vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt pakṣasya na hi anya yoga vyavacchedena eva viśeṣaṇam bhavati kintu ayoga vyavacchedena api yatra dharmiṇi dharmasya sadbhāvaḥ saṃdihyate tatra ayoga vyavacchedasya nyāya prāpta tvāt atra ca dṛṣṭāntaḥyathā caitraḥ dharnuḥ dharaḥ iti caitre hi dhanurdhara tvam saṃdihyate kim asti na asti iti tatas caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ iti tad sadbhāva pratipādikā śrutīḥ pakṣa antaram adhanurdhara tvam śrotuḥ āśaṅka upasthāpitam nirākaroti iti ayoga vyavacchedaḥ atra nyāya prāptaḥ para abhimata vyavaccheda nirācikīrṣayā āha na anya yoga vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt anyatra ananuvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā iti sambandhaḥ 
[16,i^4_17,i]	atra api dṛṣṭāntaḥ yathā pārthaḥ dhanurddharaḥ iti sāmānya śabdaḥ api ayam dhanurdhara śabdaḥ prakaraṇa sāmarthya ādinā prakṛṣṭa guṇa vṛttiḥ iha pārthe hi dhanurddhara tvam siddham eva iti na ayoga āśaṅkā tādṛśam tu sa atiśayam kim anyatra asti na asti iti anya yoga śaṅkāyām śrotuḥ yadā pārthaḥ dhanurdharaḥ iti ucyate tadā anya yoga vyavacchedaḥ nyāya prāptaḥ pratipādya āśaṅkā upasthāpitayoḥ eva pakṣayoḥ parasparam virodhāt eka nirdeśena anya yoga vyavacchedasya nyāya bala āyāta tvāt tat iha pakṣe asti ayam dharmaḥ na vā iti saṃśītau pakṣa dharmaḥ iti ukte pakṣasya dharmaḥ eva na adharmaḥ dharmaḥ ca āśrita tvāt viśeṣaṇam tena ayogaḥ vyavacchidyate na anya yogaḥ tad aṃśa vyāptyā tasya pratipādita tvena dṛṣṭānte saṃdeha abhāvāt tad aṃśaḥ tad dharmaḥ iti tad śabdena pakṣaḥ parāmṛśyate na dharmaḥ dharmasya dharma asambhavāt aṃśaḥ ca dharmaḥ na eka deśaḥ pakṣa śabdena dharmi mātra vacanāt na tad aṃśaḥ tasya eka deśa abhāvāt iti 
[17,ii^1]	tasya pakṣa dharmasya sataḥ vyāptiḥ yaḥ vyāpnoti yaḥ ca vyāpyate tad ubhaya dharma tayā pratīteḥ yadā vyāpaka dharma tayā vivakṣyate tadā vyāpakasya gamyasya tatra āta sat saptabhyartha pradhānam etat na ādhāra pradhānam dharmāṇām dharmaā antara tva abhāvāt tena ayam arthaḥ yatra dharmiṇi vyāpyam asti tatra sarvatra bhāvaḥ eva vyāpakasya svagataḥ dharmaḥ vyāptiḥ tatas ca vyāpya bhāva apekṣayā vyāpyasya eva vyāpta tā pratītiḥ na tu evam avadhāryate vyāpakasya eva tatra bhāvaḥ iti hetvabhāva prasaṅgāt avyāpakasya api mūrta tva ādeḥ tatra bhāvāt na api tatra eva iti prayatna anantarīyaka tva ādeḥ ahetu ta āpatteḥ sādhāraṇaḥ ca hetuḥ syāt nitya tvasya prameyeṣu eva bhāvāt yadā tu vyāpya dharma tayā vivakṣā vyāpteḥ tadā vyāpyasya vā gamakasya tatra eva vyāpake gamye sati 
[17,ii^2]	yatra dharmiṇi vyāpakaḥ asti tatra eva bhāvaḥ na tad abhāve api vyāptiḥ iti atra api vyāpyasya eva tatra bhāvaḥ iti avadhāraṇam hetvabhāva prasakteḥ eva na āśritam avyāpyasya api tatra bhāvāt na api vyāpyasya tatra bhāvaḥ eva iti sa pakṣa eka deśa vṛtteḥ ahetu tva prāpteḥ sādhāraṇasya ca hetu tvam syāt prameya tvasya nityeṣu avaśyaṃbhāvāt iti vyāpya vyāpaka dharmatā saṃvarṇanam tu vyāpteḥ ubhayatra tulya dharma tayā eka ākārā pratītiḥ saṃyogi vat mā bhūt iti pradarśana artham tathā hi pūrvatra ayoga vyavacchedena avadhāraṇam uttaratra anya yoga vyavacchedena iti kutas ubhayatra eka ākāra tā vyāpteḥ tat uktam liṅge liṅgī bhavati eva liṅginī eva itarat punar niyamasya viparyāse asambandhaḥ liṅga liṅginoḥ iti 
[18,i_19,i]	etena ācāryeṇa saṃyoga balāt gamaka tve yaḥ doṣaḥ uktaḥ na ca kenacid aṃśena na saṃyogī hutāśanaḥ dhūmaḥ vā sarvathā tena prāptam dhūmāt prakāśanam iti saḥ iha na avatarati iti ākhyātam bhavati tathā hi saṃyogasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt eṣa prasaṅgaḥ na tu vyāpteḥ na hi yādṛśī vyāpaka dharma vyāptiḥ tādṛśī eva vyāpya dharmaḥ iti tathā ca āha sambandhaḥ yadi api dviṣṭhaḥ sahabhāvi aṅga liṅginoḥ ādhāra ādheya vat vṛttiḥ tasya saṃyogi vat na tu iti tena vyāpakaḥ vyāpyaḥ na bhavati vyāpyaḥ ca na vyāpakaḥ iti tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ iti vacanāt na saṃyogi pakṣa uktaḥ doṣaḥ na api ubhayoḥ gamya gamaka tā prasaṅgaḥ yathā uktāt hetu lakṣaṇāt vyāpakasya eva gamya tva pratīteḥ vyāpyasya eva gamakatā sampratyayāt iti 
[19,ii]	yadi tarhi pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ iti etat hetu lakṣaṇam tatas pakṣa dharma tvam tad aṃśa vyāptiḥ ca iti dvi rūpaḥ hetuḥ syāt anyatra ca tri rūpaḥ uktaḥ tat katham na vyāghātaḥ iti āha etena tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanena anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vai uktaḥ veditavyaḥ iti sambandhaḥ anvaya vyatireka rūpa tvāt vyāpteḥ iti bhāvaḥ tathā hi yaḥ eva yena anvitaḥ yat nivṛttau ca nivartate saḥ eva tene vyāptaḥ ucyate iti tad ātmaka tvāt vyāpteḥ vyāpti vacanena anvaya vyatireka abhidhānam tatas vyāpti vacanena rūpa dvaya abhidhānāt na vyāghātaḥ iti 
[19,iii_19,iv^1]	tau ca jñapaka hetu adhikārāt niścitau niścayaḥ ca tayoḥ na ekena eva pramāṇena api tu yathāsvam yasya yat ātmīyam pramāṇam niścāyakam tena yasya ca yat niścāyakam pramāṇam tat uttaratra vakṣyati anvayaḥ vyatirakaḥ vā iti tulya ka kṣatā sūcanā arthaḥ vā śabdaḥ tena sādharmya vaidharmyavatoḥ prayogayoḥ ekena eva dvitīya gateḥ vidhi pratiṣedha rūpa tayā vyāvṛtti bhede api paramārthataḥ tādātmyāt na ubhaya upadarśanam iti sūcitam bhavati vyatirekaḥ hi sādhya nivṛttau liṅgasya nivṛtti dharmaka tvam svabhāva bhūtaḥ dharmaḥ iti anvaya rūpa tā vastutas asya na virudhyate pakṣa dharmaḥ ca kim yathāsvam pramāṇena niścitaḥ uktaḥ iti sambandhaḥ niścaya prasaṅgena saḥ api atra pratipādyate niścitasya gamaka tvām ākhyātum iti pradarśana arthaḥ vā śabdaḥ 
[19,iv^2]	pratyakṣeṇa ca svayam sva lakṣaṇa ākāra tve api anantara sāmānya vikalpa jananāt prasiddhiḥ upacārataḥ niścayaḥ ucyate pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya anadhigata artha adhigantṛ tva abhāvam darśayitum tena yadi api sāmānya rūpam liṅgam avasthāpyate tathā api sva lakṣaṇa pratītiḥ eva tad vyavasthā nibandhanam iti pratyakṣataḥ pakṣa dharmasya sādhya dharmiṇi prasiddhiḥ ucyate etat ca anantaram eva vyaktīkariṣyate anumānataḥ vā sādhya dharmiṇi pakṣa dharmasya prasiddhi rniścayaḥ pramāṇa phala bhedāt ca anumānataḥ anumānena niścayaḥ iti āha atra udāharaṇe yathākramam yathā pradeśe dhūmasya dhūma sāmānyasya pratyakṣataḥ niścayaḥ iti 
[20,i_21,ii]	yaḥ tu manyate yaḥ pradeśaḥ agni sambandhī saḥ apratyakṣaḥ yaḥ tu pratyakṣaḥ nabhaḥ bhāga rūpa āloka ādi ātmā dhūmavat tayā dṛśyamānaḥ na saḥ agnimān atas katham pradeśe dhūmasya pratyakṣatas prasiddhiḥ tasmāt dhūmaḥ eva dharmī yuktaḥ sa agniḥ ayam dhūmaḥ dhūma tvāt iti evam sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ iti tasya api sa agneḥ dhūma avayavasya apratyakṣa tvāt paridṛśyamānasya ca ūrddhava bhāga vartinaḥ agninā saha āvṛtteḥ katham dhūma sāmānyasya sādhya dharmiṇi pratyakṣatas prasiddhiḥ dhūma avayavī pratyakṣaḥ iti ced na avayava vyatirekeṇa tasya abhāvāt loka adhyavasāyataḥ tasya eka tve vā pradeśasya api tāvataḥ kalpitam eka tvam na nivāryate pradeśe eva ca lokaḥ agni pratipadyate na dhūme deśa kāla ādi apekṣayā eva ca kārya hetuḥ gamakaḥ yat āha iṣṭam viruddha kārye api deśa kāla ādi apekṣaṇam anyathā vyabhicāri syāt bhasma iva aśīta sādhane iti tatas deśa ādi apekṣā agni sādhane dhūmavat tayā gṛhyamāṇasya deśasya dharmitā na virudhyate yathā balākāvataḥ vṛkṣa ādeḥ ddeśa ādi apekṣayā jala sādhana tvam iti śabde vā kṛtaka tvasya pratyaya bheda bhiditvā ādinā anumānena iti 
[21,iii]	atra yathā upavarṇitam pratyakṣataḥ pakṣa dharmasya sādhya dharmiṇi prasiddhau abhiprāyam apratipadyamānaḥ kumārilaḥ katham pratyakṣeṇa avikalpena sāmānya ātmanaḥ liṅgasya dhūma ādeḥ svarūpa grahaṇam api tāvat yujyate dharmiṇaḥ vā kutas eva tad sambandha grahaṇam iti pratyavatasthe tena hi pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvāt ca anumāna ādeḥ ddharmam pratyanimitta tvam iti etat bhāṣyam katham pratyakṣa pūrva tvam anumāna ādinaḥ bhavet yadā smṛtya samartha tvāt nirvikalpa indriyasya dhīḥ na ca avikalpya liṅgasya dharmi sambandhayoḥ tathā gṛhītiḥ iti ākṣipya pratyakṣa agrahaṇam yat tu liṅga ādeḥ avikalpanāt tat neṣṭa tvāt vikalpasya api artha rūpa upakāriṇaḥ asti syālocana ajñānam prathamam nirvikalpakam bāla mūka ādi vijñāna sadṛśam śuddha vastu jam tatas param punar vastu dharmaiḥ jāti ādibhiḥ yayā buddhyā avasīyate sā api pratyakṣa tvena sammatā 
[22,i^1]	iti bruvatā saugatānām eva ayam liṅga dharmitad sambandha agrahaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ doṣaḥ yeṣām avikalpakam eva pratyakṣam na asmākam sa vikalpam api pratyakṣam icchatām iti uktam bhavati tatas tad upavarṇita doṣa pratividhānāya āha sa dhūmam hi ityādi ayam atra samudāya arthaḥ pratyakṣam hi purovasthitam auttara adharyeṇa dhūma pradeśa ādikam vidhi rūpeṇa dhūma ādi sva lakṣaṇam sakala sajātīya vijātīya vyāvṛttam ca sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ sarvāsām artha mātrāṇām parasparam asaṃkīrṇa rūpa tvāt tad sāmarthya bhāvi yathā sthānam anukurvat pāśca attya vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpa dvayam janayati yena dhūma pradeśa ākhyau dharma dharmiṇau tayoḥ ca auttara adharyam evam etat na anyathā iti vikalpayati yathā anubhavam abhyāsa pāṭava ādi pratyaya antara sahakāriṇām vikalpānām udayāt tatas dharma dharmiṇoḥ svarūpa niścayaḥ sambandha niścayaḥ ca pratyakṣa nibandhanaḥ sampadyate 
[22,i^2]	tathā hi ayam eva dhūma pradeśayoḥ sambandhasya niścayaḥ yaḥ atra ayam iti adhyavasāyaḥ sa ca avikalpena api pratyakṣeṇa yathā uktena prakāreṇa sampāditaḥ eva na ca auttara adharya avasthitāt vastu dvayāt anyaḥ eva kaścid ādhāra ādheya bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ yatas tasya pratyakṣeṇa ananubhūta tvāt paścāt vikalpanam syāt vastu bhūtasya tasya anyatra niṣedhāt tasmāt ayam tat eva tathā avasthitam artha dvayam āśritya kalpanā samāropitaḥ eva tena sambandhaḥ sambandhi iti bheda antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepābhyām dharma dharmitayā vyavahāraḥ loke na tu pāramārthikaḥ sāmānya vyavahāraḥ api vijātīya vyāvṛttān eva bhāvān āśritya kalpanā samāropitaḥ eva pratanyate teṣām eva bhinnānām api anubhava dvāreṇa vijātīya vyāvṛtta tayā prakṛtyā eva eka ākāra parāmarśa pratyaya hetutvāt tathā ca āha eka pratyavamarśa artha jñāna ādi eka artha sādhane bhede api niyatāḥ kecid svabhāvena indriya ādi vat 
[23,i]	tatas sāmānya vikalpa janana dvārā tad pratibhāsinaḥ dhūma ākārasya vijātīya vyāvṛtta rūpasya sāmānya rūpa tayā pratyakṣeṇa eva gṛhīta tvāt na hi vijātīya vyāvṛttiḥ vyāvṛttāt anyā eva kācid yasyāḥ pratyakṣeṇa agrahaṇam syāt tasmāt yathā paridṛṣṭam dhūma ādi sva lakṣaṇam eva anyatas vyāvṛtta ātmanā vikalpyate iti pratipatradhyavasāya vaśāt smṛtiḥ eva dvividhaḥ vikalpaḥ pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvī vastutas punar nirviṣayaḥ eva tatas yat āha sāmānyasya ananubhūta tayā smārtam etat abhedena vijñānam iti yaḥ vadet tasya vandhyā sute api asti nūnam smaraṇa śakta tā iti tat api apāstam iti 
[23,ii]	athavā aparam kumārilena abhihitam sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam pratyakṣam sāmānya lakṣaṇa viṣayam anumānam iti vacanāt dhūma ādi sāmānyam anumāna grāhyam eva tatra ca anavasthāḥ liṅga grāhiṇaḥ api anumānasya tad anya liṅga balena utpatteḥ tasya ca sāmānya rūpa tayā tad anya anumāna māna viṣaya tvāt tathā tad anyasya api iti kasyacid ekasya api liṅginaḥ pratipattiḥ yuga sahasraiḥ api na sambhavati kim aṅga punar ekena puruṣa āyuṣkeṇa iti tathā ca āha sāmānyam na anumānena vinā yasya pratīyate na ca liṅga vinirmuktam anumānam pravartate asāmānyasya liṅga tvam na ca kenacid iṣyate na ca anavagatam liṅgam kiñcid asti prakāśakam tasya api ca anumānena syāt anyena gatiḥ punar tad udbhūtiḥ ca liṅgāt syāt sāmānya jñāna saṃhitāt tasya ca api anumāna tvam liṅgena ca tad udbhavaḥ anumāna antarāt eva jñātena evam ca kalpane liṅga liṅgī anumānānām ānantyāt eka liṅgini gatiḥ yuga sahastreṣu bahuṣu api na vidyate 
[23,iii]	iti āśaṅkayā āha sa dhūmam hi ityādi evam manyate yasya anumā anantareṇa sāmānyam na pratīyate bhavatu tasya ayam doṣaḥ asmākam tu pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvinā api vikalpena prakṛti vibhramāt sāmānyam pratīyate liṅga vikalpasya ca sva lakṣaṇa darśana āśraya tvāt paramparayā vastu pratibandhāt avisaṃvādaka tvam maṇi prabhāyām iva maṇi bhrānteḥ kārya hetu tvam api vikalpa avabhāsinaḥ dhūma sāmānyasya liṅga tayā avasthāpyamānasya kārya darśana āśraya tayā tad adhyavasāyāt ca na hi dhūmasva lakṣaṇasya liṅgatā avasthāpayitum yuktā tasya asādhāraṇasya sa pakṣe vṛtti abhāvāt tad aṃśa vyāpti ayogāt sādhya sādhana saṃkalpe vastu darśanā sambhavāt ca iti 
[24,i]	yat tu uktam sāmānya lakṣaṇa viṣama numānam iti tatra na evam avadhāryate sāmānya lakṣaṇa viṣayam anumānam eva iti pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya api tad viṣaya tvāt tad anyasya ca vikalpasya kintu sāmānya lakṣaṇa viṣayam eva anumānam iti avadhāryate sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tva niṣedha artham iti tatra saha dhūmena vartate iti sa dhūmaḥ pakṣa dharma tā pratipadana artham evam uktam vidhi vikalpasya ca etat eva bījam tam sa dhūmam pradeśam dṛṣṭavataḥ pratyakṣeṇa iti sambandhaḥ kīdṛśam artha antara vivikta rūpam artha antaraiḥ sajātīya vijātīyaiḥ viviktam asaṅkīrṇam rūpam asya iti vigrahaḥ sarva bhāvānām sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ svabhāvasāṅkarya abhāvāt anyathā sarvasya sarvatra upayogāt ati prasaṅgaḥ anena pratiṣedha vikalpasya nimittam ākhyātam sāmānya utprekṣāyāḥ ca bījam tat uktam itaretara bhedaḥ asya bījam saṃjñā yad arthikāḥ iti 
[24,ii_25,i]	tathā hi artha antara vyāvṛttim paraspara vyāvṛttānām api samānām utpaśyataḥ bhinnam eṣām rūpam tirodhāya abhinnam svabhāvam āropayantī kalpanā utpadyate asādhāraṇa ātmanā iti artha antara vyāvṛttena svabhāvena na tu yathā kumārilaḥ manyate artha antara vivekaḥ abhāva pramāṇa grāhyaḥ na pratyakṣa avaseyaḥ iti na hi vastu bala bhāvinā pratyakṣeṇa anyathā darśana sambhavaḥ bhrānta tā prasaṅgāt tena ātmanā dṛṣṭavataḥ sataḥ puṃsaḥ anantaram smārtam liṅga jñānam utpadyate iti sambandhaḥ smṛtiḥ eva smārtam liṅga pratibhāsi jñānam liṅga jñānam anena pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvini vikalpe yat sāmānyam ābhāti tasya līṅga vyavasthām āha paramārthataḥ kim viṣayam yathā dṛṣṭa bheda parama artha viṣayam 
[25,ii_25,iv]	darśana vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpānām pramāṇa apramāṇa cintām ārabhate tatra teṣu darśana vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpeṣu tad ādyam yat etat asti hi ālocana ajñānam prathamam iti ādau vikalpa pravṛtteḥ bhavam iti ādyam ākhyātam asādhāraṇa viṣayam sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam darśanam tat eva pramāṇam na vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpau api tasya eva pramāṇa lakṣaṇa yoga ādi tarayoḥ ca tad asambhavāt tathā hi anadhigata viṣaya tvam artha kriyā sādhana viṣaya tvam ca pramāṇa lakṣaṇam tat darśanasya eva asti tatra ādyam iti apūrva artha vijñāna tvam ākhyātam asādhāraṇa viṣayam iti artha kriyā sādhana viṣaya tvam sva lakṣaṇasya eva artha kriyā sādhana tvāt 
[25,v^1]	tatra pratiṣedha vikalpasya tāvat pratyakṣa gṛhīta artha viṣaya tayā smṛti tvam pratipādayan āha tasmin asādhāraṇe tathābhūte artha antaraiḥ asaṅkīrṇa rūpe darśanena asaṅkīrṇa rūpa sāmarthya bhāvinā dṛṣṭe adhigate sati tathā hi vyatiriktam api bhāva aṃśāt abhāva aṃśam icchatāḥ bhāva aṃśaḥ svabhāvena asaṅkīrṇa rūpaḥ kalpanīyaḥ anyathā saḥ eva abhāva aṃśaḥ na sidhyet na ca svabhāvena asaṅkīrṇa rūpa tāyām asatyām pṛthak bhūta abhāva aṃśa sadbhāve api sā yuktimatī sva hetu bala āyātasya saṅkīrṇa rūpasya akiñcitkara abhāva aṃśa sambhave api tyāga ayogāt 
[25,v^2]	na ca tena eva tad vināśanam vināśa hetu ayogasya pratipādayiṣyamāṇa tvāt tena saṅkīrṇa rūpa vināśane ca varam sva hetoḥ eva svabhāvataḥ asaṅkīrṇa rūpāṇām udayaḥ astu kim parivrāḍma udaka nyāya upagamena tasmāt svabhāvataḥ eva bhāvānām para rūpa vikala tvam abhāva aṃśaḥ na anyaḥ sa ca tathābhūtaḥ darśanena gṛhītaḥ eva tasmin tathābhūte dṛṣṭe sa padārthaḥ yena vastunā asādhāraṇaḥ samāna svabhāvaḥ na bhavati tad rūpa vikala svabhāva tvāt tat asādhāraṇa tām tena tena ātad rūpeṇa asamāna svabhāva tām etat eva vyanakti 
[25,v^3]	tatas artha antarāt bhedam vailakṣaṇyam anya rūpam idam na bhavati iti abhilapantī abhimukhayantī dṛṣṭa vailakṣaṇye pravartamāna tayā smṛtiḥ utpannā pratyakṣa balena yadi tu liṅga balena utpadyeta vyavaccheda viṣayā api smṛtiḥ na syāt iti bhāvaḥ kim viṣayā atad vyāvṛtti viṣayā tad śabdena darśana viṣayasya vastunaḥ parāmarśaḥ kṛtaḥ na tat atat vijātīyam atasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ atad vyāvṛttiḥ sā viṣayaḥ yasyāḥ sā tathā atha adṛṣṭaḥ eva artha antarebhyaḥ bhedaḥ mayā api kalpyate iti pratipad tradhyavasāyāt ca evam uktam parāmarthataḥ nirviṣaya tvāt sā na pramāṇam na abhāva pramāṇa phalam iti arthaḥ na hi smṛti janaka tvena pramāṇatā yuktā kasmāt na pramāṇam yathādṛṣṭasya ākāraḥ abhyāsa pāṭava ādi pratyaya antara sāpekṣaḥ viśeṣaḥ tasya grahaṇāt na hi dṛṣṭim iti eva vikalpena gṛhyate darśana aviśeṣāt sarva ākāreṣu vikalpa udaya prasaṅgāt api tu kaścid eva abhyāsa ādi pratyaya apekṣaḥ iti ākāra grahaṇena ācaṣṭe 
[26,i]	bhavatu yathā dṛṣṭa ākāra grahaṇam pramāṇam tu kasmāt na bhavati iti parasya tad ukta pramāṇa lakṣaṇa viraham darśayan āha prāk ālocanā jñāna udaya kāle asādhāraṇam assaṅkīrṇa rūpam dṛṣṭvā asādhāraṇam artha antara rūpam na bhavati iti abhilapataḥ vikalpayataḥ pratiṣedha vikalpasya apūrva artha adhigama abhāvāt apūrva artha vijñāna tā virahāt apūrva artha vijñānam ca pramāṇam bhavatā ucyate iti bhāvaḥ 
[27,i]	yadi uktena prakāreṇa pratiṣedha vikalpaḥ na pramāṇam vidhi vikalpaḥ tarhi pramāṇam bhaviṣyati na hi tasya apūrva artha vijñāna tva abhāvaḥ sambhavati tad pratibhāsinaḥ anugatasya sāmānya ākārasya asādhāraṇa rūpa avalambinā darśanena anadhigamāt tat kutas asya aprāmāṇyam tat uktam tatas param punarvastu ityādi tat etat kumarila vacanam āśaṅkya vidhi vikalpasya api prāmāṇyam apanudan āha artha kriyā sādhanasya sva lakṣaṇasya ālocanā jñānena darśanāt adṛṣṭasya punar tad sādhanasya artha kriyā sādhanasya svabhāvasya vikalpena apratipatteḥ vidhi vikalpaḥ na pramāṇam yadi api tena anadhigatam sāmānyam adhigamyate iti varṇyate tathā api tat artha kriyā sādhanam na bhavati iti tad adhigantā taimirika ādi jñāna prakhyaḥ vidhi vikalpaḥ na pramāṇam 
[27,ii]	tatas param punar vastu dharmaiḥ jāti ādibhiḥ yayā buddhyā avasīyate iti ca ucyate tatra punar vastu grahaṇena nirvikalpaka pratyakṣa viṣayasya eva vastunaḥ jāti ādi viśiṣṭasya vikalpa buddhyā avasāyaḥ ucyate tasya ca nirvikalpa jñānena eva adhigamāt na tatra prāmāṇyam jāteḥ tu artha kriyā sādhana tva abhāvāt anadhigatāyāḥ adhigame api keśa ādi jñānasya iva na prāmāṇyam atas eva artha kriyā sāmarthya virahiṇā sāmānyena indriyāṇām samprayoga abhāvāt pratyakṣa tā api asambhavinī cakāreṇa smṛti tvāt ca iti pūrva ukta kāraṇa samuccayaḥ smṛti tvam ca asya uttaratra pratipādayiṣyate anumāna vat iti vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ yathā pratyakṣeṇa artha kriyā sādhane pradeśa ākhyaiḥ dharmiṇī adhigate api anadhigatasya agneḥ artha kriyā sādhanasya āsāmāni a ākāreṇa parokṣasya sva lakṣaṇa ākāreṇa pratipattum aśakyatvāt pratipattiḥ na evam vidhi vikalpena sāmānyakāreṇa anadhigamartha kriyā sādhanam adhigamyate taisya ālocanā jñānena eva adhigamāt tasmin smṛtiḥ eva asau iti na pramāṇam iti 
[28,i]	artha kriyā sādhana viṣayam eva pramāṇam na itarat iti kutas etat iti ced artha kriyā arthī hi puruṣaḥ yasmāt hita ahita prāpti parihāra arthī sarvaḥ na kākatālīya nyāyena kaścid eva prekṣāvān buddhi purva kārī pramāṇam apramāṇam vā pramāṇāt eva sarvadā pravarteya apramāṇāt mā kadācid vipralambha sambhavāt ubhayam anveṣate na vyasani tayā tatas ayam artha kriyā sādhana viṣayam eva pramāṇam bravīti tasya artha kriyā sādhane pravṛtti aṅga tvāt na itarat tad viparīta tvāt tathā hi pramāṇam avisaṃvāda kam apratārakam ucyate loke api yat ca artha kriyā sādhanam anadhigacchan na tatra pravartayati kutas eva tat prāpayet tat katham avisaṃvādaka tayā prekṣā pūrva kārī pramāṇam ācakṣīta 
[28,ii^1]	yadi evam sāmānyam api artha kriyā sādhanam eva tatas tad viṣayaḥ vidhi vikalpaḥ pramāṇam bhaviṣyati iti ced āha na cana eva sāmānyam kāñcid tad sādhya tayā upagatām abhinna jñāna abhidhāna lakṣaṇām anyām vā vyakti sādhyām artha kriyām upakalpayati kīdṛśam sva lakṣaṇa pratipatteḥ vyakti pratipatteḥ ālocanā jñāna saṃjñitāyāḥ urddham uttara kālam tad sāmarthya utpanna vikalpa vijñāna grāhyam iti tad śabdena sva lakṣaṇa pratipattiḥ sambadhyate tatas param punarvastu ityādi paraiḥ abhidhānāt evam bravīti darśana pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya pratyakṣa pramāṇa tām nirākartum 
[28,ii^2]	sarvam eva tu sāmānyam na kāñcid artha kriyām upakalpayati yat tu sāmānyam anumāna vikalpa grāhyam tat kāraṇa vyāpaka sambaddha liṅga niścaya dvāra āyātam sambaddha sambandhāt anadhigata artha kriyā sādhana viṣayām artha kriyām upakalpayati iti tad viṣayaḥ vikalpaḥ pramāṇam idam tu na evam adhigata tvāt artha kriyā sādhanasya ālocana ajñānena iti atra udāharaṇam yathā nīlam dṛṣṭvā nīlam iti jñāne pratibhāsamānam iti śeṣaḥ na sāmānyam kāñcid artha kriyām upakalpayati iti prakṛtena sambandhaḥ 
[29,i]	nanu ca liṅga vikalpa pratibhāsi sāmānyam prakṛtam tat kim anyat udāhriyate sarvasya darśana pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya para upagatām pratyakṣa pramāṇa tām tulya nyāyatayā nirākartum kāṃpu nar nīlam iti vikalpa jñāne darśana pṛṣṭha bhāvini pratibhāsamānam sāmānyam artha kriyām na upakalpayati yadi vyakti sādhyām tadā anyaḥ api padārthaḥ anyadīyām artha kriyām na upakalpayati iti tasya api anartha kriyā sādhana tvāt avastutva prasaṅgaḥ atha sva sādhyām tat asiddham abhinna jñāna abhidhāna lakṣaṇāyāḥ svasādhyāyāḥ karaṇāt iti āśaṅkayā āha tat eva hi yat tad ālocana ajñāne na upalabdham nīla sva lakṣaṇam nīla vyaktiḥ tathāvidha sādhya artha kriyā kāri tathāvidha śabdena sāmānyam atra abhipretam tādṛśa paryāya tvāt asya sādhāraṇa rūpasya ca tādṛśa tvāt tena tathāvidha sādhyām nīla sāmānya sādhyāma bhinna jñāna abhidhāna lakṣaṇām artha kriyām kartum śīlam asya sva lakṣaṇasya iti tat tathā uktam 
[29,ii]	evam manyate yathā bhinnāḥ api vyaktayaḥ kayācid pratyāsattyā tad eka kārya pratiniyama lakṣaṇayā tat ekam abhinnam sāmānyam upakurvanti tad apara sāmānya yogam antareṇa api anyathā anavasthā prasaṅgāt tathā abhinna jñāna abhidhāna ātmikām api artha kriyām sādhayiṣyanti kim apramāṇakena pramāṇa bādhitena ca sāmānyena upagatena tathā hi anumāna ādike jñāne yathāvidham asya aspaṣṭam rūpam pratibhāsate na tathāvidham vyaktiṣu dṛśyamānāsupalakṣayāmaḥ ekam eva hi vyakti darśana kāle spaṣṭam nīla ādi rūpam vibhāvayāmaḥ tat katham adṛṣṭa kalpa nayā ātmānam svayam eva vipralabhemahi vyakti rūpa saṃsargāt ayaḥ golaka van hivat avibhāvanam iti ced na sarvatra bheda abheda vyavasthāyāḥ abhāva prasaṅgāt asya uttarasya anyatra api sulabha tvāt na ca sāmānyasya dve rūpe staḥ spaṣṭam aspaṣṭam ca yena ekena darśane pratibhāseta anyena anumāna ādi jñāne padārtha dvaya upagama prasaṅgāt pratibhāsa bhedasya eva sarvatra bhāva bheda vyavasthā nibandhana tvāt sāmānyasya apara sāmānya prasakteḥ niḥsāmānyasya ca asya upagamāt 
[30,i^1]	etena etat api nirastam yat āha sarva vastuṣu buddhiḥ ca vyāvṛtti anugama ātmikā jāyate dvaya ātmaka tvena vinā sā ca na yujyate na ca atra anyatarā bhrāntiḥ upacāreṇa ca iṣyate dṛḍha tvāt sarvadā buddheḥ bhrāntiḥ tad bhānti vādinām iti yatas yadi indriya buddhim abhipretya ucyate tadā asiddham aspaṣṭasya nīla ādi ākārasya spaṣṭa nīla ādi ābhāsāyām tatra anupalakṣaṇāt spaṣṭasya api ca dvitīyasya anuyāyinaḥ tad bhāve ca vyakti dvaya antarālam api āpnuvataḥ katham tad anugamaḥ vyaktau ca upalabhyasya sataḥ tatra anupalakṣaṇam kutas na hi tasya vyakta avyakta rūpa sambhavaḥ eka tvāt 
[30,i^2]	tathā ca āha vyaktau ekatra sā vyakta abhedāt sarvatragāḥ yadi jātiḥ dṛśyeta sarvatra sā api na vyakta pekṣiṇi iti ekatra api ca vyaktau upalabhyamānāyām sakala trailokya vyāpi rūpam sakala sva āśraya vyāpi vā dṛśyeta na hi ekasyāḥ kiñcid dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭam vā nāma kṣaṇikatā ādi vat dṛṣṭāyām api ekatra eva āśraye darśana avasāyaḥ na sarvatra iti ced na vikalpena tad darśana abhyupagamāt na hi niścaya viṣayīkṛtam ca aniścitam ca iti yuktam tatas sarva gata rūpa darśane sarva arthānām darśana prasaṅgaḥ na hi tad darśane tad sahacāriṇaḥ upalabhyasya tad abhinna svabhāvasya ca anupalambhaḥ yuktaḥ tatas katham indriya buddheḥ dvi ātmaka tā 
[31,i]	atha anumāna ādi buddhim tasyām api sva lakṣaṇa apratibhāsanāt kutas dvaya ātmaka tvam na hi tāsu sāmānya grāhiṇīṣu aspaṣṭaḥ vyakti ākāraḥ iva lakṣyamāṇaḥ sva lakṣaṇa pratibhāsaḥ tad abhāve api tāsām bhavāt ākāra antareṇa ca sva jñāne apratibhāsanāt aneka ākāra ayogāt ekasya apratiprasaṅgāt ca tasmāt na iyam bhinna artha grāhiṇī abhinnā sāmānya buddhiḥ pratibhāti sva lakṣaṇa udbhavā satī kintu ana ādi vitatha vikalpa abhyāsa vāsanā janitā satī tathā avabhāsate dṛḍha tvam ca buddheḥ na avināśi tvam kṣaṇika tva abhyupagamāt kintva bādhyamāna tvam na ca asyāḥ tat sambhavati leśataḥ bādhakasya ukta tvāt vistarataḥ tu syāt vāda bhaṅgāt yathāvasaram iha eva tatra tatra vidhāsyamānāt bādhakam avadhāryam tasmāt yathā vyaktayaḥ sāmānya antaram antareṇa tat ekam upakurvanti tathā abhinna jñāna abhidhāne api pravartayiṣyanti iti tat eva nīla sva lakṣaṇam sāmānya sādhya tva upagata artha kriyā kāri 
[31,ii^1]	yaḥ tu sāmānyam na anyat iṣṭam ced tasya vṛtteḥ niyākam go tvena api vinā kasmāt go buddhiḥ na niyamyate yathā tulye api bhinna tve keṣucid vṛtti avṛtti tā go tva ādeḥ animittā api tatha buddhiḥ bhaviṣyati iti pūrva pakṣayitvā viṣayeṇa hi buddhīnām vinā na utpattiḥ iṣyate viśeṣāt anyat icchanti sāmānyam tena tat dhruvam tāḥ hi tena vinā utpannā mithyā syuḥ viṣayāt ṛte na tu anyena vinā vṛttiḥ sāmānyasya iha duṣyati iti mithyātva prasaṅga doṣaḥ uktaḥ na asau tathāgata samayanayā avadāta buddhīn bādhate sāmānya buddhīnām bādhaka pratyaya nibandhanasya mithyātvasya upagata tvāt tathā hi kasmāt sāsnādimatsu eva go tvam yasmāt tad ātmakam 
[31,ii^2]	tādātmyam asya kasmāt ced svabhāvāt iti gamyatām iti vacanāt vyakti svabhāvam ca sāmānyam na ca asādhāraṇam vyakti udaya vināśayoḥ ca na udaya vyaya yogi iti uyuktam viruddha dharma adhyāsataḥ bheda prasaṅgāt iti āha ca tādātmyam ced matam jāteḥ vyakti janmani ajāta tā nāśe anāśaḥ ca kena iṣṭaḥ tadvat ca ananvayaḥ na kim vyakti janmani ajāta ced āgatāḥ na āśraya antarāt prāk āsīt na ca tad deśe sā tayā saṅga tā katham vyakti nāśe na ced naṣṭā gatāḥ vyakti antaram na ca tat śūnye na sthitā deśe sā jātiḥ kva iti kathyatām vyakteḥ janma ādi yoge api yadi jāteḥ sa na iṣyate tādātmyam katham iṣṭam syāt anupapluta cetasām iti 
[32,i^1]	yadi nīla sva lakṣaṇam eva sāmānya sādhya artha kriyā kāri tat eva tarhi adhigacchan vikalpaḥ pramāṇam bhaviṣyati iti āha tat ca nīlakha lakṣaṇam tena ātmanā nīla sādhya artha kriyā kāriṇā svabhāvena dṛṣṭam eva ālocanā pratyayena tatas niṣpādita kriye karmaṇi aviṣeṣa ādhāyi vikalpa jñānam katham pramāṇam syāt atha matam sāmānyam eva tarhi adhigacchat nīla vikalpaḥ pramāṇam astu tat ca sāmānyam artha kriyā kāri yatas nīla sādhyām eva artha kriyām nīlena saha sambhūya kariṣyati 
[32,i^2]	vyakti svabhāvāni eva hi sāmānyāni iti āha na ca na eva tat sva lakṣaṇa grahaṇa uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ nīla vyakti darśana uttara kālam bhavana śīlasya liṅga grahaṇa uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ tu pūrva uktena prakāreṇa vyakti sādhya artha kriyā sāmānyasya kalpitasya vyavasthāpayitum śakyate iti bhāvaḥ nīla vikalpasya viṣayeṇa nīla sāmānyena nīla sādhya artha kriyā rañjana ādikā kriyate tasya vyakti svābhāvya ayoge sati kalpita rūpasya tad asambhavāt na ca nitya svabhāva tām ābibhrāṇena nīla vikalpasya viṣayeṇa nīla sādhya anyā vā artha kriyā kriyate krama yaugapadya virodhāt iti manyate 
[33,i]	tat evam nīlam dṛṣṭvā nīlam iti jñāne pratibhasamānam sāmānyam na kāñcid artha kriyām upakalpayati iti prasādhya anartha kriyā kāri viṣayasya api vikalpasya pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt ativyāptiḥ iti tatra apūrva artha vijñānam iti pramāṇa lakṣaṇe mīmāṃsakaiḥ viśeṣaṇam upādeyam iti darśayan āha tasmāt yatas evam anartha kriyā sādhana viṣaya tayā darśana pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya prāmāṇyam ayuktam tasmāt asmat abhimatam pramāṇam avisaṃvādi jñānam iti pramāṇa lakṣaṇam vyudasya anadhigata artha viṣayam pramāṇam tatra apūrva artha vijñānam pramāṇam iti api etasmin api āha upuruṣikayā anyasmin pramāṇa lakṣaṇe kriyamāṇe ati vyāpti parihārāya viśeṣaṇīyam viśeṣaṇam upādeyam katham viśeṣaṇīyam anadhigate sva lakṣaṇe iti anena hi viśeṣaṇena anumāna vikalpasya ca prāmāṇyam sidhyati ālocanā jñāna pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ ca vikalpasya prāmāṇyam vyudasyate iti sarvam sustham 
[33,ii]	tat evam vidhi vikalpasya anartha kriyā sādhana viṣaya tayā anadhigata sāmāni adhigame api prāmāṇyam nirākṛtya caśabda samuccitam smṛti tvam pratiṣedha vikalpena sādhāraṇam aprāmāṇya kāraṇam darśayan āha adhigate tu sva lakṣaṇe ālocanā jñānena tad sāmarthya janmā sva lakṣaṇa adhigama bala bhāvī vikalpaḥ tad anukārī sākṣāt anutpatteḥ ddarśana saṃskāra ādheya vaśat ca spaṣṭa nīla sva lakṣaṇa ākāra anukārī dṛśya vikalpyayoḥ ca ekīkaraṇāt evam ucyate vastutas tu na kiñcid asau anukaroti sa smṛtiḥ eva kutas kāryataḥ tad viṣaya tvāt na paramārthataḥ kāryam atra sva lakṣaṇe puruṣasya pravartanam tad adhyavasāyaḥ ca yatas ca kāryataḥ tad viṣaya tvāt smṛtiḥ eva atas na pramāṇam darśana bala utpannaḥ vikalpaḥ tathā hi smṛteḥ api anubhūta sva lakṣaṇa aṃśa viṣayāyāḥ na paramārthataḥ tad viṣaya tvam sva lakṣaṇasya indriya buddhau iva sphuṭa rūpa tayā smṛtau apratibhāsanāt kintu yathā uktāt kāryataḥ eva tat ca vidhi vikalpe api samānam iti katham asau smṛtiḥ na syāt iti 
[34,i]	tatra etat syāt nanu anumāna vikalpaḥ smṛti rūpaḥ api pramāṇam iṣyate tathā hi yat eva anagni vyāvṛttam vastu mātram mahānasa ādau anubhūtam āsīt tat eva pradeśa viśeṣe dhūma darśanāt smaryate tadvat vidhi vikalpaḥ api pramāṇam bhaviṣyati iti atas āha anadhigatasya vastunaḥ rūpasya anadhigateḥ iti evam manyate yat mahānasa ādau anagni vyāvṛttam vastu mātram prāk anubhūtam na tat tad deśa ādi sambandhi tayā eva anumāna vikalpena smaryate kintu yatra pradeśe prāk ananubhūtam tad sambandhi tayā tatas sādhya dharmi dṛṣṭānta dharmi grāhi darśana dvayān adhigatasya anagni vyāvṛttasya vastu rūpasya ayoga vyavacchedena adhigamāt yuktam asya prāmāṇyam na tu darśana pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya tad viparīta tvāt iti 
[34,ii]	yadi nāma anadhigatam vastu rūpam na adhigacchati pramāṇam tu kasmāt na bhavati iti ced āha vastu adhiṣṭhāna tvāt ityādi vastu adhiṣṭhāna tvam ca pramāṇa vyavasthāyāḥ pramāṇa vyāpāra viṣayam abhipretya ucyate na ālambana lakṣaṇam anyathā anumānasya parikalpita sāmānya ālambana tayā vastu adhiṣṭhāna tva abhāvāt avyāpinī pramāṇa vyavasthā syāt yadi vastu adhiṣṭhānā pramāṇa vyavasthā katham viprakṛṣṭa viṣayāyāḥ anupalabdheḥ prāmāṇyam iti ced tatra api pradhāna ādi vikalpasya eva bhāvānupādāna tayā sādhya tvāt tasyāḥ api vastu adhiṣṭhāna tā asti eva iti adoṣaḥ 
[35,i]	atha vastu adhiṣṭhānā eva pramāṇa vyavasthā iti kutas etat iti āha artha kriyāyām sukha duḥkha lakṣaṇāyām yat yogyam śaktam tad viṣaya tvāt tad arthinām artha kriyā arthinām pravṛtteḥ prāpti tyāga lakṣaṇāyāḥ yadi nām artha kriyā yogye tad arthinām pravṛttiḥ tathā api katham vastu adhiṣṭhānā pramāṇa vyavasthā artha kriyā yogya adhiṣṭhānā hi tathā sati syāt iti ced āha artha kriyāyām yat yogyam tat lakṣaṇam eva hi vastu tatas artha kriyā yogya adhiṣṭhāna tvena vastu adhiṣṭhāna tvam katham na syāt iti bhāvaḥ 
[35,ii]	idam ca vastu āśrayeṇa pramāṇa vyavasthā pratipādanam anadhigate sva lakṣaṇaḥ iti ukte kadācid paraḥ brūyāt vastu mātra nibandhanāḥ hi pramāṇa vyavasthā na sva lakṣaṇa āśraya eva tatas yadi api anadhigatam sva lakṣaṇam na adhigacchati tathā api anadhigata vastu rūpam adhigacchataḥ vikalpasya prāmāṇyam bhaviṣyati iti tad asiddha tā udbhāvanā artham uktam anadhigata vastu rūpa ityādi tad asiddha tā udbhāvane ca anadhigata vastu rūpa adhigantuḥ eva prāmānyam na itarasya iti kutas iti paryanuyoge artha kriyā yogya ityādi uktam tathā ca vastu viṣayam api prāmāṇyam bruvatā sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam eva uktam bhavati tasya eva artha kriyā sāmarthya lakṣaṇa tvāt sāmānyasya ca tad viparīta tvāt iti manyate 
[35,iii]	punar api anubhava uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ nīla vikalpasya prāmāṇyam apanetum upacaya hetum āha tatas api yathā uktāt vikalpāt na kevalam nīla sva lakṣaṇa anubhavāt vastuni eva sva lakṣaṇaḥ eva tat adhyavasāyena sva lakṣaṇa adhyavasāyena anyathā tatra pravṛtti ayogāt puruṣasya pravṛtte adhigate sva lakṣaṇe tad sāmarthya janmā vikalpaḥ na pramāṇam iti sambandhaḥ pūrvam anadhigata vastu rūpa an adhigateḥ aprāmāṇyam uktam adhunā tu adhigatasya eva adhigamāt iti vidhi pratiṣedha rūpa tayā upapattyoḥ bhedaḥ yat vā kāryataḥ tad viṣaya tvāt iti yat uktam tat eva upacaya hetu vyājena sphuṭīkṛtanam 
[36,i^1]	yadi nāma tat adhyavasāyena vastuni eva puruṣasya pravṛttiḥ tathā api anadhigata sāmānya grāhiṇaḥ asya darśanāt pṛthak prāmāṇyam kim iti na iṣyate iti ced āha pravṛttau sva lakṣaṇaḥ eva satyām pratyakṣeṇa ālocanā jñāna ākhyena abhinna yogakṣema tvāt yogaḥ aprāptasya viṣayasya pariccheda lakṣaṇā prāptiḥ kṣemaḥ tad artha kriyā anuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇam paripālanam abhinnau yogakṣemau asya iti sa tathā uktaḥ tatra vikalpasya nirvikalpa pratyakṣeṇa abhinnaḥ yogaḥ sva lakṣaṇa adhyavasāyataḥ abhinnaḥ kṣemaḥ ālocanā vijñānāt iva vikalpāt api sva lakṣaṇaḥ eva pravṛtteḥ ayam asya abhiprāyaḥ yadi vikalpaḥ nirvikalpa cetasaḥ prameya antara viṣayaḥ tadā tatra eva puruṣam pravartayatu tad sādhyām artha kriyām adhigantum 
[36,i^2]	na eva vā pravartayet tad viṣaya tva abhimatasya sāmānyasya abhinna jñāna lakṣaṇāyāḥ eva artha kriyāyāḥ upagamāt vikalpa udayāt eva ca tad siddheḥ na hi nīla anubhavāt prameya antara viṣayāḥ pīta ādi pratyayāḥ puruṣam nīla vastuni pravartayanti sādhita artha kriyā vā kvacid api iti tasmāt ālocana ajñānān aiva ayam prameya antara viṣayaḥ viśeṣeṇa yaiḥ eva vyākhyāyate nirvikalpaka bodhena dvaya ātmakasya api vastunaḥ grahaṇam iti tatas nīla darśanasya eva nirvikalpasya prāmāṇyam yuktam na tat abhinna upayogasya smṛteḥ iva vikalpasya api darśanāt pṛthak eva anyathā niṣphalām pramāṇa antara kalpanām kurvataḥ smṛti chā dveṣa prayatna ādi pramāṇa manuṣajyate iti pramāṇānām iyattā viśīryeta iti 
[37,i^1]	yadā ekasmin eva nīla ādi vastuni dhārāvāhīni indriya jñānāni utpadyante tadā pūrveṇa abhinna yogakṣema tvāt uttareṣām indriya jñānānām aprāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ na ca evam atas anekāntaḥ iti pramāṇa saṃplava vādī darśayan āha pūrva pratyakṣa kṣaṇena ityādi etat pariharati na uttareṣām prāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ kutas nānā yogakṣema tvāt tathā hi pratikṣaṇam viṣaya pariccheda lakṣaṇaḥ yogaḥ tad artha kriyā anuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇaḥ ca kṣemaḥ paripālana rūpaḥ bhidyate tatas vipakṣe vṛtti abhāvāt na hetuḥ anaikāntikaḥ kadā nānā yogakṣema tvam kṣaṇa viśeṣa sādhya artha vāñchāyām yadā kṣaṇa viśeṣa sādhye arthe hita ahita lakṣaṇe vāñchā prāpti parihāra icchā yoginām para upakāram uddiśya bhavati kasyacid kathañcid kvacid upayogāt tadā 
[37,i^2]	yathā darśana mārge duḥkhe dharma jñāna kṣāntiḥ ddamānām anuśayānām vāsanām nirodhayati tad viruddha āśaya utpādanāt duḥkhe dharma jñānam kleśa vivikta tā lakṣaṇām nirvāṇa prāptim utpādayati anuśaya viruddha āśaya dārḍhya utpādanāt tat eṣām grāhakāṇi para citta jñānāni pṛthak eva pramāṇāni para hita ādhāna dīkṣāvatām ca samasta vastu vistara vyāpi jñāna āloka avabhāsita antarātmanām bhagavatām kaścid eva artha kṣaṇaḥ kasyacid eva para arthasya anugrāhakaḥ vibandhakaḥ vā iti sarva bhāvān pratikṣaṇam vīkṣamāṇānām adhyakṣa cetasām tad viṣa ya kṣaṇānām bhinna artha kriyāsu upayogataḥ nānā yoga kṣema tvāt 
[37,i^3]	tat yadi pratikṣaṇam kṣaṇa viveka darśinaḥ adhikṛtya ucyate tadā bhinna upayogi tayā pṛthak prāmāṇyāt na anekāntaḥ atha sarva padārtheṣu ekatva adhyavasāyinaḥ sāṃvyavahārikān puruṣān abhipretya ucyate tadā sakalam eva nīla santānam ekam artham sthira rūpam tad sādhyām ca artha kriyām ekātmikām adhyavasyanti iti prāmāṇyam api uttareṣām aniṣṭam eva iti kutas anekāntaḥ iti darśayan āha sādhāraṇe hi iti 
[37,i^4]	tad santāna vartinām sarva kṣaṇānām ekatvena adhyavasitānām vyavahartṛbhiḥ yat sādhāraṇam pratikṣaṇam anya anyakāraṇa tayā vibhinnam api paramārthataḥ viparyāsāt ekatāya abhiniviṣṭam rañjana ādikam nīla ādika kārtyam tatra na teṣām uktareṣām jñāna kṣaṇānām sāmarthya sya artha prāpaṇa śakteḥ bhedaḥ pūrva pratyakṣa kṣaṇa viṣayaḥ eva tebhyaḥ api pravṛtteḥ ādyasya eva tatra prāmāṇyam tathā hi artha kriyā arthinām tad sādhana prāpaṇa samarthe jñāne pramāṇa vyavahāram kurvatām aviklava dhiyām artha kriyā sādhana bhedāt eva prāmāṇya bheda vyavahāraḥ jñāneṣu yuktaḥ anyathā smṛti ādeḥ api prāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ katham apākriyeta ādriyeta vā niṣphalā pramāṇa vyavasthā prekṣāvatā iti 
[38,i]	keṣām iva sādhāraṇe kārye na sāmarthya bhedaḥ iti āha apara apare ca te dhūmāḥ ca taiḥ pramitāḥ ca te sannikṛṣṭa agrayaḥ ca teṣu iva tat viṣayāṇam iva anumāna jñānām agni mātra sādhye arthe sandhukṣaṇa ādike vāñchite tad artha kriyā sādhana prāpaṇa vyakti bheda abhāvāt yathā prāmāṇya bhedaḥ na yuktaḥ viduṣām tathā atra api yadā tu pañcatapaḥ taptu kāmaḥ bhavati tadā aparāpara dhūma pramita sannikṛṣṭa agni viṣayāṇām api anumānānām sāmarthya bhedāt prāmāṇyam anivāritam eva 
[38,ii_39,i]	tat evam yathā nīlam dṛṣṭvā nīlam iti jñānam iti udāharaṇe nīla vikalpasya prāmāṇyam nirākṛtya prakṛte yojayan āha etena nīla sva lakṣaṇa darśana uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ nīla vikalpasya prāmāṇya nirākaraṇena tat neṣṭa tvāt vikalpasya artha rūpa upakāriṇaḥ iti brūvatā kumārilena pradeśa ādi darśana uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ dharmi vikalpasya tatā sambandha pratipatti kāle agni sva lakṣaṇa darśana sāmarthya bhāvinaḥ agni sāmānya viṣayasya sādhya dharma vikalpasya dhūma ālocanā jñāna pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ dhūma sāmāni avabhāsinaḥ liṅga vikalpasya ādi grahaṇāt dharma dharmi sambandha vikalpasya ca pramāṇa pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ dharmya ādi svarūpa mātra viṣaya ālocana ākhya pratyakṣa pūrvakasya na ca avikalpya liṅgasya dharmi sambandhayoḥ tathā gṛhītiḥ iti ākṣepa bhayāt yat abhyupagatam prāmāṇyam tat pratyuktam pratyākhyātam pūrvakam eva sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam darśanam yat pareṇa ālocanā jñānam iti vyavahṛta tat pramāṇam na tu tad vala bhāvī vikalpaḥ yathā uktena nyāyena iti sthitam etat pakṣa dharmasya sādhya dharmiṇi pratyakṣataḥ anumānataḥ vā prasiddhiḥ niścayaḥ iti tat evam pratyakṣataḥ pakṣa dharma niścayam bruvatā prasaṅgena darśana pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya prāmāṇya nirākaraṇāt pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham iti pratipāditam 
[39,ii^1]	yadi evam kasmat anumāna vyutpādana artham idam ārabhyate iti uktam na sāmānyena samyak jñāna vyutpādana artham iti saṅkhayā ādi vipratipattiḥ api atra tad viṣayāḥ nirastā eva parokṣa artha pratipatteḥ anumānam eva āśrayaḥ kasmāt yatas pakṣa dharmaḥ eva tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ eva ca hetuḥ kāraṇam tasyāḥ na anyaḥ iti abhidhānāt parokṣa artha viṣayam sarvam pramāṇam anumāne antarbhāvitam iti saṅkṣepataḥ saṅkhayā vipratipattiḥ samyak jñāna viṣayā nirastā 
[39,ii^2]	tathā vyāpaka aṃśasya gamya tva pratīteḥ tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanena sāmānya viṣayam anumānam na sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam iti ākhyātam tasya asādhāraṇa tvāt asādhāraṇasya ca vyāpaka tva ayogāt vikalpa aviṣaya tvāt ca tatra tad ādyam asādhāraṇa viṣayam iti ācakṣāṇena sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam eva pratyakṣa muktam darśanam eva pramāṇam iti ākhyānāt pramāṇam eva phalam iti sūcitam tasya artha pratīti rūpa tvāt tathā tasya dvidhā prayogaḥ iti vakṣyamāṇa tvāt para artha anumānam kathayiṣyate tasya trirūpa liṅga ākhyāna rūpa tvāt saṅkṣepataḥ ca anumāna vyutpādanam api abhimatam tat ca sarvatra asya iva iti kasmāt anumāna vyutpādana artham iti uktam 
[40,i]	satyam prādhānyāt tu tad grahaṇam tatā hi pradhāna puruṣa artha upayoginaḥ tattvasya catur ārya satya lakṣaṇasya anumānataḥ eva niścayāt tasya prādhānyam tathā pratyakṣe api viṣaye vivāda sambhave na anumānāt anyat nirṇaya nibandhanam iti atas api asya prādhānyam pravartaka tvāt ca prādhānyam asya tathā hi yad anubhūta phalam sukha duḥkha sādhanam anubhūyamāna phalam vā dṛśyamānam tad pravṛtti viṣayaḥ nispanna tvāt phalasya tasmāt yat anāgata phalam sukha duḥkha sādhanam pratyakṣam api tatra api anumānam eva pravartakam na hi tasya anāgate sukha duḥkhe prati yogyatām pratyakṣam nirddhārayati phalasya parokṣa tvāt tat uktam na hi apratyakṣe kārye kāraṇa bhāva gatiḥ iti 
[40,ii]	tasmāt pūrva anubhūta sukha duḥkha sādhana sādharmyāt pratyakṣa viṣayasya api vastunaḥ anāgata phala yogya tā niścayaḥ na pratyakṣataḥ tathā ca āha tat yathā dṛṣṭa sādharmyāt tathā aprasādhitam na anumeya tām atipatati iti katham tarhi dvayoḥ api pravartaka tvam na hi ābhyām artham paricchidya pravartamānaḥ artha kriyāyām visaṃvādyate iti uktam sukha duḥkha sādhanasya jala anala ādeḥ svarūpasya pratyakṣatas prasiddheḥ phalam anāgatam prati yogyatāyāḥ anumānataḥ iti ubhayoḥ api pravartaka tvam samyak jñāna pūrvaka tvam ca hita ahita prāpti parihārayoḥ aktam na tu anāgata phalam prati yogyatāyāḥ pratyakṣataḥ aniścayāt na hi arvāk darśinām bhāvi phala yogya tāyāḥ tatas niścayaḥ tatas prādhānyāt anumāna grahaṇam iti alam ati vistareṇa iti 
[41,i^1]	tatra svabhāva kārya anupalambhānām pakṣa dharma niścayaḥ tulya upāya sādhya tayā bhedena eva uktaḥ anvaya vyatireka niścayasya tu bhinna upāya sādhya tayā bhedena eva nirddeśaḥ kāryaḥ iti svabhāva hetau tāvat anvaya niścayam sva pramāṇa nibandhanam darśayan āha anvaya niścayaḥ api na kevalam pakṣa dharma niścayaḥ uktaḥ kintu anvaya niścayaḥ api svabhāva hetau ucyate iti śeṣaḥ sādhana dharma sya yat bhāva mātram sattā mātram mugdara ādi nimittantara anapekṣam tasya anubandhaḥ anugamanam vyāptiḥ tasya siddhiḥ yā sa svabhāva hetau anvaya niścayaḥ 
[41,i^2]	kasya sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anubandha siddhiḥ sādhya dharmasya sādhyaḥ ca asau asiddha tvāt dharma dharmi samudaya eka deśa tvāt dharmaḥ ca iti tathā uktaḥ yatra yatra sādhana dharmasya bhāvaḥ tatra tatra sādhya dharmasya api nimitta antara anapekṣaḥ bhavaḥ iti etasya arthasya siddhiḥ svabhāva hetau anvaya niścayaḥ katham punar sādhya dharmaḥ sādhana dharma bhāva mātram anubadhnāti tad bhāva tayā sa sādhana dharmaḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ yasya tasya bhāvatayā tad bhāva tayā yaḥ hi sādhana dharmaḥ sādhya dharmasya svabhāvaḥ sa katham tam na anubadhnīyāt nīrūpa tva prasaṅgāt 
[41,ii]	nanu tad svabhāva tve bheda abhāvāt katham sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ iti āha vastutas paramārthataḥ sādhya sādhana saṃkalpa kāle tu paramparayā tad ta d vayā vṛtta padārtha nibandhanāyām kalpanā buddhau bhedena pratibhāsanāt sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ na vihanyate na hi asau pāramārthikam sādhya sādhana dharmayā ūrddharmiṇaḥ ca kṛtaka tva ādau bhedam avalambate sambandha abhāvena sādhya sādhana bhāva ayogāt 
[41,iii^1]	eka artha samavāyaḥ kṛtaka tva anitya tva ādeḥ sambandhaḥ iti ced na tasya api tatas artha antara tve ayam anayoḥ asmin arthe samavāyaḥ iti sambandha abhāvasya tad avastha tvāt sambandha antara kalpanāyām ca anavasthā prasaṅgāt samavāyāt vṛtti kalpanāyām ca kṛtaka tva ādayaḥ nitya abhimateṣu api ātma ādiṣu varteran yaḥ eva hi kṛtaka tva ādeḥ śabde samavāyaḥ yabdalāt tatra eva tat vartate saḥ eva nitya abhimateṣu api tasya eka tvena upagata tvāt iti ātma ādau vṛttiḥ kṛtaka tva ādeḥ kena nivāryeta 
[41,iii^2]	atha yaḥ eva abhūtvā bhavana dharmā bhūtvā ca abhavana dharma asthira rūpaḥ bhāvaḥ tatra eva kṛtaka tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ vartante iti vyavasthāpyate sā eva tarhi abhūtvā bhavana svabhāva tā bhūtasya ca asthira svabhāva tā tad viparīta rūpa samāra upa vyavaccheda viṣayāyāḥ kalpanā buddheḥ nibandhanam kim na iṣyate tayā eva parama artha abhedavata ūrddharmayoḥ sādhya dharmiṇi vṛtteḥ kim antarāla gaḍunā kṛtaka tva ādinā vyatirekavatā upagatena tathā hi na sattā mātreṇa kṛtaka tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ sādhya dharma pratipatti nibandhanam teṣām sadā sannihita tvena anavaratam tad dharma pratīti prasaṅgāt kintu vikalpa pratibhāsinaḥ eva 
[41,iii^3]	sa ca vikalpaḥ sva pratibhāsinam evakāram bahīru upa tayā adhyavasitam anusaran kṛtakān iti ādi rūpa tām vastunaḥ pratipadyate paramārthataḥ asaṃsparśe api tad rūpasya paramparayā tad upādāna tvāt vyatiriktāḥ tu dharmāḥ tud utpatti nimitta mātra tayā parikalpyante tat varam yat eva tad kalpanāt nibandhanam tat eva tathāvidha vikalpa prasava nimittam astu tasya avaśyam abhyupagamanīya tvāt tad abhyupagame ca caritārthāḥ vyatirekavantaḥ dharmāḥ iti alam tad kalpanayā avaśyam ca vyatiriktā anitya tā dvāreṇa api vastunaḥ eva anavasthāyinam ātmānam pratipadyate tad anurūpa artha kriyā arthitayā pravṛtteḥ anyathā vyatiriktā anitya tayā nitya tvāt tad avagama arthi tvena ayam anitya sādhya artha kriyā arthī nityam śabda ādikam āśaṅka mānaḥ kim anitya tā vicāram prati āhīta āsthaḥ vyatiriktāyām ca anitya tāyām avagatāyām tatra eva pravartatām kim iti nitye śabda ātmani tad dvāreṇa pratipatteḥ iti ced tat kim anena vyavadhinā varam avyavahitasya eva pratipattiḥ astu tena eva arthi tvāt iti tat etat atipracarccyamānam ati gahanam sampadyate iti āstām tāvat 
[43,i^1]	ye api jaiminīyāḥ manyante yeṣām atyanta vyatirekavantaḥ dharmāḥ teṣām eva ayam naiyāyika ādīnām doṣaḥ asmākam tu kathañcid bheda abhedavatām dharmāṇām tad svabhāvatayā na eṣa doṣaḥ iti teṣām api vastutas sādhana dharma rūpa tā upagame sādhya dharmasya kathañcid bheda abhyupagame na kiñcid phalam utpaśyāmaḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvasya kalpita bheda dvāreṇa api upapatteḥ na ca aikātmye kathañcid api bhedaḥ yuktaḥ ekasmāt svabhāvāt abhedāt tatas api tayoḥ kathañcid bheda abhedau staḥ eva iti ced na anavasthā prasaṅgāt tathā hi dharmayoḥ tad eka svabhāvāt api bhedavatoḥ tena svabhāvena kathañcid abheda nimittam abhinnaḥ aparaḥ svabhāvaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ tathā tena api aparaḥ iti anantā eva bhinna abhinna svabhāva paramparā syāt 
[43,i^2]	na ca kalpanā buddhau ananta ubhaya rūpa svabhāva paramparā pratibhāsate iti kim iti tad kalpa nayā ātmānam vipralabhante bhavantaḥ kathañcid ca bheda upagamāt katham bheda pakṣa bhāvinām doṣāṇām anavasaraḥ yam ca ātmānam purodhāya imau dharmau ayam dharmī iti vyavasthāpyate yadi tena bhedaḥ tadā bhedaḥ eva iti kutas anekānta vādaḥ atha abhedaḥ tadā ayam sādhana dharmaḥ ayam sādhya dharmaḥ dharmī ca ayam iti katham pāramārthikam tritayam sidhyet tasmāt tad tad para rūpa vyāvṛtti samāśrayāyām kalpanā buddhau bhedavatām iva dharma dharmiṇām pratibhāsanāt sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ tanmātra anubandhaḥ tu vastutas tad tad svabhāva tayā eva yuktaḥ iti manyamānena vastutas tad bhāva tayā iti uktam 
[44,i]	kā punar asau vastutas tad bhāva tā yayā hetu bhūtayā sādhya dharmasya sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anubandhaḥ sidhyati iti āha sā vastutas tat bhāva tā sādhyasya viparyayaḥ vipakṣaḥ tatra hetoḥ yat bādhakam pramāṇam tad viparīta dharma pratyavasthāpakam yena bādhyamānaḥ hetuḥ tatra na pravartate viruddhayoḥ ekatra sahabhāva asambhavāt tasya yā vṛtti pravṛttiḥ bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttiḥ tad sādhya tvāt ca vastutas tad bhāva tāyāḥ sā bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttiḥ uktā tasyām hi satyām vipakṣāt nivṛttaḥ hetuḥ sādhya dharmavati eva dharmiṇi vartate iti sādhya dharmasya anartha antarasya sādhana dharma svabhāva tā sidhyati tayā ca vastutas tad bhāva tayā sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anubandhaḥ sādhya dharmasya sidhyati iti anvaya niścayaḥ yatra yatra sādhana dharmaḥ tatra tatra sādhya dharmaḥ iti evaṃrūpaḥ jāyate 
[44,ii]	atra udāharaṇam yathā yat sat tat kṣaṇikam eva avadhāraṇena vyāptim āha sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anubandhasya ca etat rūpam ākhyātam nimitta antaram antareṇa sat iti eva kṛtvā kṣaṇikam iti upadarśanāt sa ca vastutas tad bhāva tayā sidhyati iti tad siddhi upāyam bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttim darśayati akṣaṇika tve kṣaṇika viparyaye sati artha kriyā virodhāt arthasya kāryasya kriyā niṣpattiḥ tasyāḥ virodhāt tad lakṣaṇam sārtha kriyā lakṣaṇam yasya vastu tvasya artha kriyā sāmarthya ātmana tat tathā uktam artha kriyayā hi tad sāmarthya rūpam vastu tvam lakṣyate tat evaṃvidham vastu tvam hīyate nivartate tad viparyaya rūpasya asattvasya ākarṣaṇāt etat ca bādhakam pramāṇam vyāpaka anupalabdhi rūpam uttaratra avasara prāptam svayam eva vakṣyati tad anayā bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā sādhya dharmasya vastutas sādhana dharma svabhāva tā sidhyati tayā ca vastutas tad bhāva tayā sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anubandhaḥ iti 
[45,i^1]	evam svabhāva hetau viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā tādātmya siddhitaḥ anvaya niścayam pratipādya korya hetau pratipādapan āha kārya hetau anvaya niścayaḥ iti prakṛtam kaḥ punar asau kārya kāraṇayoḥ bhāvaḥ kārya tvam kāraṇa tvam ca tasya yā siddhiḥ pratītiḥ sā kārya hetau anvaya niścayaḥ yathā ca kārya kāṃraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ bhavati tathā upadarśayan āha yathā ityādi yathāśabdaḥ upadarśana arthaḥ idam dhūma ādikam asya agneḥ upalambhe sati upalabhyate iti sambandhaḥ anena kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhau pratyakṣa vyāpāram āha na ca kevalam pratyakṣam kārya kāraṇa bhāvam asat digdham sādhayati kintu prāc pravṛttān upalambha sahāyam iti darśayitum āha upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam ānupalabdham iti 
[45,i^2]	yadi tat dhūma ādikam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam satsu anyeṣu upalambha pratyayeṣu dṛśya ātmakam sat na upalabdham bhavati agni ādi sāmagrī sannidhānāt prāk tādātmya ādi sāmagryām upalabhyamānāyām upalabhyamānam tat kāryam sidhyati na tu upalambha pratyaya antara vaikalyāt anupajāta upalabdhi yogya rūpam sat tad deśa sannihitam api anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tayā agni ādi sāmagrī sannidhānāt prāc anupalabdham iti upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya ca anupalambhe na agni ādi sāmagrī sannidhānāt prāk anyatas āgamanam tad deśa kāla saṃ nihitāt katakuṭyā derutpattiḥ tad deśe ca asannidhānam iti tritayam apākriyate etāvadbhiḥ ca prakāraiḥ atad kāryatā bhavantī bhavet tatas anupalambhena atad kāryatā śaṅkā nirāsāt tad bhāve bhāva grāhi pratyakṣa nibandhanaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ asandigdhaḥ sidhyati 
[45,ii^1]	na ca agni indhana ādi bhāve niyata sannidheḥ adṛśya ātmanaḥ kutaścid dhūmasya bhāvaḥ syāt iti āśaṅkanīyam agni indhana ādi bheda anuvidhānāt dhūmasya candana aguru karpūra keśa ūrṇa ādīn dhana bhede tad anurūpa bhedasya asya darśanāt alpa mahat indhana vikāra kāriṇaḥ ca agneḥ tad anurūpasya na ca agni indhana ādi sannidhau adṛśya ātmanaḥ niyata sannidhāna tā yuktā pratibandha abhāvāt pratibandhe vā tad kāryatā tad kāraṇa tā vā syāt tad kārya tve na agni indhana samparka anantaram dhūma janma syāt tad bhāva abhāva anuvidhānāt eva ca asya api tad kārya tvam tat ca dhūme api samānam na api indhana ādi kāraṇa tvam adṛśya ātmanaḥ indhana ādeḥ sva hetoḥ eva vṛkṣa ādeḥ bhāva darśanāt tatra api tathā abhāva kalpanāyām tat eva uttaram vācyam 
[45,ii^2]	punar ca udye saḥ eva parihāraḥ anavasthā ca etena ekasāmagrī adhīna tā api pratyuktā tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt eva ca dhūmasya tat kāraṇam kalpeta tat ca agni ādau api tulyam tat api tatra kāraṇam astu iti ced na agnayā ādi bhāve avaśyambhāvinaḥ anyasya api kāraṇa tva kalpanāyām nimitta abhāvāt kārya vyatireka nibandhana tvāt kāraṇa bhāva kalpanāyāḥ yathā agni indhanāḥ dera iva anyatara abhāve abhavataḥ bhavatu vā anyasya api tad bhāve niyata sannidheḥ kāraṇa tā na tu tāvatā agni ādeḥ kāraṇa tva hāniḥ yatas dhūma darśanāt tad niścayena pravṛttau tad visaṃvādaḥ syāt na hi sarva sattva karma ādhipatya janita tve api jagat vaicitryasya dṛṣṭa kāraṇa hānitaḥ tad kārya darśanāt vā pravṛttānām atad prāptiḥ iti alam ati prasaṅgena 
[46,i]	kiṃrūpaḥ punar asau kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ anupalambha sahāya pratyakṣa nibandhanaḥ iti āha tad bhāve bhāvaḥ tad abhāve abhāvaḥ ca iti yaḥ eva hi kāraṇa abhimatasya bhāve bhāvaḥ eva kārya tvena abhimatasya bhāvaḥ tad abhāve kāraṇa tva abhimatasya abhāve abhāvaḥ eva kārya tvena abhimatasya abhāvaḥ ca saḥ eva kārya kāraṇa abhāvaḥ na anyaḥ 
[46,ii]	sa hi tābhyām anyaḥ bhavan svabhāvataḥ apratipanna kārya kāraṇa rūpayoḥ vā bhavet yat vā svabhāvena eva kārya kāraṇa ātmanoḥ yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā sarvatra eva akārya kāraṇa bhūte api vastuni bhavet tad niyama kāraṇa abhāvāt tatas sarvam sarvasya kāryam syāt svabhāvena ca atad rūpasya anya yoge api na tad rūpa tā na hi bhāvāḥ pratiniyata rūpa tyāgena anya yoge api rūpa antaram ābhajante yatas na anya yogaḥ teṣām pūrva rūpam nāśayati vināśa hetu ayogāt vakṣyamāṇakāt na api apūrvam utpādayati tasya tatas artha antara tva prasaṅgāt na hi teṣu niṣpanneṣu aniṣpannaḥ bhinna hetukaḥ vā tad svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ ayam hi bhedaḥ bheda hetuḥ vā viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ kāraṇa bhedaḥ ca tatas ced na bhedaḥ anya nimitta abhāvāt ekam dravyam viśvam syāt ityādi prasajyeta pratibhāsa bhedaḥ api hi itaretara abhāva rūpa tayā viruddha dharma adhyāsa tām na atikrāmati tatas ca pūrvake vastunī tad avasthe eva iti na tayoḥ anya yoge api kārya kāraṇa rūpa tā āpattiḥ 
[47,i^1]	atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā svabhāvataḥ eva tayoḥ kārya kāraṇa rūpa tvāt anyaḥ tad bhāvaḥ katham na vaiyarthyam anubhavet kārya kāraṇa vuddhī api tad bhāva bhāvi tva mātra nibandhane na artha antara nimitte tasya upapalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya kārya kāraṇa rūpa vivekinā rūpa antareṇa apratibhāsanāt tathāvidhasya api grahaṇa kalpanāyām atiprasaṅgaḥ anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tāyām katham kārya kāraṇa bhāva buddhī tad nibandhane na hi tat artha antaram sva sattā mātreṇa tabt uddhī pravartayati sadā sannihita tvena asya tayoḥ sarva dā udaya prasaṅgāt na ca viśeṣaṇam agṛhītam viśeṣye sva viśiṣṭa pratyaya nibandhanam iti ayuktā asya anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tā na ca dṛṣṭasya api anupalakṣaṇam yuktam kārya kāraṇa buddhyoḥ tad nibandha natā upagamāt na hi yat nimitaḥ yaḥ anyatra ātabduddhi bhāji tabdyavasāyaḥ sa tad anupalakṣaṇe yuktaḥ devadatte daṇḍi vyavasāya vat daṇḍa anupalakṣaṇe na ca artha antarasya kārya kāraṇābhyām sambandhaḥ ghaṭate sambandha antara kalpanāyām anavasthā prasakteḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva abhyupagame kārya kāraṇābhyām asahabhāvitā sadbhāvasya 
[47,i^2]	tatas ca kārya kāraṇa kāle tasya asannidhānāt katham kārya kāraṇa buddhi hetu tā niruddhayoḥ adhyāhṛtya tad pratyaya kalpanāyām ca kalpita viṣayaḥ eva kārya kāraṇa tā adhyavasāyaḥ syāt na vastu viṣayaḥ sa ca viśiṣṭa bhāva abhāva nibandhanaḥ abhyupagataḥ eva iti kimartha antara kalpanayā kalpita viṣaya tve tad adhyavasāyasya tasyāḥ vaiyarthyāt kārya kāraṇayoḥ ca ayaugapadyāt hani tābhyām asau janyate pratyeka janyaḥ ca katham kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ yadā ca kāraṇena janyate tadā kim sva kārya sahitaḥ janyate atha kevalaḥ 
[47,i^3]	kevalaḥ api kim sva kāryāt prāk atha paścāt yadi sva kārya sahitaḥ tudubhayoḥ anyatas eva bhāvāt parasparam asambandhaḥ iti kārya sambandhitā asya hīyeta atha kevalaḥ sva kāryāt prāk tadā kṣaṇikatayā kāraṇasya tam eva janayitvā dhvaṃsāt katham sva kārya krīyā tasyām ca asatyām katham tad apekṣam asya kāraṇa tvam tasmin ca asati katham akāraṇena kārya kāraṇa sambandhaḥ janyate atha sva kāryam kṛtvā paścāt janyeta tadā api sva kārya kāle eva vinaṣṭa tvāt asataḥ tad uttara kāla bhāvi kārya kāraṇa bhāva jananam kutas tad bhāvaḥ ca sambandhaḥ ucyate 
[48,i]	 janyatāyām vā yadi samagrāḥ svarūpataḥ eva tām janayanti kārye kaḥ eṣām śakti vyāghātaḥ yatas anyatra kalpyate tatra api apara sāmagrī yoga apekṣāyām ca anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ tatas samagrāḥ eva janakāḥ 
[48,ii]	teṣām ca kāraṇa tvam ekaika apāye kārya vyatirekataḥ samunnīyate iti āha satsu api anyeṣu tad sāmagrī antargateṣu hetuṣu janakeṣu pratyekam teṣām vyañjanaka tvāt asya abhāve janakatvena nirddhāryamāṇa tayā vivakṣitasya abhāve na bhavati iti anena anupalambhasya viṣayaḥ uktaḥ pratyakṣa vṛttiḥ tu pūrva uktā eva anupalambha rahitā tad bhāve bhāva grāhiṇī saṃbandhyate 
[49,i]	tathā ca ayam api tad bhāve bhāvaḥ tad abhāve abhāvaḥ ca kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ kiṃsādhanaḥ iti āha pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhanaḥ pratyakṣa pūrvakaḥ anupalambhaḥ tad vivikrānya padārtha grāhi pratyakṣa ātmakaḥ sādhanam asya iti pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhanaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ yaḥ tu anupalambha sāpekṣeṇa pratyakṣeṇa sādhyate iti prāk uktaḥ saḥ anupalambha pūrvakam pratyakṣam sādhanam asya iti anupalambha pratyakṣa sādhanaḥ iti vaktavyaḥ tasya kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya anvaya vyatireka ātmanaḥ siddhiḥ niścayaḥ yathā uktābhyām pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām kārya hetau anvaya niścayaḥ iti sambandhate
