[49,ii]	nanu ca anvaya niścayaḥ nāma kārya hetoḥ sarvatra kāryasya bhavataḥ sva kāraṇa sattayā anugamanam iti evam avasāyaḥ tat katham kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ eva asau ucyate iti āśaṅkya kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhi nibandhana tvāt anvaya niścayasya kāraṇe kārya upacārāt ananya upāya sādhyatām darśayitum darśana mātra nibandhanam ye tam icchanti tat mata niṣedha artham asau evam uktaḥ iti darśayan āha kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva hi kārya kāraṇa bhāve sati eva hiḥ yasmāt artha antarasya sādhyāt vyatiriktasya yaḥ tu avyatiriktaḥ tasya viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā tādātmya niścayāt eva anvaya niścayaḥ iti pūrvam uktam eva iti artha antara grahaṇam tasya artha antarasya evam syāt katham yatra nāma kvacid dhūmaḥ tatra avaśyam agniḥ iti niyamena agneḥ tatra bhāvaḥ iti evaṃrūpaḥ anvaya niścayaḥ yaḥ tu akārya kāraṇa bhāve api rasasya artha antarasya rūpeṇa anvaya niścayaḥ saḥ eka sāmagrī adhīna tayā tasya sva kāraṇa avyabhicāra dvārakaḥ eva iti adoṣaḥ 
[50,i]	atha yadi nāma kāryam agneḥ dhūmaḥ tathā api kim iti yatra asau tatra avaśyam agniḥ bhavati yatas kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhi nibandhanaḥ anvaya niścayaḥ ucyate iti āha agneḥ bhāve eva sattāyām eva hiḥ yasmāt bhāvaḥ sattā dhūmasya kāryatvam iti tasmāt kārya kāraṇa bhāve sati eva yathā uktaḥ anvaya niścayaḥ iti yadi hi yatra dhūmaḥ tatra avaśyam agniḥ na syāt tadā agnim antareṇa api asya bhāvāt agni bhāvaḥ eva bhāva lakṣaṇam kārya tvam hīyeta 
[50,ii]	idānīm anupalabdhau anvaya niścayam āha anupalabdhau api na kevalam svabhāva kārya hetvoḥ anvaya niścayaḥ uktaḥ kintu anupalabdhau api anvaya niścayaḥ ucyate kiṃrūpaḥ asau iti āha asat vyavahārasya sādhya dharmasya yogyatāyāḥ ca sādhya tvāt tad yogya tā asat vyavahāraḥ abhipretaḥ tasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya yā anupalabdhiḥ tad anya upalabdhi rūpā tanmātre nimitta antara anapekṣaṇī yā vṛttiḥ pravṛttiḥ asat vi avahārasya tasyāḥ sādhanam siddhiḥ anupalabdha vanvaya niścayaḥ kutas punar asat vyavahārasya tanmātre vṛttiḥ bhavati iti āha nimitta antara abhāva upadarśanāt iti yadā hi asat vyavahārasya yathā ukta anupaladbhi vyatiriktam buddhi vyapadeśa artha kriyā viraha ādikam nimittam na bhavati iti sādhyate tadā yathā ukta anupalabdhi mātre asya vṛttiḥ siddhā bhavati tayā ca anupalabdhau anvaya niścayaḥ anyathā hi nimitta antara apekṣā śaṅkāyām satyām api yathā ukta anupalabdhau na avaśyam asat vyavahārasya bhāvaḥ iti kutas anvaya niścayaḥ syāt nimitta antara abhāvaḥ tu vistarataḥ vāda nyāya uktaḥ iti tatas eva avadhāryaḥ 
[50,iii_51,i]	athavā sat vyavahārasya yad nimittam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya sattvam tat asat vyavahāra nimittāt anya tvāt nimitta antaram tatra anupalabdheḥ abhāvaḥ upadarśyate yena pramāṇena tat evam uktam tena sati vastuni tasyāḥ asambhava niścayāt anupalabdhau anvaya niścayaḥ tat ca tad vyatireka cintāyām darśayiṣyāmaḥ tat evam trayāṇām api hetūnām yathāsvam pramāṇena anvaya niścayaḥ uktaḥ svabhāva hetau viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā tādātmya siddhi nibandhana tvāt kārya hetau pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhi nimitta tvāt anupalabdhau nimitta antara abhāva prasādhaka pramāṇaḥ tad abhava siddhi hetu tvāt ca iti 
[51,ii_51,iii^1]	samprati trayāṇām api hetūnām sva sva pramāna nibandhanam vyatireka niścayam pratipādayitu kāmaḥ āha vyatireka niścayaḥ api na kevalam anvaya niścayaḥ yathāsvam pramāṇa nibandhanaḥ tayoḥ uktaḥ api tu vyatireka niścayaḥ api kārya svabhāva hetvaḥ ryathāsvam pramāṇa nimittaḥ ucyate kaḥ punar asau sādhya abhāve abhāva siddhiḥ yāvatat ātmaka tad ātmakau hetū kāraṇa vyāpaka rūpa sādhyasya sādhakau sādhya abhāve ca abhāva siddhiḥ tayoḥ kena pramāṇena kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhibhyām kārya hetau kāraṇa anupalabdhyā sādhya abhāve abhāva niścayaḥ svabhāva hetau vyāpaka anupalabdhyā kadā punar te anupalabdhī sādhike tasya bhavataḥ kārya kāraṇa vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva siddhau pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhau satyām kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ kārya hetau sādhya abhāve abhāvasya sādhikā viparyaye ca bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā tad bhāvatā siddhitaḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva siddhau satyām vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ svabhāva hetau sādhya abhāve abhāvasya sādhikā iti tat evam bruvatā ubhayatra tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇa pratibandha niścayāt eva dvayoḥ api anvaya vyatirekayoḥ niścayaḥ iti uktam bhavati atas eva anyatra kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā ityādi uktam kīdṛśībhyām 
[51,iii^2]	dṛśya viṣayābhyām dṛśyaḥ viṣayaḥ yayoḥ te tathā ukte yadi kāraṇa vyāpakau upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptau bhavataḥ tadā tad anupalabdhī sādhya abhāve abhāvam sādhayate iti yāvat kadā punar tayoḥ dṛśya viṣaya tā viśeṣaṇam apekṣyate iti āha uddiṣṭa viṣayasya uddiṣṭaḥ kathitaḥ viṣayaḥ ādhāraḥ vaidharmya dṛṣṭānta lakṣaṇaḥ yasya sādhya abhāve abhāvasya tasya upadarśane kriyamāṇe tatra api kasmāt dṛśya viṣaya tā apekṣyate iti ced āha anupalabdhi ityādi anyathā yadi dṛśya viṣaya tā viśeṣaṇam anupalabdhyoḥ na apekṣyate yadā anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam viṣayam vaidharmya dṛṣṭānta rūpam upādatte tadā anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptau tatra kāraṇa vyāpakau api bhavataḥ iti anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasyaḥ kāraṇasya vyāpakasya vā kvacid viprakṛṣṭe viṣaye sumeru ādau abhāva asiddheḥ katham ābhyām sādhya abhāve abhāva siddhiḥ syāt kāraṇa vyāpaka an upalabdhyoḥ eva asiddha tvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[52,i]	atha anuddiṣṭa viṣayasya api abhāvasya upadarśane anupalabdhyoḥ ddaśya viṣaya tā viśeṣaṇam kim itti na apekṣyate iti āha anuddiṣṭa viṣayam anuddiṣṭaḥ viṣayaḥ vaidharmya dṛṣṭānta rūpaḥ yasmin sādhya abhāve hetvabhāva khyāpane tat pratibandha mātra siddhau satyām dṛśya viṣaya tā viśeṣaṇam antareṇa api yasmāt sidhyati iti tasmāt na tatra anuddiṣṭa viṣaye vyatireka sādhane anupalabdhyaḥ rdṛśya viṣaya tāviśeṣaṇam apekṣyate aṅgīkriyate tathā hi aśeṣa padārtha parigraheṇa sāmānyena api bruvataḥ yaḥ yatra pratibaddha svabhāvaḥ tādātmya tad utpattibhyām sa tad abhāve avaśyam eva na bhavati iti niḥsvabhāva tva ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt tat uktam svabhāve api avinābhāvaḥ bhāva mātra anurodhinī tad abhāve svayam bhāvasya abhāvaḥ syāt abhedataḥ tathā kāryam dhūmaḥ hutabhujaḥ kārya dharma anuvṛttitaḥ sa bhavan tad abhāve api hetumat tām vilaṅghyet iti 
[52,ii_52,iii]	tatas tatra dṛśya viṣaya tā apekṣyamāṇā anupakārikā eva iti na tayā kiñcid iti bhāvaḥ pratibandha mātra siddhau iti anena ye pratibandham hetoḥ na varṇayanti kintva darśana mātrāt eva vyatirekam āhuḥ teṣām tad asambhavam ca darśayati tathā hi asati pratibandhe yadi sarve sādhya virahiṇaḥ arthāḥ dṛśyāḥ bhavanti tadā teṣu anupalabdhasya sādhanasya abhāvaḥ śiṣyet tat āha kumārilaḥ api gatvā gatvā tu tān deśān yadi arthaḥ na upalabhyate tadā anya kāraṇa abhāvāt asan iti avagamyate iti 
[53,i]	deśa ādi viprakarṣi tayā tu adṛśya tve sati api tatra hetau anupalambha mātrasya sambhavāt sandigdhaḥ asau a aśeṣe sādhya abhāve sādhana abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ vyatirekaḥ tathāvidhasya eva yatra yatra sādhya abhāvaḥ tatra tatra sādhana abhāvaḥ iti vīpsā padābhyām abhidhānāt anvaya niścayaḥ api prāc pratibandha nibandhanaḥ eva varṇitaḥ tatas tena api pareṣām darśana nibandhanām anvaya siddhim icchatām abhāvaḥ asya api kathitaḥ eva sarva arthānām hetumatām sādhya dharmavat tayā draṣṭum aśakyatvāt anumātṛbhiḥ aśeṣa deśa ādi viṣayasya ca sādhya anugamasya yatra yatra hetuḥ tatra tatra sādhyam iti vīpsayā pratipādanāt na ca katipaya deśa ādau sādhana dharmasya sādhya dharmeṇa sahabhāvasya bhūyas darśane api vyāptiḥ sidhyati asati pratibandhe kvacid bahulam tathā adṛṣṭānām api anyāthātvasya api sambhavāt tad asambhave bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt 
[54,i]	tat etāvatā granthena pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ iti vyākhyātam adhunā tridhā eva saḥ iti etat vyākhyātum āha etad lakṣaṇaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ san yaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ iti etat lakṣaṇam yasya saḥ etad lakṣaṇaḥ tridhā eva saḥ saḥ iti etasya vyākhyānam hetuḥ iti tridhā eva iti asya vivaraṇam tri prakāraḥ eve ti tān hetūna svena svena nāmnā kīrtayati svabhāvaḥ kāryam anupalabdhiḥ ca iti cakāraḥ hetu tva samuccaya arthaḥ iti śabdaḥ samāptim sūcayan avadhāraṇa artham eva sphuṭayati yathā anitye kasmiṃścid śabda ādau sādhye sattvam iti svabhāva hetu upadarśanam agnimati pradeśe sādhye dhūmaḥ iti kārya hetoḥ pradarśanam abhāve ca abhāvasya vyavahāre ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ iti anupalabdheḥ upanyāsaḥ 
[55,i]	kasmāt punar trividhaḥ eva hetuḥ iti āśaṅkaya trividha hetu vyatiriktānām arthānām hetvābhāsa tayā hetu viruddhayā vyāpteḥ triṣu eva hetu tvam niyatam bhavatiti hetvābhāsa tām pramāṇavatīm tad vyatirekiṇām darśayan āha atra eva svabhāva kārya anupalabdhi ākhye trividha hetau avinābhāvasya niyamāt iti trividha hetu vyatirikteṣu artheṣu avinā abhāva abhāvāt iti arthaḥ tatas ca avina abhāva vikala tvāt svabhāva kāryānupalabdhi vyatirekiṇaḥ arthāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ prameya tva ādi vat iti uktam bhavati avinā abhāva abhāvaḥ ca trividha hetu vyatirikta tvāt eva tādātmya tad utpattyoḥ avinā abhāva vyāpi kayoḥ abhāvāt vyāpaka anupalabdhitaḥ avagataḥ 
[55,ii]	atha kaḥ ayam avinābhāvaḥ kasya ca asau katham vā atra eva niyataḥ ucyate iti atas āha yathā uktā vyāptiḥ vyāpakasya tad kāraṇa tayā tad bhāva tayā ca yatra tat vayāpyam kāryam svabhāvaḥ vā sannihitaḥ tatra bhāvaḥ eva vyāpyasya vā kāryasya svabhāvasya vā yatra tad kāraṇa svabhāva ākhyam vyāpakam sannihitam tatra eva dharmiṇi na tad abhāve api bhāvaḥ iti yā vyāpaka vyāpya dharma tayā vyāptiḥ uktā sā yathā uktā vyāptiḥ avinā abhāvaḥ kasya pakṣa dharmasya sādhya dharmi dharmasya saḥ evaṃrūpaḥ avinābhāvaḥ trividhāt yathā uktāt hetoḥ anyatraḥ tad vyatirekiṇī arthe na asti yatas atra ca trividhe asti tādātmya tad utpattyoḥ avinā abhāvena vyāptayoḥ bhāvāt kṛtaka tva anitya tva vadanayoḥ vyāpyavyāpaka bhāvāt iti tasmāt atra eva trividhe hetau tad anyatra abhāva mukhena niyataḥ ucyate tat anena hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare iti asya avinā abhauva niyamāt iti upapatti sahitasya arthaḥ pradarśitaḥ yathā ca trividhāt hetoḥ anyatra āvinābhāvaḥ na asti tathā prāk eva uktam 
[56,i]	yadi vā svabhāvāt anyaḥ arthaḥ artha antaram tat ca kāryāt api anyat kāraṇam anubhayam vā anupalabdheḥ api anyat yathā uktāyāḥ anupalabdhi mātram upalabdhiḥ vā pratiṣedhyasya tad anyasya api viruddhasya aviruddhasya vā tatra artha antaram yadi anantara kāryam tasya arvāk darśibhiḥ itara vivekena lakṣayitum aśakyatvāt aliṅga tvam kārya darśanāt viveka avasāye api sādhya sidyuttara kāla bhāvī pakṣa dharmatāvasāyaḥ anvaya anugamanam ca vyartham vyavahita kāryam api kāraṇam na kāryasya liṅgam antarāla pratibandha vaikalya sambhavena vyabhicārāt tat uktam sāmagrī phala śaktīnām pariṇāma anubandhini anaikāntika tā kārye pratibandhasya sambhavāt iti yogyatā anumāne tu na artha antaram liṅgam 
[56,ii]	na api anubhayam apratibandhena gamaka tva ayogāt katham kṛttikā udaya vijñānāt rohiṇyāsattiklṛptiḥ iti ced nanu sā api na eva asati pratibandhe yuktāḥ viśeṣa abhāvena sarvatas sarva pratīti prasaṅgāt iti ukta tvāt tasmāt nakṣatra cakrasya saṅkrānti hetuḥ eva kāla vyavadhānena kaścid kalpayitavyaḥ yathā bhūta saṃkṣobhaḥ paścāt kāla bhāvinaḥ varṣasya iti hetu dharma anumānena kārya liṅga jā eva kalpayitavyā 
[56,iii]	anupalabdhi mātram api saṃśaya hetuḥ pramāṇa nivṛttau api artha abhāva asiddheḥ upalabdhiḥ api pratiṣedhyasya katham abhāvam sādhayet abhrānta upalambhasya abhāva ayogāt viruddha upalabdhiḥ tu pratiyogi abhāvam sādhayati kintu sa virodhaḥ tad bhāve sati anya anupalambhāt eva siddhaḥ iti tad dvāreṇa anupalabdhiḥ eva prayuktā bhavati anyathā niṣiddha upalabdheḥ abhāva asiddheḥ aviruddha upalabdhiḥ punar pratiṣedhe anaikāntikī sahabhāva sambhavāt aviruddhānām na ca aparaḥ prakāraḥ sambhavati iti nāvinā abhāvaḥ anyatra vidyate iti 
[57,i]	idānīm svabhāva hetoḥ tāvat lakṣaṇam āha tatra hetu traye svabhāva hetoḥ tāvat lakṣaṇam ucyate sādhyate yena tat sādhanam tat ca asau dharmaḥ ca tasya bhāvaḥ tad bhāvaḥ saḥ eva sādhana dharma bhāva mātram tasya anvayaḥ sa yasya asti sādhya dharmasya avayave samudāya upacārāt tasmin svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ sādhya dharmasya śruta tvāt tasya eva svabhāvaḥ iti gamyate katham punar asau sādhya dharma svabhāvaḥ yāvatā bhedena pratīyate iti atas āha aparasmāt aparasmāt ca asataḥ akṣaṇikāt ca yā vyāvṛttiḥ tasyāḥ yaḥ bhedaḥ avadhi bheda upakalpitaḥ tena hetu bhūtena sādhya dharmāt sādhana dharmasya yaḥ bhedaḥ tasmin sati api vastutas paramārthataḥ liṅga svabhāvaḥ eva sādhya dharma svabhāvaḥ eva tathā hi yaḥ eva asataḥ vyāvṛttaḥ saḥ eva akṣaṇikāt api tatas ekasmāt dharmiṇaḥ bheda abhāvāt sādhya sādhana dharmau api paramārthataḥ na eva bhidyete iti 
[57,ii]	yadi vastutas liṅgi svabhāvaḥ eva sādhana dharmaḥ tat kasmāt sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anvayini iti sādhya dharmaḥ viśeṣyate yaḥ hi yasya svabhāvaḥ sa katham tanmātra anvayī na syāt nīrūpa tva prasaṅgāt atad svabhāva tā vā iti atas āha hetuḥ svabhāvaḥ yasya sādhya dharmasya tasmin hetu svabhāve sādhya dharme sati anvaya vyabhicāra abhāvāt sādhana dharma bhāva mātrasya yaḥ anvayaḥ tasya vyabhicāra abhāvāt sambhave vyabhicāre ca viśeṣaṇam yuktam atra tu sambhavaḥ eva na vyabhicāraḥ iti viśeṣaṇam ayuktam eva tathā api sva bhava hetu lakṣaṇe kriyamāṇe yat etat sādhya dharmasya tanmātra anvayena sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anugamanena viśeṣaṇam tat parama tāpekṣam naiyāyika ādīnām vipratipatteḥ tad mata apekṣam na tu sva mata apekṣam 
[58,i]	tām eva para vipratipattim darśayan āha pare hi naiyāyika ādayaḥ artha antara nimittaḥ janakāt arthāt anyaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ vegavat dravya yoga ādiḥ tad nimittam te hi evam āhuḥ vegavat dravya yogāt avayaveṣu karmāṇi utpadyante tebhyaḥ avayava vibhāgaḥ tatas tad saṃyoga vināśaḥ tadā ārabdham kārya dravyam api naśyati iti evam artha antaram nimittam tatas eva artha antara nimittapekṣamāṇam kṛtaka tva ādi bhāve api abhāvāt atadbhāva mātra anvayinam tasya kṛtaka tva ādeḥ bhāvaḥ sattā sā eva tanmātram tasya anvayaḥ sa yasya asti sādhya dharmasya anitya tva lakṣaṇasya tad viparītam api kṛtaka tva ādeḥ svabhāvam icchanti yatas tatas viśeṣaṇam kṛtam tena ca viśeṣaṇena tathāvidhasya artha antara nimittasya vināśasya atad svabhāvatām āha lakṣaṇe viśeṣaṇa kāraḥ sva sattā mātra bhāvini eva svabhāva tvam na anyatra iti viśeṣaṇena sūcanāt 
[58,ii_58,iii^1]	tathā tasmin artha antara nimitte sādhye hetoḥ kṛtaka tva ādeḥ vyabhicāram anaikāntika tām ca āha atra udāharaṇam yathā hetumati vināśe sādhye kṛtaka tvasya hetoḥ atatsvabhāva tā vyabhicāraḥ ca iti nanu ca kṛtaka tva svabhāva tā anitya tāyāḥ bheda upagamāt na iṣṭā eva paraiḥ tat kim ucyate atadbhāva mātra anvayinam api svabhāvam icchanti iti evam manyate vyatiriktau api kṛtaka tva anitya tva ākhyau dharmau abhyupagacchadbhiḥ avaśyam abhūtvā bhavanam bhūtvā ca abhavanam anavasthāyi svabhāva tvam abhyupagantavyam anyathā ātma ādiṣu api kṛtaka tva anitya tve viśeṣa abhāvāt bhavetām tatas yat eva abhūtvā bhavanam bhūtvā abhavanam ca anavasthāyi tvam upādīyate bhāvasya tayoḥ eva tad darśana bala utpanna kṛtaka tva aniyatva bheda avabhāsi kalpanā dvāreṇa sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ astu kim vyatirikta dharma kalpanayā kalpayitvā api vastu ātmanaḥ eva artha kriyā nibandhana tayā tad arthibhiḥ cintya tvāt 
[58,iii^2]	tat uktam sat asat pakṣa bhedena śabda arthānapavādibhiḥ vastu eva cintyate hi atra pratibaddhaḥ phala udayaḥ artha akriyā samarthasya vicāraiḥ kim tad arthinām ṣaṇḍhasya rūpa vairūpye kāminyāḥ kim parīkṣayā iti tasmāt dṛṣṭāḥ api bhāvāḥ kenacid ātmanā tad anya vyāvṛttena kathañcid niścitāḥ tad anyena api atad rūpa vyāvṛttena ātmanā bhrānti kāraṇa sadbhāvāt aniścīyamānāḥ niścitā niścitayaḥ rūpayoḥ pramāṇa antarataḥ pratibandha avasāyā purovartinaḥ anumānataḥ niścīyate iti anitya tā svabhāva bhūtasya eva kṛtaka tvasya vināśam prati liṅgatā yuktā tathā ca vināśa svabhāvaḥ eva kṛtaka tva ākhyaḥ hetuḥ taiḥ yathā ukta nyāya ādiṣṭaḥ bhavati tasya atanmātra anvayitve artha antara nimitta tayā viśeṣaṇena atad svabhāva tā kathyate 
[59,i]	syāt matam kṛtaka tvena sākṣat hetumān vināśaḥ anumīyate tatas prāk pradhvaṃsā bhava viśeṣaṇā sattā tad samavāyaḥ vā anitya tā vyavasthāpyate atas eva ātma ādiṣu anitya tā prasaṅga abhāvaḥ vināśaḥ iti ca na bhāva abhāvam pradhvaṃsa lakṣaṇam manyāmahe kṛtaka tvam tu sva kāraṇa sattā samavāyam tasya viśeṣaṇena vināśa asvabhāvatā khyāpane na kiñcid aniṣṭam iti 
[59,ii^1]	tat ayuktam tathāvidhasya vināśasya hetumattā virodhāt svayam eva ca etat ācāryaḥ vakṣyati na ca tena anumitena kiñcid tasya artha kriyā sāmarthya vikala tvāt sukha duḥsva sādhane jñātvā yathārham pratipitsavaḥ hi kiñcid parīkṣante na vyasani tayā tasmāt anena asthira svabhāva tā eva bhāvasya anumātavyā sā eva ca hetumatī kalpanīyā anyathā bhāva avilakṣaṇasya pradhvaṃsa abhāvasya mugdara ādeḥ udaye api tasya bhāve anupayogāt sa bhāvaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva iti katham tad viśeṣaṇā sattā tad samavāyaḥ vā anitya tā syāt avicalita rūpasya ca bhāvasya mugdara ādi kṛta pradhvaṃsa abhāva viśeṣaṇau sattā samavāyau yadi anitya tā kim na ātma ādeḥ api 
[59,ii^2]	iti prasaṅga tad avasthaḥ eva sva kāraṇa samavāyaḥ api ca abhūtvā bhavanam anicchataḥ na sidhyati abhūtvā bhavataḥ eva ca yā sattā sā eva kṛtaka tvam varṇyate na ca sattā samavāyayoḥ nitya tayā upagatayoḥ niratiśaya tvāt prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāvau viśeṣaṇam yujyete abhūtvā bhavana upagame ca tat eva kṛtaka tvam asthira svabhāva tā ca vināśaḥ astu kim niṣphalayā apramāṇikayā pramāṇa badhitaya artha antara kalpanayā evam kṛtaka tva vināśayoḥ tādātmya upagamaḥ avaśyambhāvī pareṣām api tatas vināśasya āsthāyitva lakṣaṇasya artha antara nimittatā upagame kṛtaka tvasya atad svabhāva tā viśeṣaṇena khyāpyate tad niṣpatta a aniṣpannasya bhinna hetukasya ca tad svabhāva tva ayogāt 
[60,i_60,ii]	tathā tasmin sādhye kṛtaka tvasya vyabhicāraḥ tathā hi ye yatra hetu antara apekṣiṇaḥ na te tatra avaśyambhāvinaḥ yathā vāsasi rāgaḥ hetu antarā apekṣī ca kṛtakeṣu api bhāveṣu pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ iti viruddha vyāpta upalabdhiḥ nanu vāsasi rāgasya parimita hetu tvāt tasya ca sva kāraṇa āyatta sannidhāna tvāt tad āśrayasya ca vidhura pratyaya upanipātena asthira tayā na avaśyam bhavitā yuktā eva na punar vināśasya tad hetūnām ānantyāt avaśyam kasyacid ghaṭa ādiṣu sannidheḥ na ca vināśasya āśrayam prāk tad hetu sannidheḥ kecid upaghnānti yatas tad abhāvāt vināśaḥ na ārabhyeta iti 
[60,iii^1]	tat ayuktam yatas yadi api bahulam vināśa kāraṇāni santi tathā api teṣām sva karaṇa āyatta sannidhi tvāt tathā tad kāraṇānām ca sa nnihitānām api virodhinām api ānatyāt tad bhāve tad śakti pratibandhāt na avaśyam hetavaḥ phalavantaḥ iti kaścid na vinaśyet api iti vyabhicāraḥ na nivartate nanu ayam vāsasi rāgaḥ sa apekṣaḥ api yadi sarvatra upalabhyeta tatas kim avaśyambhāvī na syāt syāt yadi tathā upalabhyeta sa tu anyathā api gṛhyate yadi evam na tarhi sarvatra upalabdhasya vināśasya anyathā bhāva śaṅkayā manasi khedaḥ ādhātavyaḥ kim vā punarbhavān samasta vastu vistara vyāpi jñāna ālokaḥ 
[60,iii^2]	yena evam vadati tathā abhāve vā katham anumāna vṛttiḥ dṛṣṭe na vaiphalyam aśnuvīta kasyacid tu hetu kṛta vināśa darśane api hetu āyatta janmanam anyathā api darśanāt upajāta āśaṅkaḥ deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭeṣu katham tathā abhāvam niścinvīta kṛtakam api ca ayam bhava bhāva lakṣaṇam vināśam nityam upaiti tad vināśa upagame bhāvasya unmajjana prasaṅgāt na ca asya ghaṭa ādeḥ iva vināśa hetuḥ upalabhyate kaścid iti tat uktam ghaṭa ādiṣu yathā dṛṣṭāḥ hetavaḥ dhvaṃsa kāriṇaḥ na evam nāśasya saḥ ahetuḥ tasya saṃjāyate katham iti tatas kṛtaka tva vināśe sādhye tena eva vyabhicāraḥ kim na iṣyate 
[61,i]	bhāvānām ayam aikāntikaḥ eva dharmaḥ iti ced kutas punar etat avasitam teṣām anyathā bhāvasya anupalambhāt iti ced nanu ayam anupalambhaḥ bhavan api ātma ādeḥ anivartakaḥ sattāyāḥ katham anyatra anyathā bhāvam nivartayati tasya anumānena upalambhāt iti yadyucyeta tadā tatra api anumāne vipakṣe vṛttim anupalambhaḥ eva hetoḥ katham nivartayati iti yat kiñcid etat tasmāt sādhu uktam hetumati vināśe kṛtaka tvasya asvabhāva tām vyabhicāram ca āha iti alam ati jalpitena iti 
[61,ii]	idānīm yadi api sva artha anumānam prakṛtam tathā api kaścid prayoga darśana abhyāsāt prayoga bhaṅgayā eva pratipadyate iti sva artha anumāne api tad svambhavāt prasaṅgena para artha anumānam ca vyutpādayitum āha tasya svabhāva hetoḥ dvidhā trailakṣaṇya pratipādakaḥ vacana udāhāraḥ prayogaḥ tam eva darśayati samānaḥ dharmaḥ yasya tasya bhāvaḥ tena sādharmyeṇa ekaḥ prayogaḥ aparaḥ visadṛśaḥ dharmaḥ yasya tasya bhāvaḥ tena vaidharmyeṇa 
[62,i_62,ii]	yathākramam anayoḥ udāharaṇam āha yathā yat sat yat yat sat iti vīpsā pradhānaḥ yat śabdaḥ tat sarvam iti tad śabdaḥ api vīpsā pradhānaḥ eva atra sarva grahaṇena ca aśeṣa parigrahāt bahis vyāpteḥ nirāsaḥ yathā ghaṭa ādayaḥ iti yasya sattva kṣaṇika tvayoḥ pratibandha prasādhakam pramāṇam ghaṭa ādau pravṛttam tam prati tatra smṛti samādhāna artham dṛṣṭānta vacanam na sādhya siddhi artham dṛṣṭānta mātrataḥ sādhya siddheḥ abhāvāt na hi ekasya tathā bhāve sarvaḥ tathā bhavati atiprasaṅgāt san ca śabdaḥ iti pakṣa dharma upasaṃhāraḥ vaidharmya prayogasya udāharaṇam tathā ityādi tathā śabdaḥ samuccaye vaidharmyeṇa ca prayogaḥ udāhriyate atra api sarva grahaṇam vibhakti vipariṇāmena sambandhanīyam kṣaṇika tva abhāve sarvasmin sattva abhāvaḥ iti 
[62,iii^1]	prayoga dvaye api sarva grahaṇasya phalam darśayan āha sarvasmin sādhana dharmavati dharmiṇi na dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇī eva sādhya dharmasyo pasaṃharaṇam upasaṃhāraḥ ḍhaukanam tena yā vyāptiḥ vyāpakasya tatra bhāvaḥ eva ityādi rūpā tasyāḥ pradarśanam pratipādanam tat eva lakṣaṇam yayoḥ tau tathā uktau tatas ca ye sādhya dharmiṇam parihṛtya bahis vyāptim pradarśayanti te yadi api dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sādhya dharmeṇa sādhana dharmaḥ vyāptaḥ tāvatā asya sarvatra tathā abhāva abhāvāt sādhya siddhiḥ ayuktā iti nirastāḥ bhavanti sarvatra vā sādhya dharmeṇa sādhana dharmasya vyāptiḥ tad bhāve sā tathāvidhā eva kin na pradarśyate yena asamarthā bahis vyāptiḥ ākhyāyate 
[62,iii^2]	na hi sa śyāmaḥ tad putra tvāt paridṛśyamāna putra vat iti tad putra tvasya śyāma tvena sādhyāt bahis paridṛśyamāna putre vyāpti pradarśane api sādhya siddhiḥ bhavati tasmāt yā eva sarva upasaṃhāreṇa vyāptiḥ pramāṇa siddha pratibandha nibandhanā sādhya siddhau samarthā sā eva tad smṛtaye pradarśanīyā na ca sarva upasaṃhāreṇa vyāpti pradarśane api dharma viśiṣṭaḥ dharmī api tadā eva pratīyate yatas pakṣa dharma upadarśana uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ anumānasya smṛti tvam syāt tasyāḥ sādhya dharmiṇi sādhya dharmāvinābhūta sādhana dharma pratīti nibandhana tvena tad upadarśanāt prāc asambhavāt tad pūrvikāyām ca vyāptau anantaram viśeṣa viṣayam anumānam katham smṛtiḥ syāt iti 
[63,i]	nanu ca sādharmya prayogasya vyāpti pradarśana lakṣaṇa tvam yuktam sādhana dharme sati sādhya dharmasyavaśyām bhāvita apradarśanāt vaidharmya prayogasya tu katham tatra hi kevalam sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvaḥ kathyate na tu hetau sati sādhyasya bhāvaḥ eva iti na eṣa doṣaḥ na hi atra sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvaḥ tuccha rūpaḥ darśyate tasya hetu rūpa tā virodhāt vastu dharmaḥ hi sattva ādikaḥ hetuḥ tasya ātmanaḥ eva abhāvaḥ katham hetu svarūpam bhaviṣyati yatas tri rūpaḥ hetuḥ bhavet kintu nivṛttau nivṛtti dharmaka tvam svagataḥ dharmaḥ upadarśyate vaidharmya prayogeṇa tathāvidhe ca sādhana dharme avaśyaṃtayā sādhya dharmasya bhāvaḥ pratīyate eva anyathā tad nivṛttau nivṛtti dharmaka tvasya eva ayogāt iti na vyāpti pradarśana lakṣaṇa tvam vaidharmya prayogasya na yujyate 
[63,ii]	nanu dvividhe api prayoge pratijñā prayogaḥ na upadarśitaḥ tat katham tad artha avagatiḥ tad artha pratyāyanāya ca sādhana prayogaḥ abhimataḥ iti atas āha atra anayoḥ prayogayoḥ pakṣa dharma sambandha vacana mātra sāmarthyāt eva vakṣyamāṇakāt pratijñā arthasya dharma dharmi samudāya lakṣaṇasya sādhyasya pratīteḥ hetoḥ na pratījñāyāḥ prayogaḥ upadarśitaḥ paraḥ sāmarthyam anavavudhyamānaḥ āha apradarśite vacanena prameye sādhye katham na kathañcid tad pratītiḥ pratijñā artha pratītiḥ iti evam ced yadi manyase tadā sva artha anumāna kāle svayam param pratipādakam antareṇa pratipattau prameyasya kaḥ upadarśayitā na eva kaścid svayam eva tu sādhya vinābhūta sādhana dharma darśanāt prameyam pratipadyate tatha para artha anumāne api tatas eva tad pratītiḥ astu kim pratijñā vacanena 
[64,i]	yadi svayaṃpratipatti kāle na kaścid prameyasya upadarśayitā katham tarhi tad pratipattiḥ iti atas āha pradeśa stham sādhya dharmiṇi sthitam dhūmam sādhana dharmam upalabdhavataḥ pratyakṣeṇa dṛṣṭavataḥ sataḥ tasya dhūmasya agninā sādhya dharmeṇa pramāṇataḥ pratibandha niścaya balāt prāc pratipannāyāḥ vyāpteḥ avinā abhāvasya smaraṇe sati tad sāmarthyāt eva pakṣa dharma grahaṇa vyāpti grahaṇa sāmarthyāt eva pratijñā prayoga rahitāt agniḥ atra iti evaṃrūpā pratijñā artha pratītiḥ bhavati 
[64,ii]	syāt matam tatra api asya karṇa piśācikā ādiḥ prameyam kathayati eva iti atas āha na ca na eva tatra sva artha numāna kāle kaścid karṇa piśācikadira dṛśyaḥ agniḥ atra iti evam asmai pratipattre prameyam nivedayati kathayati yadi bhavān satya vādī na evam vaktum arhati tathā hi vayam api pradeśa stha dhūma darśanāt tasya agninā vyāpti smaraṇa sāpekṣāt agnim pratipadyāmahe na ca asmabhyam kaścid nivedayati agniḥ atra iti bhavati ca tad pratipattiḥ tathā tad anyasya api sā yukta rūpā eva iti 
[64,iii]	yadi api na kaścid nivedayati tathā api svayam eva prameyam vyavasthāpya tad pratipattaye liṅgam anusariṣyati iti ced āha na api na kevalam na kaścid nivedayati svayam api prāk eva liṅga vyāpārāt na pratipadyate kiñcid agni ādikam kasmāt iti ced pramāṇam hetum antareṇa vinā agniḥ atra iti evam pratīteḥ nimitta abhāvāt trirūpaḥ hi hetuḥ parokṣa artha pratīteḥ nimittam tad abhāve sā katham bhavet atha liṅgam antareṇa api evam pratītiḥ bhavat iti brūyāt tadā pratīta aviṣyamāṇāyām liṅgasya vaiyarthyam tasya anumeya pratipatti artha tvāt tena vinā tad pratipattau katham asya niṣprayojana tā na syāt 
[65,i]	atyanta mūḍha tām ca parasya darśayan āha svayam eva svatantraḥ eva agniḥ atra iti vyavasthāpya katham svatantraḥ vyavasthāpayati akasmāt pramāṇam antareṇa vyavasthāpanāt tad pratipattaye nirnimitta vyavasthāpita prameya pratipatti artham paścāt liṅgam tad nimittam anusarati iti kaḥ ayam pratipatteḥ kramaḥ paripāṭiḥ tathā hi prathamam liṅga anusaraṇam tatas sādhya pratipattiḥ iti vipaścitām kramaḥ ayam tu apūrvaḥ anumātāḥ yaḥ tad viparyayam āśrayate iti upahasati yat tat loke gīyate śīraḥ muṇḍayitvā nakṣatram pṛcchati iti tad tulya tvāt asya kramasya tasmāt pakṣa dharma grahaṇa vyāpti smaraṇa sāmarthyāt eva svayam pratipadyate tat ca pratipādakam kathitemavā iti na kiñcid prameya nirddeśena 
[65,ii]	yadi nāma sva artha anumāna kāle svayam eva sādhyam pratipadyate tat yuktam eva liṅgasya api tatra svayam eva pratipatteḥ para artha anumāne tu paratas yathā liṅgam pratyeti tathā prameyam api paratas eva pratyetavyam atas yuktaḥ eva pratijñā prayogaḥ iti atas āha pareṇa api na kevalam svayam eva prāk vyavasthāpyamānam plavate pareṇa api vādinā tat prameyam ucyamānam plavat eva tad vacanasya sandigdha artha bhidhāyaka tayā sādhya niścaya anaṅga tvāt prameya gāmbhīryā anavāgāhinaḥ paramparayā api atad sambaddhasya vivakṣā mātra nibandhana tayā upari eva avasthāpanāt kasmāt plavate iti ced upayoga abhāvāt na asya sādhya pratītim prati kaścid upayogaḥ tad pratyāyana samartha āsya anabhidhānāt iti yāvat 
[66,i]	para stu upayoga mātram kadācid brūyāt iti āśaṅkayā āha viṣaya upadarśanam hetoḥ yaḥ viṣayaḥ sādhyam tad upadarśanam pratijñā vacanasya upayogaḥ ced matam atra āha tena eva viṣayeṇa tāvat śabdaḥ krame viṣayasya upadarśyamānasya arthavat tāyām tad upadarśanam pratijñā vacanasya prayojanam bhavet viṣayeṇa eva tu darśyamānena kaḥ arthaḥ kim prayojanam 
[66,ii^1]	nanu sādhya pratītiḥ sādhyarmya vat prayoga ādi pratītiḥ ca viṣaya upadarśanasya arthaḥ tatas tudupadarśanam pratijñā vacanasya prayojanam tathā hi asati sādhya nirdeśe yat kṛtakam tat anityam iti ukte kim ayam sādharmyavāna prayogaḥ uta vaidharmyavān iti na jñāyeta ubhayam hi atra āśaṅkyate kṛtaka tvena anitya tve sādhye sādharmyavān nitya tvena akṛtaka tve vā vaidharmyavān iti anityaḥ śabdaḥ akṛtakaḥ vā iti tu pratijñā vacane sati ubhayam asandigdham avagamyate hetu viruddha anaikāntika pratītiḥ ca na syāt 
[66,ii^2]	pratijñā pūrvake tu prayoge anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti hetu bhāvaḥ pratīyate nityaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti viruddha tā pratyatna ānantarīyakaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti anaikāntika tvam hetoḥ ca trairūpyam na gamyeta tasya sādhya apekṣayā vyavasthānāt sati pratijñā vacane avayave samudāya upacārāt sādhya dharmī pakṣaḥ iti tatra vṛttasya kṛtaka tvasya pakṣa dharma tvam sādhya dharma sāmānyena ca samānaḥ arthaḥ sa pakṣaḥ iti tatra vartamānasya sa pakṣe sattvam na sa pakṣaḥ asapakṣaḥ iti sādhya dharma virahiṇya vṛttasya āsa pakṣe api asattvam pratīyeta iti āśaṅkayā āha yadi prati iti sādhyasya niścaya lakṣaṇā sādharmya vat prayoga ādeḥ ca svarūpa avadhāraṇa ātmikā 
[66,ii^3]	anyathā pratijñā vacanam antareṇa na syāt tadā yat uktam sādhya sidhi artham sādharmya vat prayoga ādi jñāna artham ca viṣaya upadarśanam iti tat sarvam śobheta yāvatā svartha anumāna kāle pratijñā vacanam antareṇa api pakṣa dharma grahaṇa sambandha smaraṇataḥ sādhya siddhi lakṣaṇā bhavati eva pratītiḥ iti ākhyātam eva tadvat para arthe api anumāne bhaviṣyati yatas evam tasmāt eṣa pratijñā prayoga vādī yadā svayam sādhyam pratyeti tadā svayam sādhyasya pratītau viṣayaḥ upasthāpyate yena pratijñā vacana dvāreṇa puṃsā kenacid tena vinā api pratiyan sādhyam niścinvan liṅga sāmarthya deva yadā asmābhiḥ pratipādyate tadā asmān kāryiṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā vyaktam pratijñā prayoga lakṣaṇam mūlyam mṛgayate kaḥ iva parva brāhmaṇaḥ iva yathā dakṣiṇām antareṇa api anyadā aurdhvarathikaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ bhuñjānaḥ anyadā śrāddha ādi parvaṇi arthinam śraddhālum bravīti yadi me ghṛtapūram ghṛtapūram prati rūpakam dadāsi tatas aham bhuñje na anyathā iti tena tulyaḥ bhavān api iti 
[67,i^1]	kiñca yat api bravīṣi para artha anumāna kāle yathā liṅgam pareṇa anabhidhīyamānam na pratyeti pratipādyaḥ tathā sādhyam api iti tadā etat yujyate yadi asau vādi vacana mātreṇa liṅgam api niścitya tad anusāreṇa sādhyam avagacchet para prati iti arthinaḥ ca tadā vayam api pratijñām kin na prayuñjmahe liṅga vacana rahitām asmad vacanasya eva tam prati pramāṇa tayā tatas eva anumeya pratīteḥ tad vacanasya caritārtha tvāt na ca etat asti yatas asmad vacanāt api na kevalam sva artha anumāna kāle asmad vacanam antareṇa iti apiśabdaḥ kintu yadā api asmat vacanam pravṛttam tadā api na eva asmad vacanāt liṅgam api pratyeti kutas eva sādhya siddhye anusariṣyati 
[67,i^2]	api tu svayam asya yadi tat liṅgam kutaścid pramāṇataḥ siddham bhavati asmad vacanena tu kevalam tatra smṛti samādhāna mātram kriyate tadā svayam siddham eva liṅgam anusṛtya sādhyam pratyeti na asmad vacanāt pānīyam api pibati iti tasmāt kaḥ anayoḥ pratijñā vacanā vacana ātmikayoḥ avasthayoḥ viśeṣaḥ ubhayatra svayaṃsiddha liṅga sāmarthyāt eva sādhya pratīteḥ na kaścid tatas sva para artha anumānayoḥ svayaṃsiddha liṅga anusaraṇam tatas sādhya pratītim ca prati viśeṣa abhāvāt pratijñā upanyāsaḥ para artha anumāne api vyarthaḥ eva liṅgam api hi tāvat atra na abhidhīyate yadi tat pūrva prasiddham svayam anusmaret kim aṅga punar sandigdha artha abhidhāyakam pratijñā vacanam upādīyate 
[68,i]	syāt matam yadi nāma sādhya siddhau pratijñā vacanasya na upayogaḥ tad arthaḥ asya prayogaḥ mā bhūta sādharmya tvad prayoga ādi jñāna artham tu tad upadānam avasthitam eva tasya anyathā pratīti abhāvāt iti atas āha dṛṣṭā ca sādharmya vat prayoga ādeḥ pratijñā vacanam antarena api pratītiḥ tatas tad arthaḥ api pratijñā upanyāsaḥ na śobhate 
[68,ii]	kutas punar sādharmya vat prayoga ādeḥ asati sādhya nirddeśe pratītiḥ iti āha pakṣa dharma sambandha vacana mātrāt iti evam manyate na eva hi kaścid yat kṛtakam tat anityam etāvat mātram abhidhīyāḥ te sādhana nyūna tayā eva asya parājayāt kintu avaśyam hetoḥ dvarmiṇī upasaṃhāram karoti iti tatra yadi kṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti brūyāt tadā sādharmya vat prayoga pratītiḥ atha nityaḥ ca iti abhidadhyāt tadā vaidharmyavataḥ iti sambandha vacana pūrvakāt pakṣa dharma vacanāt prayoga dvaya avagatiḥ 
[68,iii]	hetu viruddha anaikāntikāḥ api pakṣa dharma vacana mātreṇa na pratīyante yadā tu sambandha vacanam api kriyate tadā katham apratītiḥ tathā hi yat kṛtakam tat anityam iti pakṣa dharma vacane sati ukte hetuḥ avagamyate vidhiyamānena ānūdyamānasya vyāpteḥ yat kṛtakam tat nityam iti abhidhāne viruddhaḥ viparyaya vyāpteḥ yat kṛtakam tat prayatna anantarīyakam iti pradarśane vyabhicārāt anaikāntika adhyavasāyaḥ 
[68,iv^1]	trairūpyam api hetoḥ gamyate eva yatas vyāpti pradarśana kāle vyāpakaḥ dharmaḥ sādhya tayā avagamyate yatra ca vyāpyaḥ dharmaḥ dharmiṇī upasaṃhriyate sa vyāpaka adharma viśiṣṭa tayā avagamyamānaḥ sādhya samudāya eka deśa tayā pakṣaḥ iti upasaṃhṛtasya vyāpya dharmasya pakṣa dharma tva avagatiḥ sā ca vyāptiḥ yatra dharmiṇī upadarśyate sa sādhya dharma sāmānyena samānaḥ arthaḥ sa pakṣaḥ pratīyate iti sa pakṣe sattvam avagamyate sāmarthyāt ca vyāpaka nivṛttau vyāpya nivṛttiḥ yatra avasīyate saḥ asapakṣaḥ iti asapakṣe api asattvam api niścīyate iti yadi pakṣa ādibhiḥ api jñātaiḥ kiñcid prayojanam na tu vyavahartaṇām pakṣa ādi saṅketa apekṣā parokṣa artha gatiḥ bhavati tathā hi yat kvacid dṛṣṭam tasya yatra pratibandhaḥ tad vidaḥ tasya tat gamakam tatra iti hi loke vastu gatiḥ bhavati na pakṣa di saṅketa grahaṇa apekṣā 
[68,iv^2]	tatra yatheṣṭam śāstra kārāḥ gamaka rūpa pratipattaye sva saṅketena anyathā vā lakṣaṇam praṇayantu na tu vyavahāra kāle tad anusaraṇam kvacid upayujyate tad saṅketa pratipāditam eva tu yathoktam gamakam rūpam upayogi vyavahartṝṇām tat ced pratipannam tāvatā eva sādhya siddhiḥ san jātāḥ iti pakṣa sa pakṣa ādi saṅketā parijñāne api na kiñcid plūyate atas eva ācārya pādaiḥ na antarīyaka artha darśanam tad vidaḥ anumānam iti gamaka rūpa mātram eva pakṣa ādi saṅketa anapekṣam pratipāditam sva prajñāparādhāḥ tu tatra api kaiścid asantaḥ eva doṣāḥ prakīrtyante iti kim atra brūmaḥ tasmāt sādharmya vat prayoga ādi jñāna artham api pratijñā vacanam pakṣa dharma sambandha vacana mātre eva yathā uktena prakāreṇa pratīteḥ ayuktam iti kaḥ tasya pratijñā vacanasya upayogaḥ na evam kaścid 
[69,i^1]	svayam ca ayam vādī yena krameṇa anumeyam pratipannavān tam ullaṅghya para pratipattaye kramāntaram āśrayan pravañcaka tayā dhūrtaḥ eva pratīyate na sat vṛttaḥ iti upadarśayan āha sva niścaya vat ityādi yathā ātmanaḥ niścayasya utpādanam kṛtam tathā eva anyeṣām api niścaya utpādanāya ca para hita nirataiḥ sādhanam ucyate tatra etasmin nyāye sati svayam ayam vādī prameyasya upadarśanena upadarśakena vacanena vinā api sva artha anumāna kāle pratipadya prameyam param saṃśayita ādikam pratipādayan sva pratipannam prameyam avabodhayan apūrvam sva pratipatti kāle pūrvam yaḥ prameya pratipattau kramaḥ upāyaḥ anubhūtaḥ tasmāt anyam āśrayate iti kim atra krama antara āśrayaṇe kāraṇam 
[69,i^2]	na eva kiñcid para vyāmohanam muktvā tathā hi yadi sva pratipatti kramaḥ pratīti nibandhanam kim tad parityāgena krama antara āśrayaṇam katham tena svayam pratipannavān asi iti yatas evam tasmāt na prameyasya sādhyasya vacanena pratijña ākhyena kiñcid prayojanam kutas anyathā api vinā api tena pratipatteḥ sādhya pratīteḥ utpatteḥ iti upasaṃhāraḥ 
[70,i]	evam pratijñām sādhana vākyāt apanīya aparam api upanaya nigamana ādikam para parikalpitam sādhana vākyāt apanetum uktam eva nyāyam atidiśan āha etena anyathā api pratipatteḥ utpatteḥ iti nyāyena upanaya nigamana ādikam ādi grahaṇāt saṃśaya jijñāsā ādikam pratyuktam pratyākhyātam tatra udāharaṇa apekṣaḥ tathā iti upasaṃhāraḥ na tathā iti vā sādhyasya upanayaḥ pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam pratijñāḥ iti tu pratijñāyāḥ etena iti etat eva darśayati etāvatā eva pakṣa dharma sambandha vacana mātreṇa eva upanaya ādi rahitena sādhya pratīteḥ bhāvāt utpatteḥ iti 
[70,ii^1]	atra uddyota karaḥ prāha pratijñā tāvat viṣaya nirddeśa artham avaśya kartavyā yatas lokaḥ prathamam karma cchedya ādikam nirūpayati tatas kuṭhāra ādikam sādhanam vyāpārayati upanayena api yāvat dṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭa sāmarthyaḥ hetuḥ ddharmiṇi na upasaṃhriyate tāvat kutas sādhya pratītiḥ sva artha anumāna dṛṣṭaḥ ca pratyavamarśa pratyaya arthaḥ anena darśyate tathā hi sva artha anumāne prathamam pradeśe dhūmam paśyati tatas yatra yatra aham dhūmam adrākṣam tatra tatra agnim api iti vyāptim smarati tatas dhūmaḥ ca atra iti punar pratyavamṛśati sa pratyavamarśa arthaḥ para artha anumāne upanayena ucyate nigamanam api avaśya abhidhānīyam yatas yadi api pūrvam anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti uktam na tu tāvatā asya niścayaḥ jātaḥ samprati tu pramāṇa bala āyātaḥ arthaḥ tad sampratyaya artham anena nigamyate aśeṣa pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ ca anena upasaṃhriyate tathā hi āgamaḥ pratijñā hetuḥ anumānam dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratyakṣam upamānam upanayaḥ tat etasya pramāṇa catuṣṭasya api vyāpāraḥ nigamanena upasaṃhriyate iti katham asya na sāphalyam 
[70,ii^2]	iti etat āśaṅkayā āha ḍiṇḍika rāgam parityajya ḍiṇḍikāḥ nagna ācāryāḥ te niṣphalam upari upari nāma lekhane prasaktāḥ tatas teṣām iva pareṇa ukte tasya upari mayā avaśyam ayukta tayā niṣphalam api abhidhānīyam iti asthāna abhiniveśam tyaktvā akṣiṇī nimīlya bahis vikṣepam upasaṃhṛtya cintaya tāvat kimiyatā pakṣa dharma sambandha vacana mātrakeṇa vākyena sādhyasya pratītiḥ syāt na vā iti yāvatā yāvān eva para artha anumāne arthaḥ abhidhānīyaḥ iti asmābhiḥ anujñāyate tāvān eva anyūna anatiriktaḥ sva artha anumāne api pratīti hetuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tasya kaḥ iha śakteḥ vyāghātaḥ yena asau para artha anumāne api pratītim na kuryāt 
[70,ii^3]	bhāve pratīteḥ kim prapañca mālayā pratijñā upanaya nigamana lakṣaṇayā bāla pratāraka tad upayoga upavarṇana lakṣaṇayā vā tathā hi pratijñā upanaya nigamana prayoge api yadi pramāṇa niścitā svasādhya vyāptiḥ sādhana dharmasya na syāt sādhya dharmiṇi vā sadbhāvaḥ tadā asya na eva pratīti hetu tā tad sambhave tu pratijña ādi abhāve api sva artha anumānaḥ iva gamaka rūpā vaikalyāt sā na nivāryate iti kimasthāna nirbandhena iti na hi sādhya dharma ākṣepaṇa sāmarthya virahe sādhana dharmasya vādi vacana mātrāt sādhya niścayaḥ yuktaḥ hetu upanyāsa vairthya prasaṅgāt tasya tad ākṣepa sāmarthye vā pratijñā vacanasya iti 
[71,i]	yatu uktam viṣaya pradarśanāya pratijñā iti atra śāstra kṛtā eva dattam uttaram yaḥ ca sādhanam prayukte tena aham anena sādhanena amuṣmin sādhye pratītim sādhayiṣyāmi iti karma nirūpya eva tat prayuktam iti na laukika nyāya atikramaḥ anyathā yadi sādhanāt yasya sādhya pratītiḥ upajāyate tena eva karma nirūpaṇīyam katham tad abhāve sva artha anumāne sādhya siddhiḥ sādhana nibandhanā syāt yaḥ ca agni dhūmayoḥ sambandham cetasi vyavasthāpya kva agniḥ kva agniḥ iti agnim paryeṣate sa pradeśe dhūma darśana mātrāt eva agnim pratipadyate iti katham sva artha anumāne pratyavamarśa pratyayaḥ syāt atha kadācid asau dṛṣṭaḥ tatra iti para arthe api asya upādānam tadā dadhi ādikam api bhuktvā kadācid dhūmāt agnim pratipannavān iti kinna dadhi bhojana ādeḥ api kādācid kasya upādānam 
[72,i_72,ii]	yat punaruktam āgamaḥ pratijñā iti tatra yadi vādi vacanam eva āgamaḥ tadā tatas eva sādhya siddheḥ hetu ādi upadānam anarthakam atha pratijñā arthasya āgame pāṭhāt āgamaḥ pratijñā tadā na kvacid āgame paṭhyate atra pradeśe agniḥ iti katham āgama tvam pratijñāyāḥ hetuḥ anumānam iti api ayuktam na hi pakṣa dharma tva mātram hetuḥ tasya tri rūpa tvāt dṛṣṭāntaḥ api na sarvaḥ pratyakṣaḥ iti katham dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratyakṣam bhavet upamānam tu pramāṇam eva na bhavati katham tat vyāpāraḥ upasaṃhriyeta nigamanena yadi ca avaśyam dṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭa sāmarthyaḥ hetuḥ dvarmiṇī upaneyaḥ tadā upanayaḥ eva astu kim kṛtaka tvāt iti pakṣa dharma nirddeśena saḥ eva dṛṣṭa sāmarthyam hetum upasaṃhariṣyati pakṣa dharma tām ca darśayiṣyati iti na kiñcittena tatas yatra ca pratijñāyāḥ prathamatas eva prayogaḥ na iṣyate tatra tasyāḥ punarvacanam kutas nigamanam bhaviṣyati iti āha iti tasmāt iyān eva pakṣa dharma sambandha vacana mātra ātmakaḥ sādhana vākye prayogaḥ jyāyāt na pañca avayava ātmakaḥ iti sthitam 
[72,iii]	atra sādhana vākye na kevalam pratijña ādi prayogaḥ na yuktaḥ para upagataḥ pūrvam hetuḥ prayoktavyaḥ paścāt dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti krama niyamaḥ api na kaścid kutas sarvathā yadi pūrvam hetuḥ paścāt vyāptiḥ atha pūrvam vyāptiḥ paścāt pakṣa dharmaḥ prayujyate tathā api gamaka tvāt 
[73,i]	nanu tasya dvidhā prayogaḥ iti ayuktam uktam yatas trividhaḥ hetuḥ anvayī vyatirekī anvaya vyatirekī ca iti naiyāyikāḥ tatas tasya tri ghā prayogaḥ sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām ca iti vaktavyam iti atas āha sambandha vacane api na kevalam krama niyamaḥ na yuktaḥ kintu artha bhedaḥ api na kaścid ubhayatra api tri rūpa sadbhāvāta tatas sarve eva hetuḥ anvaya vyatirekī na tu anvayī vyatirekī vā kaścid vetuḥ asti iti bhāvaḥ tat kutas tri vidhyam prayogasya syāt iti manyate kutas punar artha bhedaḥ na asti iti ced āha ubhayathā sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca prayoge yadi api vidhi pratiṣedha rūpa tayā dharma bhedaḥ pratīyate tathā api tad bhāvasya eva sādhana dharmasya sādhya svabhāvatāyāḥ eva sādharmya vaidharmya prayogābhyām khyāpanāt 
[73,ii]	nanu sādharmya prayoge hetu bhāve sādhyasya bhāvaḥ vaidharmye ca sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvaḥ śabdāt avagamyate na tādātmyam tat kim ucyate tad bhāvasya eva khyāpanāt iti atas āha na hi ityādi yadi sādharmya prayoge tad bhāvaḥ na ākṣipyeta tadā sādhanasya atad svabhāvasya bhāve kim iti ekāntena avaśyantayā sādhyasya bhāvaḥ kādācid kaḥ tu bhavatu nāma yat kṛtakam tat anityam iti ekānta bhāvaḥ ca hetau sati sādhyasya vyāptyā sādharmya prayoge abhidhīyate sa ca tādātmyam antareṇa anartha antarasya na sambhavati iti sāmarthyāt tadā ākṣipati 
[73,iii]	katham iva atad svabhāvasya bhāve na ekāntena anya bhāvaḥ iti āha kṛtaka tvā ityādi yadi pratyatna ānantarīyaka tvam antareṇa api kṛtaka tvasya bhāvāt a tad svabhāva tvam anitya tve api ayam eva vṛttāntaḥ tatas ca tādātmya virahāt prayatna ānantarīyaka tvasya anitya tvena anvayaḥ na syāt tad nivṛttau vā nivṛttiḥ iti katham tatas tat pratīyate na eṣa doṣaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka padārtha svabhāvasya eva anitya tvasya tena sādhanāt tatra ca tādātmya sadbhāvāt anvaya vyatirekau anivāritau anitya tva kṛtaka tvam atra apekṣayā tu tādātmya virahaḥ asya abhihitaḥ iti 
[74,i^1]	nanu agni nivṛttau atad svabhāvasya api dhūmasya nivṛttiḥ dṛṣṭa anvayaḥ ca iti āha kāryasya iti anvaya vyatirekayoḥ hi pratibandhaḥ nibandhanam tena tayoḥ vyāpteḥ tad abhāve tayoḥ api abhāvāt tatra artha antarasya dhūmasya agnau tad utpatti lakṣaṇaḥ pratibandhaḥ anvaya vyatireka nimittama sti iti bhavetām tau yatra tu anartha antarasya tau ucyete tatra avaśyam tādātmyena bhavitavyam iti abhiprāyaḥ atra udāharaṇam yathā anayoḥ eva kṛtaka tva prayatna anantarīyaka tvayoḥ viparyayeṇa na eka nivṛttau anya nivṛttiḥ yat pratyatna āntarīyakam na bhavati tat kṛtakam api na bhavati iti evaṃrūpā 
[74,i^2]	yatas evam tasmat anvaya vi atirekayoḥ yathā lakṣaṇam hetu bhāve sādhyasya avaśyam bhāvaḥ sādhya abhāve ca hetoḥ avaśyam abhāvaḥ iti ekaḥ api sādharmya mukheṇa vaidharmya mukheṇa vā prayuktaḥ dvitīyam ākṣipati sva vyāpaka pratibandha ākṣepāt tasya api ca itareṇa vyāpteḥ tasmāt ubhayatra trairūpya pratīteḥ ekasya śabdataḥ aparasya arthataḥ iti sambandha vacane api prayogaḥ eva vidhi mukhena pratiṣedha mukhena vā bhidyate na arthaḥ iti siddham tatas tasya dvidhā prayogaḥ sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca na tu sādharmya vaidharmyabhyām api tad arthasya anyatareṇa eva prakāśanāt 
[74,ii_75,i]	sarvaḥ hetuḥ anvaya vyatirekyā iva vastutas na kaścid anvayī vyatirekī vā nāma iti etat upasaṃharan āha iti na ekatrā nvaya mukhena vyatireka mukheṇa vā sādhana vākye dvayoḥ ranvaya vyatirekayoḥ prayogaḥ sākṣāt śabdena pratipādanam iṣyate vaiyarthyāt pratīta pratyāyane prayojana abhāvāt tām eva arthataḥ aparasya pratītim sphuṭayan āha tad svabhāvatayā ityādi yadi tad svabhāvatayā sādhyena hetoḥ anvayaḥ sidhyati tatas eva tad abhāve abhāvaḥ api sidhyati eva tad svabhāvasya tad abhāve svayam nairātmyena bhāva ayogāt tathā tad svabhāvatayā sādhya abhāve sādhanasya abhāva siddhau ca satyām tatas eva sādhyena hetoḥ anvayasya api siddheḥ iti 
[75,ii^1]	yaiḥ tu vyākhyāyate sādharmyavati prayoge tad abhāvaḥ eva vipakṣe hetoḥ abhāva khyātiḥ yathā syāt na anyatra vipakṣe viruddhe vā hetu abhāva prasaṅgāt viruddhataḥ eva vyavaccheda prasaṅgāt ca iti niyama khyāpana arthaḥ vyatireka prayogaḥ iti sa tad arthaḥ api ayuktaḥ kutas anya viruddhayoḥ api na kevalam tad abhāvasya vipakṣa tvāt yasya hi anyaḥ eva vipakṣaḥ anya dharma yogī vā anyaḥ na vivakṣita dharmān āśrayaḥ viruddhaḥ eva vā saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇena eva virodhena na paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tayā api vipakṣaḥ tasya anitya tvāt anyān ātma ādi dharmavati arthe kṛtaka tva ādi vṛtteḥ hetu abhāva prasaṅgaḥ 
[75,ii^2]	auṣṇye ca sādhye agni lakṣaṇasya hetoḥ viruddhāt eva śītāt na anuṣṇa śītāt api anyatas vyavaccheda prasaṅgāt na ekāntena auṣṇyam agniḥ grasayet iti tasya ayam doṣaḥ syāt tam pratyācāryeṇa uktam yadi ekasya vipakṣa tvam iṣyate tadā tad abhāvasya eva iṣyatām na viruddhasya anyasya vā tasya anyatra api vivakṣita dharmān āśraye viruddhe ca bhāvāt tad abhāvam antareṇa tayoḥ anya viruddha tva ayogāt na tu asmākam trividham api vipakṣam icchatām vivakṣita dharmān āśrayam ca anyam iti bhāvaḥ 
[75,iii^1]	yadi svabhāva hetau anvaya vyatirekayoḥ sādhana dharmasya sādhya svabhāva tā nibandhanam iti anvayena vyatirekeṇa vā sādharmyevaidharmyavatoḥ prayogayoḥ abhidhīyamānena tādātmya ākṣepa dvāreṇa arthāditarākṣepaḥ ucyate tadā pramāṇa siddhā eva tad svabhāva tā tayoḥ nibandhanam na śabda mātrataḥ pratīyamāna iti abhiprāyavān āha katham idam ityādi yena iti sataḥ naśvara svabhāva tvena sattva lakṣaṇasya hetoḥ kṣaṇika tva svabhāva tvena iti yāvat pṛcchataḥ ca ayam abhiprāyaḥ iha dvividhāḥ santaḥ kṛtakāḥ ca ghaṭa ādayaḥ akṛtakāḥ ca ākāśa ādayaḥ 
[75,iii^2]	tatra ye tāvat akṛtakāḥ te sat akāraṇa vat nityam iti nitya lakṣaṇa yogāt anityāḥ eva na bhavanti kutas eva kṣaṇikāḥ iti na sattvasya kṣaṇika tva svabhāva tā ye api santaḥ kṛtakāḥ teṣām api mugdara ādi anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyitayā vināśasya sa hetuka tvāt tad vetva sannidhau avināśāt kṛtaka ātmanaḥ api sattvasya kṣaṇika tva svabhāva tā na samasti eva iti na anvaya vyatirekayoḥ sambhavaḥ iti avaśyam ca vināśaḥ daṇḍa ādi anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyī dṛṣṭa tvāt tathā hi abhighāta agni saṃyoga nāśa pratyaya sannidhim vinā saṃsargitām yāti na vināśaḥ ghaṭa ādibhiḥ 
[76,i_76,ii^1]	anyatra api ca anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam eva hetumat tā vyavahāra nivandhanam abhyupeyate saugataiḥ api tat iha api asti iti kinna tad vyavahāraḥ pravartyatte iti nanu ca anvaya niścayam pratipādayatā bādhaka pramāṇa vṛtti vaśāt tad svabhāva tā pūrvam eva pratipāditāḥ anvaya niścayaḥ api svabhāva hetau ityādi vacanāt tat kutas asya pūrva pakṣasya avasaraḥ satyam kintu pūrva ācāryaiḥ kṛtaka tvasya kṣaṇikatāyām sādhyāyām paraiḥ kṛtakānām ante avaśyam hetu nibandhana vināśa upagamāt tad vetva yoga pratipādanena anapekṣā vināśam prati viparyaye bādhakam pramāṇam tādātmya prasādhakam uktam tat prasaṅga mukhena kṛta kalkṣaṇasya eva sattvasya tad ātma tām gamayati na anyasya iti darśayitum 
[76,ii^2]	artha kriyā virodha lakṣaṇam tu sarvasya sattvasya iti vastu mātreṇa prāk uktam api vipañcayitum pūrva pakṣa upanyāsaḥ akṛtaka lakṣaṇam tu sattvam na sambhavati eva niyāmakam hetum antareṇa deśa kāla svabhāva niyama ayogāt tatas pūrva ācāryaiḥ na tasya eka aṅga vaikalyāt eva sat akāraṇa vat nityam iti nitya tā sambhavaḥ iti na tad ātma tām prati yatnaḥ kṛtaḥ śāstra kāraḥ tu sāmānyena sattvasya kṣaṇika svabhāva tām kṛtaka lakṣaṇasya api ca deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭasya api vastu sthityā eva tad ātmatām artha kriyā virodhena na para upagata avaśyambhā vi vināśasya ahetuka tayā viśeṣa abhāvāt utpanna mātrasya abhāva prasaṅgena pratipādayiṣyati 
[77,i_77,ii^1]	tatra pūrva ācārya uktam sarvasya sataḥ kṛtakasyavaśyam ante hetu kṛtaḥ vināśaḥ iti yaḥ paririṣyate tam pratyanapekṣa tvam khyāpayitum upakramate vināśa hetu ayogāt iti yadi tarhi nāśasya hetuḥ na asti sa teṣām kṛtakānām satām avaśyam bhāvī vināśaḥ kutas na hi ākasmikaḥ kaścid svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ iti āha svabhāvataḥ eva bhavati asmāt kāryam iti bhāva śabdaḥ hetu vacanaḥ tena sva hetubhyaḥ eva naśvarāḥ naśana śīlāḥ sūcī agre sarṣapāḥ iva anavasthāyinaḥ sva ātmani bhāvāḥ jāyante na eṣām kṛtaka lakṣaṇānām satām bhāvānām sva hetubhyaḥ niṣpannānām anyatas abhighāta āde rvināśa utpattiḥ kutas tasyāḥ bhighāta agni saṃyoga ādeḥ tad hetu tayā upagatasya asāmarthyāt tathā hi agni saṃyoga ādi kāle tritayam lakṣayāmaḥ 
[77,ii^2_78,i]	tat eva kāṣṭha ādikam vināśyam aṅgāra ādikam avasthā antaram kāṣṭha ādi nivṛtti lakṣaṇam ca abhāvam tuccha rūpam na aparam yatra agni saṃyoga ādeḥ vyāparaḥ cintyeta etāvatyām ca vastu gatau na kvacid atra vināśa hetauḥ sāmarthyam yujyate yatas na hi vināśa hetuḥ bhāva sya indhana ādeḥ sva hetubhyaḥ sthira rūpasya utpannasya svabhāvam evā sthira ātma tā lakṣaṇam karoti kutas tasya indhana ādeḥ sva hetubhyaḥ eva nirvṛtteḥ na hi sthira ātmanaḥ nirvṛttasya anyathā bhāvaḥ tad ātmā śakyate kartum tasya hetu antarāt paścāt bhavataḥ artha antara tva prasaṅgāt tasya eva anyathā tva ayogāt tatra hetu vyāpārasya kalpayitum aśakyatvāt athavā tritaye samīkṣyamāṇe yat tāvat vināśyam kāṣṭha ādi na tad svabhāvam eva agni saṃyoga ādiḥ vināśa hetuḥ karoti tasya sva hetubhyaḥ eva nirvṛtteḥ iti 
[78,ii_78,iii]	kumārilaḥ tu manyate na agni saṃyoga ādinā bhāva svabhāvaḥ eva kriyate kintu indhana ādeḥ pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ sa ca indhana ādi rūpa vikalam aṅgāra ādikam uttaram bhāva antaram eva tat uktam na astitā payasaḥ daghni pradhvaṃsa abhāva lakṣaṇam iti tathāvidhasya ca abhāvasya hetumat ta upagamaḥ na eva virudhyate tathā ca āha kaścid bhāva antara vinirmuktaḥ bhāvaḥ atra anupalambha vat abhāvaḥ sammataḥ tasya hetoḥ kinna samudbhavaḥ iti 
[78,iv]	tat etat kaumārilam darśanam apanudan āha na api ityādi yadi uttaram kārya ātmakam bhāva antaram eva abhāvaḥ tadā agni saṃyoga ādayaḥ aṅgāra ādi janmani vyāpriyantaḥ iti iṣṭam eva asmākam kintu bhāva antara karaṇe abhyupagamyamāne agni ādīnām indhana ādau avyāpārāt tad avastham eva indhana ādikam tatas ca yathā agni saṃyogāt prāk indhana ādeḥ upalabdhiḥ anyā ca tad sādhya artha kriyā tathā aṅgāra ādi utpattau api upalabdhi ādeḥ prasaṅgaḥ 
[78,v]	nanu bhāva antarasya pradhvaṃsa abhāva rūpa tāyām tad utpattau indhana ādīnām pradhvasta tvāt asatām katham tathā upalabdhi ādi prasaṅgaḥ satyam evam manyate sarvasya indhana ādeḥ anyasya gavā ādeḥ api tathā abhāvaḥ mā bhūt iti aṅgāra ādeḥ dhvaṃsa vyavasthāyām nibandhanam abhidhānīyam tasmin sati tad nivṛttiḥ iti ced aho vacana kauśalam yatas nivṛtteḥ tuccha sva bhāva tā anaṅgīkaraṇāt tat eva bhāva antaram aṅgāra ādikam nivṛttim brūṣe tat ayam arthaḥ sampannaḥ aṅgāra ādi bhāve aṅgāra ādi bhāvāt aṅgāra ādikam dhvaṃsaḥ kāṣṭha ādeḥ iti na ca aṅgāra ādi bhāve tad bhāvaḥ sva ātmani hetu bhāva ayogāt agni ādibhyaḥ ca tad utpāda vacanāt indhana ādi upamarddena aṅgāra ādi bhāvāt asya dhvaṃsaṃrūpa tā iti ced kaḥ ayam upamarddaḥ nāma yadi nivṛttiḥ sa aṅgāra ādi lakṣaṇā eva iti na pūrvasmāt viśiṣyate tasmāt svarasataḥ nivartate kāṣṭha ādiḥ agni ādibhyaḥ tu aṅgāra ādi janma iti eva bhadrakam anyathā kāṣṭha ādeḥ tathā upalabdhi ādi prasaṅgaḥ katham na syāt 
[79,i_79,ii]	api ca yadi bhāva antaram pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ ye ete anupajāta vikārāḥ pradīpa buddhi ādayaḥ dhvaṃsante teṣām katarat bhāva antaram pradhvaṃsaḥ vyavasthāpyate te api avyakta tām ātma bhāvam ca vikāram eva dhvaṃsam samalambante iti ced na pradīpa ādeḥ bhāva rūpa avyakta tā bhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt yadi hi śakti rūpa tā pattiḥ avyakta tā tadā śakteḥ kārya darśana unnīyamāna rūpa tvāt tad abhāve katham pradīpa ādayaḥ śakti ātmanā avasthitāḥ kalperan atha upalabdhi yogya tā vikala ātma tā pattiḥ avyaktiḥ atra api tad ātmanā avasthitau na eva pramāṇam asti na ca apramāṇakam ādriyante vacaḥ vipaścitaḥ ātmanaḥ ca asattvāt katham tad bhāvaḥ buddhi ādīnām vikāraḥ pariṇāmaḥ ca anyatra vihita pratikriya tvāt na iha pratanyate iti alam prasaṅgena syāt matam bhāva antareṇa aṅgāra ādinā āvṛta tvāt indhana ādeḥ tathā upalabdhi ādayaḥ na bhavanti iti atas āha na api ityādi svabhāva antaram anyasya indha na ādeḥ āvaraṇam apinayujyeta tad avasthe avicalita rūpe tasmin indhanādau satya āvaraṇasya api na kevalam anupalabdhi ādeḥ ayogāt 
[80,i]	na kevalam bhāva svabhāvaḥ bhāva antaram vā vināśa hetunā na kriyate bhāva abhāvaḥ api na kriyate iti āha na api ityādi kutas iti ced abhāvasya vidhinā paryudāsena vivakṣitāt bhāvāt anyatayā kāryatva upagame kriyamāṇe kim indhana ādi rūpaḥ eva asau atha arthāntaram iti vyatireka avyatireka avikalpa anatikramāt tatra ca uktaḥ eva doṣaḥ 
[80,ii]	nanu prasajya pratiṣedha ātmā tuccha rūpaḥ asau agni ādi janyaḥ abhyupeyate tad bhāve ca indhanadinām naiḥsvābhāvyāt kutas pūrva doṣa avasaraḥ sa ca avaśyam agni ādi bhāva abhāva anuvidhāyitayā tad kāryaḥ tad bhāva vyavahārasya anyatra api tad nibandhana tvāt tat uktam san bodha gocara prāḥ tadbhāve na upalabhyate naśyan bhāvaḥ katham tasya na nāśaḥ kārya tām iyat prāc abhūtvā bhavan bhāvaḥ hetubhyaḥ jāyate yathā bhūtvā api na bhavan tadvat hetubhyaḥ na bhavati ayam iti 
[80,iii^1]	atas āha bhāva pratiṣedha ityādi ayam abhiprāyaḥ yadi anapekṣita bhāva antara saṃsargaḥ cyuti mātram eva tuccha rūpam dhvaṃsaḥ tadā tatra kāraka vyāpāraḥ na eva sambhavati bhavana dharmiṇī eva tad sambhavāt tasya api abhūtvā bhāva upagamāt kārya tā na virudhyate iti ced na bhavana dharmaṇaḥ bhāva rūpa tā prāpteḥ abhāva tva hāneḥ yatas bhavati iti bhāvaḥ bhaṇyate na aparam aṅkura ādeḥ api bhāva śabda pravṛtti nimittam artha kriyā sāmarthyām iti ced sarva sāmarthya virahiṇaḥ tarhi asya katham pratīti viṣaya tā na hi akāraṇam pratīti viṣayaḥ atiprasaṅgāt 
[80,iii^2]	tad aviṣayasya vā katham hetumat ta avagatiḥ vastu tā vā yena ucyate tuccha rūpam eva tat vastu iti pratīti janaka tve vā katham na sāmarthya sambandhi tā saditi pratyaya aviṣayasya katham bhāvatā iti ced kārya tāpyasya katham sva hetu bhāve bhāvāt iti ced katham tarhi sat paratyaya aviṣaya tā tathā hi yadi sva hetu bhāve bhavati iti pratīyate sat iti api pratīyeta yatas asti iti sat iti vadanti vidvāṃsaḥ na ca asti bhavati bhāvaḥ san iti śabdānām artha bhedaḥ paramārthataḥ kaścid 
[80,iii^3]	abhāva ātmaka tayā eva bhavati asau iti ced na vyāhata tvāt yatas na bhavati iti abhāvaḥ ucyate sa katham bhavati iti vyapadiśyate pratiṣṭhitena kenacid rūpeṇa sva jñāna ātmani apratibhāsanāt na bhavaḥ iti ced atyanta parokṣāṇām cakṣuḥ ādīnām abhāvatā prasaṅgaḥ na teṣām jñāna hetu rūpa tayā pratibhāsanāt iti ced na asya api bhavitṛ rūpa tayā avabhāsanāt sarva rūpa vivekasya ca katham bhūtyā sambandhaḥ kenacid rūpeṇa unmajjanam hi bhavanam jñāna viṣaya tayā asya api ca ted hetu rūpa tayā avabhāsanasya tulya tvāt ahetoḥ ca viṣaya tva ayogāt asmākam tu abhāva buddhyaḥ sva vāsanā paripāka anvayāḥ nirviṣayā eva abhāvasya ca bhavitṛ tve katham praryudāsāt prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ bhidyeta asat rūpasya vidhānena paryudāsāt sa bhidyate iti ced na asat rūpsya bhavana virodhāt bhavati iti hi bhūtyā sattayā abhisambadhyate tatra katham sat rūpasya vidhānam paryudāsaḥ eva ekaḥ nañarthaḥ ca syāt sarvatra vidheḥ prādhānyāt saḥ api vā na bhavet yadi hi kiñcid kutaścid nivartyeta tadā tad vyatireki saṃspṛśyeta tad paryudāsena 
[80,iii^4]	tat ca na asti sarvatra nivṛttiḥ bhavati iti ukte vastu antarasya eva kasyacid vidhānāt tathā anena vastu antaram eva uktam syāt na tayoḥ vivekaḥ aviveke ca na paryudāsaḥ aprastuta abhidhānam ca syāt bhāva nivṛttau prastutāyām asat ātmanaḥ vastu antarasya eva vidhānāt na ca asya sva rūpeṇa asat ātmaka tvam sva rūpeṇa api asataḥ kāryatva virodhāt para rūpeṇa tu sarvam eva vastu asat ātmakam iti na asya ghaṭa ādeḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ bhavatu vā ayam a bhāvaḥ agni ādibhyaḥ tad bhāve kim iti na upalabhyante kāṣṭha ādayaḥ tathā hi agni ādīnām anya kriyāyām caritārtha tvāt anivṛttāḥ eva tebhyaḥ indhana ādayaḥ prāgvat upalabhyeran tad upamarddena dhvaṃsasya utpatteḥ iti ced katham tad upamarddaḥ na tāvat pradhvaṃsa abhāvena indhana sattā kāle tasya abhāvāt na agni ādibhiḥ dhvaṃsa āvirbhāvaḥ eva teṣām vyāpāra upagamāt na ca utpannaḥ pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ indhana ādīn vihanti yaugapadya prasaṅgāt dhvaṃsena vināśane ca vikalpa trayasya tad avastha tvāt tatas ca anavasthā saḥ eva dhvaṃsaḥ indhana ādeḥ agni ādi janmā nivṛttiḥ atas asya anupalabdhiḥ iti ced 
[80,iii^5]	katham anyaḥ anyasya nivṛttiḥ atiprasaṅgāt yadi ca ayam hetumān tad bhedāt ātma bhedam kim na anubhavati śāli yava aṅkura ādayaḥ api kāraṇa bhedāt eva ātma bhedam atyanta vilakṣaṇam anubhavantaḥ adhyakṣataḥ eva avasīyante na tu evam anapekṣita bhāva antara saṃsargaḥ cyuti mātra lakṣaṇaḥ dhvaṃsaḥ tasya abhighāta agni saṃyoga ādi kāraṇa bhede api tuccha rūpa tayā eka rūpasya sva jñāna ātmani avabhāsanāt na hi bhāva śūnyatām vihāya aparam tatra kiñcid rūpam īkṣāmahe vistarataḥ ca etat kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhau vicāritam iti āstām tāvat iha tasmāt agni ādi saṃyoga kāle na tasya kiñcid bhavati na bhavati eva kevala miti eva upagantu yuktam yatas na ayam kasyacid bhāvena naṣṭaḥ nāma kintu yatas svayam asthira rūpa tayā bhūtaḥ tatas naṣṭaḥ nāma tena na asya abhavanam anyat vā kiñcid bhavati tathā ca bhavana dharmaṇaḥ kasyacid abhāvāt bhāvam bhavantam kutaścid na karoti iti kriyā pratiṣedhaḥ eva agni saṃyoga ādeḥ syāt evam ca sati kartā agni saṃyoga ādiḥ na bhavati iti akartuḥ ahetutvam iti tasmai nna vināśa hetuḥ kaścid 
[82,i]	na kevalam asāmarthyādhi nāśa hetu ayogaḥ kintu vaiyarthyāt ca tat eva āha yadi svabhāvataḥ naśvaraḥ naśana śīlaḥ sva ātmani anavasthāyī sthātum aśaktaḥ yathā sūcī agre sarṣapaḥ tasya na kiñcid nāśa kāraṇaiḥ kim kāraṇam svayam nāśāt tad svabhāva tayā eva asthira svabhāva tayā eva na hi prakṛtyā eva sthātum aśakte sūcī agre sarṣape tad asthitaye prayāsaḥ phalavān bhavet 
[83,i]	atra eva vyāptim ādarśayati yaḥ hi ityādi na punar tad bhāve tad svabhāva tve janakāt hetoḥ rhetu antaram apekṣate na hi prakāśa ādayaḥ ityādinā dṛṣṭānta vivaraṇam tad ātma tāyāḥ hetu antara anapekṣaṇena vyāptim tādātmya sādhakena pramāṇena darśayati tad ā ātmanaḥ yaḥ yasya svabhāvaḥ tad svabhāvasya tādātmya abhāve hetu antaram apekṣamāṇasya sva hetoḥ niṣpannasya api tad svabhāva tva abhāve nairātmyasya niḥsvabhāva tāyāḥ prasaṅgāt tadvat prakāśa ādi vat na punar paścāt tad ātmatāyām asthiti dharma ātma tāyām hetu antaram apekṣate iti pramāṇa phalam asthiti dharmā ced naśvara svabhāvaḥ ced svabhāvataḥ sva hetubhyaḥ niṣpannaḥ bhāvaḥ iti pakṣa dharma upasaṃhāraḥ viruddhvi āpta upalabdhiḥ ca iyam hetu antara apekṣā anapekṣayoḥ paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tayā virodhāt hetu antarā anapekṣayā ca tat svābhāva tāyāḥ vyāpta tvāt 
[83,ii]	atra ca paraspa vacana avakāśam aśaṅkayā āha bīja ādi vat ityādi syāt etat ityādinā etat eva vibhajate kevalāḥ na janayanti iti kutas iti ced salila kṣiti ādeḥ sva hetu vyatiriktasya aṅkura ādi janana svabhāvānām api bīja ādīnām tad ātmatāyām apekṣaṇāt tatas ca na punar tad bhāve hetu antaram apekṣantaḥ iti anekāntaḥ tadvat bhāvaḥ api indhana ādiḥ sva hetoḥ naśvara ātmā niṣpannaḥ api vināśe vinaśvara ātma tāyām syāt iti dārṣṭa antikam na bīja ādi vat anekāntaḥ kutas tad svabhāvasya aṅkura ādi janana svabhāvasya bīja ādeḥ aṅkura ādi jananāt tad ātma tāyām hetu antara anapekṣaṇāt yaḥ ca kṣiti ādīkam apekṣamāṇaḥ na janayati kuśūla ādi avasthaḥ tasya ajanakasya ca atad svabhāva tvāt aṅkura ādi janana svabhāva tva abhāvāt tatra tad ātmatā lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ na vartate eva iti na tena anekāntaḥ 
[83,iii^1]	nanu pratyabhijñā pratyakṣate eva bija ādīḥ eka svabhāvaḥ lakṣyate tatra kutas ayam jana svabhāva tva ajanana svabhāva tva lakṣaṇaḥ bhedaḥ yatas anekāntaḥ na syāt na ca apramāṇam pratyabhijñā tatra apūrva artha vijñānam ityādi pramāṇa lakṣaṇa yogāt sat samprayogeṇa indriyāṇām bhāvataḥ ca pratyakṣam eva pratyabhijñānam na ca pratyakṣāt gariṣṭham pramāṇam asti yatas tad viṣayasya bheda siddhyā bādhām anubhavat apramāṇam etat syāt iti āśaṅkayā āha atas eva janakatvā janaka tvāt eva viruddha dharma adhyāsāt tayoḥ avasthayoḥ janakā janaka avasthayoḥ bīja ādeḥ vastu bhedaḥ svabhāva bhedaḥ niśceyaḥ adhyavasātavyaḥ 
[83,iii^2]	yathā hi śāli bījam tad aṅkura janana svabhāvam tad bhāve śāli aṅkura bhāva darśanāt pratyakṣatas avagamyate yava bījam ca atad janana svabhāvam tad bhāve śāli aṅkura anupalabdhyā tad vivikta yava bīja grāhi pratyakṣa rūpayā pratīyate tathā atra api avasthā dvaye śālibījasya tad aṅkura viviktā vivikta avasthā agrāhi pratyakṣa balāt eva sva aṅkura jana kājanaka svabhāva tā kinna niścīyate iṣyate eva avasthayoḥ bhedaḥ avasthāvataḥ tu abhedaḥ iti ced na tasya avasthā rūpa vivekinā rūpa antareṇa pratyakṣe pratibhāsana prasaṅgāt na hi yat anātma rūpa vivekena sva jñāne na pratibhāsane tasya pratyakṣatā yuktā avasthā tadvatoḥ svabhāva bheda abhāvāt katham rūpa antareṇa pratibhāsanam iti ced nanu avasthābhyaḥ anavāpta rūpa bhedasya avasthānām iva ātmanaḥ tad bhede satyabhedaḥ na saṅgacchate tatas ca asya avasthānām iva ātma bhedam anubhavataḥ katham avasthātṛ tvam 
[83,iii^3]	 avasthā bhede api abhinna rūpasya tathā vyavasthānāt kathañcid bhedasya api bhāvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced yadi yama ātmānam purodhāya ayam avasthātā avasthāḥ ca imāḥ iti bhaṇyate tena avasthā tad vatoḥ bhedaḥ tadā bhedaḥ eva iti kathañcid iti andha padam etat tatas asya pratyakṣatāyām anātma rūpa vivekinā rūpa antareṇa avabhāsana prasaṅgaḥ na nivartate atha tena ātmanā bhedaḥ avasthāvat bheda prasaṅgaḥ avasthātuḥ tadvat avasthānām abhedasya vā tayoḥ api kathañcid bheda abhedau iti ced tayoḥ tarhi avasthā tadvat ātmanoḥ bhedavatoḥ kathañcid animittam rūpa antaram iṣṭam syāt tathā ca tasya api tābhyām kathañcid bhedaḥ anyathā tad eka svabhāvāt atyantam abhedāt avasthā tadvatoḥ parasparam atyantam bheda abhedau prasajyeyātām 
[83,iii^4]	rūpa antarasya kathañcid bhede tad nibandhanam aparam rūpam tathā asya api tat anyat iti aparimita rūpa tā eva ekaikasya vastunaḥ samāsajyeta na ca aparimita rūpa pratibhāsi pratyakṣam anubhavāmaḥ ananubhavantaḥ ca katham tad kalpanayā ātmanā eva ātmānam vipralabhemahi tasmāt avasthā rūpa vivekena upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalambhāt aparimita rūpa tā prasaṅgāt ca kathañcid bheda abhedavataḥ avasthātuḥ asattvam eva tāḥ ca avasthāḥ jana kājanaka svabhāva bhedavatyaḥ pratyakṣataḥ eva avagamyante iti tad eka tva adhyavasāyi pratyabhijñānam tabdādhām anubhavat katham pramāṇam syāt yatas bīja ādinām aṅkura ādi janana svabhāvānām api tad ātmatāyām hetu antara apekṣaṇāt prāktanasya hetoḥ anaikāntika tā bhavet 
[85,i]	bhavatu vā avasthātā kaścid tasya api etat eva bhedam sādhayati tathā hi tayoḥ janakā janaka avasthayoḥ iti saptamī dvivacanam etat tadā bhavati tat ayam arthaḥ janaka avastha āyāma janaka avasthāyām ca vastunaḥ dharmi lakṣaṇasya bhedaḥ svabhāva nānātvam atas eva jana kājanaka svabhāva tvāt eva pratyakṣau asitāt niśceyaḥ niścaya lakṣaṇaḥ tatra vyavahāraḥ kartavyaḥ viṣayasya viruddha dharma adhyāla sakṣaṇasya darśanāt iti 
[85,ii^1]	na ca śākyate vaktum avasthāḥ eva aṅkura ādi janana svabhāvāḥ na avasthātā iti tasya sarva sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇasya asattva prasaṅgāt tatas yat eka rūpa tayā pratyabhijñānam bhāveṣu tat pūrva uttara kālayoḥ jana kājanaka svabhāva bheda vyavasthāpaka pratyakṣa nibandhanām anubhavat vādhām katham iva pramāṇam syāt tad pratibhāsinaḥ ca abhinna rūpasya alīka tve akṣa samudbhavām api vṛttim anubhavataḥ asya sat samprayoga ja tvā abhāvāt taimirika ādi dhiyām iva kutas pratyakṣatā na ca artha kriyā nibandhanam rūpam apāsya bīja ādeḥ aparaḥ paramārthataḥ svabhāvaḥ asti yasya adhigamāt pratyabhijñānam pramāṇam bhavet artha kriyā sāmarthya lakṣaṇa tvāt parama artha satas 
[85,ii^2]	tasmāt sadṛśa apara bhāva nibandhanaḥ eva ayam keśa kadalī stamba ādiṣu iva ākāra sāmya tā mātra apahṛta hṛdayānām bhrāntaḥ eva tattva adhyavasāyaḥ mantavyaḥ tatas sataḥ api pratikṣaṇam bhedasya anupalakṣaṇam bālānām yadā tu vidhura pratyaya upanipātāt visadṛśa apara bhāva prasavaḥ tadā asya tattva adhyavasāyī pratyabhijñā pratyayaḥ na bhūtim avalambate na ca tad eka ākāra parāmarśa pratyaya janaka tvāt aparam sādṛśyam bheda aviśeṣe api ca sva hetu bala āyāta prakṛti vaśāt kecid eva eka ākāra parāmarśa pratyaya lakṣaṇām artha jñāna ādi lakṣaṇām vā artha kriyām kurvanti na aparaḥ iti vipañcitam pramāṇa vārtikaḥ eva śāstra kṛtā iti na iha prapañcyate 
[86,i^1]	avaśyam ca bīja ādeḥ janakā janaka avasthayoḥ vastu bhedaḥ yathā uktaḥ avagantavyaḥ iti darśayitum ana mānam abhedasya bādhakam āha bhāvānām bīja ādīnām sva kārya janakaḥ yaḥ svabhāvaḥ tasya teṣu satsu anyathātva abhāvāt kadācid ajanakatva asambhavāt tad svabhāvasya aṅkura ādi janaka svabhāvasya paścāt iva salila ādi kāraṇa sannidhāna iva prāk api kuśūla ādi avasthiti kāle api sva kārya janana prasaṅgāt tathā hi salila ādi sannidhāne api bīja ādiḥ sva rūpeṇa eva kāryam karoti na para rūpeṇa yaḥ ca asya tadā akārya janakaḥ svabhāvaḥ sa ced prāk api asti saḥ eva ayam iti pratyabhijñāyām puras avasthāyinaḥ janaka svabhāvasya prācya rūpa abheda adhyavasāyāt tatas kim iti prāk api tat kāryam na kuryāt iti prayogaḥ yat yadā yat janana svabhāvam tat tadā tat janayati eva 
[86,i^2_87,i]	ajanakasya janakatva svabhāva virodhāt anyasya api vā tad svabhāvatā āpatteḥ yathā tat eva bīja ādikam salila ādi sannidhi kāle kuśūla ādi avasthāsu api ca idam bīja ādikam sva kārya janana svabhāvam eva pratyabhijñayā vyavasthāpyate iti svabhāva hetu prasaṅgaḥ na ca janayati tasmāt na tad janana svabhāvam iti viparyaya prayogaḥ yat yadā yat janana svabhāvam nirvartyam kāryam na janayati na tat tadā tad janana svabhāvam tat yathā śāli aṅkura janana svabhāva nirvartyam kāryam ajanayat kodrava bījam na janayati ca salila ādi kāraṇa sannidheḥ prāk tad kārya janana svabhāva nirvartyam sva kāryam bīja ādikam iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ tatas anumānataḥ api bādhām anubhavat pratyabhijñānam katham pramāṇam syāt nanu ca anena bādhyamānasya anumānasya aprāmāṇyāt katham bādhaka tvam aniścita pramāṇa bhāvena kutas bādhā na api itaretara āśraya tvam na hi pratyabhijñānasya aprāmāṇyāt etat anumānam pramāṇam kintu sva sādhya pratibandhāt sa ca viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa balāt niścitaḥ iti 
[87,ii]	na pratyakṣāt anyat gariṣṭham pramāṇam iti ced na pratyabhijñāyāḥ pratyakṣa tva asiddheḥ na hi iyam anumānena pratyakṣa ātmikā satī bādhyate iti brūmahe kim kṛtam ca pratyakṣasya garīyaḥ tvam tad vayarthasya asambhave abhāvāt pramāṇam ucyate tat ca anumānasya api artha pratibaddha liṅga janya tayā samānam iti na asya kaścid viśeṣaḥ yadi ca anumāna virodham aśnuvānā api pratyabhijñā pramāṇam tat ākārasya sāmyāt tat eka tām pratiyatī nīla itara kusuma ādeḥ pratītiḥ kim na pramāṇam na hi kusuma phala ādi kārya darśana unnīyamānaḥ bhedaḥ pratyakṣataḥ tathā abhāvam anubhavati vistarataḥ ca pratyabhijñā prāmāṇya nirāsaḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhau eva vihitaḥ iti āstām tāvat iha 
[87,iii_88,i]	yatas evam uktena prakāreṇa janakā janaka avasthayoḥ bīja ādeḥ vastu bhedaḥ tasmāt yaḥ antyaḥ avasthā viśeṣaḥ yad anantaram aṅkura ādi kārya prasavaḥ saḥ eva aṅkura janana svabhāvaḥ kārya darśana unnīyamāna rūpa tvāt tad janana svabhāva tāyāḥ yadi tarhi saḥ eva aṅkura janana svabhāvaḥ pūrva bhāvinām avasthā bhedānām atad janana svabhāva tvāt katham teṣu tad kāraṇa vyapadeśaḥ aṅkura arthibhiḥ vā tad upādānam iti atas āha pūrva bhāvinaḥ tu kuśūla ādi avasthiti kāla bhāvinaḥ tu avasthā viśeṣāḥ aṅku kāraṇasya antyasya avasthā viśeṣasya kāraṇāni pratyaya antara upadhīyamāna viśeṣebhyaḥ paramparayā tebhyaḥ tad utpatteḥ atas teṣu upacārataḥ kāraṇa vyapadeśaḥ aṅkura arthibhiḥ ca upādānam yatas tad svabhāvasya bīja ādeḥ jananam na hetu antara apekṣam yat jānakam apekṣate na tasya tad jana svabhāva tvam iti tasmāt na anekāntaḥ bīja ādi vat tad svabhāva tvāt iti asya hetoḥ iti upasaṃhāraḥ 
[88,ii]	tat evam yadā tāvat pratyabhijñānam pratyakṣa pramāṇa tayā sthairya siddhaye paraiḥ ūcyate bīja ādi vat anekāntam pratipādayitum tadā tasya uktena prakāreṇa pratyakṣa anumānābhyām bādhyamāna tvāt tad ātmatā na asti iti kutas tatas ekatā bhāvānām yatas anekāntaḥ syāt iti pratipāditam yadā tu pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt pūrva apara kālayoḥ eka svabhāvā bīja ādayaḥ iti hetutayā ucyate paraiḥ tadā ayama siddhaḥ hetuḥ na ca sa pakṣe kvacid vartate iti āha kṣaṇikeṣu bhāveṣu asmābhiḥ iṣyamāṇeṣu aikya abhāvāt iti sambandhaḥ 
[88,iii]	atha yasya api kṣaṇikāḥ bhāvāḥ tasya api bīja ādīnām pratikṣaṇam aikya abhāve api viśeṣa anupalakṣaṇāt antya kṣaṇa vat sarveṣām janaka svabhāvānām api tad bhāvam prati salila ādi apekṣa tvāt tad avastham anaikāntika tvam iti āśaṅkayā āha apara apara utpatteḥ kṣaṇikaiḥ api na anekāntaḥ aparebhyaḥ aparebhyaḥ ca pratyayebhyaḥ pratikṣaṇam utpatteḥ kṣaṇikānām bhinna śakti tvāt anti a kṣaṇa vat janaka svabhāva tā virahāt kutas taiḥ api anekāntar syāt na hi kāraṇa bheda upadhīyamāna janmanām viśeṣa anupalakṣaṇe api abhinna svabhāva tā yuktā hetu bhedān anuvidhāne ahetuka tā prasaṅgāt tathā ca vakṣyati apara apara pratyaya yogena pratikṣaṇam bhinna śaktayaḥ santanvantaḥ saṃskārāḥ yadi api kutaścid sāmyāt samāna rūpāḥ pratīyante tathā api bhinnaḥ eva eṣām svabhāvaḥ tena kiñcid eva kasyacid kāraṇam iti 
[89,i]	yat uktam tad svabhāvasya jananāt iti asya an ekāntam udbhāvayan āha paraḥ te bīja kṣiti ādayaḥ antyāḥ ante bhavāḥ pratyekam aṅkura janane samarthāḥ khaṇḍaśas kāraṇebhyaḥ kārya utpāda abhāvāt bhavadbhiḥ iṣyante iti kinna janayanti pratyekam tatas ca eṣām ekaḥ eva kaścid aṅkuram janayati tad anye tu tad svabhāvāḥ api na janayanti iti tad svabhāvasya jananāt iti anekāntaḥ tadvat kuśūla ādi avasthāḥ api bīja ādayaḥ aṅkura ādi janana svabhāvāḥ api na jānayiṣyanti iti taiḥ aneka antar tad avasthaḥ eva iti manyate paraḥ 
[89,ii]	atra āha iti yat evam tvam manyase pareṇa sāmānyena abhidhānāt sāmānyena eva uttaram āha janayanti eva na atra sva kārya janane anyathā bhāvaḥ ajanaka tvam āśaṅkanīyam kutas svabhāvasya avaiparītyāt yai hi na janayeyuḥ janana svabhāvāḥ eva na syuḥ tad svabhāvāḥ ca iṣyante iti avaśyam janayanti tathā ca kutas anaikāntaḥ iti bhāvaḥ 
[89,iii]	pratyekam antyānām janaka tve kāryasya ekena jananāt apareṣām upayogasya nirviṣaya tvāt ajananam eva iti manyamānaḥ āha paraḥ teṣu antyeṣu sahakāriṣu saha yugapad karaṇa śīleṣu samartha svabhāveṣu tad kārya kriyā yogyeṣu abhyupagamyamāneṣu satsu kāryasya ekena eva janita tvāt kaḥ aparasya upayogaḥ na eva kaścid tat kim ucyate janayanti eva iti etat pariharati na vai na eva bhāvānām bīja ādīnām kācid prekṣā pūrva kāritā buddhi pūrva kāri tā yatas prekṣā pūrva kāritvāt ayam asmāsu anyatamaḥ ekaḥ api samarthaḥ kārya janane kim atra asmābhiḥ kartavyam iti ālocya apare nivarteran audāsīnyam bhajamānāḥ tad kārya janane na vyāpriyeran yasmāt te bīja ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ nirabhiprāya vyāpārāḥ paryālocanā śūnya vyāpārāḥ ekatas utpadyamāne kārye sarve eva vyāpriyante bhavana dharmaṇi ca kārye teṣām prāgbhāvaḥ eva vyāpāraḥ tad anyasya ayogāt yadi hi vyāpṛtāt anyaḥ eva vyāpāraḥ tadā tatas eva kārya utpādāt vyāpāravataḥ kāraka tvam eva hīyate 
[90,i]	tasya asau vyāpāraḥ tatas tasya kāraka tvam iti ced nanu evam vyāpāra upayogasya kārya anupayogini tatra upacārāt pāramārthikam asya kāraka tvam hīyeta kaḥ ca asya vyāpāreṇa sambandhaḥ samavāyaḥ ced na tasya prāk eva nirasta tvāt samavāyāt ca vyāpāravat tve anyasya api tad kārya anupayoginaḥ tad bhāva prasaṅgaḥ samavāyasya iha iti buddhi hetoḥ eka tvena sarvatra samāna tvāt abhimatena eva vyāpṛtena tabdyā pāra utpādanāt na ati prasaṅgaḥ iti ced nanu tena tad utpādanam tatra samavāya udeva ucyate sa ca sarvatra samānaḥ yena ca pariśrameṇa vyāpāram janayati tena kāryam eva kinna utpādayati yena vyavadhānam āśrīyate yathā ca sva sannidhi mātrena eva ayam vyāpāram janayati na vyāpāra antareṇa anavasthā prasaṅgāt tathā tatas eva kāryam api iti ukta prāyam 
[90,ii_90,iii]	tasmāt bhāvini kārye prāgbhāvaḥ eva kāraṇasya vyāpāraḥ sa ca sarveṣām asti iti sarve eva kārya utpattau vyāpriyante iti vyapadiśyante tat api kāryam sarvebhyaḥ eva jāyate sarveṣām bhāvaḥ eva tad bhāvāt na hi kāryasya kāraṇa abhimata bhāvaḥ eva bhāvam antareṇa aparam janma tathā abhāve hi tatra eva kāraṇa vyāpārāt kārya kriyā eva eṣām na sambhavet tatas ca satsu api kāraṇeṣu katham asya bhāvaḥ upalabdhiḥ vā syāt tad sambandhinaḥ janmanaḥ karaṇāt iti ced na asatā tena sambandha ayogāt svatas eva sattve vā janma artha anupapatteḥ janma kāle ca upalabhyasya ātmanaḥ prāk api bhāvāt tathā upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ rūpa antareṇa bhāve natasya bhāvaḥ syāt rūpa bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt bhāva bhedasya tasmāt upalabhya ātmanaḥ janmanaḥ prāc anupalambhāt asattvam tatas asya janma sambandhi tā kutas tasmāt kāryam eva abhūtvā hetu bhāve bhavati iti bhāvaḥ eva asya tatas janma iti sarvebhyaḥ tat jāyate 
[91,i^1]	nanu ekasya api tat janane sāmarthyāt apareṣām tatra sannidhi lakṣaṇaḥ vyāpāraḥ vyarthaḥ eva iti na tatra pareṣām bhāvaḥ saṅgacchate iti ced āha sva hetoḥ kṣiti bīja salila ādi sāmagrī lakṣaṇasya pariṇāmaḥ kārya utpāda anuguṇa viśeṣavataḥ pratikṣaṇam upadhīyamāna atiśayasya kṣaṇa antarasya prasavaḥ tatas upanidhiḥ kārya deśe sannidhānam dharmaḥ yeṣām te tathā abhavantaḥ kārya deśe sannidhīyamānāḥ na upālambham arhanti ekasya api etad kārya karaṇe samartha tvāt kim atra bhavantaḥ sannihitāḥ iti na paryanuyogam arhanti na hi tad apara sannidhim antareṇa tatra ekasya api bhāvaḥ upapadyate kutas tad prakṛteḥ tad prakṛti tvāt iti bhāva pradhānaḥ nirddeśaḥ 
[91,i^2]	kṣiti bīja salila ādi sāmagrī pariṇāma janya svabhāva tvāt ekaikasya samarthasya tad abhāve kutas kevalasya sambhavaḥ sāmagrī śabda vācyaiḥ kāraṇa bhedaiḥ samartha sva sva lakṣaṇa antara ārambhāt tatas ca pratikṣaṇam upadhīyamāna atiśayasya utpādāt kevalānām ca tad janana svabhāva vaikalyāt tad apara pratyaya yoga janya svabhāva tvāt samartha janakasya hetoḥ etat ca yathāvasaram tatra tatra vyaktīkariṣyati tasmāt yad sāmagrī janya svabhāvaḥ yaḥ bhāvaḥ sa tatra eka abhāve api kāraṇa vaikalyāt na sambhavati iti eka sāmagrī janmanām sahabhāvaḥ niyataḥ sarveṣām teṣām bhāvaḥ eva kāryasya bhāvāt sarve eva janayanti iti tad svabhāvasya jananāt iti atra na anekāntaḥ iti 
[92,i]	yena abhiprāyeṇa te antyāḥ samarthāḥ kinna janayanti iti uktam tam prakaṭayan āha samarthāḥ ityādi siddhāntavādi api janayanti eva iti yat abhiprāyavata uktam tam ādarśayati na tatra eva ityādi etat eva vyācaṣṭe tasya eva ityādi ayam abhiprāyaḥ idam atra samartham idam asamartham iti pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhanābhyām anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyavahriyate anya nimitta abhāvāt tau ca anvaya vyatirekau ekatra eva kārye dṛśyete na apara aparatra iti tasya eva ekasya janane samarthāḥ gamyante iti na apara para jananam te tu yat avasthāḥ janayantaḥ dṛśyante kim tad janana svabhāvāḥ tadā eva āhosvit prāk api iti atra vivādaḥ tatra prāk api tad svabhāva tve paścāt iva prāk api jana prasaṅgaḥ iti pratikṣaṇam bhedaḥ ucyate iti 
[92,ii^1]	siddhāntavādi āha na yathāsvam ityādi evam manyate kim punar idam kāraṇam abhimatam bhavataḥ yadi pratyekam cakṣuḥ ādikam tat ayuktam sāmagrī janya svabhāva tvāt kāryasya tasyāḥ eva kāraṇa tvāt nanu tad avasthāyām pratyekam eva sāmagrī śabda vācyānām janana svabhāva tva abhyupagamāt pratyekam eva cakṣuḥ ādikam kāraṇam yadi evam kaḥ ayam niyamaḥ yat anekasmāt bhavatā anekena bhavitavyam viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt ekena eva tat kāryam kartavyam iti ca na niyama kāraṇam utpaśyāmaḥ ekam ca tat kāryam karoti iti kutas avasitam tad bhāve bhāvāt iti ced anekatra api samānam etat 
[92,ii^2]	tat uktam tasya eveikasya janane samarthāḥ na anyasya iti na aparā para jananam iti na ca anekasmāt bhavat anekam prāpnoti yatas na asmākam bhavatām iva kāraṇam eva kārya ātma tām upaiti yatas aneka pariṇateḥ aneka rūpa tvāt kāryasya aneka tā syāt kintu apūrvam eva keṣucid satsu bhavati tat ca aneka bhāvaḥ eva bhāvāt tat kāryam ucyate tasya kutas aneka tā prasaṅgaḥ yat tva bhinnam rūpam janakam ucyate tasya eka sthitau api bhāvāt tad kārya janana svabhāvāt ca tatas kārya prasava prasaṅgaḥ tad anya sannidhau tasya viśeṣa abhāvāt tadā api vāna janayet tasmāt yā iṣum bhāva abhāvavatsu kāryam bhāva abhāva vat dṛṣṭam te eva viśeṣāḥ janakāḥ iti kutas anekāntaḥ 
[93,i^1]	atha sāmagrīm kāraṇam āśritya ucyate na kāraṇa bhedāt kārya bhedaḥ syāt iti tat na yathāsvam yasyāḥ sāmagryāḥ yaḥ ātmīyaḥ svabhāvaḥ tad bhedena tad viśeṣa upayogataḥ tasya vijñāna lakṣaṇasya kāryasya viśeṣāḥ sāmagrī bhedāt bhinnāḥ svabhāvāḥ teṣu upayogataḥ tad upayogaiḥ bhinna sāmagrī vyāpāraiḥ kāryāḥ ye svabhāva viśeṣāḥ kāryāṇa aṃviśiṣṭāḥ svabhāvāḥ teṣām asaṅkarāt paraspara vyāvṛtta rūpa tvāt sāmagrī bhedāt bhinna rūpa tā eva kāryāṇām iti kathat na kāraṇa bhedāt kārya bhedaḥ syāt 
[93,i^2_94,i]	tathā hi ekā sāmagrī manaskāra tad sāgduṇya ādi lakṣaṇā tatas vikalpa vijñāna mātram jāyate aparā manaskāra indriya mātra lakṣaṇā tatas bhrānta indriya vijñāna sambhavaḥ tad anyā viṣaya indriya manaskāra ātmikā tatas api abhrānta vijñāna sambhūtiḥ iti bhinna sāmagrī janmanām kārya svabhāva viśeṣāṇām asāṅkaryāt asti eva sāmagrī lakṣaṇa kāraṇa bhedāt kāryāṇām bhedaḥ iti nanu yadā viṣaya indriya manaskārebhyaḥ vijñāna sambhavaḥ tadā teṣām upayoga viṣayasya eka tvāt katham asāṅkaryam tathāvidhasya sāṅkaryasya iṣṭa tvāt adoṣaḥ tat uktam tatra eva ekatra sāmarthyāt ityādi katham tarhi teṣām tad janaka tvam yadi tad bhedāt na bhidyate kāryam kim nu vai samagrāṇām anyāni a kārya jananena janaka tvam yatas tad abhāve tat na syāt janaka tvam hi eṣām tad bhāvaḥ eva kasyacid bhāvāt tatra ekasya anekasya vā bhāve teṣām eka aneka janaka tvam ucyate 
[94,ii]	nanu ekasyāḥ sāmagryāḥ anekasya bhāve sāmagrī antara janyebhyaḥ bhavatu bhedaḥ parasparataḥ tu katham tad atad rūpa hetu ja tvāt hi bhāvāḥ tad atad rūpiṇaḥ iṣyante tatra yadā cakṣū rūpamanaskārebhyaḥ vijñāna janma tadā cakṣu ūrū pakṣaṇayoḥ api bhāvāt vijñānena abhinna hetu ja tvāt tayoḥ vijñāna ātma tā vijñānasya vā tad rūpa tā katham na prasajyeta āha ca tat atad rūpiṇaḥ bhāvāḥ tadad rūpa hetu jāḥ tad rūpa ādi kim ajñānam vijñāna abhinna hetu jam iti 
[94,iii]	na eṣa doṣaḥ teṣām yathāsvam svabhāva bhedena nimitta upādāna tayā tad upayogāt manaskāraḥ hi vijñānasya upādāna kāraṇam cakṣuṣaḥ tu sva vijñāna janana yogyasya janamani sahakāri kāraṇam evam itaratra api yathāyogam vācyam tatas anyādaśī sāmagrī cakṣuḥ kṣaṇasya janikā anyādaśī ca vijñāna ādeḥ iti tad vailakṣaṇyāt eva kāryāṇām vailakṣaṇyam 
[94,iv]	syāt etat sarveṣām anvaya vyatirekau anuvidhīyete tadā cakṣuḥ ādi kṣaṇaiḥ iti kutas ayam bhedaḥ iha upādāna bhāvena idam upayujyate anyatra tu saha kāri bhāvena iti bodha rūpa tā ādeḥ anukāra an anukārābhyām tad bhāve vyabhicāra avi abhicārataḥ ca tathā hi vijñānam manaskārasya bodha rūpa tām anukaroti na cakṣuḥ ādeḥ jaḍa ādi bhāvam evam anyat api pratyeyam niyamena ca vijñāna mātra bhāve samanantara pratyayasya vyāpāraḥ na cakṣuḥ ādeḥ cakṣuḥ kṣaṇa antara udaye ca pūrva bhāvinaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ na sva vijñāna yogya tā hetoḥ samanantara pratyayasya evam rūpasya api vācyam tasmāt avasthā bhede api yat eka ākāra parāmarśa pratyaya nibandhana tayā sva santati patita kārya prasūti nimittam tat upādānakāraṇam yat santāna antare prāc avastha apekṣa viśeṣa udaya nibandhanam tat sahakāri kāraṇam sā ca iyam bhāvānām sva hetu parampara yātā prakṛtiḥ yayā kiñcid kāryam sva santāna vyavasthā nibandhanam janayanti aparam ca santāna antara vyapadeśa nibandhanam iti tasyāḥ eva sāmagryāḥ avāntara viśeṣa kṛta tvāt cakṣū rūpa vijñā na kṣaṇānām parasparataḥ vailakṣaṇyam na virudhyate 
[95,i_95,ii]	tasmāt yadi kāraṇa bhedāt kāraṇa aneka tvāt kāryasya bhedaḥ aneka tvam tadā pratibandha abhāvāt anekāntaḥ na ca tat abhyupagamyate iti na kācid kṣatiḥ atha sāmagrī lakṣaṇasya kāraṇasya bhedaḥ sāmagrī antarāt vailakṣaṇyam kāryasya api bhedaḥ atad kāraṇebhyaḥ bhinna svabhāva tā ucyate tadā tasya iha bhāvāt katham na kāraṇa bhedāt kārya bhedaḥ syāt iti abhiprāyavatā na kāraṇa bhedāt kārya bhedaḥ na syāt kutas yathāsvam ityādi abhihitam 
[95,iii^1]	ubhayam ca etat kāryeṣu pramāṇa paridṛṣṭam iti darśayan āha yathā ityādi mṛd piṇḍa ādibhyaḥ hi bhavataḥ ghaṭasya na kāraṇa aneka tve api aneka rūpa tā na api sāmagryantara janyādabhinna svabhāva tā iti udāharaṇa arthaḥ tatra sāmagryantara janyāt tāvat bhedam darśayati mṛd piṇḍāt ityādi iha mṛd piṇḍa kulāla sūtrāṇi vyagra svabhāvāni kāraṇa antara sahitāni iṣṭakā ādi lakṣaṇāni tad anya janyebhyaḥ abhinna svabhāvāni yāni kāryāṇi sādhayanti tebhyaḥ vilakṣaṇam eva samagrāṇi ghaṭa ātmakam kāryam janayanti tathā hi kulāla ādi nirapekṣaḥ mṛd piṇḍaḥ tad anya janyāt vṛkṣa ādeḥ vilakṣaṇam eva upādāna bhāvena mṛd ātmakam kāryam janayan dṛṣṭaḥ kulāla ādi sahitaḥ api tad ātmakam eva ghaṭam 
[95,iii^2]	tak tāraṇā hita viśeṣaḥ ca kevala mṛd piṇḍāt bhinna svabhāva tayā taktāryāt api iṣṭakā ādeḥ vilakṣaṇam eva karoti evam kulāla ādikam api tad anya upādāna sahitam saha kāri bhāvena yat kāryam karoti tad vilakṣaṇam eva mṛd piṇḍa sahitam tad kāraṇa āhita viśeṣam ghaṭa ātmakam kāryam janayati iti samudāya arthaḥ tatra mṛd piṇḍāt bhinnaḥ svabhāvaḥ ghaṭasya ye tad anya upadāna kāraṇa tayā mṛd svabhāvāḥ na bhavanti vṛkṣa ādayaḥ tebhyaḥ bhavati kulālāt mṛd piṇḍa upāda anāhita atiśayāt saha akāri bhāvena upayujyamānāt tasya eva ghaṭasya mṛd piṇḍa upādāna tayā mṛdā ātmanaḥ sataḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ pṛthu budhna udara ādi ākāraḥ tad ātma tayā tad anyebhyaḥ yeṣām mṛd piṇḍaḥ tad anya nimitta sahitaḥ upādānam iṣṭaka ādīnām tebhyaḥ bhinnaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhavati
