[141,ii^1]	siddhāntavādi āha na idam anantara uktam vikalpa dvayam atikrāmati kīdṛśam vikalpa dvayam kim nityaḥ bhāvaḥ ityādi nanu ca kāla antara sthitiḥ adharma tām upagacchataḥ na eva nitya vikalpasya avakāśaḥ na tad upagame api nityatā eva upagatā bhavati tathā hi yadi ayam saṃvatsara sthiti dharmā sva hetubhiḥ janitaḥ tadā saṃvatsara parisamāptau yaḥ asya ādau udaya kāle saṃvatsara sthiti dharmā svabhāvaḥ yatas ayam saṃvatsaram sthitaḥ saḥ eva tad ante api tatas aparam saṃvatsaram avatiṣṭheta tad ante api prathama utpanna saṃvatsara sthiti dharma svabhāva aparityāgāt apara apara saṃvatsara sthiti prasaṅgāt kāla antara sthiti dharmatā upagame api nityatā eva upagatā bhavati iti nitya vikalpaḥ durnivāraḥ vināśa hetu sannidhau svayam nivartate iti ca upagamāt anitya vikalpaḥ naśvara ātma tā vikalpaḥ 
[141,ii^2]	tathā hi vināśa hetu abhimata sannidhau svayam vinaśyataḥ yaḥ asya svabhāvaḥ saḥ eva bhāvasya eka rūpa tvāt utpanna mātrasya iti tadā eva vināśa prasaṅgāt katham asya kālantara sthiti dharma tā sambhavati evam vikalpe kṛte pāścātya vikalpa upagame kāla antara sthitiḥ eva asya truṭyati iti nitya vikalpaḥ eva anena upagantavyaḥ tatra vināśa hetu sannidhau svayam nāśa upagame prāk nityaḥ bhūtvā paścāt anityaḥ vinaśvara svabhāvaḥ bhavati iti brūte evam ca brūvāṇaḥ bhāva dvayam ca āha vakṣyamāṇa apekṣaḥ cakāraḥ kīdṛśam bhāva dvayam nitya anityau svabhāvau bhedau yasya tathā yaḥ asau nityaḥ svabhāvaḥ prāktanaḥ tasya nitya abhimatasya svayam paścāt nāśam brūvāṇaḥ sarvadā pratikṣaṇam eva nāśam prāha anyathā pūrva uktena nyāyena paścāt api na āśā sambhavāt atha pratikṣaṇam asya nāśaḥ na bhavati tadā paścāt api tad ayogāt sarva daiva anāśam prāha iti kṛtvā pūrvasmin nitya abhimate svabhāve vināśa hetuḥ asamarthaḥ akiñcitkaraḥ eva 
[142,i]	nanu ca vināśa hetoḥ na eva sāmarthyam upagatam parena virodhi sannidhim apekṣya svayam nāśa upagamāt na atas eva tad nibandhanatva prasaṅgāt nāśasya anyathā hi akiñcitkaraḥ kim iti asau apekṣyate hetu bhāvasya apekṣā lakṣaṇa tvāt sva hetavaḥ eva atra aparādhyanti yat akiñcitkare api tatra apekṣāyām niyuñjate iti ced kaḥ punar ayamasthāna abhiniveśaḥ teṣām yat tatra tathā niyuñjate tasmāt upakāri apekṣāyām eva hetavaḥ niyuñjānāḥ śobhante anyathā te api kārya ātmānaḥ na eva tad niyogam ādriyeran katham ca akiñcitkaraḥ virodhī nāma na hi asya avirodhi tva abhimatāt viśeṣaḥ kaścid iti yat kiñcid etat 
[142,ii]	yat api uktam yathā anyeṣām kṣaṇika vādinām akiñcitkaram api mugdara ādikam apekṣya ghaṭa ādi pravāhaḥ nivartate tathā asmākam api kāla antara sthāyī bhāvaḥ iti tat api para samayān abhijñatayā ucyate yatas na asmākam pravāhaḥ nāma kṣaṇa vyatiriktaḥ asti yaḥ akiñcid kara mugdara ādi sannidhau nivarteta kṣaṇāḥ eva hi kevalam santi te ca sva nivṛttau na mugdara ādikam apekṣante svarasataḥ eva nirodhāt yā tu teṣām kapāla ādi vṛtti lakṣaṇā paryudāsa vṛttyā nivṛttiḥ yasyām satyām eka tva abhiniveśinaḥ lokasya sadṛśa apara bhāva rūpasya vibhrama nimittasya apagamāt nivṛttā ghaṭa ādayaḥ iti vyavahāraḥ tatra akiñcitkara tvam mugdara ādīnām na eva asti tad bhāvaḥ eva teṣām bhāvāt vegavat mugdara ādi sahakāriṇaḥ ghaṭa kṣaṇāt paraspara upasarpaṇa ādi āśrayāt pratyaya viśeṣāt sañjāta atiśayāt kapāla deḥ bhavana dharma tvāt tasya ca tad janna svabhāva tvāt iti 
[143,i_143,iii]	svabhāva dvaya upagama prasaṅgāt iti parijihīrṣayā paraḥ āha na prāk ityādi kutas etat eka svabhāva tvāt sarvadā eka svabhāvasya sarvadā nitya tā eva na paścāt anitya svabhāvatā sambhavaḥ iti siddhāntavādi āha sa tarhi bhāvaḥ sarvadā nitya svabhāvaḥ svabhāvena nāśam anāviśan apratipadyamānaḥ katham naṣṭaḥ nāma kutas tad svabhāva vināśayoḥ nitya svabhāva tāyāḥ vināśasya ca anitya rūpa tāyāḥ ca aparaspara rūpa tvāt paraspara parihāra rūpa tvāt upasaṃharan āha yatas evam sthiti dharmaṇām vināśaḥ na eva yujyate tasmāt sati asya vināśe yadi avaśyambhāvī kṛtaka rūpasya sataḥ vināśaḥ iṣyate paraiḥ tadā vināśa svabhāvena vinaśyati na avatiṣṭhate iti vināśaḥ kartari bahula vacanāt ghañ sa svabhāvaḥ yasya tena vināśa svabhāvena āsthiti dharmaṇā tena kṛtaka rūpeṇa satā vastunā sva hetubhyaḥ bhavitavyam anyathā vaśī ambhāvitayā upagatasya kṛtaka ātmanām satām vināśasya eva ayogāt bhavatu evam iti ced āha tathā api svayam vināśa svabhāva tve api na kevalam avinaśvara svabhāva tve svabhāvānyathā tva asambhavāt vyarthaḥ vināśa hetuḥ iti prathama vikalpa upanyāsaḥ eva uktam na punar ucyate yatas evam tena ityādi sugamam 
[143,iv_144,i]	tat evam vināśam pratyanapekṣām asāmarthya vaiyarthyābhyām tad hetu ayogena kṛtaka lakṣaṇasya sattvasya pūrva ācārya darśitām pratipādya yathā asau viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa tām anubhavati tada darśayan āha tasmāt vināśaḥ ityādi prayogaḥ tu evam ye yad bhāvam pratyanapekṣāḥ te tad bhāva niyatāḥ tat yathā antyā kāraṇa sāmagrī sva kārya utpādane anapekṣaḥ ca kṛtaka rūpaḥ san bhāvaḥ vināśe avaśyambhā vi vināśa tayā upagataḥ paraiḥ iti svabhāva hetu prasaṅga prayogaḥ viparyaye bādhakam pramāṇam pūrva ācārya pradarśitam tatas tad bhāva niyata tve na aśasya ākādācitka tvāt udaya anantaram nāśaḥ iti yaḥ san kṛtaka lakṣaṇaḥ bhāvaḥ sa vināśī vinaśvara svabhāvaḥ naśvara tāyāḥ sādhya dharmasya nivṛttau ca kṛtaka lakṣaṇa sattva nivṛttiḥ iti kṛtvā kṛtaka lakṣaṇasya sattvasya kṣaṇikatāyām anvaya vyatireka siddhiḥ sampadyate anapekṣayā anukrānta sattva kṣaṇika tvayoḥ tādātmya siddheḥ tad nibandhanayoḥ anvaya vyatirekayoḥ api niścayāt tat evam pūrva ācāryān prati akṛtakasya sataḥ abhāvāt sat akāraṇa vat nityam iti nitya lakṣaṇa virahāt eva na tat nitya tvam yat tu sat utpattimat tat uktena nyāyena avaśyaṃnāśitayā upagatam paraiḥ kāla antara sthāyi na bhavati iti prati pāditam 
[144,ii^1]	yadā tu yat sat tat kṣaṇikam eva iti sāmānyena ucyate kṛtaka akṛtaka lakṣaṇam sataḥ bhedam anapekṣya prauḍha vādi tayā kṛtakasya api ca avaśyambhāvī vināśaḥ iti para upagamaḥ na apekṣyate tadā vināśam pratyanapekṣa tvam eva sarvasya na sidhyati yeṣām hi vināśaḥ bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ ghaṭa ādīnām teṣām eva tat ha etva yogat tatra anapekṣā yujyate ye tu deśa ādi vyavahitāḥ parvata ādayaḥ vā vinaśām āviśantaḥ na dṛṣṭāḥ teṣām avaśyam vināśi tvā upagama nibandhana abhā ādantye api ayam vināśam pratyanapekṣaḥ eva vinaśyanna aviśeṣāt ādau api tad bhāva niyataḥ iti vaktum aśakyatvāt tad svabhāva sāpekṣa tvāt 
[144,ii^2]	vināśam pratyanapekṣa tva asiddherakṛtakānām ca ākāśa ādīnām vināśi svabhāva sāpekṣāṇām iti anapekṣayā sataḥ naśvara svabhāvatā siddheḥ anvaya vyatirekayoḥ tad nibandhanayoḥ ayogam utpaśyan artha kriyā virodha lakṣaṇam eva tadā bādhakam pramāṇam tādātmya prasādhakam abhidhānīyam iti manyamānaḥ pūrva pakṣam utthāpayan āha svabhāvataḥ naśvara tve api uktena nyāyena paridṛśyamāna vināśānām ghaṭa ādīnām kaścid deśa ādi vyavahitaḥ parvata ādiḥ vā anupalabdha vināśaḥ kṛtakaḥ api sat rūpa ākāśa ādiḥ vākṛtakaḥ sat na atad svabhāvaḥ api avināśi svabhāvaḥ api syāt 
[144,ii^3_145,i]	api śabdaḥ sambhāvanāyām tasya vināśi svabhāva saṃsādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt āśaṅkayate etat tatas ca vināśi svabhāva sāpekṣa tvāt tad anapekṣa tvam asiddham iti tad vaśāt sādhyasya kṣaṇika tvasya sattva svabhāva tva asiddheḥ tad nibandhanā na anvaya vyatireka siddhiḥ iti kim punar atra āśaṅkā nimittam yena kaścid atad svabhāvaḥ api āśaṅkayate iti āha na hi sarvaḥ sarvasya svabhāvaḥ iti vicitra svabhāvāḥ hi bhāvāḥ dṛśyante kecid sa pratighāḥ kecid apratighāḥ tathā nīla ānīla ādi svabhāvāḥ tathā kecid vināśinaḥ anye tu avināśi svabhāvāḥ śaṅkayantaḥ iti pūrva pakṣa āśaṅkā na kaścid atad svabhāvaḥ api syāt a iti āśaṅkanīyam tathā abhāve hi akṣaṇika tvam tasya syāt tasmin ca satya vastu tva prasaṅgāt kutas atad svabhāva tā śaṅkā katham punar akṣaṇika tve avastu tva prasaṅgaḥ yatas sattvasya kṣaṇika tva svabhāva tayā anvaya vyatireka siddhiḥ iti atas āha śaktiḥ hi ityādi 
[145,ii]	evam manyate iha tāvat idam eva vicāraṇīyam kiṃlakṣaṇam etat bhāvānām sattvam yuktam iti tatra na sattā yoga lakṣaṇam avyāpteḥ sāmānya diṣu abhāvāt vandhyā suta ādiṣu api bhāvāt ati vyāpteḥ vā vandhyā suta ādīnām asattvāt katham sattā yogaḥ iti ced na itaretara āśrayāt yatas teṣām asattvam sattā yoga virahāt eva tad virahaḥ ca asattvāt iti yadi ca satām eva sattā yogaḥ evam tarhi anyat sattva lakṣaṇam abhidhānīyam sattā yogasya ca vaiyarthyam tat eva vastunaḥ sattvāt sarva artha kriyā sāmarthya virahāt sattā yoga abhāvaḥ teṣām iti ced evam sati yat eva artha kriyasām arthya yuktam tasya eva sattā yogaḥ iti artha kriyā sāmarthyam eva bhāva lakṣaṇam āyātam iti apārthakaḥ sattā yogaḥ ittham ca evam anyathā sāmānya ādīnām katham svarūpam sattvam syāt artha kriyā sāmarthyam tu sarveṣām asti iti tat eva bhāva lakṣaṇam 
[146,i]	utpāda vyavyaghnauvya yuktam sat iti etat api ayuktam dhrauvyeṇa utpāda vyayayoḥ virodhāt ekasmin dharmiṇī ayogāt kathañcid utpāda vyayau kathañcid dhrauvyam iti ced yathā utpāda vyayau na tathā dhrauvyam yathā ca dhrauvyam na tathā utpāda vyayau iti na ekam vastu yathā ukta lakṣaṇam syāt tatas anyasya bhāva lakṣaṇasya ayogāt śakteḥ ca antaśas sva jñāna janane api upagamāt paraiḥ anyathā ṣaṭpadārtha ādi vyavasthāna ayogāt sā eva bhāva lakṣaṇam sarva śakti virahaḥ punar abhāva lakṣaṇam 
[146,ii_146,iii]	sarva grahaṇam ca sarvasya vastunaḥ vastu antara śakti viraha rūpa tvāt abhāvatā nirāsa artham yasya tu na kvacid śaktiḥ saḥ eva ekāntena abhāvaḥ ucyate śakti lakṣaṇam eva sattva makṣaṇike syāt tatas kṣaṇikā ātma tā sattvasya na sidhyati iti kutas anvaya vyatirekau iti ced āha na ca eva akṣaṇikasya kvacid kārye antaśas jñāna lakṣaṇe api śaktiḥ asti tat kutas tasya tad lakṣaṇam sattvam atīta ādeḥ iva bhaviṣyati yatas sattvasya kṣaṇikā ātma tā na sidhyet 
[146,iv]	nanu ca śakteḥ atīndriya tvāt kāraṇānām kārya rambha niyama abhāvāt ca katham tat virahaḥ akṣaṇikasya bhavet yatas asya sarva śakti viraha lakṣaṇena asattvena virodhinā nirākriyamāṇam sattvam kṣaṇikā ātma tām eva anubhavet yatas anvaya vyatirekau syātām iti atas āha krama yaugapadyābhyām ityādi na eva pratyakṣatas kārya virahāt vā sarva śakti virahaḥ akṣaṇika tve ucyate kintu tad vyāpaka virahāt tathā hi krama yaugapadyābhyām kārya kriyā vyāptā prakāra antara abhāvāt tatas kārya kriyā śakti vyāpakayoḥ tayoḥ akṣaṇika tve virodhāt nirvṛtteḥ tad vyāptāyāḥ kārya kriyā śakteḥ api nivṛttiḥ iti sarva śakti viraha lakṣaṇam asattva m akṣaṇika tve vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ ākarṣati viruddhayoḥ ekatra ayogāt tatas nivṛttam sattvam kṣaṇikeṣu eva avatiṣṭhamānam tad ātmatām anubhavati iti yat sat tat kṣaṇikam eva iti anvaya vyatireka rūpāyāḥ vyāpteḥ siddhiḥ niścayaḥ bhavati 
[147,i^1]	nanu ca prakāra antara abhāvāt kāryam aṅkura ādikam bīja ādinā krama yaugapadyābhyām eva kriyate iti ucyate saḥ eva tu prakāra antara virahaḥ kārya ātmanaḥ kutas siddhaḥ prakāra antarasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tve katham atyantā sambhavaḥ kevalam deśa ādi niṣedha mātram eva syāt anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvena asattā niścayaḥ viprakarṣiṇām iti kutas tad abhāva siddhiḥ tatas prakara antareṇa artha kriyā sambhavāt krama yaugapadya nivṛttau api na artha kriyā sāmarthya nivṛttiḥ iti kutas akṣaṇika tve sati sarva sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇam asat tvam yatas sattvasya kṣanika ātmatayā anvaya vyatirekau syātām na ubhayathā api adoṣāt tathā hi kramaḥ nāma paripāṭiḥ kārya antarāsāhityam kaivalyam aṅkura ādeḥ yaugapadyam api tasya aparaiḥ bbīja ādi kāryaiḥ sāhityam prakāra antaram ca aṅkura ādeḥ tad ubhaya avasthā virahe api anyathā bhavanam 
[147,i^2]	tasya ca aṅkura ādi svabhāvasya anya sahitasya kevalasya vā abhāve pratyakṣa bodha gamyamāne sati upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptaḥ eva svabhāvaḥ krama yaugapadya bhāva bahirbhūtaḥ na upalabhyate vastunaḥ upalabhyasya anya sāhitye kaivalye ca apanīte tad vivikta deśa ādi pratibhāsinaḥ pratyakṣasya udayāt svabhāva anupalambhataḥ eva abhāva niścaya ādi lakṣaṇa vyavahāra vṛtteḥ tasya ca aṅkura ādi bhāvasya avasthā dvaya bahis bhāva niṣedhe kayoḥ cit deśa kālayoḥ deśa antara ādau krameṇa aṅkura ādi bhāvavatīratarasmin vā bhāve api na kācid kṣatiḥ tatas pratyakṣatas eva prakāra antara abhāva siddheḥ katham krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā śaktiḥ avyāptā syāt śāstra kāraḥ tu yathā pratyakṣatas eva prakāra antara abhāva siddhiḥ tathā svayam etena kramākrama ādayaḥ api iti atidiśan vakṣyati 
[148,i^1]	anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tve api prakāra antarasya krama yaugapadyayoḥ anyaḥ anyavya vaccheda rūpa tvāt eva abhāva siddhi tathā hi anyonya vyavaccheda rūpāṇām eka niṣedhena apara vidhānāt tasya apratiṣedhe vidhi pratiṣedhayoḥ virodhāt ubhaya pratiṣedha ātmanaḥ prakāra antarasya kutas sambhavaḥ atra prayogaḥ yatra yat prakāra vyavacchedena yat itara prakāra vyavasthānam na tatra prakāra antara sambhavaḥ tat yathā nīla prakāra vyavacchedena ānīla prakāra antara vyavasthāyām pīte 
[148,i^2]	asti ca krama yauga padyayoḥ anyatara prakāra vyavacchedena tad itara prakāra vyavasthānam vyavacchidyamāna prakāra aviṣayīkṛte sarvatra kārya kāraṇa rūpe vastuni iti viruddha upalabdhiḥ vyavacchidyamāna prakāra itara vyavasthānam ca prakāra antara sambhavaḥ ca tatas bahis bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ iti anayoḥ tattva anyatva rūpayoḥ anyonya parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tvāt na ca atra api bādhaka antara āśaṅkayā anavasthānam āśaṅkanīyam pūrva prasiddhasya virodhasya smaraṇa mātra tvāt viruddha upalabdhiṣu bahis ddharmiṇi hetoḥ sadbhāvam upadarśya virodha sādhanam eva bādhakam tat ca iha asti tatas viruddhayoḥ ekatra asambhāvāt pratiyogi abhāva niścayaḥ śīta uṣṇa sparśayoḥ iva bhāva abhāvayoḥ iva vā iti kutas anavasthā 
[148,ii_149,i]	tatra na krameṇa akṣaṇikaḥ kāryāṇi karoti aviśeṣāt akāraka avasthāyām iva sahakārī apekṣā ca dvividhasya api sahakāri tvasya ayogāt anupanyasanīyā sarveṣām ca eka kriyā kāle eva kriyā prasakteḥ tad kārakasya svabhāvasya tadā eva bhāvāt na api yugapad pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt punar tad kriyā prasaṅgāt ca kṛta tvāt na iti ced na sāmarthya an apāyāt anyathā prāk api akāraka rūpa viśeṣāt akriyā syāt kṛtasya kartum aśakyatvāt iti ced śakta aśakta tayā tarhi ekatra eva kārye bheda prasaṅga śāli kodrava bīja ādeḥ iva nityaḥ ca yadā yugapad karoti tatas prāk api bhāvāt tadā eva tad kriyā prasaṅgaḥ punar tatas api pūrvataram iti evam na kadācid yugapad kriyā syāt pūrva uttara kālayoḥ ca ekadā yugapad kāriṇaḥ anyadā sarva artha kriyā sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇam asattvam syāt iti katham na kṣaṇika tā kriyā upagame vā krama pakṣaḥ eva tatra ca uktaḥ doṣaḥ evam akṣaṇika tve sati cakṣuḥ ādi āyatanānām asattva prasaṅgāt kṣaṇikatāyām eva sattvam iti yat sat tat kṣaṇikam eva iti sataḥ naśvara ātma tā siddheḥ anvaya vyatireka rūpa vyāpti siddhiḥ iti 
[150,i]	tat evam svabhāva hetau tādātmya siddhi nibandhanam anvaya vyatireka niścayam pratipādya kārya hetau kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhi nimitta tvāt tayoḥ tasyāḥ ca pratyakṣa anupalambha nibandhanāyāḥ prāk eva darśita tvāt tagdatam aparam api pareṣām bhrānti kāraṇa panetum tad viṣayam darśayan āha artha antare hetoḥ vyatirikte vastuni gamye kāryam hetuḥ anartha antare tu svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ iti uktam kasmāt punar artha antare kāryam eva hetuḥ iti āha avyabhicārāt iti kāryam eva hi artha antaram na vyabhicarati na anyat yathā uktam prāk tatas kāryam eva artha antare gamye hetuḥ ucyate saṃyoga vaśāgdamaka tve 
[150,ii^1]	na ca kenacid ityādinā yaḥ sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāva prasaṅgaḥ ācāryeṇa uktaḥ parasya tam iha api kārya hetau paraḥ kadācid prasañjayet iti āśaṅkamānaḥ āha kārya kāraṇa ityādi yadi hi kāryam hetuḥ ucyate tadā kārya kāraṇa bhāvena kāraṇena asya gamaka tvam tathā ca sati sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ prāpnoti agneḥ sāmānya dharma vat viśeṣa dharmāḥ api tārṇa pārṇa ādayaḥ gamyāḥ syuḥ dhūmasya api viśeṣa dharma vat dravya tva pārthiva tva ādayaḥ api sāmānya dharmā gamakāḥ bhaveyuḥ kutas sarvathā janya janaka bhāvāt janya janaka bhāvaḥ hi kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ucyate 
[150,ii^2]	sa ca na agni dhūmayoḥ aṃśena api tu sarveṇa prakāreṇa tathā hi yathā agniḥ agni tva dravya tva sattva ādibhiḥ sāmānya dharmaiḥ janakaḥ tathā tārṇa pārṇa tva ādibhiḥ viśeṣa dharmaiḥ api yathā ca dhūmaḥ dhūma tva pāṇḍu tva ādibhiḥ sva niyataiḥ viśeṣa dharmaiḥ janyaḥ tathā sāmānya dharmaiḥ api sattva dravya tva ādibhiḥ tatas ca yathā tayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tathā eva gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ prāpnoti tasya eva tad nibandhana tvāt iti pūrva pakṣa āśaṅkā atra āha na sarvathā janya janaka bhāvaḥ tatas ca kutas tathā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ syāt kasmāt 
[150,ii^3]	iti ced tad abhāve teṣām tārṇa pārṇa tva ādinām viśeṣa dharmāṇām abhāve bhavataḥ dhūma mātrasya tebhyaḥ eva viśeṣa dharmebhyaḥ bhavati iti evam ātmanaḥ tad utpatti niyamasya abhāvāt tathā tad abhāve agni abhāve bhavataḥ dravya tva ādeḥ sāmānya dharmasya agneḥ eva ayam bhavatī ti evaṃrūpasya tad utpatti niyamasya abhāvāt kutas sarvathā janya janaka bhāvaḥ yatas sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ syāt na hi asati tad utpatti niyame janya janaka bhāvaḥ vyavasthāpayitum yuktaḥ yatas evam tasmāt kāryam dhūma ādikam svabhāvaiḥ yāvadhi rdhūma tva ādibhiḥ sva gataiḥ ittham bhūta lakṣaṇā ca tṛtīyā avīnā bhāvi vinā na bhavati 
[150,ii^4]	kaiḥ vinā na bhavati kāraṇe yāvadbhiḥ svabhāvaiḥ iti atra api sambadhyate kāraṇa āśritaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ svabhāvaiḥ vinā te kārya gatāḥ svabhāvāḥ na bhavanti hetuḥ taiḥ teṣām iti gamyate kva avinābhāvi kāraṇe kāraṇa viṣaye aparaḥ arthaḥ kāraṇe ādhārasaptamī idānīm kāraṇa sthaiḥ svabhāvaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ agni tva dravya tva ādibhiḥ avinābhāvi teṣām kāraṇa gatānām sāmānya dharmāṇām hetuḥ kāryam gamakam kasmāt iti āha tad kāryatva niyamāt teṣām eva kāraṇa gatānām sāmānya dharmānām tat kāryam iti evaṃrūpasya niyamasya sadbhāvāt na hi tān sāmānya dharmān kadācid api kāryam vyabhicarati 
[151,i^1]	evam kāraṇa gatam aṃśam pāścātyena arthena nirūpya prāktanena arthena kārya gatam aṃśam nirūpayan āha taiḥ eva ca ityādi kāryam api taiḥ eva dharmaiḥ sva gataiḥ kāraṇa gatānām dharmāṇām gamakam yathā antarā sambhavinaḥ dhūma tva pāṇḍu pārṇa tva ādayaḥ viśeṣa rūpāḥ taiḥ kāraṇa gataiḥ sāmānya dharmaiḥ vinā na bhavanti atra api tad kāryatva niyamāt iti apekṣyate teṣām eva kārya gatānām viśeṣa dharmāṇām kāraṇa gata sāmānya dharma apekṣayā kāryatva niyamāt na hi te viśeṣa dharmāḥ kārya gatāḥ kāraṇa stha sāmānya dharmaiḥ vinā kadācid api bhavanti 
[151,i^2]	tatas teṣām eva kāryatva niyamaḥ na anyeṣām dravya tva ādīnām kāraṇa stha sāmānya dharmaiḥ vinā bhavatām tat evam kāraṇasya sāmānya dharmāḥ eva gamyāḥ na viśeṣa dharmāḥ kāryasya api viśeṣa dharmāḥ eva gamakāḥ na sāmānya dharmāḥ tad kāryatva niyamāt ye tu kāraṇasya viśeṣa dharmā yaiḥ tad kāryatva niyamaḥ kārya mātrasya na asti iti na te gamyāḥ ye ca kāryasya sāmānya dharmāḥ dravya tva ādayaḥ teṣām api tad kāryatva niyama abhāvāt eva gamaka tvam na asti iti kārya kāraṇa bhāvena gamaka tve kutas sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ pareṣām iva prasajyeta 
[152,i^1]	parasya aniṣṭha āpādanam āśaṅkayā āha aṃśena ityādi yadi hi kāraṇasya sāmānya dharmāḥ eva gamyāḥ kāryasya api viśeṣa dharmāḥ eva gamakāḥ tad kāryatva niyamādiṣyante hanta tarhi aśena janya janaka bhāvaḥ prāptaḥ kāraṇasya sāmānya dharmāḥ eva janakāḥ na viśeṣa dharmāḥ kāryasya api viśeṣa dharmāḥ eva janyā na sāmānya dharmāḥ iti syāt sarvathā ca janya janaka bhāvaḥ abhimataḥ iti ubhi upagama virodhaḥ etat pariharati na aṃśena janya janaka bhāva prasaṅgaḥ niraṃśa tvena vastunaḥ sarva ātmanā tad abhyupagamāt gamya gamaka bhāvasya api sarvathā abhimata tvāt 
[152,i^2]	tat āha tad janyaḥ ityādi yadi hi kāryasya taiḥ kāraṇa gataiḥ viśeṣa dharmaiḥ janyaḥ yaḥ viśeṣaḥ sa grahītum śakyate tadā tad janya viśeṣa grahaṇe abhimata tvāt kāraṇa gata viśeṣa dharmāṇām gamya tvasya tathā liṅga viśeṣaḥ dhūma tva ādi upādhiḥ viśeṣaṇam yeṣām dravya tva ādīnām sāmānyānām kārya gatānām teṣām ca abhimata tvāc damaka tvasya tathā hi aguru dhūma grahaṇe bhavati eva tad agneḥ anumānam dhūma tva viśeṣaṇena ca dravya tva ādinā agneḥ anumānam na hi sarvathā janya janaka bhāvaḥ asti iti eva tathā eva gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ bhavati tasya jñāna apekṣa tvāt 
[152,i^3]	tathā hi na sattā mātreṇa liṅgasya gamaka tvam tasya jñāpaka tvāt jñāpakaḥ hi sva niścaya apekṣaḥ jñāpyam artham jñāpayati na anyathā katham tarhi uktam tad abhāve bhavataḥ tad utpatti niyama abhāvāt iti sarvathā janya janaka bhāva abhyupagame tad abhāve bhāvasya eva abhāvāt iti atas āha aviśiṣṭa ityādi yadi hi tad janya viśeṣa grahaṇa rahitam aviśiṣṭam kārya mātram upādīyate liṅga viśeṣa upādhi rahitam vā dravya ādikam tadā aviśiṣṭa sāmānya vivakṣāyām kāraṇa gata viśeṣa abhāve api dhūma mātrasya bhāvāt tad aviśiṣṭasya ca dravya tva ādeḥ agni abhāve api bhāvāt vyabhicāraḥ iti sarvathā janya janaka bhāvaḥ na iṣyate tad abhāvāt gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ ca na tu viśeṣa vivakṣāyām tatra vyabhicāra abhāvāt tathā hi yadi nāma dhūma mātram tārṇa pārṇa ādi viśeṣa abhāve bhavati na tu tat janyaḥ viśeṣaḥ sa yadi grahītum śakyate tadā viśeṣasya gamya tvam asti eva niścitasya eva liṅga tvāt tathā yadi api dravya tva sattva mātram agni abhāve api bhavati na tu dhūma ātmakam iti tad viśiṣṭasya avyabhicārāt gamaka tvam api na vāryatas iti 
[153,i^1]	atra parasya vacana avakāśam āśaṅkayā āha kasyacid dhūma ādeḥ kadācid kasmiṃścid kāle kutaścid agni ādeḥ bhāve api sati sarvaḥ dhūma ādiḥ tādṛśaḥ yādṛśaḥ ekadā agni ādeḥ bhavana dṛṣṭa tad jātīyaḥ tathāvidha janmā yathāvidhāt saḥ ekaḥ bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ tādṛśāt eva janma yasya sa tathāvidha janma iti etat kutas pramāṇāt avasitam yena ucyate kārya hetau kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhi nibandhanau anvaya vyatirekau iti tathā hi yadi nāma pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām kasyacid dhūmasya agni ādi sāmagrī kārya tvam avagatam kim etāvatā anyasya api tādṛśasya tādṛśa kārya tā sidhyati tatra tad nibandhanayoḥ pratyakṣānupalambhayoḥ avyāpārāt yatra eva hi tayoḥ vyāparaḥ tasya eva tad kāryatā bhavatu tad anyasya tu kim āyātam yena tathavidhāt asya janma syāt 
[153,i^2]	evam hi kasyāścid dhūma vyakteḥ agni ādi janya tā dṛṣṭā iti kin na ghaṭa ādeḥ api sā abhyupagamyate anya tvena viśeṣa abhāvāt kaḥ evam sati doṣaḥ iti ced tathā ca pramāṇa abhāvena tathāvidha janma tvā niścayāt atādṛśāt api janma āśaṅkāyām tādṛśasya dhūma ādeḥ agni ādinā anvaya vyatirekau na niścitau iti kutas kārya hetoḥ gamaka tvam na hi yaḥ asau ekaḥ deśa kāla avasthā niyataḥ agni viśeṣa hetukaḥ dhūmaḥ adhigataḥ pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām tasya eva anvaya vyatirekau pratipattavyau tasya deśa antara ādau asambhavāt kim tarhi tādṛśasya sāmānya ātmanaḥ eva liṅga tvāt tasya ca ātathāvidhāt api janmāśaṅkāyām kutas tathāvidhena anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vā tat uktam avasthā deśa kālānām bhedāt bhinnāsu śaktiṣu bhāvānām anumānena pratītirati durllabhā iti 
[154,i^1]	siddhāntavādi āha na atadbhāvinaḥ ityādi evam manyate iha ekadā dhūma ādeḥ agni ādi sāmagrī janyatayā pratyākṣa an upalambhābhyām niścita rūpa tve api tādṛśasya atādṛśāt api bhāvaḥ samāśaṅkyate yathā paridṛṣṭāt anya tvena tatra yaḥ asau agni ādi sāmagrī janyaḥ dhūma viśeṣaḥ ekadā niścitaḥ tad apekṣayā yathā anyaḥ dhūma viśeṣaḥ tādṛśaḥ yaḥ anyādṛśāt api bhāvānām vicitra śakti tayā bhavet iti śaṅkayate tathā saḥ api ekadā agni ādi sāmagrī janyatayā niścitaḥ tad anya apekṣayā tādṛśaḥ eva tatra yadi tad anyasya tādṛśasya ātādṛśāt janma syāt tadā tādṛśasya svabhāvasya na agni ādi sāmagrī janya svabhāva tā iti paridṛṣṭasya api dhūmasya na agni ādi sāmagrī kāraṇam iti āyātam tādṛśasya svabhāvasya agni ādi sāmagrī vilakṣaṇa kāraṇa janya svabhāva tvāt tatas ca agni ādi sāmagryāḥ akāraṇa tvāt yaḥ mayā ekadā tatas bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ dhūmaḥ saḥ api na bhavet 
[154,i^2]	na hi yat yasya kāraṇam na bhavati tat tatas sakṛt api jāyate tasya ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt iti atadbhāvinaḥ iti tad śabdena vivakṣitam agni ādi kāraṇam parigṛhyate na tat atat tad vilakṣaṇam atādṛśam śakra murddha ādikam atasmāt bhavitum śīlam yasya tasya atad bhāvinaḥ tādṛśasya tad lakṣaṇasya dhūma vastunaḥ sakṛt api ekadā api tatas agni ādeḥ abhāvāt bhāva virodhāt bhavati ca tādṛśaḥ agni ādi sāmagrītaḥ tatas tādṛśasya svabhāvasya tādṛśam eva kāraṇam iti avagamyate sakṛt pravṛttābhyām eva pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām iti kutas vyabhicāra āśaṅkā tena yādṛśaḥ dhūmaḥ agni ādi sāmagryā bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ sakṛt tādṛśasya tasya tad janya svabhāva tayā tādṛśāt eva bhāvāt yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agni ādi sāmagrī iti anvaya vyatireka niścayaḥ 
[155,i]	athavā anyathā vyākhyāyate iha pratyakṣa anupalambha nibandhanā kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ prāk uktā tad nibandhanau anvaya vyatirekau pratipādayitum tat ca ayuktam tathā hi kasyacid dhūmasya agni ādi sāmagrī anantara bhāvinaḥ ādyasya kadācid prathama utpāda kāle kutaścid agni ādi sāmagryāḥ bhāve api utpāde api sarvaḥ tādṛśaḥ yādṛśaḥ prathama kṣaṇa bhāvī dhūma u dvitīya ādi kṣaṇeṣu api tādṛśaḥ pratyakṣatas eva tasya pūrvakṣaṇa avilakṣaṇa tayā pratīteḥ tathāvidha janmā iti yathāvidhāt agni indhana sāmagrī lakṣaṇāt kāraṇāt ādyaḥ dhūma kṣaṇaḥ utpannaḥ tathāvidhāt janma yasya sa tathāvidha janma iti etat kutas na eva tasya dhūma ādeḥ abhāvāt evam ca yadi atas dṛṣṭam tasya anyatas api bhāvasya darśanāt sarvatra anāśvāsaḥ iti manyamānaḥ āha tathā ca anagnitaḥ dhūmāt api dhūmasya bhāve śakra mūrddha ādeḥ api tasya bhāva avirodhāt agninā dhūmasya nanu aya vyatirekau iti ced manyase iti pūrva pakṣa āśaṅkā 
[155,ii_155,iii^1]	tat uktam kṣaṇika tve katham bhāvāḥ kvacid āyatta vṛttayaḥ prasiddha kāraṇa abhāve yeṣām bhāvaḥ tatas anyatas atas ca anagnitaḥ māt yathā dhūmasya sambhavaḥ śakra mūrdhnaḥ tathā tasya kena vāryeta saṃbhavaḥ iti siddhāntavādi āha na agni indhana sāmagrī janyaḥ yādṛśaḥ dhūmaḥ tādṛśaḥ eva dhūmāt api bhavati kāraṇa bhedena kutaścid sāmyāt sarūpa tayā avasīyamānasya api anyādṛśa tvāt tādṛśaḥ hi agni indhana sāmagrī kṣaṇa antara janyaḥ ādyaḥ eva aparaḥ kṣaṇaḥ tathā tad anya ādyaḥ eva apara agni in dhana sāmagrī janyaḥ iti tādṛśasya dhūmasya dhūmāt asambhavāt na kvacid anāśvāsaḥ kāryaḥ tathā yādṛśaḥ dvitīya kṣaṇa bhāvī prathama dhūma kṣaṇa janitaḥ dhūma kṣaṇaḥ tādṛśaḥ apara prathama dhūma kṣaṇa janitaḥ eva dvitīyaḥ dhūma kṣaṇaḥ na tṛtīya ādiḥ evam tṛtīya kṣaṇa ādiṣu api aṅkura ādiṣu ca sarvatra vācyam 
[155,iii^2]	kutas punar ayam vibhāgaḥ iti ced āha atadbhāvinaḥ atasmāt anagni indhana ādi rūpāt dhūmāt bhavana śīlasya prathama kṣaṇa avilakṣaṇasya dhūmasya sakṛt api ekadā api tatas agni ādi sāmagryāḥ abhāvāda bhāva ayogāt yathā hi prathama kṣaṇa apekṣayā dvitīyaḥ tādṛśaḥ tathā tad apekṣayā prathamaḥ api iti tādṛśatva aviśeṣāt tādṛśasya anagnitaḥ bhāve tādṛśaḥ na agni janya svabhāvaḥ iti sakṛt api tatas na bhavet bhavan vā tad janya svabhāva tām ātmānaḥ tādṛśaḥ khyāpayati iti kutas anyādṛśāt bhavet tasmāt anyādṛśāt bhavat anyādṛśaḥ eva tatas na vyabhicāraḥ 
[156,i]	nanu sarveṣām dhūma kṣāṇānām kaṇṭha kṣaṇana akṣi sruti kālīkaraṇa ādikāyām artha kriyāyām upayogāt katham tādṛśa svabhāva tā na syāt na tasyāḥ api artha kriyāyāḥ kṣaṇa bheda upadhīyamāna rūpāyāḥ tādṛśa tva abhāvāt tatra api tulya doṣa tvāt katham tarhi loke sarvatra dhūma vyavahāraḥ iti ced sadṛśa apara bhāva nibandhana eka tva adhyavasāya vaśāt kṣaṇikarvyavahāra ayogāt ca sādṛśye sati katham na tādṛśatā iti ced tādṛśāt anya tvāt sadṛśasya tathā hi go sadṛśaḥ bhavati gavayaḥ na tu tādṛśaḥ goḥ eva aparasya tādṛśa tvāt parama arthena ātādṛśe api tādṛśa abhimānaḥ manda matīnām bhavan katham nivārtyet tathā hi tattva adhyavasāyaḥ api tāvat atasmin arvāk dṛśām vinivārayitum na pāryate kim aṅga punar tādṛśa tva adhyavasāyaḥ yathā uktam samāna varṇa saṃsthāne santāne atyatra jāyate atasmin tad matiḥ puṃsām kim uta ekatra saṃtatau iti 
[157,i^1]	tattva cintakāḥ tu tādṛśātādṛśa kāraṇa bhedāt tādṛśā tādṛśatām bhāvānām anumanyante na tādṛśatām tat yat yatādṛśāt api tadṛśaḥ bhavet tadā tasya tat janyaḥ svabhāvaḥ iti atad bhāvinaḥ sakṛt api tatas bhāvaḥ na syāt amum eva artham samartha yamanaḥ āha paraspara apekṣayā ityādi kāraṇa apekṣayā hi janya svabhāvam kāryam kārya apekṣayā ca janaka svabhāvam kāraṇam yatas hi kāraṇāt yat bhavat dṛṣṭam tasya tad janya svabhāvaḥ itarasya ca tad janakaḥ iti pratīyate anyathā tasya tatas bhāva ayogāt itarasya ca tad janana ayogāt yadi nāma evam tatas prakṛte kim siddham 
[157,i^2]	iti atas āha tatra etasmin nyāye sati yadi dhūmaḥ yādṛśaḥ ādyaḥ agni ādi sāmagrī janitaḥ tādṛśaḥ dvitīya ādi kṣaṇa bhāvī agni ādi sāmagryāḥ agni indhana ādi kāraṇa kalāpāt tad janaka svabhāva tayā nirddhāritā danī atas agni indhana ādi sāmagrī janitādādyāt dhūma kṣaṇāt bhavet tadā tasya tādṛśasya dhūma svabhāvasya tad janyaḥ agni ādi sāmagrī janyaḥ svabhāvaḥ na bhavati kintu dhūma janyaḥ eva iti kṛtvā sakṛt api tatas agni ādi sāmagrītaḥ na bhaveta tādṛśasya hi svabhāvasya anyatas bhāve tad janya svabhāva tā na agni ādi janya svabhāva tā iti kutas sakṛt api tatas bhāvaḥ yujyeta atra dṛṣṭāntaḥ artha antara vat iti yathā hi artha antaram atad janya abhimatam anyatas bhavat na tad janya svabhāvam na agni ādi sāmagrī janya svabhāvam iti sakṛt api tatas na bhavati tadvat tādṛśaḥ dhūmaḥ api iti tatas bhavat anyādṛśaḥ eva asau iti gamyate 
[157,ii]	syāt matam agni ādi sāmagryāsa avatat janya svabhāvaḥ api tādṛśaḥ balāt janyate kaḥ tasya tapasvinaḥ aparādhaḥ iti atas āha na api na kevalam sva yam atad janya svabhāva tayā tatas na bhavet kintu agni ādi sāmagrī api tam tādṛśam dhūmam yādṛśaḥ dvitīya ādi kṣaṇa bhāvī na janayet kutas atajjanana svabhāva tvāt tādṛśasya hi anyatas bhāve saḥ eva tad janana svabhāvaḥ na agni ādi sāmagri iti tad janana svabhāva vikalā katham tam janayet atra api udāharaṇam sāmagryantara vat iti yathā sāmagrī antaram atad janana svabhāva abhimatam na janayati tadvat agni ādi sāmagrī api tathā hi sā ātmīyam svabhāvam anusṛtya eva pravartate tatas kutas asau sāmagrī balāt jāyeta 
[158,i^1]	syāt matam agni ādi sāmagrī janya svabhāvaḥ api tādṛśaḥ dhūmaḥ dhūma janya svabhāvaḥ api yathā saḥ eva dhūmaḥ indhana janya svabhāvaḥ agni janya svabhāvaḥ ca ubhayatas bhavati tathā tādṛśaḥ api dhūmaḥ ubhaya sāmagrī janya svabhāvatayā ubhayatas bhaviṣyati iti atas āha na ca na eva dhūmasya tādṛśasya tat atat janyaḥ agni ādi sāmagrī janyaḥ dhūma janyaḥ ca svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ yuktyā saṅgataḥ kutas eka svabhāva tvāt tādṛśasya dhūma rūpasya bheda abhāvāt na hi tasya kāla bhede api tādṛś rūpa tā bhidyate bhede hi anyādṛśasya anyādṛśāt bhāve vivāda ayogāt tasya yadi tādṛśā tādṛśa kāraṇa janya tā syāt tatas tādṛśā tādṛśa svabhāva tā eva syāt tat eva darśayan āha dhūmādhūma ityādi 
[158,i^2]	dhūma śabdena yādṛśaḥ agni ādi sāmagrī janyaḥ tādṛśaḥ svabhāvaḥ abhipretaḥ adhūma śabdena anya adṛśa kāraṇa janyaḥ dhūma janitaḥ anyādṛśaḥ tayoḥ ca tādṛśa ātādṛśa kāraṇa janya tayā eva tādṛśa ātādṛśa svabhāva tā avagantavyā vakṣyamāṇanītyā tena agni dhūma lakṣaṇāt dhūmādhūma janana svabhāvāt tādṛśā tādṛśa janana svabhāvāt tādṛśā tādṛśa tayā asya bhavataḥ dhūmādhūma svabhāvaḥ tādṛśā tādṛśa svabhāvaḥ syāt kutas tādṛśaḥ eva kutas etat iti āha kārya svabhāvānām ityādi kāryāṇām hi ye svabhāvāḥ paraspara asaṃbhavinaḥ te paraspara vilakṣaṇa kāraṇa sāmagrī svabhāva kṛtā na svābhāvikāḥ ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt tatas tādṛśātādṛśāt bhavataḥ dhūmasya tādṛśa ātādṛśa svabhāva tā eva syāt 
[159,i]	syāt matam na eva tādṛśa ātādṛśa svabhāvatāyām tādṛśā tādṛśa kāraṇa apekṣā kāryāṇām utpatti mātraḥ eva kāraṇa apekṣaṇāt ityataḥ āha akāraṇa apekṣaṇe ca tādṛśātādṛśa rūpa tāyām tādṛśā tādṛśa kāraṇa anapekṣaṇe ca tādṛśātādṛśa tāyāḥ ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt na hi tādṛśā tādṛśa svabhāvayoḥ abhūtvā bhāva vyatirekeṇa anyā kācid utpattiḥ yatra tādṛśa ātādṛśa svabhāva kāraṇa nirapekṣāṇām api tad apekṣā syāt tasmāt utpatti śabdena tādṛśa ātādṛśa svabhāva tā eva ucyate iti tatra kāraṇa apekṣā upagame katham tādṛśā tādṛśa tāyām kāraṇa apekṣā na syāt tasmāt sāmagrīṇām tādṛśā tādṛśa tvāt eva kāryāṇām tādṛśa ātādṛśa svabhāva vibhāgaḥ iti kutas anyādṛśāt tādṛśa sambhavaḥ iti 
[159,ii^1]	yat tu uktam yathā ekaḥ dhūmaḥ agni indhanābhyām vilakṣaṇābhyām janyate tathā eka lakṣaṇam api kāryam vilakṣaṇāt api sāmagrī antarāt bhaviṣyati iti tat ayuktam yatas na asmābhiḥ vilakṣaṇānām janaka tvam vāryate janayanti eva paraspavilakṣaṇāḥ api sva hetu pariṇāma upanidhi dharmāṇaḥ tad avasthā niyatāḥ tat ekam kāryam tasya tu teṣām ca paraspara apekṣayā janya janaka svabhāvatā niyamāt tādṛśasya tādṛśāt eva janma ucyate na anyādṛśāt tasya atad janana svabhāva tvāt tad abhāve api anyatas bhavataḥ tad utpatti niyama abhāvāt aniyame ca kārya kāraṇa bhāva ayogāt yadi tu agniḥ iva indhana upādāna upakṛtaḥ tad upādāna upakṛtam ca indhanam iva tad avasthā niyatamatādṛśam api dhūma ādikam tādṛśam dhūmam janayet pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām ca tathā avagamyeta tadā agni ādi vat saḥ api tad janana svabhāvatā niyamāt tādṛśa janakaḥ kena na anumanyeta 
[159,ii^2]	tad abhāve api tu tādṛśasya bhāve tayoḥ janya janaka svabhāva tā niyama abhāvāt kutas kārya kāraṇa tā iti ahetu tā eva tādṛśasya anyādṛśāt bhavataḥ syāt yatas evam tasmāt saḥ agni indhana ādi sāmagrī viśeṣaḥ mantavyaḥ yaḥ ādya dhūma jananaḥ na anyaḥ sa dhūmaḥ ādyaḥ yaḥ gni ādi sāmagrī viśeṣeṇa janitaḥ na anyaḥ aḥ iti kṛtvā kārya kāraṇayoḥ evam yathā uktena nyāyena janya janaka rūpasya svabhāvasya niyamāt yādṛśam yasya kāraṇam ekadā pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām eva avadhāritam tat vijātīyāt tatas anyādṛśāt kāraṇāt utpattiḥ tādṛśasya kāryasya na bhavati anyādṛśasya eva na vāryatas iti 
[160,i]	tat evam tādṛśātādṛśa kāraṇa kṛtaka tvam tādṛśā tādṛśa kārya svabhāvasya pratipādya upasaṃharan āha tat tasmāt yādṛśam kāryam yādṛśāt kāraṇāt dṛṣṭam pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām niścitam ekadā tat tnna vyabhicarati tādṛśam anyādṛśāt na bhavati yana evam tena kāraṇena siddhe kārya kāraṇa bhāve tādṛśasya kāryasya tādṛśam eva kāraṇam iti niścaye sati yathā uditena nyāyena kāryasya kāraṇena vyāptiḥ anvaya vyatireka rūpā siddhā bhavati 
[160,ii^1]	na vijātīyāt utpattiḥ iti dṛṣṭa kāraṇa vijātīyāt kāraṇāt anyādṛśān na utpattiḥ iti asamumartham apratipadyamānaḥ kāryasya vijātīyāt kāraṇāt na utpattiḥ iti ayam atra arthaḥ abhimataḥ iti manvānaḥ paraḥ codayan āha nanu svatas vijātīyāt api kāraṇāt kiñcid kāryam bhavat dṛṣṭam tat katham na vijātīyāt utpattiḥ iti asya na dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ syāt katham yathā iti āha tat yathā gomaya ādeḥ ādi grahaṇāt śṛṅga candra kānta ādeḥ śālūka ādi ādi grahaṇāt śara udaka ādi tathā hi gomayāt śālūkasya bhāvaḥ śṛṅgāt śarasya candrakāntāt apāma na ca gomaya ādikam śālūka ādeḥ na vijātīyam tat kim ucyate na vijātīyāt utpattiḥ iti siddhānta vādī parasya bhrāṃtatām darśayan āha na vijātīyāt utpattiḥ iti 
[160,ii^2]	yatas hi kāraṇāt yat bhavat dṛṣṭam tat tatas anyādṛśāt na bhavati iti ayam atra arthaḥ vivakṣitaḥ na tu kārya vijātīyāt iti na ca tasya vyabhicāraḥ tat āha tathāvidham eva hi gomaya ādi rūpam tādṛśam śālaka ādī nāmā dinimittam śālūka ādi prabandhasya yaḥ ādiḥ prathamaḥ ārambha kṣaṇaḥ tasya kāraṇam iti kṛtvā śālūka ādi prabandhasya ādeḥ na kāraṇa abhedaḥ anyādṛśāt utpattiḥ sarvasya tad ādeḥ gomaya ādi nimitta tvāt yadā tu prabandhena pūrva kṣaṇa nimittānām uttara uttarakṣaṇānām santānena utpatti lakṣaṇā vṛttiḥ bhavati śarasya tadā śarāt bhāvaḥ tat evam yasya prabandha ādeḥ śṛṅga ādibhyaḥ bhāvaḥ na tādṛśasya śara ādeḥ yasya ca śāra ādeḥ tuduttara uttarasya bhāvaḥ na tādṛśasya śṛṅga ādeḥ iti na dṛṣṭa kāraṇa vijātīyāt kāraṇāt tādṛśasya sambhavaḥ iti kārya hetoḥ anvaya vyatireka niścayaḥ 
[161,i^1]	yadā api śālūka ādayaḥ pūrva pūrva sva jāti nibandhanāḥ anādi santāna pravṛttāḥ iṣyante tadā api gomaya ādibhyaḥ keṣāñcit bhāve api tādṛśa tva abhāvāt na vyabhicāraḥ iti darśayan āha asti ca ityādi yasya śālūka santānasya gomaya ādi kāraṇam yasya ca sarvadā sva jāti nimitta tvam tayoḥ gomayetara janmanoḥ śālūkayoḥ asti eva svabhāva bhedaḥ paraspara m anyādṛśa tvam rūpasya abhede api sati tulya ākāra tve sati katham anyādṛśa tvam iti ced āha nahi ityādi yasmāt na ākāra tulya tā eva bhāvānām tattve tādṛśa tve nimittam yatas gomayetarajat manoḥ śālūkayoḥ ākāra sāmyāt tādṛśa tvam eva syāt na jāti bhedaḥ kutas etat iti āha abhinna ākārāṇām api ityādi 
[161,i^2]	yeṣām api hi samāna ākāra tā keṣāñcid bhāvānām teṣām api yatas ākārāt anyatas viśeṣāt jāti bhedaḥ dṛśyate tatas na ākāra sāmyam eva jāti ekatve nibandhanam tathā hi ākāra sāmye api kvacid puṣpāt bhedaḥ dṛśyate nīla itara kusumayoḥ iva sūryayoḥ kvacid phalāt bandhyā itarayoḥ iva karkoṭakyoḥ kvacid rasāt vanya itarayoḥ iva trapuṣayoḥ kvacid gandhāt vṛkṣa itara prabhavayoḥ iva campakayoḥ kvacid prabhāvāt sparśa upayogaḥ traṃsinyoḥ iva haritakyoḥ iti tasmāt ākāra sāmya nibandhanam yadi api tat eva idam iti pratyabhijñānam sajātīyatām gomayetarajat manoḥ śālakayaḥ rūpa kalpayati tathā api vilakṣaṇa sāmagrī janya tayā tayoḥ jāti bhedaḥ eva avagantavyaḥ na eka jāti tā tatas eva pratyabhijñānasya bhrānta tayā tad kalpitasya tādṛśa tvasya alīka tvāt 
[162,i]	yadi punar gomaya itara ādi janmanaḥ śālū kāka ādeḥ agni dhūma ādi janmanaḥ vā dhūma ādeḥ pratyabhijñā vaśāt vilakṣaṇa sāmagrī nibandhana tve api samāna svabhāva tā eva syāt kaḥ doṣaḥ syāt iti atas āha anyathā hi ityādi yadi hi yā sva jāti lakṣaṇa pratyaya antara sahitā sāmagrī yā ca sva jāti nirapekṣā gomaya ādi rūpā śālūka ādeḥ dhūmasya vā yā agnī na dhana ādi lakṣaṇā yā ca śakra mūrdu ādi svabhāvā dhūma ādi ātmikā tasyāḥ vilakṣaṇāyāḥ api sāmagryāḥ avilakṣaṇam tādṛśam eva kāryam dhūmaśālūka ādikam utpadyeta tadā na kāraṇasya sāmagrī rūpasya bheda abhedābhyām vailakṣaṇya availakṣaṇyābhyām kāryasya bheda abhedau vailakṣaṇyā vailakṣaṇye tad jātīya vijātīya ātmake syātām iti kṛtvā viśvasya sakalasya padārtha rāśeḥ ahetukau bheda abhedau sajātīya vijātīya tve syātām tasmāt yatra vilakṣaṇā sāmagrī tatra kutaścid sāmyāt sarūpa tve api vijātīyatā eva kāryasya iti 
[162,ii]	nanu dhūma indhana ādi sāmagrī bhede api dhūmasya na jāti bhedam āmananti vidvāṃsaḥ atad rūpa parāvṛtteḥ ubhayatra samāna tvāt na eṣa doṣaḥ kṣaṇa bheda āśraya sūkṣma avāntara jāti bhede api sthūla santāna āśraya vijātīya vyāvṛtteḥ samāna tvāt śābaleyādyava antara jāti bhedepya go vyāvṛtti nibandhana go jāti vat gavām sarva dhūmānām eka santāna vyavasthā api upādāna kāraṇa kṣaṇa bhede api eka ākāra pratyaya nibandhana tayā samāna tvāt ādyasya indhana prabhavasya katham iti ced na indhana jāti anuvidhānāt sarva dhūmānām tathā hi aguru karpūra candana ādi jāti bhedam anukurvanti eva tad dhūmāḥ kāsa śvāsa ādi hara dravya nirmita varti bhedam ca tad dhūmāḥ tad rasa vīrya vipāka anuvidhānāt na ca ākāra anyatayā vijātīya tvam yatas na ākāra abheda bheda nibandhena sajātīya vijātīya tve na hi śāli aṅkura ādayaḥ tabdīja ādi a ākāram anukurvate na ca tad jātīya tām aśāli ādi vyāvṛtti nibandhanām na anubhavanti tasmāt indhanam eva tayā upādāna kāraṇam agni ādi sahakāri pratyaya āhita viśeṣam tathāvidham dhūma kāryam aṅgāra ādi bhinna ākṛti janayati iti alam ati prasaṅgena 
[163,i^1]	nanu ca yadi nāma sāmagrī bhede api kāryasya bhedaḥ na jātaḥ tadā kāraṇa bhede sati api tasya abhāvāt tasya ahetuka tāstu abhedasya tu kim āyātam yena ubhayoḥ ahetuka tvam ucyate iti atas āha tathā hi ityādi yadā hi sāmagrī bhede sati api kāryasya bhedaḥ na jātaḥ iti tasya ahetuka tvam na hi hetau sati abhavataḥ kathañcid api hetumat ta upapadyate tadā yaḥ api asau abhedaḥ kāryasya saḥ api sāmagryoḥ bhinna tvāt asati abhede jātaḥ iti kutas tasya api hetumat tā yathā hi hetau sati abhavataḥ na hetumat tā tathā hetau asati api bhavataḥ hetumat tā kutas syāt hetu bhedasya eva abheda nibandhana tvāt naḥ iti ced na tarhi ayam bhedaḥ kvacid padam ābadhnīyāt śālī kodrava ādeḥ api hetu bhedasya abheda hetu tvāt nimittam antareṇa kalpanāyām viśeṣa abhāvāt 
[163,i^2]	pratibhāsā bhedasya ca kutaścid bhrānti nimittāt paramārthataḥ bhede api upalakṣaṇāt syāt etat yaḥ hi atādṛśāt api tādṛśa udbhavam icchati tasya bheda abhedayoḥ ahetuka tvam iṣṭam eva bhāvāḥ eva kevalam hetumantaḥ iti atas āha tad vyatiriktaḥ ca ityādi na hi bheda abheda vyatiriktaḥ kaścid bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ asti yaḥ tayoḥ ahetuka tve api hetumān syāt tasya tābhyām anya tve asya imau bheda abhedau iti sambandha abhāva prasaṅgāt tad anya sambandha kalpanāyām anavasthā doṣāt ananya tve api bheda abhedayoḥ bhāva svabhāvasya ca sva ātmani eva avasthānāt anupakārāt ca kutas sambandhi tā upakāra kalpanāyām ca yadi bhāva svabhāvaḥ sva hetubhyaḥ eva na kutaścid bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ vā samutpannaḥ iti iṣyate tadā tad bhāve api svabhāvānyathātva abhāvāt kutas bhinna abhinna tā bhāva svabhāvasya syāt 
[163,i^3]	 atha vyatirikta bheda abheda vaśāt bheda abhedau svabhāvaḥ pratipadyeta tau api yadi bhinnau tadā bhāva svabhāvaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva iti na tasya kutaścid svarūpataḥ bhedaḥ abhedaḥ vā syāt punar tad vaśāt bheda abheda kalpanāyām bhāva svabhāvasya tad avastham tādavasthyam anavasthā ca bheda abhedayoḥ atha abhinnau tadā bhāva svabhāvaḥ eva bheda abhedābhyām kriyate iti syāt tasya rūpa antareṇa karaṇa asambhavāt tasya ca hetu antarāt paścāt bhavataḥ tatas anyatva āpatteḥ na ca bhāva svabhāvaḥ kriyate tasya sva hetoḥ eva nirvṛtteḥ sva hetubhyaḥ eva bhāva svabhāvasya kutaścid bhinna abhinna ātmanaḥ utpatti kalpanāyām vā bheda abhedayoḥ vyatirekavatoḥ vaiyarthyam bheda abheda buddheḥ api tatas eva siddheḥ 
[163,i^4]	tasmāt vaiśeṣika ādi kalpitayoḥ bheda abhedayoḥ viśeṣa sāmānya ātmanoḥ ayogāt bhāva svabhāvaḥ eva bheda abheda śabda vācyaḥ tayoḥ ahetuka tve bhāva svabhāvasya eva ahetuka tvam āpatitam tatas bhāvānām ahetuka tvāt nityam sattvam asat tvam vā syāt ahetuka tve hi bhāvānām yadi kadācid sattvam sarvadā eva syāt atha kadācid asattvam tat api sarvadā syāt kādācid ka tvam tu sattvasya ayuktam kim kāraṇam apekṣyasya ahetuka tve sati kasyacid abhāvāt yasmai dapekṣayā hi tasya āpeṣaṇīyasya hetoḥ bhāve bhavantaḥ abhāve ca na bhavantaḥ kādācid kāḥ kadācid bhavāḥ yujyante na anyathā iti tasmāt na vilakṣaṇāt kāraṇāt avilakṣaṇasya kāryasya utpattiḥ abhyupagantavyā yathā uktena nyāyena ahetuka tva ādi prasaṅgāt 
[164,i^1]	punar api vilakṣaṇāyāḥ sāmagryāḥ avilakṣaṇasya kāryasya utpattau doṣa antaram āha vyavasthāvān ca pratiniyataḥ sādhyeṣu ghaṭa paṭa ādiṣu sādhanānām mṛd tantu ādīnām loke yaḥ niyogaḥ ghaṭa arthī mṛd piṇḍam eva tatra niyuṅkte na tantūn paṭa arthī ca tantūn eva na mṛd piṇḍam iti ādikaḥ sa na syāt kasmāt iti āha kāraṇānām sāmagrīṇām yāḥ śaktayaḥ ātma atiśaya lakṣaṇāḥ tāsām pratīni yame kācid eva sāmagrī kvacid eva kārye upayujyate na anyā anyatra iti evaṃrūpe hi yasmāt kiñcid eva mṛdā ādikam kasyacid eva ghaṭa ādeḥ sādhanāya upādīyate na aparam tat vilakṣaṇam tantu ādikam kasmāt evam iti ced tasya eva mṛd ādeḥ tatra ghaṭa ādau śakte ryogya tvāt anyasya tantu ādeḥ tatra aśakteḥ kasmāt tasya eva tatra śaktiḥ na anyasya iti atas āha tayoḥ mṛd ādeḥ tantu ādeḥ ca tad jana svabhāva tvena ghaṭa ādi janana svabhāva tvena itara svabhāva tvena ca ghaṭa ādyajanana svabhāvena ca bhedāt anya tva bhāvāt 
[164,i^2]	na hi mṛd tantu ādi rūpa tātaḥ anyat eva tat janana itara svabhāva tvam nāma yadā tu sāmagrīṇām paraspara vilakṣaṇānām api śakti pratiniyamaḥ na iṣyate vilakṣaṇāt api avilakṣaṇa kārya upagamāt tadā tad janana svabhāva vilakṣaṇāt api dhūma ādi janana svabhāvam yat kāraṇa gnīndhana ādi sāmagrī lakṣaṇam tad vilakṣaṇāt api śakra mūrdu ādeḥ kṣaṇa āśrayeṇa vā dhūma ādeḥ tasya agni indhana ādi sāmagrī janyasya dhūmasya tad kṣaṇasya ca utpattā viṣyamāṇāyām na tad janana śakteḥ pratiniyamaḥ vivakṣita dhūma ādi kārya janana śakti pratiniyamaḥ ititasmāt yat kiñcid kāryam yatas kutaścid kāraṇāt syāt utpadyeta na yathādṛṣṭam eva yathādṛṣṭāt sarvam sarvatas jāyeta iti yāvat tasmāt śakti pratiniyamaḥ kāraṇānām abhyupagantavyaḥ tatas vilakṣaṇa sāmagrī janmanaḥ kāryasya kutaścid sāmyāt sarūpasya upalakṣaṇe api anyādṛśa tā eva iti sarvaḥ tādṛśaḥ tathāvidha janma iti siddham 
[165,i^1]	syāt matam vilakṣaṇāyāḥ api sāmagryāḥ tad lakṣaṇa kārya janana śaktiḥ samānā iti tad lakṣaṇam kāryam bhaviṣyati kasyāścid eva ca tathā abhāvāt na yathā udita doṣa avasaraḥ iti atas āha tad janana śakti sāmye tu ityādi uktam eva tāvat atra pūrva pakṣe na ca dhūmasya tad atad janya svabhāvaḥ iti ādikam dūṣaṇam abhyupagamya api idam āha yādṛśī hi agni sahakāriṇaḥ tad ādhīyamāna vikārasye ndhanasya sva bhedena dhūma bheda hetoḥ śaktiḥ ātma atiśayaḥ tādṛśi eva śakra mūrddhnaḥ dhūmasya vā yadi tad sāmagrī janya dhūma vilakṣaṇa kārya janana śaktiḥ ātma atiśaya lakṣaṇā tadā tad śakti sāmye tat eva agni indhana ādikam eva arthāt nāma antareṇa uktam syāt tad vilakṣaṇasya tad avilakṣaṇa ātmā atiśaya asambhavāt 
[165,i^2_166,i]	saḥ eva hi agniḥ yaḥ indhana vikāram ādadhānaḥ dhūmam janayati tat ca indhanam yat agninā ādhīyamāna vikāram dhūmam sva jātim anukārayati yadi ca śakra mūrdu ādeḥ api evam bhavatā abhyupagamyate tadā kevalam nāmni vivādaḥ syāt artha abhedam abhyupagamya tathā abhidhānāt yatas evam iti tasmāt kāryam dhūma ādikam dṛṣṭam ekadā pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām niścitam atad rūpa vyavṛttena ātmanā kāraṇam indhana ādikam santāna apekṣayā kṣaṇa apekṣayā vā na vyabhicarati tad vilakṣaṇāt anyatas na bhavati iti kārya hetau anvaya vyatireka niścayaḥ sidhyati iti 
[167,i^1]	tat evam karya hetau yatas yat bhava dṛṣṭam sakṛt pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām tādṛśasya sarvasya tathāvidhāt eva janma na tat vijātīyat iti ekasyāḥ api kārya vyakteḥ kutaścid bhāva darśane vyāptyā anvaya vyatireka siddhiḥ iti pratipāditam anupalabdhau tu yathā uktāyām nimitta antara abhāva upadarśana nibandhanayoḥ na anvaya vyatirekayoḥ vipratipattiḥ svarūpaḥ eva tu pare vipratipadyante tathā ahi kecid upalabdhi abhāva mātram anupalabdhim abhāvasya prasajya pratiṣedha ātmanaḥ pramāṇa antara tvena gamikām icchanti īśvara sena prabhṛtayaḥ apare tu pratiṣedhya viṣaya jñāna rūpeṇa apariṇāmam ātmanaḥ tad anya vastu viṣayam vijñānam eva vā abhāvasya gamakam pratyakṣa anumānābhyām pramāṇa antaram āhuḥ mī māṃsakāḥ 
[167,i^2]	na hi anya vastu viṣayam jñānam pratyakṣa anumāna ātmakam abhāvam pratipadyate tasya bhāva aṃśa viṣaya tvāt abhāva aṃśasya ca tatas anya tvāt abhāva aṃśe tu na asti iti jñānam janayat tad abhāva pramāṇa ākhyām labhate yathā indriyam sva viṣaya pratipatti janaka tvena pratyakṣa ākhyām tathā anye anya bhāva lakṣaṇām tad jñāna lakṣaṇām vā anupalabdhim abhāvasya eva sādhanam āhuḥ na abhāva vyavahārasya anupalabdheḥ liṅgādāt abhāva siddhau svayam eva tad vyavahāra pravṛtteḥ 
[167,i^3]	naiyāyikāḥ tu na asti iti jñānam eva kevala pradeśa ādi grāhi jña anantara bhāvi pratyakṣam na pramāṇa antaram abhāvasya tuccha rūpasya pariccheda ātmakam ācakṣate tat eva asya ghaṭa ādeḥ pratiṣedhyasya anupalabdhi śabdena yadi ucyate na kaścid virodhaḥ iti tat evam anupalabdhau bhedam gatāḥ buddhayaḥ prativādinām iti tad nirāsa artham anupalabdhi svarūpam tāvat upadarśayan āha upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya ityādi upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptīḥ upalambha pratyaya antarāṇām samanantara adhipati pratyaya saṃjñitānām sākalyam ālambana pratyayasya svabhāva viśeṣaḥ ca yaḥ svabhāvaḥ satsu anyeṣu upalambha pratyayeṣu san pratyakṣaḥ eva bhavatī ati evaṃrūpā śāstra kṛtāni atra vyākhyātāḥ naiyāyika vipratipatti nirāsa artham 
[167,i^4]	te hi upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpti śabdena mahāt tva aneka dravyavat tva rūpāṇi dravyāṇām āhuḥ mahat tvāt aneka dravyavat tvāt rūpāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti vacanāt evam ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ sati api vastuni sambhavati iti asat vyvahāra siddhau anaikāntikī iti ācakṣate na hi cākṣuṣasya api raśmeḥ mahattva aneka dravyavat tva rūpāṇi upalambhakāni bhavanti na ca tāvatā anupalambha api asat vyavahāraḥ tatra śakyate kartum yat āha bhāṣya kāraḥ na anumānataḥ upalabhyamānasya pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ abhāve hetuḥ iti indriya tvāt tvac ādi vat kila prāpya kāri cakṣuḥ iti anumānataḥ cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ upalabhyate tasya pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ katham abhāva vyavahāram sādhayet 
[167,i^5]	iti tat evam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anu palabdhim asat vyavahāre anaikāḥ ntikīm āhuḥ naiyāyikāḥ tad nirāsam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteḥ aviparīta rūpa upadarśanena śāstra kāraḥ abhyadhāt yadā hi upalambha pratyaya antara sākalyam svabhāva viśeṣaḥ ca yathā uktaḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ ucyate na mahat tva ādikam tadā kutas vyabhicāra avakāśaḥ sati vastuni tasyāḥ asambhavāt mahat tva ādikam tu asambhavāt eva na upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpti śabdena vācyam na hi rūpa ādi vyatiriktam dravyam tad pratibhāsa vivekina ākāra antareṇa sva jñāne pratibhāsate na ca apratibhāsamānam anātma rūpa vivekinā rūpeṇa pratyakṣatām anubhavati atiprasaṅgāt 
[167,i^6]	tat kutas asya asataḥ mahat tva ādi sambhavaḥ na ca svarūpeṇa amahataḥ tad sambandhe api asya mahat tā sambhavaḥ apara rūpeṇa vā grahaṇe katham tat grāhi jñānam abhra antam tatas na mahat tvam dravyasya upalambhakam rūpam vā tasya api sva rūpeṇa grahaṇe dravya ātmanaḥ atyanta parokṣa tvāt dravya rūpasya ca tad vivekena anupalakṣaṇāt na tathā grāhaka tvam na ca mahat tvam rūpam vā dravya udaya kāle abhyupagamyate yatas dravyam guṇasya samavāyi kāraṇam iṣyate tat ca pratilabdha ātmakam eva tathā ātām anubhavati iti prathame kṣaṇe dravyam nirguṇam eva 
[167,i^7]	na ca asya dvitīye kṣaṇe prāktana rūpa tyāgaḥ asti rūpa antaram vā āvirbhavati yatas prāc apratipanna ādhāra bhāvam mahat tva ādi guṇa pratibandhāt ādhāra tām yāyāt na ca ajanakaḥ ādhāraḥ janaka tve ca kṣaṇikatā artha kriyā virodhāt akṣaṇikasya tatas kutas sāmavāyi kāraṇasya sambhavaḥ yatas sva utkalitam kāryam janayat tathā vyapadiśyate na ca etat kṣaṇika tve sambhavati akṣaṇika tve vā prāga anādhārasya paścāt ādhāra abhāvaḥ samavāyi kāraṇā sambhavāt eva aneka dravyavat tvam api asmabhavi yasmāt anekam dravyam ārambhakam samavāyi kāraṇa ātmanā yasya vidyate tat evam vyapadiśyate dravya abhavāt ca na aneka dravyavat tvam 
[167,i^8]	sattve api mahat tva ādeḥ na iyam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ asmākam abhimatā yā tu abhimatā na tayā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ asat vyavahāra siddhā anaikāntikī iti śāstra kāraḥ darśayāmbabhūva upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya yā anupalabdhiḥ kāraṇasya vyāpakasya vā pratiṣedhyāt anyasya sā abhāva hetuḥ kāryasya vyāpyasya ca abhāva vyavahāra hetuḥ ca yā tu pratiṣedhyasya eva upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ sa abhāva vyavahāra hetuḥ eva iti vā śabdena darśayati yā tu anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ pratyakṣa anumāna nivṛtti lakṣaṇā sā saṃśaya hetuḥ pramāṇa nivṛttau api artha abhāva asiddheḥ nimitta abhāvāt tu sat vyavahāra pratiṣedha hetuḥ iti avagantavyam 
[169,i^1]	tatra ye tāvat upalabdhyabhāva mātram anupalabdhim icchanti vijñānam vā anya vastuni iti vacanāt tad anya vastu vijñānam eva vā tad nirāsa artham jñātṛ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇām anupalabdhim darśayitum upalabdhim eva tāvat dvividhām darśayan āha atra anupalabdhi vākye yā upalabdhiḥ śrūyate kriyā rūpā sā yadā kartṛstha tayā apekṣyate tadā tasyāḥ upalabhamānasya katuḥ dharma tve apekṣyamāṇe tat jñānam upalabhamānasya yat jñānam tat upalabdhiḥ ucyate upalabhamānaḥ ca buddhīndriya deha kalāpaḥ eva ca pūrva kṣaṇa saṅgṛhīta upalabdhijanakaḥ ucyate tathā hi upalabdheḥ janakaḥ āśrayaḥ vā kartā paraiḥ ucyate 
[169,i^2]	na ca indriya ādeḥ anyasya janaka tvam sambhavati yatas anvaya vyatireka nibandhanaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva vyavahāraḥ tau ca anvaya vyatirekau na indriya ādeḥ anyasya sambhavataḥ satsu indriya ādiṣu niyamena upalabdheḥ bhāvāt yadi hi indriya ādiṣu satsu api kadācid upalabdhiḥ na upajāyate tadā satsu api anyeṣu sakaleṣu hetuṣu kārya anutpattiḥ kāraṇa antara vaikalyam sūcayati iti tad vyatirikta kāraṇa antaram parikalpyeta na ca etat asti tat katham ātmanaḥ tad utpattau nimitta bhāvaḥ abhyupagamyeta atiprasaṅgāt yat āha yasmin sati bhāvati eva yat tatas anyasya kalpane tad hetu tvena sarvatra hetunām anavasthitiḥ iti 
[170,i]	āśraya tvam api janakasya eva iti tat api ātmanaḥ na sambhavati sthāpaka tvāt āśrayaḥ iti ced na kṣaṇika tve sthiteḥ abhāvāt upalabdheḥ akṣaṇika tve api svayam eva avināśāt avasthānāt tathā hi upalabdheḥ avināśaḥ eva sthitiḥ ucyate na pāta abhāvaḥ tasyāḥ guru tva abhāvāt saṃyoga abhāvena guru tvāt patanam iti ca pareṣām kṛtāntaḥ samavāyāt āśrayaḥ iti ced nanu saḥ api ādhārya ādhāra bhūtānām eva iṣyate na ca āpatana dharmikāyāḥ upalabdheḥ ādhāreṇa kiṃcid samavāyāt ca āśraya tve anyasya api tad bhāva prasaṅgaḥ tasya sarva ātmasu samāna tvāt eka tvena asya upagamāt krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā virodhāt ca na asya ātmanaḥ sattvam tatas asya kutas janaka tvam āśraya tvam vā iti alam kṣuṇṇa kṣodīkaraṇena iti 
[170,ii^1]	evam upalabdhim ādarśya anupalabdhim ādarśayan āha tasmāt upalabdhi jñānāt anyā vastu antara viṣayāḥ upalabdhiḥ jñāna ātmikā anupalabdhiḥ katham punar upalabdhiḥ eva anupalabdhiḥ ucyate iti āha vivakṣita ityādi yathā bhakṣya abhakṣya prakaraṇe vivakṣitāt bhakṣyāt anya tvāt abhakṣyaḥ grāmya kukkuṭaḥ bhakṣyaḥ api san tad anyasya ucyate yathā ca sparśanīyā sparśanīya adhikāre vivakṣitāt sparśanīyāt anya tvāt asparśanīyaḥ cāṇḍāla ādiḥ a tad anyasya sparśanīyaḥ api san ucyate tadvat upaladbhiḥ eva anupalabdhiḥ mantavyā nañaḥ pratiṣedha viṣaya tvāt katham bhāva viṣaya tā iti ced āha paryudāsa vṛttyā iti paryudāsena pratiṣedhyasya arthasya rvajanena yā viśiṣṭe arthe vṛttiḥ tayā nañaḥ āgṛhīta pratiṣedhasya bhāva viṣaya tā 
[170,ii^2]	yatra vidheḥ prādhānyam pratiṣedhaḥ artha gṛhītaḥ vidhi bhāj sva padena na ucyate eka vākyatā ca tatra paryudāsa vṛtti tā vidheḥ ca prādhānyam vivakṣita upalabdheḥ anya upalabdhiḥ bhavati iti evam vākyena anya upalabdheḥ vidhānāt anya upalabdhi sāmarthyāt eva vivakṣita upalabdheḥ pratiṣedhaḥ pratīyate vivakṣita upalabdheḥ anivartane tad apekṣayā anyasyāḥ vidhāna ayogāt sva padena nañā vidhi bhāj na ucyate kim tarhi anya śabdena paryudāsā āśrayeṇa anya śabdasya eva vākye prayogāt anyāḥ upalabdhiḥ anupalabdhiḥ iti nañaḥ ca subantena sāmarthyam na tiṅantena iti eka vākya tvam naḥ upalabdhiḥ anupalabdhiḥ iti prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ punar etat viparītaḥ mantavyaḥ tatra hi pratiṣedhasya prādhānyam vidhiḥ arthāt gamyate vākya bhedaḥ sva padena nañā pratiṣedha bhāj sambadhyate 
[171,i]	tat evam jñātṛ dharma lakṣaṇām anupalabdhim vyākhyāya jñeya dharma lakṣaṇām pratipādayan āha upalabhyamāna dharma tve ityādi yadā karma stha kriyā apekṣayā upalabhyamānasya vastunaḥ dharmaḥ upalabdhiḥ vivakṣyate tadā viṣaya svabhāvaḥ upalabdhiḥ mantavyā kīdṛśaḥ viṣaya svabhāvaḥ iti āha sva viṣaya ityādi pratiṣedhyasya ghaṭa ādeḥ yat ātma viṣayam vijñānam tat janane yā yogyata tad lakṣaṇaḥ viṣaya svabhāvaḥ upalabdhi śabdena ucyate yadi viṣaya svabhāvaḥ upalabdhiḥ katham yogya tā lakṣaṇaḥ tathā hi yogyatā dharmaḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ ca bhedaḥ eva iti atas āha yogyatāyāḥ ityādi yogya tā hi paramārthataḥ bhāva rūpā eva na vastu rūpāda bhidyate anyathā bhāvaḥ yogyaḥ eva na syāt yogyatā asya iti ca sambandha abhāvataḥ na syāt sambandha kalpanāyām anavasthā iti ukta prāyam 
[171,ii^1]	tat evam upalabheḥ viṣaya dharma tām pratipādya anupalabdheḥ api pratipādayan āha tasmāt anyaḥ ityādi tasmāt pratiṣedhyāt ghaṭa ādeḥ sva viṣaya jñāna janana yogyāt yaḥ anyaḥ upalambha janana yogyaḥ eva na tad viparītaḥ svabhāvaḥ ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa rūpaḥ saḥ eva ca atra anupalabdhi śabdena ucyate prāktanam eva nyāyam atra ādiśan āha pūrvavat iti vivakṣita upalabdheḥ anya tvāt abhakṣya asparśanīya vat paryudāsa vṛtya iti katham punar ayam naña anya artha vṛttiḥ sāmānya śabdaḥ san ghaṭa vivikta pradeśasya tat jñānasya eva vā ghaṭa viviktasya anupalabdhi tvam paryudāsa vṛttyā prakalpayati na punar aviśeṣeṇa sarveṣām eva anya śabda vācyānām iti atas āha yatra yasmin ityādi 
[171,ii^2]	yatra deśe kāle avasthāyām vā avyavadhāna ādi lakṣaṇāyām yasmin pradeśa rūpa ādau upalabhyamāne niyamena avaśyaṃtayā yasya anyasya padārthasya ghaṭa rūpa ādeḥ upalabdhiḥ bhavati sa ghaṭa rūpa ādiḥ padārthaḥ tad saṃsṛṣṭaḥ tena pradeśa rūpa ādinā saṃsṛṣṭaḥ katham ekasmin upalabhyamāne parasya api niyama upalabdhiḥ iti ced yogyatāyāḥ aviśeṣāt pradeśa ghaṭayoḥ hi sva viṣaya vijñāna janane yogyatā tulyā yadā hi pradeśa rūpam vyavadhāna vipra karṣa ādi rahitam vijñāne su a ākāram samarpayati tadā ghaṭa rūpam api tatra tathāvidham su a ākāram samarpayati eva yadi nāma yogyatā tasya tena tulyā sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ tu katham tad saṃsṛṣṭa tā iti atas āha eka jñāna saṃsargāt iti ekatra hi jñāne dvau api tau su a ākāra dvāreṇa saṃsṛṣṭau na sākṣāt tat vijñānam padārtha dvaya ākāram ājāyamānam tayoḥ ātmani saṃsargam darśayati 
[171,ii^3]	kim iti punar tat jñānam padārtha dvaya ākāram avaśyam bhavati yatas tayoḥ jñāna dvārakaḥ saṃsargaḥ iti atas āha tayoḥ satoḥ ityādi yau etau tulya yogya tā rūpau tau yadi santau bhavataḥ tadā na eva eka ākāra niyatā pratipattiḥ bhavati kasmāt asambhavāt na hi eṣa sambhavaḥ asti yad tulya yogya tā ru upayoḥ ekaḥ eva pratibhāseta na aparaḥ iti tathā hi aviśiṣṭa tvāt yogyatāyāḥ kaḥ tatra su a ākāram na samarpayet anubhava siddham ca yugapad aneka pratibhāsanam na ca anubhava viruddham ācakṣāṇāḥ viduṣām avadheya vacasaḥ bhavanti ladhu vṛtti tvāt yaugapadya abhimānaḥ iti ced na bādhaka pratyaya viraheṇa bhrānti kalpanā anupapatteḥ sarvatra tathā abhāva aprasaṅgāt 
[171,ii^4]	karaṇa dharmaḥ eva ayam yat ekasmin eva karmaṇi kriyām niṣpādayatinā anekatra karaṇam ca indriyam tatas na aneka pratipatti hetuḥ iti ced katham pradīpa ādiḥ anekatra bahūnām pratipatti janakaḥ kartṛ bhedāt adoṣaḥ iti ced kartṛ eka tvāt tarhi kriyā ekatra karmaṇi iti katham karaṇa dharmaḥ ityādi vacaḥ na plavate na ca pratikṣaṇa viśara aruṣu bhāveṣu paramārthataḥ kartṛ karaṇa ādi bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ kriyā vā kācid na ca sarva kāraka anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyini kārye kasyacid atiśayaḥ asti yena ayam kartā karaṇam ca idam ityādi parikalpyeta tasmāt aviśiṣṭa yogyatayoḥ kutas eka rūpa niyatāyāḥ pratipatteḥ sambhavaḥ iti siddhaḥ eka jñāna saṃsargaḥ tulya yogya tā rūpa tvasya ca etat eva liṅgam na hi asati tulya yogya tā rūpa tve yugapad eka indriya janita jñāna pratibhāsitā rūpa rasavat sambhavati iti 
[173,i]	tatra yeṣām saugatānām idam darśanam eka āyatana saṅgṛhīte anekatra api ekam eva indriya jñānam ājāyate iti teṣām mukhyaḥ eva eka jñāna saṃsargaḥ ye tu tatra api pratyartham bhinnāni eva eka indriya nimittāni eka kālāni tad viṣayāṇām yugapad sannihitānām sva jñāneṣu sāmarthya aviśeṣāt atas eva ekatayā loke adhyavasīyamānāni jñānāni upajāyante iti varṇayanti teṣām eka indriya ja tvena eka āyatana viṣaya tvena ca eka kāleṣu eka tva vyapadeśaḥ loke tathā adhyavasāyāt aupacārikaḥ 
[173,ii]	yadi nāma eka jñāna saṃsargāt tad saṃsṛṣṭaḥ tathā api sāmānyena sarvam anya mayam nan kinna pratipadayati iti atas āha tasmāt ityādi yasmāt aviśiṣṭa tvāt yogyatāyāḥ yathā uktena prakāreṇa ekatra jñāne dvayoḥ api saṃsargaḥ tasmāt aviśiṣṭam yogya tā rūpam yayoḥ tatas eva eka jñāna saṃsargiṇau tau tasmāt tayoḥ evaṃrūpayoḥ paraspara apekṣam eva na sarva anya padārtha apekṣam anya tvam iha anupalabdhi adhikāre abhipretam loke tu yadi api aśeṣa padārtha antara apekṣam anya tvam nañā kvacid ucyate vyāpti nyāya samāśrayāt tathā api tat iha na gṛhyate pratyāsatteḥ āśrayaṇāt eka jñāna saṃsarga lakṣaṇā prattyāsattiḥ āśrīyate na anyā pramāṇa cintā adhikārāt anyathā anupalabdhiḥ anaikāntikya iva syāt tasmāt tattva cintakaiḥ tathāvidham anya tvam āśrayaṇīyam yat anupalabdheḥ avyabhicāra nibandhanam tat ca yathoktam eva iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[174,i^1]	tat evam eka jñāna saṃsarga apekṣayā anya tvam pratipādya anupalabdhim darśayan āha sa kevalaḥ ityādi saḥ eva yadā kevalaḥ pradeśaḥ yathā ukta ghaṭa apekṣaya tasmāt anyaḥ ucyate tadā ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa jñānam vā anupalabdhiḥ na tu yathesvarasenaḥ manyate upalabdhi abhāva mātram anupalabdhiḥ iti vakṣyamāṇa doṣāt ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa svabhāvaḥ vā na tu tad vivikta jñānam eva yathā āha kumārilaḥ vijñānam vā anya vastuni iti yathā hi anya vastu viṣayam jñanam anubhūyamānam pratiyogi smaraṇa apekṣam tad abhāva vyavahāra nibandhanam tathā tad viviktaḥ pradeśaḥ api 
[174,i^2]	tathā hi kasyacid pratipattuḥ yatas kevala pradeśa ākāram eva jñānam mayā saṃvedyate na tu ghaṭa ākāram api tasmāt atra ghaṭaḥ na asti iti evam na astita ajñānam utpadyate kasyacid tu yatas kevalaḥ pradeśaḥ ayam dṛśyate na tu ghaṭa sahitaḥ tasmāt na asti atra ghaṭaḥ iti evam tasmāt ubhayoḥ na astita ajñāna janmani tulyam sāmarthyam iti dvayoḥ api anupalabdhi vyavasthā yuktā iti tatra yadā tat jñānam tadā jñātṛ dharma lakṣaṇa anupalabdhiḥ kartṛstha kriyā apekṣayā yadā tad svabhāvaḥ tadā jñeya dharma lakṣaṇā karma stha kriyā apekṣayā iti 
[174,ii]	evam anupalabdhim paryudāsa vṛttyā vyavasthāpya sādhyam asyāḥ darśayan āha sā abhāvam ityādi sarva anya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta vivikte api pradeśa ādau dṛśyamāne yatra ghaṭa ādau pratiyogini arthi tva ādibhiḥ smṛtiḥ asya bhavati tasya abhāvam sādhayati abhāva vyavahāram vā kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhī abhāvam abhāva vyavahāram ca sādhayataḥ svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ tu abhāvi avahāram eva abhāva vyavahāraḥ ca jñāna abhidhāna pravṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ tatra na asti atra ghaṭaḥ iti evam ākāram jñānam evaṃvidha vastu abhidhāyakam ca abhidhānam niḥśaṅkasya ca tatra pradeśe gamana āgamana lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ iti 
[175,i]	atra īśvarasena kumārilayoḥ vacana avakāśam āśaṅkaya siddhānta vyavasthām eva kurvatā tad mate niraste api āhatya tad mata nirāsa artham āha katham anya bhāvaḥ ityādi īśvarasenaḥ hi manyate kārya svabhāva hetubhyām bhāva rūpābhyām anupalabdheḥ pṛthak karaṇāt avaśyam abhāva rūpa tvam asyāḥ anyathā pṛthak karaṇam anarthakam eva syāt tvayā ca anyasya pratiṣedhya viviktasya pradeśa ādeḥ tat jñānasya vā bhāva rūpa anupalabdhiḥ ākhyāyate tat nūnam anya bhāvaḥ tad abhāvaḥ yena evam abhidhīyate na ca etat yujyate bhāva abhāvayoḥ virodhāt eka ātma tā anupapatteḥ iti 
[175,ii]	kumārilaḥ api evam manyate yā iyam jñātṛ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇā dvidhā anupalabdhiḥ abhāva rūpā tvayā ucyate tasyāḥ bhavatu na astita ajñānam prati sādhana bhāvaḥ kintu saḥ eva anyasya pratiṣedhya viviktasya vastunaḥ pratiṣedhya jñānāt anyasya vā tat jñānasya yaḥ bhāvaḥ bhāva aṃśaḥ sa katham abhāvaḥ pratiṣedhasya tat jñānasya vā katham abhāva aṃśaḥ na eva yujyate dharma rūpa tayā bhāva abhāva aṃśayoḥ bhedāt sati api dharmi rūpeṇa abhede tayoḥ ca udbhava abhibhavābhyām grahaṇa agrahaṇa vyavasthā iti yat āha dharmayoḥ bhedaḥ iṣṭaḥ hi dharmya bhede api naḥ sthite udbhava abhibhava ātma tvāt grahaṇam ca avatiṣṭhate iti 
[175,iii]	ukta uttara tām asya darśayan āha uktam uttaramatra codye yathā paryudāsa vṛttyā apekṣātaḥ pratiṣedhyam tat jñānam vā apekṣya tad viviktaḥ arthaḥ tat jñānam vā abhāvaḥ anupalabdhiḥ ca ucyate iti īśvarasenasya prativacanam na hi prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ eva ekaḥ nañarthaḥ kintu paryudāsaḥ api tatas anya bhāvasya abhāva rūpa tā na virudhyate prasajya pratiṣedha rūpa tā api anya bhāvasya yathā tathā uttaratra vakṣyate svabhāva hetoḥ tu anulabdheḥ pṛthak karaṇam pratipatrabhiprāya vaśāt pratipattā hi svabhāva hetau vastu pratipatti adhyavasāyī anupalabdhau tu abhāva pratipatti adhyavasāyī paramārthataḥ tu pratiṣedhya abhāva vyavahāra yogya tā vastu bhūtā eva pradeśasya sādhyate iti na svabhāva hetoḥ svabhāvān upalabdhiḥ bhidyate iti 
[176,i]	yat tu anapekṣita artha antara saṃsargam pratiṣedha mātram anupalabdhiḥ iti īśvarasenaḥ manyate tad nirākurvan āha na pratiṣedha mātram ityādi kasmāt iti āha tasya sādhana asiddheḥ ityādi na hi abhāvasya sarva sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇasya sādhana tvam siddhi hetu tvam sidhyati sarva sāmarthya viraha rūpasya tad ayogāt hetu tve vā katham na sāmarthyayogitā bhāva rūpa tā vā sāmarthya lakṣaṇa tvāt vastunaḥ abhāvasya ca anapekṣita sahakāriṇaḥ anādheya atiśaya tayā na asti iti jñāna janane nityam tad janana prasaṅgaḥ tatas ca sādhaka tva ayogāt abhāva vyavahāraḥ eva na sidhyet athavā tasya prasajya pratiṣedha ātmanaḥ upalabdhi abhāvasya sādhanam eva kiñcid na sidhyati iti sa hi abhāva tvāt apareṇa upalabdhi abhāvena sādhyaḥ syāt saḥ api apareṇa iti anavasthānam na ca indriya vat ajñātasya pratiṣedha jñāna hetu tā sadā sannihita tvena anapekṣita sahakāriṇaḥ nityam tad udaya prasaṅgāt idam ca artha dvayam katham abhāvaḥ kasyacid pratipattiḥ pratipatti hetuḥ vā tasya api katham pratipattiḥ iti atra antare svayam eva vipañcayiṣyati 
[176,ii]	kumārilasya api uttaram āha tasya anyasya pratiyoginā vastu antareṇa asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya na hi asau vastu antaraiḥ saṃsṛṣṭa svabhāvaḥ eka rūpaḥ tathā tve hi abhāva aṃśaḥ api na kvacid sidhyet tasya evaṃvidhasya bhāva siddhiḥ eva bhāva aṃśa siddhiḥ eva aparasya pratiyoginaḥ vastu antarasya abhāva siddhiḥ abhāva aṃśasya tvad abhimatasya siddhiḥ astu bhāva aṃśasya eva abhāva aṃśa rūpa tā upapatteḥ iti manyate tathā hi abhāva aṃśaḥ api para rūpa asaṃsṛṣṭa tayā eva abhāvaḥ iti vyapadiśyate anyathā tad ayogāt sā ca bhāva aṃśasya api samānā iti saḥ eva abhāvaḥ astu tad nimittasya samāna tvāt kim anyena abhāva aṃśa upagatena atas eva asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya iti viśeṣaṇam yatas evam iti tasmāt anya bhāvaḥ api anyasya vastunaḥ bhāvaḥ api tvad abhimataḥ bhāva aṃśaḥ api na kevalam abhāva aṃśaḥ tvad matyā bhāvaḥ iti vyapadiśyate asmābhiḥ tatas bhāva aṃśasya abhāva rūpa tā saṅgatā eva iti na kiñcid virudhyate iti 
[177,i^1]	yat uktam jñātṛ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇayā svabhāva anupalabdhyā abhāva vyavahāraḥ eva sādhyate na abhāvaḥ iti tat paraḥ vighaṭayitum yat ca uktam na pratiṣedha mātram anupalabdhiḥ tasya sādhana asiddheḥ iti dvitīye vyākhyāne pratiṣedha mātrasya anupalabdhiḥ iti etasya sādhanam darśayitum āha anya bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ ityādi evam manyate lokaḥ hi kevala pradeśa darśanāt ghaṭa abhāvam eva prathamam pratipadyate kevala pradeśa jñāna saṃvedana dvāreṇa ghaṭa jñāna abhāva pratipattyā vā tatas ghaṭa abhāvasya vyavahāram tena loka pratīti anusāreṇa pratiṣedhyāt anyasya pradeśasya pratiṣedhya jñānāt vā tat jñānasya yaḥ bhāvaḥ tad lakṣaṇaḥ abhāvaḥ svayam pramāṇena indriya pratyakṣeṇa sva saṃvedana pratyakṣeṇa ca siddhaḥ alam ghaṭa abhāvam sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa ca yathākramam sādhayitum sa ca ghaṭa abhāva vyavahāram iti evam vyavasthāpayitum yuktam 
[177,i^2]	na ca evam api vyavasthāpane asmad pakṣasya kācid kṣatiḥ tathā hi pāramparyeṇa api yat anupalabdheḥ tvad abhyupagatāyāḥ siddham tat tatas eva siddham bhavati iti pratiṣedha mātrasya anupalabdhi tve tad sādhana pratipādane api ayam abhiprāyaḥ yathā bhavataḥ jñātṛ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇā bhāva rūpā dvividha anupalabdhiḥ tathā mama api jñātṛ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇa upalabdhi abhāvaḥ api anupalabdhi saṃjñitaḥ dvividhaḥ bhaviṣyati tatra jñeya dharma lakṣaṇena anya bhāvena pratyakṣa siddhena pratiṣedhya abhāvaḥ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇa upalabdhi abhāva rūpaḥ anupalabdhi saṃjñitaḥ setsyati jñātṛ dharma lakṣaṇena ca anya bhāvena kevala pradeśa jñāna ātmanā sva saṃvedana siddhena jñātṛ dharmaḥ pratiṣedhya jñāna abhāva rūpaḥ anupalabdhi samākhyātaḥ setsyati tatas ca kutas anavasthā yena sādhana asiddhiḥ syāt iti 
[177,i^3]	tatra anya bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ iti pratiṣedhyāt tad jñānāt ca yaḥ anyaḥ bhāvaḥ pratiṣedhya viviktaḥ pradeśaḥ tat jñānam ca tad ātmakaḥ abhāvaḥ vivakṣitāt bhāvāt pratiṣedhyāt bhāvāt tajñānāt ca anya tvāt anupalabdhi tvena bhavataḥ abhimataḥ svayam sva rūpeṇa pramāṇena indriya pratyakṣeṇa sva saṃvedana pratyakṣeṇa ca siddhaḥ sanstasya pratiṣedhyasya abhāva vyavahāram jñāna abhidhāna pravṛtti lakṣaṇam sādhayet tad siddhi siddhaḥ vā tasya anya bhāva lakṣaṇasya abhāvasya yathā uktasya siddhyā siddhaḥ vā tad abhāvaḥ tasya pratiṣedhyasya tat jñānasya vā abhāvaḥ iti evam apīṣyamāṇe na kaścid viśeṣaḥ tvad abhimata anupalabdhitaḥ asmad abhimata anupalabdheḥ tatas asmad darśanam kim iti pratikṣipyate 
[177,i^4]	nanu asti eva evam iṣyamāṇe viśeṣaḥ anya bhāva lakṣaṇa anupalabdhiḥ itarayā vyavahitā tad abhāva vyavahāram sādhayet itarā tu sākṣāt iti āha sa viśeṣaḥ na asti yena viśeṣeṇa anupalabdhyā abhāva rūpayā vastu saṃsparśa rahitayā asmad abhimatayā bhāva vyavahāra siddheḥ virodhaḥ syāt anyasya tu viśeṣasya sataḥ api abādhaka tvāt asat sama tvam eva yat api uktam tasya sādhana abhāvāt abhāva vyavahāra asiddhi prasaṅgaḥ iti tat api asat yatas saḥ eva tvad abhimataḥ anya bhāvaḥ pratiṣedhya vivikta bhū tala ātmakaḥ tad viṣayā ca upalabdhiḥ anupalabdhi tvena iṣṭā bhavataḥ tad abhāvasya anupalabdhi tvena asmad matasya pratiṣedhya abhāvasya tad upalabdhi abhāvasya ca kim kasmāt na sādhanam liṅgam iṣyate tathā hi sati loka pratītiḥ anusṛtā bhavati kim punar kasmāt punar abhāvasya dvividhasya siddhiḥ eva tad abhāva siddhiḥ na tad sādhyā kācid anyā vidyate iti asmad mata niṣedha artham loka atikrāntam iṣyate iti pūrva pakṣaḥ 
[178,i]	atra āha apṛthak siddheḥ anya bhāvāt tad abhāvasya pṛthak siddheḥ abhāvāt kutas liṅga liṅgitā tathā sambandha abhāvāt cā anya bhāva tad abhāva yoḥ na liṅga liṅgitā iti prathamam tāvat kāraṇam vivṛṇvan āha anya bhāvaḥ tad vivikta deśa ātmakaḥ tāvat na sādhanam liṅgam pratiṣedhya abhāvasya tad upalabdhiḥ api tad abhāvasya na sādhanam iti paścāt vakṣyate tad artham eva tāvat śabdaḥ kasmāt anya bhāvaḥ na sādhanam iti āha yad siddhau yasya vastunaḥ siddhau pratītau yasya aparasya vastunaḥ na siddhiḥ na pratītiḥ tat vastu tasya vastunaḥ liṅgam bhavati iti ayam liṅga liṅginoḥ nyāyaḥ tatra udāharaṇam dhūma agni vat iti yathā yadā dhūma pratītau na agniḥ pratīyate tadā tayoḥ lliṅga liṅgi bhāvaḥ bhavati na tu dhūma pratīti kāle eva pratīyamāne agnau yadi nāma evam tatas kim iti atas āha anyasya vastunaḥ yaḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāva tad siddhyā eva tat prati iti eva tad abhāvaḥ tasya pratiṣedhyasya abhāvaḥ prasidhyati pratīyate anya bhāvasya eva tad abhāva ātmaka tvāt tad siddheḥ eva tad siddhi lakṣaṇa tvāt 
[179,i^1]	naiyāyikāḥ tu manyante pratiṣedhya abhāvaḥ hi prasajya pratiṣedha ātmakaḥ tuccha rūpaḥ tasya katham tad anya bhāva rūpa tā bhāva abhāvayoḥ virodhāt tatas katham tad anya bhāva siddhyā eva tad abhāva siddhiḥ syāt iti atas āha tasya tad anya bhāvasya pradeśa lakṣaṇasya tasmāt anyena pratiṣedhyena ghaṭa ādinā asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya rahita ātmanaḥ kevalasya pratiṣedhyena śūnya ātmanaḥ anena kevala pradeśasya api prasajya pratiṣedha ātmaka tām āha katham bhāvasya tuccha rūpa tā svabhāvaḥ virodhāt iti ced na para rūpeṇa tasya api tuccha rūpa tvāt 
[179,i^2]	yathā hi anapekṣita bhāva antara saṃsargaḥ prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ śūnya vikalpa pratibhāsī pratiṣedhyena tuccha rūpaḥ tad rūpa virahāt tathā tad anya bhāvaḥ api pratiṣedhya asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpaḥ tatas katham asya pratiṣedhyena tuccha rūpa tā virudhyeta sva rūpeṇa hi ayam atuccha rūpaḥ syāt na para rūpeṇa anyathā katham asya anya bhāva tvam parasya vā tatra abhāvaḥ syāt yaḥ hi yat abhāva rūpaḥ na bhavati saḥ eva asau bhavati tad svarūpa vat tatas sarvasya jagataḥ paraspara ātma tā prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt sarva bhāvāḥ para rūpeṇa niḥsvabhāvāḥ svarūpeṇa rūpavat tve apī tyanavadyam 
[179,ii^1]	kaḥ tarhi prasajya pratiṣedhat paryudāsasya bhedaḥ na kaścid kevalam anapekṣita rūpa antaram abhāva mātram prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ iti loke kathyate rūpa antaram tu para rūpa śanyam paryudāsaḥ iti na tu rūpa antaram para rūpa tuccha ātmakam na bhavati anubhūyate eva ca rūpa antaram tad rūpa śūnya tayā katham tasya prasajya pratiṣedha ātma tā na syāt para rūpeṇa sāmarthyāt tatas tad pratītiḥ iti ced na akāraṇa pratītau sāmarthya asambhavāt tādātmya abhāve hi prasajya pratiṣedhasya paryudastāt pratītau tad kāraṇa tve sati syāt pratipattiḥ na anyathā 
[179,ii^2]	tasya tad anyā saṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya yat tattvam tasya pratiṣedhya tuccha rūpa tāyāḥ vyavasthāpakam pramāṇam pratyakṣa rūpam tatas eva na tad uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ na asti iha ghaṭaḥ iti vikalpāt tasya gṛhīta grāhitayā smṛti tvena apramāṇa tvāt anyasya ghaṭa ādeḥ tatra asataḥ vyavacchedasya abhāvasya siddheḥ tad abhāva ātmakasya eva pradeśasya tena grahaṇāt dvividhaḥ hi ayam pradeśaḥ ghaṭa asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpsaḥ tad vyāvṛtta rūpa tayā tatas anyaḥ ghaṭavān api kevalaḥ ca ghaṭam prati apratipanna ādhāra bhāvaḥ tasya tat vivekena pratyakṣeṇa grahaṇe ghaṭāt anya tvam ghaṭa virahaḥ ca gṛhītaḥ eva bhavati iti na vastu asaṃkara siddhi artham iha idam na asti iti evam artham ca pramāṇa antaram anveṣaṇīyam vistarataḥ ca etat uttaratra vakṣyate iti āstām tāvat yatas ca anya bhāva siddhyā eva tad abhāvaḥ uktena nyāyena siddhyati tatas na anya bhāvaḥ pratiṣedhya abhāvasya liṅgam 
[180,i^1]	dvitīyam kāraṇam vyācakṣāṇaḥ āha sambandha abhāvāt ca iti anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ na kaścid sambandhaḥ asti tatas kutas liṅga liṅgi bhāvaḥ iti etat ca kadā ucyate yadā tad abhāva rūpa tā anya bhāvasya para an abhyupagatā apekṣyate tad anya bhāvāt pṛthak eva tad abhāvaḥ tuccha rūpaḥ iṣyate paraiḥ anyathā uktena nyāyena anya bhāvasya eva tad abhāva rūpa tve tādātmyāt katham sambandha abhāvaḥ pratyakṣa siddha tā ca tadā eva na pakṣa antareṇa abhihitā tat ca tasya iti ādyasya eva vivaraṇam vyatireka mukhena eka artha samavāyaḥ iti para darśanena uktam 
[180,i^2]	pareṣām hi naiyāyika ādīnām vyatiriktau eva kṛtaka anitya tva ākhyau dharmau ekasmin eva dharmiṇi samavetau iti kṛtakasya anitya tvena ekasmin arthe dharmiṇi samavāyaḥ sambandhaḥ dhamasya vā iti sambandhaḥ eva udāharaṇa antaram atra ekartha samavāyaḥ iti saṃyogaḥ saḥ eva samavāya śabdena uktaḥ saṃyoga samavāyayoḥ kalpita tvāt bhedena vyapadeśe anādarāt pareṣām tu agni dhūmau sva avayaveṣu eva samavetau iti na tayoḥ eka artha samavāya ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ vā iti dhūmasya agneḥ upari darśanāt laukikaḥ sambandhaḥ uktaḥ janya janaka bhāvaḥ vā iti pāramārthikaḥ sambandhaḥ abhihitaḥ paramārthataḥ agneḥ janaka tvāt itarasya ca janya tvāt iti 
[181,i]	nanu ca īśvarasenena saha vicāraḥ prakrāntaḥ tat kim iti naiyāyika abhimasya api sambandhasya anya bhāva tadabhāvayoḥ abhāvaḥ ucyate satyam prasaṅgena tu tad matasya api niṣedha artham uktam pūrvam hi anya bhāva grāhi pratyakṣa siddha tvāt pratiṣedhya abhāvasya na tad artham pratyakṣa antaram na asti iha ghaṭaḥ iti evam ākāram kalpanīyam iti prasaṅgataḥ kathitam adhunā tu prasaṅgāt idam ucyate yadā anya bhāva grāhi pratyakṣa siddhaḥ ayam tad abhāvaḥ na bhavati tadā pratyakṣa antaram na asti iha ghaṭaḥ iti evam ākāram viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva lakṣaṇāt sannikarṣāt iṣṭam bhavatā na ca asati sambandhe anya bhāva tadabhāvayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ atiprasaṅgāt tatas kutas tad lakṣaṇāt sannikarṣāt tad abhāve pratyakṣam bhavet iti 
[181,ii^1]	evam sambandha svarūpam ākhyāya tasya iha asambhavam āha na evam yathā kṛtaka tva anitya tvayoḥ agni dhūmayoḥ vā eka artha samavāya ādi lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ na evam kaścid bhāva abhāvayoḥ sambandhaḥ yena asya tad abhāvasya anya bhāvaḥ sādhanam syāt yau ekatra arthe dharmi rūpe pravartete tayoḥ eka artha samavāyaḥ bhavati anya bhāvaḥ ca pradeśa ākhyaḥ sva avayaveṣu yeṣu vartate na tatra ghaṭa abhāvaḥ evam hi pradeśa avayaveṣu ghaṭaḥ na asti iti syāt na pradeśe na ca asya pradeśa avayavaiḥ ārambhaḥ te hi dravya ātmānaḥ dravya antaram eva ārabhante na ca ghaṭa abhāvaḥ dravyam nava eva hi dravyāṇi iṣyante 
[181,ii^2]	na ca kriyāvat ādikam dravya lakṣaṇam tatra asti na ca guṇa rūpa tayā tatra vartate catur viśatiḥ eva hi guṇāḥ iṣyante na ca ayam teṣām anyatamaḥ na api karma rūpa taya pañcasu karmasu anantarbhāvāt tad lakṣaṇa virahāt ca eka dravyam iti ādikam hi tad lakṣaṇam na ca etad abhāve sambhavati iti na api sāmānya ādi rūpa tayā tad rupavirahāt eva na api anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ saṃyogaḥ agni dhūmayoḥ iva dravyayoḥ eva tad abhyupagamāt na ca tad abhāvaḥ dravyam iti uktam na api ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ yatas saḥ api saṃyoga nimittaḥ ucyate iha kuṇḍe badarāṇi iti 
[181,ii^3]	samavāya nimittaḥ vā iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ iti na ca abhāvasya adravya ātmanaḥ saṃyogaḥ samasti na api samavāyaḥ pañcānām eva hi dravya ādīnām padārthānām samavāyi tvam iṣyate na ca abhāvaḥ pañcasu antar bhavati iti na ca tad ā ātmā anupakāre satya ādhāra vyapadeśaḥ sambhavati upakāre vā janya janaka bhavaḥ na ca tad abhāvaḥ janyaḥ kārya tā prasaṅgāt kārya tā ca asya asambhavinī yatas sva kāraṇa samavāyaḥ sattā samavāyaḥ vā kāryatā ucyate bhavadbhiḥ anya bhāvaḥ tu pradeśa ākhyaḥ asya na kāraṇam trayāṇām eva hi dravya guṇa karmaṇām dravyam kāraṇam iṣṭam 
[181,ii^4]	na ca abhāvaḥ dravya ādi lakṣaṇaḥ iti sattā samavāye api sat pratyaya viṣaya tā tad abhāvasya syāt na abhāva pratyaya viṣaya tā pradeśa abhāve api ca ghaṭa abhāva sambhavāt kutas tad kārya tā na ca asya prativiṣayam bhedaḥ eka ākāra jñāna viṣaya tvāt sambandhi bhedāt bhede vā sāmānya ādiṣu api tad prasaṅgaḥ samavāya upyasya anantaram eva nirastaḥ iti kutas sva kāraṇa sattā samavāya rūpā kārya tā tad abhāvasya syāt etena janya janaka bhāvaḥ prayuktaḥ tatas sarvathā sambandha abhāvāt na anya bhāvaḥ tad abhāvasya sādhanam iti 
[182,i^1]	paraḥ sambandha antaram darśayan āha asti viṣaya ityādi yathā hi arthaḥ viṣayaḥ śabdaḥ viṣayi iti tayoḥ viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ sambandhaḥ evam anya bhāva tadabhāvayoḥ viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ sambandhaḥ bhaviṣyati pradeśa ākhyena anya bhāvena ghaṭa abhāvasya pratyāyanāt iti pūrva pakṣa āśaṅkā śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ syāt iti abhisambandhaḥ kim rūpaḥ kārya kāraṇa lakṣaṇaḥ katham punar artha kārya tā śabdasya tad pratipādana abhiprāye sati artha pratipādana vivakṣāyām satyām tad prayogāt śabda uccāraṇāt tena arthena vivakṣā viparivartinā śabdasya kārya kāraṇa lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ syāt yadi api ca śabda arthayoḥ buddhi parikalpita sāmānya rūpa tā tathā api artha pratibhāsinyā vivakṣayā śabda sāmānya utprekṣā nibandhanasya śabda sva lakṣaṇasya utthāpanāt tad mukhena kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ucyate 
[182,i^2]	avinā abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ vā iti para prasiddhyā ucyate paraḥ hi avinābhāva lakṣaṇaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ iti vyavaharati tatas sambandha nivandhana pratipādya pratipādaka rūpaḥ viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ tad abhāvāni abhāvayoḥ api evam bhaviṣyati iti ced āha ayam ca anantara ukta prakāraḥ atra tad abhāvāni abhāvayoḥ na sambhavati na hi ghaṭa abhāva pratipādana abhiprāye sati anya bhāvasya pradeśa lakṣaṇasya prayogaḥ niṣpattiḥ bhavati ghaṭa abhāva pratipādana abhiprāyāt prāk api pradeśasya sva hetubhyaḥ eva niṣpatteḥ sati api tad abhiprāye anya bhāvasya abhāvāt ca tatas ca katham tayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tad vārakaḥ avinābhāvaḥ vā syāt yatas viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ kalpyeta 
[183,i]	syāt matam yathā śabda arthayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva nimittaḥ viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ tathā anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ api iti etāvat mātreṇa śabda arthayoḥ dṛṣṭānta tā iti atas āha siddhe hi ityādi śabda arthayoḥ hi kārya kāraṇa bhāva nibandhanaḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ anyathā artha antara tve tad ayogāt tathā iha api yadi tad abhāvāni abhāvayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ sidhyet tadā tad mukhena sādhya sādhana bhāva dvāreṇa viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ syāt yāvatā saḥ eva sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ asati sambandhe kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādike na sidhyati sarvasya sādhya sādhana tā prasakteḥ 
[183,ii]	katham indriyam sva viṣaya siddhi nibandhanam iti ced paraspara upasarpaṇa ādi āśrayāt pratyaya viśeṣāt indriya viṣayayoḥ eka vijñāna utpādanayoḥ udayāt tathā vyapadeśaḥ na evam iha anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ tad ayogāt liṅga liṅgi bhāva lakṣaṇasya ca sādhya sādhana bhāvasya prakṛta tvāt tasya ca sambandham antareṇa ayogāt 
[184,i]	na eva sambandha antara nibandhanaḥ anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ api tu viṣaya viṣayi bhāva nimittaḥ eva iti ced āha anyathā yadi sambandha antaram na iṣyate kintu viṣaya viṣayi bhāvāt sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ tasmāt ca viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ tatas itaretara āśrayam idam syāt tathā ca eka asiddhau dvayoḥ api asiddhiḥ bhavet iti kiñca anya bhāvāt ca liṅga bhūtāt abhāvasya liṅginaḥ siddhau anumita aviṣyamāṇāyām asamudāyaḥ ca sādhyaḥ syāt anya bhāvena tad abhāvasya kevalasya eva sādhanāt na kevala sambandha abhāvāt sādhya sādhana bhāva ayogaḥ samudāyaḥ ca viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva āpannaḥ dharma dharmi lakṣaṇaḥ sādhyaḥ yaḥ iṣṭaḥ tad abhāva doṣaḥ ca iti caśabdaḥ 
[184,ii]	sarvatra samudāyasya sādhya tā na eva iṣṭā iti ced āha tathā ca dharma mātrasya api svatantrasya sādhyatā upagame ghaṭa abhāvaḥ tad anya bhāvāt iti evaṃrūpe prayoge ghaṭasya sarvatra deśe sarvadā ca abhāvaḥ prasajyeta dharmiṇi hi kvacid dharmasya guṇa bhūtasya sādhane tatra eva tad kāle eva ca bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ na anyat ā iti sarvatra samudāyaḥ eva sādhyaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ na kevalaḥ dharmaḥ iti 
[184,iii]	atra āha paraḥ na asamudāyasya sādhya tā anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ asambandhaḥ vā kutas pradeśa ādi ityādi iha pradeśe ghaṭaḥ na asti iti evam ghaṭa abhāvena pradeśa ādiḥ dharmī viśeṣyate sa ghaṭāt pradeśa ādeḥ bhedena avasthāpyate iti tad viśeṣaṇa tvam prāpta sādhyate na tu ghaṭaḥ na asti iti evam kevalaḥ dharmiṇaḥ kasyacigduṇa bhāvam anāpannaḥ tatas na asamudāyasya sādhyatā iti kutas tad bhāvī doṣaḥ na ca na eva asmin pakṣe liṅgasyāḥ nyabhāva ātmanaḥ liṅginaḥ ca pradeśa ādi dharmi lakṣaṇasya asambandha doṣaḥ prasajyate kuta anya bhāvasya ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa dilakṣaṇasya pradeśa ādinā dharmiṇā sambandhāt tad ātmi asadbhāvāt iti tathā hi śabda ādi dharmiṇā kṛtaka tva ādeḥ tādātmya lakṣaṇaḥ eva sambandhaḥ iṣyate bhavatā saḥ iha asti iti abhiprāyaḥ tatas ca sambandha abhāvāt ca iti ayuktam iti manyate 
[185,i^1]	siddhānta vādī tu sādhya dharma lakṣaṇasya liṅginaḥ ghaṭa abhāva ākhyasya anya bhāvena liṅgena sambandha abhāvaḥ prāk uktaḥ na dharmiṇā tatas dam uttaram sāṃbadhyate iti manyamānaḥ dharmiṇā api anya bhāva ākhyasya liṅgasya sambandha abhāvam darśayan āha na liṅga liṅginoḥ asambandhaḥ na ca iti sambadhyate tathā na asamudāya sādhanam iti kintu liṅga liṅginoḥ asambandhaḥ eva asamudāya sādhanam eva ca evam api bruvataḥ kutas pradeśa ādeḥ eva dharmi tayā avasthāpyamānasya anya bhāva tvāt anya bhāva lakṣaṇa liṅga tvāt etat eva darśayati yatra eva hi pradeśa ādau dharmi tayā tvayā kalpyamāne yat ghaṭa ādikam na asi iti ucyate lokena saḥ eva pradeśa ādiḥ tena ghaṭa ādinā saṃsṛṣṭa ssaṃsarga rahitaḥ anya bhāvaḥ liṅgatayā iṣṭaḥ na aparaḥ kaścid yatas tad darśanāt eva ghaṭa asaṃsṛṣṭa pradeśa ādi darśanāt eva asya pratipattuḥ ghaṭaḥ na asti iti vikalpaḥ liṅgi jñāna tayā upagataḥ bhavati
