[185,i^2]	tatas saḥ eva anya bhāvaḥ yat eva hi dṛśyamānam liṅgi jñānam janayati tat eva liṅgam ucyate ghaṭa asaṃsṛṣṭaḥ ca pradeśa ādiḥ evam tasmāt tat eva anya bhāva lakṣaṇam liṅgam upeyam tatas katham tasya eva anya bhāvasya vyāvṛttitaḥ api bhedam ananubhavataḥ liṅga liṅgi bhāvaḥ liṅga tvam liṅgi tvam vā nahi liṅgam eva dharmī bhavitum arhati dharmi pratipattau eva sādhya pratipatteḥ anvaya ādi anusaraṇa ayogāt tatas ca anyasya dharmiṇaḥ abhāvāt katham anya bhāva ātmanaḥ liṅgasya tad sambandhaḥ samudāya sādhyatā vā śabda kṛtaka tvayoḥ tu paramārthataḥ tādātmye api vyāvṛtti bheda nibandhanaḥ asti eva bhedaḥ tatas śabda ādi dharmi pratipattau api anitya tva ādi apratītau kṛtaka tva ādinā tat sādhyate iti yuktam 
[185,ii^1]	syāt matam sāmānya viśeṣa kalpanayā liṅga liṅgitā ekasya api bhaviṣyati iti atas āha na ca atra prakṛte anya bhāve sāmānya viśeṣa bhāva kalpanā sambhavati yena sāmānya viśeṣa vikalpena sāmānyam hetuḥ bhavet viśeṣaḥ dharmī yatas samudāya sādhyatā liṅga liṅginoḥ sambandhaḥ vā syāt kutas na sambhavati iti āha tad viśeṣa pratipatteḥ eva ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa viśeṣa pratipatteḥ eva tad abhāvasya ghaṭa abhāvasya pratīteḥ yatas ca viśeṣaḥ eva ghaṭa abhāva pratīti nibandhanam tatas kim tatra sāmānya kalpanayā kriyate iti saḥ eva viśeṣaḥ anyatra vartamānaḥ sāmānya rūpa tām pratipatsyate iti ced āha tasya ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa viśeṣasya anyatra sajātīye anvayasya anuvṛtteḥ abhāvāt kutas sāmānya ātma tā 
[185,ii^2]	 na hi asau deśa kāla avasthā niyataḥ viśeṣaḥ anyam anveti iti atra eva upacaya hetum āha pratijñārtha ityādi yadi hi ghaṭa viviktaḥ eva pradeśa viśeṣaḥ dharmī tasya eva ca hetutā iṣyate tadā pratijñāyāḥ yaḥ arthaḥ dharma dharmi samudāyaḥ tat eka deśaḥ eva dharmi lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ syāt pratijñā artha eka deśasya ca vyāvṛttitaḥ api bhedam ananubhavataḥ hetu tvam asiddham iti atha mā bhūt eṣa doṣaḥ iti na ghaṭa viviktaḥ eva pradeśa viśeṣaḥ hetuḥ iṣyate kintu pradeśa mātram ghaṭa vivikta tā viśeṣa rahitam iti atas āha na ca yatra pradeśa mātram tatra ghaṭa abhāvaḥ sa ghaṭe api pradeśe pradeśa mātrasya bhāvāt anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ syāt 
[186,i^1]	paraḥ anyathā sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvam darśayan āha tādṛśe yādṛśaḥ ghaṭa viviktaḥ kevalaḥ pradeśaḥ agratas sthitaḥ tādṛśe sarvatra pradeśe ghaṭasya abhāvaḥ iti kutas anekāntaḥ tathāvidha pradeśa viśeṣa pratītiḥ eva ghaṭa abhāva pratītiḥ tatas anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ liṅga liṅgita anupapannā iti upadarśayan āha nanu tasya eva ityādi yaḥ asau kevalaḥ pradeśa viśeṣaḥ dharmi tayā avasthāpitaḥ tasya eva yat kaivalyam kevalaḥ iti anena viśeṣaṇena ucyate bhavatā te deva ghaṭa virahaḥ ghaṭābhāvaḥ iti kathyate sa ca ghaṭa virahaḥ liṅga bhūtasya kevalasya pradeśasya pratipattau eva siddhaḥ na tu uttara kālam tatas anyaḥ eva ākāra antareṇa dhūmāt iva agniḥ sidhyati 
[186,i^2]	tatas kasya idānīm tad pratipattau eva sādhya pratītau satyām tat liṅgam na kasyacid jijñāsitasya ghaṭa abhāvasya siddheḥ anyasya kasyacid ajijñāsita tvāt kevala pradeśa pratipattau eva ghaṭa viraha pratītau ca yat etat uttara kālam yatra yatra kevalaḥ pradeśaḥ tatra tatra ghaṭa virahaḥ iti anvayasya anugamanam anusaraṇam tat ca nirarthakam ādau eva sādhya pratīteḥ yatas evam tasmāt anya bhāvaḥ kevala pradeśa lakṣaṇaḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ bheda abhāvāt na sādhanam abhāvasya iti sthitam tat evam samudāya sādhyatām liṅgasya ca dharmiṇā sambandham pratipādayitum yat uktam pareṇa pradeśa ādi dharmi viśeṣaṇasya abhāvasya sādhanāt iti tad apṛthak siddhi dūṣaṇena eva nirākṛtam 
[187,i]	viṣaya viṣayi bhāvena tu sambandha pratipādane niraste paraḥ anyathā sambandham sādhya sādhanayoḥ ddarśayan āha asti anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ sambandhaḥ virodha ākhyaḥ tatas sambandha sadbhāvāt anya bhāvāt abhāvasya siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati iti siddhānta vādī tu sādhya sādhanayoḥ virodham eva asambhāvayan pṛcchati kena kasya virodhaḥ iti na hi atra sādhya sādhanayoḥ virodhaḥ saṃbhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ paraḥ virodham abhiprāyana bhijña tayā darśayati anya bhāvena kevala pradeśa ātmanā pratiyoginaḥ yasya abhāvaḥ pramātum iṣṭaḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ tasya iti 
[187,ii]	parasya evaṃvādinaḥ asambandha abhidhāyitām ādarśayan āha kim nu vai pratiyogī ghaṭa ādiḥ pramātum iṣṭaḥ yena pratiyoginaḥ prameya tvena liṅga liṅginoḥ virodhaḥ sambandhaḥ abhidhīyate na eva pratiyogī pramātum iṣṭaḥ kintu tad abhāvaḥ iti ced āha abhāvaḥ tu pratiyoginaḥ yaḥ sādhya 
[187,iii]	kumārilaḥ tu manyate bhava aṃśāt bhinnaḥ ayam abhāva aṃśaḥ tatas na anya bhāvaḥ eva tad abhāvaḥ iti katham tat pratipattiḥ eva tad abhāva pratipattiḥ iti tathā hi ayam abhāvaḥ prāc abhāva ādi bheda bhinnaḥ na ca avastunaḥ bhedaḥ sambhavati atas ayam vastu rūpaḥ eva yat āha na ca avastunaḥ ete syuḥ bhedāḥ tena asya vastu tā iti na ca bhāva aṃśaḥ eva abhāva aṃśaḥ yuktaḥ tasya indriya saṃyoga balena pratīteḥ itara pratīteḥ ca tad asaṃyoga hetuka tvāt yat āha tad saṃyoge sat iti evam sat rūpa tvam pratīyate na asti atra idam iti ittham tu tad asaṃyoga hetukam iti 
[188,i^1]	tat katham tad pratipattiḥ eva aparasya vyavacchedanam iti tad nirāsa artham āha tasya anyasya pradeśasya kevalasya yat tat kaivalya mekākika tvam asahāya tā tat eva aparasya pratiyoginaḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ vaikalyam abhāvaḥ iti tasmāt tad anya bhāvaḥ eva bhāva aṃśaḥ eva tvad abhimataḥ tad abhāvaḥ pratiyogi abhāva aṃśaḥ na tatas pṛthak bhūtam dharma antaram iti ucyate sugata sutaiḥ tatas ca tat pratipattiḥ eva ca tasya anya bhāvasya pratipattiḥ eva ca tad apratipattiḥ tasya pratiyoginaḥ apratipattiḥ abhāva pratipattiḥ iti yāvat evam manyate yaḥ ayam abhāva aṃśaḥ bhāva aṃśāt pṛthak bhūtaḥ vastunaḥ dharmaḥ parikalpyate sa ghaṭa ādi abhāva ātmaka tām tad rūpa vaikalyāt eva anubhavati na anyathā tat ca tad rūpa vaikalyam anya vastunaḥ bhāva aṃśasya api vidyate eva tad abhāve hi tasya anya vastu tā eva hīyeta 
[188,i^2]	na hi yat yat rūpa vikalam na bhavati tat tatas anya tvam anubhavati yathā tasya eva svarūpam tathā ca abhāva aṃśaḥ api tasya na sidhyet sarvam ca viśvam ekam dravyam prasajyeta tatas ca saha utpatti ādi prasaṅgaḥ sarvasya ca sarvatra upayogaḥ syāt iti avaśyam anya vastunaḥ bhāva rūpa tā tad anya abhāva ātmikā eva tathā ca tat pratipattiḥ eva tad anya abhāva pratipattiḥ tad saṃyogaḥ eva ca indriyasya tad anya abhāva saṃyogaḥ iti kim ucyate na asti atra idam iti ittham tu tad asaṃyoga hetukam iti vikalpa apekṣayā uktam iti ced tat etat abādhakam eva pratyakṣeṇa tad ākāra utpattyā tad anya bhāva ātmake eva vastu rūpe pratipanne pāścātyasya yathā gṛhīta abhilāpinaḥ vikalpasya upagamāt vistarataḥ ca ayam abhāva vicāraḥ pramāṇa dvi tva siddhau abhāvam prameyam pramāṇam ca vicārayatā vihitaḥ iti tatas eva a avadhāryaḥ iti 
[189,i^1]	avaśyam ca tad anya bhāva pratipattiḥ eva tad abhāva pratipattiḥ tatas na vastu asaṅkara sidhi artham na asti atra idam iti abhāva vyavahāra artham ca abhāva pramāṇa parikalpanā yuktā iti darśayan āha anyathā yadi tat pratipattiḥ eva tad abhāva pratipattiḥ iti na iṣyate tadā tasya anya vastunaḥ svarūpa paricchedena tatas anyasya atad rūpasya avyavacchede anirākaraṇe tad abhāva apratipattau tad paricchedaḥ eva na syāt tasya tad anya vastunaḥ svarūpa pratipattiḥ eva na syāt kim kāraṇam tat atad rūpayoḥ tasya tad anya vastunaḥ yat rūpam pratiniyatam sakala trailokya vilakṣaṇam yat ca atad rūpam tad rūpam na bhavati para rūpam tayoḥ avivekāt avivecanāt vivekena avyavasthāpanāt asā aṅkaryeṇa aprasādhanāt 
[189,i^2]	sakala para rūpa asaṅkirṇam hi tad rūpam tat ced tad sāmarthya bhāvinā pratyakṣeṇa tathā na anukṛtam kevalam sammugdha ākāram eva tat utpannam tadā kathantena tad paricchedaḥ syāt na hi yat rūpam yat vastu tad rūpān anukāriṇā jñānena tad paricchedaḥ yuktaḥ yathā śuku śaṅkha rūpān anukāriṇā kāmalinaḥ pīta śaṅkha avabhāsinā jñānena iti pratiniyata rūpa anukāre vā tad paricchedasya katham anyā vyavacchedaḥ nāma tatas pratiniyata rūpān anukārāt eva tad anya avyavacchedaḥ tathā ca tad pariccheda abhāvaḥ iti 
[189,ii]	bhavati evam tatas kaḥ doṣaḥ iti atas āha yaḥ eṣa vyavahāraḥ sarva jana pratitaḥ kasyacid agni ādeḥ vastunaḥ darśanāt kvacid deśe tad sambandhini prāpti arthaḥ dṛṣṭasya adṛṣṭasya ca parihāra arthaḥ pravṛtti nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ sa na syāt kim kāraṇam na hi yasmāt ayam pratipattāḥ analam paśyan api saṅkīrṇa tadat rūpa pratibhāsinā pratyakṣeṇa anyathā asya darśana rūpa tā hāneḥ tathā hi asaṅkīrṇasya adarśane saṅkīrṇam api yadi na paśyet tadā loṣṭa ādi prakhyam katham kasyacid etad darśanam syāt saḥ evaṃbhūtaḥ saṅkīrṇa darśanavān pratipattā katham analam eva paśyati na salila ādikam kintu saṅkīrṇa rūpa vastu pratibhāsi jñāna tayā salila ādikam api paśyati tatas katham salila arthī tatra agnimati pradeśe na pravarteta 
[190,i]	parasya vacana avakāśam āśaṅkayā āha anupalambhena ityādi anala pratibhāsinā hi jñānena anala svarūpam eva pratīyate yaḥ tu salila abhāvaḥ sa tatra salilasya anupalambhena tatas jñāna dvayena tad atad rūpayoḥ vivekāt loke pravṛtti nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ pratiniyataḥ vyavahāraḥ sidhyati iti siddhāntavādi āha kaḥ ayam anupalambhaḥ nāma iti kadācid paraḥ brūyāt salila upalambha viraha mātram iti atas āha yadi salilaḥ ityādi kumārilasya tu salila upalambha nivṛtti mātram tuccha rūpam abhāva pramāṇa tayā nābhimatam eva 
[190,ii^1]	pratyakṣa ādeḥ anutpattiḥ pramāṇa abhāvaḥ ucyate sa ātmanaḥ apariṇāmaḥ vā vijñānam vā anya vastuni iti vacanāt kintu yaḥ asau ātmanaḥ pratiṣedhya vastu pratibhāsi jñāna ātmanā pariṇāmaḥ sa tad anya vastu pratibhāsi jñāna sahacaritaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ na kevalaḥ iti param abhyupagamayitum asya upanyāsaḥ tathā ca anya vastu vijñānam eva abhāva pramāṇa m astu kim apramāṇakasya ātmanaḥ apariṇāma ākhyena dharmeṇa parikalpitena na ca tad anya vastu vijñāna pariṇāmāt anyaḥ eva tasya apariṇāmaḥ nāma bhavataḥ abhimataḥ bhāva antarasya eva abhāva tvena upagata tvāt tulya yogya tārūpasya eka jñāna saṃsargiṇaḥ eva ca anya vastunaḥ vijñānam tathā upeyam na anyasya tad jñānāt pratiyogi abhāva siddheḥ na hi rūpa jñānāt rasa ādya bhāva pratītiḥ yuktimatī deśa ādi viprakarṣavataḥ vā 
[190,ii^2]	anya vastu vijñānam ca pratiniyata rūparpati bhāsi eva rūpa antara avabhāsi tve hi tasya salila upalambha abhāvaḥ eva na sidhyet evam ca pratiyogi abhāvaḥ pratyakṣa avabhāsitaḥ eva tad abhāva vyavahāre tu asmad abhimatā eva anupalabdhiḥ āyātā iti pratipādayitum asya upanyāsaḥ tatra yadi salila upalambha abhāvaḥ tuccha rūpaḥ anupalambhaḥ tadā katham abhāvaḥ kasyacid pratipattiḥ paricchedaḥ iti yāvat paricchedasya jñāna dharma tvāt atha na tasya pratipatti rūpatā iṣyate kintu tad hetu bhāvaḥ iti atas āha pratipatti hetuḥ vā iti na hi sarva sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇasya abhāvasya pratipattim prati hetu bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ hetu bhāve vā tasya anapekṣita sahakāriṇaḥ nityam tat jñāna jana nādabhāva jñānam eva ekam pratipattuḥ syāt jñāna antarasya avakāśaḥ eva na bhavet 
[191,i^1]	na ca ajñātasya asya na astita ajñāna jananam yuktam iti āha tasya api salila upalambha abhāvasya katham pratipattiḥ atha ayam salila upalambha abhāvaḥ svayam apratītaḥ eva salila abhāva pratītim janayati tadā kasyacid api tat eva āha tasya salila upalambha abhāvasya tatas vā salilāt anyasya anala ādeḥ vijñānam vā anya vastuni iti atas ātmanaḥ apariṇāmasya pṛthak avasthāpanāt tatra api tad aṅgīkaraṇe ca ātmanaḥ apariṇāmasya tad ātmaka tvāt na tatas bhedena vyavasthāpya ita tatas ca kasyacid api tasya tad anyasya vā apratipattau api yadi abhāvaḥ salila ādeḥ pratīyate tadā svāpa ādi avasthāsu api salila ādi a bhāvaḥ kim na pratīyate tadā api tad abhāvaḥ pratīyeta iti etat vicāritam pramāṇa viniścaye tatas eva avadhāraṇīyam vyavadhāna ādi grahaṇena ca etat darśayati anya vastunaḥ api anya tvam tad tulya yogya tā ru upāpekṣam eva na tad anapekṣam upeyam 
[191,i^2]	tathā ca asmad upavarṇita anupalabdhi siddhiḥ iti yada ca evam uktena prakāreṇa anupalambhena salila abhāva pratītiḥ na yujyate anala pratibhāsinaḥ ca jñānasya pratiniyata ākāra tā na abhyupagamyate tasmāt ayam anala darśī pratipatta analam paśyan api saṅkīrṇa rūpa pratibhāsinā jñānena analaḥ ayam na salilam iti na adhyavasyati anadhyavasyan ca salila rūpasya api pratibhāsanāt tad arthī na tiṣṭhet pravarteta na api pratiṣṭheta salila arthī na pravarteta tathā hi salilam nāma tat ucyate yat sarva udanyā santāpa ādi apanayana kṣamam sakala tad anya rūpa asaṃkīrṇa pratiniyata ākāra jñāna avabhāsi idam tu anyat eva śabala rūpam kim api avabhāsate iti tatas ca pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ viruddhayoḥ yugapad anuṣṭhātum aśakya tvāt dustaram vyasanam pratipattuḥ syāt 
[192,i]	atra parasya vacana avakāśam āśaṅkayā āha tatas eva ityādi na mayā salila upalambha nivṛtti mātrāt tu ccha rūpāt tad abhāva gatiḥ ucyate yathā ukta doṣa prasaṅgāt kintu yat etat ekasya kevalasya analasya darśanam tatas eva anyasya tatra apratibhāsamānasya salilasya abhāva gatiḥ bhavati vijñānam vā anya vastuni iti vacanāt 
[192,ii^1]	siddhāntavādi āha katham ekam ityādi kena punar sāmarthyena tad eka darśanam anya abhāvam pratyāyayati tathā hi tasmin dṛśyamāne tat eva asti iti avagacchatu tat anyat tu na asti iti kim iti pratyeti iti tasya eva paridṛśyamānasya anala ādeḥ kevalasya salila asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya darśanāt anala jñāne pratibhāsanāt salilam na asti iti niścayaḥ san jāyate tathā hi analaḥ iva salilam api yadi tatra abhaviṣyat tat api anala vat darśane pratyaya bhāsiṣyata tayoḥ sva jñānam pratyaviśiṣṭa tvāt yogyatāyāḥ na ekasya pratibhāsaḥ yuktaḥ tasmāt eka pratibhāsanam anyā bhāvanā antarīyakam iti anya abhāve tatas jñānam utpadyate anya vastuni ca vijñānam na asti iti jñānam janayati 
[192,ii^2]	tathā anyat vasut para rūpa asaṃkīrṇa svabhāva tayā eva tathā ucyate tad rūpa tayā eva ca tat jñānam anyat pratiyat evam vyapadiśyate anyathā tad ayogāt iti anya pratipattiḥ eva tad abhāva vikalpa hetuḥ iti siddhāntavādi āha idam eva ityādi nanu asmābhiḥ idam eva prāk abhihitam tayoḥ satoḥ na eka rūpa niyatā pratipattiḥ asambhavāt iti ādibhiḥ vacanaiḥ tatas yat eva anya asaṃsargiṇaḥ kevalasya pratibhāsanam tat eva tad anya abhāvasya api tasya eva kevalasya tad anya abhāva ātmaka tvāt anyasya ca abhāva aṃśasya nirasta tvāt tatas pratyakṣa avabhāsita tvāt tad abhāvasya tabdalāt pāścātyam vyavahāra pravartana rūpam na astita ajñānam vikalpakam ājāyate 
[192,ii^3]	na tu tena apratipannam kiñcid avagamyate yatas tad anya vastuni vijñānam pratyakṣa ātmakam api anavagate tad anya abhāve jñānam janayat pṛthak abhāva pramāṇa tayā vyavasthāpyeta tathā hi tad anya ākāra śūnyaḥ eva tad eka jñāna ākāraḥ saṃvedyate tatas tad saṃvedanam eva tad abhāva saṃvedanam na hi vikalpa jñānasya api tad ākāra śūnya rūpa saṃvedanāt anyat tat abhāva saṃvedanam nāma kevalam asya vikalpa rūpa tā eva atiricyate tatas yathā nirvikalpa jñāna avasite kvacid anale analaḥ atra asti iti pāścātyaḥ vikalpaḥ vyavahāra pravartana mātram na tatas pṛthak pramāṇam yathoktam prāk tathā na astita ajñānam api vikalpakam tad phaṃla t vāreṇa vā anya vastu vijñānam na pratyakṣāt pṛthak abhāva ākhyam pramāṇam iti 
[192,ii^4]	tasmāt yat eva asmābhiḥ abhihitam tad anyā bhāva pratītim prati tat eva tvayā api abhidhīyate iti kasmāt paruṣam iva ābhāti yatas tad anabhyupagamena pṛthak abhāva ākhyam pramāṇam abhyupagatam iti upahasati tathā hi agatya idānīm tvayā ucyate na madhyastha tayā anyathā idam eva kim na pūrvam eva abhihitam yatas ālajālabhidhānena ātmā parikleśitaḥ iti upasaṃharan āha tasmāt tīrādarśinā iva ityādi yathā kila vahana ārūḍhaiḥ varṇigbhiḥ śakuniḥ mucyate api nāma tīram drakṣyati iti sa yadā sarvatas paryaṭan tīram na āsādayati tadā vahanam eva āgacchati tadvat etat api draṣṭavyam yatas ca avaśyabhyupagamanīyaḥ ayam pakṣaḥ tasmāt na kiñcid anayā vidyamāna pratiṣṭhā anayā diśaḥ pratipattyā prayojanam 
[193,i^1]	tat evam parasya anya bhāva tadabhāvayoḥ liṅga liṅgi bhāvam icchataḥ sambandha abhāvāt asau ayuktaḥ iti pratipādite pareṇa asati sambandhe anya bhāva gatyā api tad abhāva gatiḥ na syāt iti codite na vai kutaścid sambandhāt ityādi abhihitam atas anya bhāvaḥ eva tad abhāvaḥ anya bhāva gatiḥ eva ca tad abhāva gatiḥ iti prasādhayatā kumārila parikalpitaḥ kasyacid abhāva niścaya artham abhāva pramāṇa vādaḥ prasaṅgataḥ nirastaḥ samprati tu vastu asaṅkara siddhiḥ ca tad prāmāṇya samāśritāḥ iti etat āhatya nirākartum pūrva pakṣam utthāpayan āha yadi eka paricchedāt evaḥ ityādi 
[193,i^2]	yadi hi ekasya kevalasya paricchedāt anyasya vyavacchedaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ sidhyati tadā sarvasya anyasya aviśeṣeṇa eva tatra deśe yatra asau ekaḥ paridṛśyate tatra abhāva siddhiḥ bhavet na tu viśeṣa parigraheṇa tulyā sva jñāna jananam prati yogyā avasthā yasya tasya eva iti tathā hi asau yathā tulya yogya tā rūpa padārtha vivikta rūpaḥ upalabhyate tad eka ākāra pratiniyamāt tad jñānaḥ ca tathā tad atulya yogya tā rūpapadārtha vivikta tmakaḥ api tatas ca tad vivikta ākāra tayā tad anyā bhava sādhane viśeṣa abhāvāt pradeśa rūpa jñānam ghaṭābhavam iva rasa ādi abhāvam api sādhayet na vā ghaṭa abhāvam api iti 
[194,i^1]	kiñca yat etat upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ abhāva sādhanī iti viśeṣaṇam uktam tat ca na vaktavyam kim kāraṇam yatas ye api anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāḥ teṣām api tatra deśe tad eka ākāra tayā jñānasya vyavacchedaḥ bhavati eva tathā hi yathā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāḥ tat eka ākāravati jñāne na pratibhāsante tatas ca vyavacchidyante tathā anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāḥ api iti kim upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya iti anena viśeṣaṇena iti evam pūrva pakṣe vyavasthite yadi tad anya vyavacchedaḥ tatas pṛthak karaṇam anya tvena vyavasthāpanam abhimatam tat abhyupagamyate eva atha tad deśa kālayoḥ abhāvaḥ tat ayuktam yena hi sāmarthyena tulya yogya tārūpasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya ca abhāvam sādhayati na tad sāmarthyam atulya yogya tā rūpe anupalbdhi lakṣaṇa prāpte vā sambhavati tayoḥ satoḥ na eka rūpa niyatā pratipattiḥ asambhavāt iti evam hi tad abhāva sādhanam 
[194,i^2]	na ca etat anyatra sambhavati iti pratipādayitum eka ātma paricchedāt ityādinā upakramate yat puras avasthitam pratyakṣe avabhāsate tasya ekasya ātmanaḥ pratiniyatasya rūpasya paricchedāt tad ākāra utpattyā vidhi vikalpa utpādanena ca yaḥ tad anyaḥ tatas anyaḥ tadvayatiriktaḥ tasya sarvasya yaḥ ātmā svabhāvaḥ tatas vyavacchedaḥ bhedanam pṛthak karaṇam anya tva sādha nam asaṅkīrṇa rūpa tā pratyāyanam bhavati katham punar eka ātma paricchedāt eva tasya tad anya ātmanaḥ vyavacchedaḥ pratyakṣeṇa kriyate yāvatā pratyakṣam puras avasthita padārtha sāmarthya bhāvi tad rūpam eva pratipadyatām yat tu tadvayatiriktam aśeṣa padārtha jātam tad ātmanaḥ tasya puras avasthitasya katham tat vyavacchedakam atas tad vyavaccheda artham abhāva pramāṇam abhyupeyam yatas vastu asaṃkara siddhiḥ ca tad prāmāṇya samāśritāḥ iti 
[195,i]	atas āha tad ātma niyata pratibhāsa jñānāt iti yatas puras avasthitasya ekasya vastunaḥ para rūpa asaṃkīrṇaḥ ātmā sarva bhāvānām svabhāvataḥ eva sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ para rūpeṇa asaṃkīrṇa svabhāva tvāt anyathā katham abhāva pramāṇataḥ api asāṃkaryam eṣām sidhyet saṃkīrṇa rūpāṇām asāṅkarya sādhane tasya bhrānta tā prasaṅgāt tasmin para rūpa asaṃkīrṇe svabhāvataḥ eva tad ātma niyataḥ yaḥ pratibhāsaḥ para rūpa pratibhāsā saṃkīrṇaḥ tad eka padārtha sāmarthya bhāvini pratyakṣe para rūpa pratibhāsā yogāt tasya bhrānta tā āpattyā pratyakṣāta ahāneḥ tat uktam tad hayartha samarthyena utpadyamānam tad rūpam eva anukuryāt iti tasya tad ātma niyata pratibhāsaya jñānāt pratyakṣeṇa sva saṃvittyā saṃvedanāt tad saṃvedanam eva hi pratyakṣasya ātad rūpāt vyavacchedanam pṛthak karaṇam tabdalena eva ca pāścātyaḥ anya ātmakam etat na bhavati iti asāṃkarya vasthā pratyayaḥ vikalpakaḥ saṃjāyate gṛhīta grāhī na tena apūrvam kiñcid pratīyate para rūpa asaṃkīrṇasya ātmanaḥ pratyakṣeṇa eva tad ākāra anukāriṇā paricchedāt iti 
[195,ii]	yadi nāma tad ātma niyata pratibhāsa jñānam tathā api katham anya ātmanaḥ tasya pṛthak karaṇam iti atas āha na hi tad ātmaḥ ityādi yasmāt tasya vastunaḥ yaḥ ātmā para rūpa asaṃkīrṇaḥ sa tad anyasya śeṣasya vastunaḥ ātmā na bhavati sarvasya tatas anya svabhāva tvāt anyathā tad anyatva hāneḥ iti tasmāt tad ātma niyata pratibhāsa jñānam eva tad anyebhyaḥ nivartanam na hi jñānena arthaḥ haste gṛhītvā anyatas nivartanīyaḥ kevalam anya rūpa asaṃkīrṇasya ekasya ātmanaḥ anukaraṇam eva asya anyatas nivartanam ucyate iti atha anya ātmānaḥ sva viṣayam na nivartayet tadā asya viṣayasya anya ātmanaḥ sakāśāt avyavacchede pṛthak avyavasthāpane para ātmanaḥ api tatra paricchedaḥ syāt anyathā tad aparicchedasya eva eka ātma pariccheda ātmanaḥ tad nivartana rūpa tā syāt tatas ca avyavacchede anya ātmanaḥ tad pariccheda prasaṅgāt pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ abhāvaḥ iti pūrvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ na hi ayam analam paśyan api iti ādikaḥ 
[196,i^1]	na kevala manya ātmanaḥ tat nivartayati tad ātmanaḥ api aśeṣam anyat iti darśayan āha tam ca agratas sthitam deśa kāla svabhāva avasthā niyatam tad anya deśa ādibhyaḥ vyāvṛtta ātmanaḥ sva hetubhyaḥ eva asya bhāvāt tad ātmanā deśa ādi niyatena ātmanā tathāvidha svabhāvasya eva anukārāt upalabhamānā buddhiḥ tathā tva pracyutim anya deśa kāla svabhāva avastha tām asya sva viṣayasya vyavacchinatti tatas pṛthakkaroti kasmāt punar anya deśa āditām tatas pṛthak avasthāpayati iti atas āha evam hi yasmāt anya deśa ta ādeḥ tatas pṛthak karaṇe sati tad deśa ādi niyataḥ padārthaḥ paricchinnaḥ bhavati tad rūpasya eva anukārāt 
[196,i^2]	yadi anyathā bhāvaḥ anya deśa āditā tad rūpān anukārāt vyavacchinnaḥ bhavati tathātvam ca tad deśa ādi niyata tvam ca tadā tasya eva dṛśyamānasya bhavati na anyasya anya deśa ādimataḥ yatas evam iti tasmāt anyathā bhūtāt anya deśa ādimataḥ tathābhūtam tad deśa ādim aṃtam vyavacchindati eva nivartayanti eva tat paricchinatti iti pūrvakasya upasaṃhāraḥ tathā tathābhūtāt anyathābhūtam vyavacchindati eva iti dvitīyasya upasaṃhāraḥ kāryaḥ iti evam uktena nyāyena ekasya pramāṇasya pratyakṣasya anumānasya vā tasya api evam eva sva viṣaya paricchedāt vṛttiḥ pravṛttiḥ sarva bhāvān dvairāśye tattve anya tve ca vyavasthāpayati tatas tad paricchedaka pramāṇa balena eva āsāṅkarya siddhiḥ kim tad arthikayā api abhāva kalpanayā iti 
[197,i]	nanu ca vikalpa vyāpāraḥ eṣaḥ idam anya ātmakam na bhavati anyathā etat ātmakam iti pratyakṣam ca nirvikalpakam iṣyate tat katham asāṃkarya siddhiḥ tatas iti atas āha tasya anvaya ityādi tat hi pratyakṣam vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpau yadā sva viṣaye janayati tadā eva asya sāphalyam tadā eva ca pramāṇam iṣyate na anyadā atas eva ekasya artha svabhāvasya apratipanna aṃśa abhāvāt sarva ātmanā paricchede api bhrānti kāraṇa sadbhāvāt kṣaṇikatā ādau anvaya vyatirekabuddhī janayitum asāmarthyāt tatra asya prāmāṇyam na iṣyate iti 
[197,ii]	syāt matam dvairāśya sādhane api asāṃkarya siddhi arthā mā bhūt abhāva pramāṇa kalpanā kintu prakāra antara abhāva siddhi arthā bhaviṣyati na hi tad abhāva siddhau pratyakṣasya kaścid vyāpāraḥ pratipāditaḥ iti atas āha tad vyatiriktā ityādi tasmāt paridṛśyamānāt vyatiriktasya aśeṣasya vastunaḥ vyavacchedena tatas pṛthakkaraṇena anya tvena yā vyāptiḥ tad sādhanāt eva prakāra antarasya tattva anyatva bahis bhūtasya abhāvaḥ sidhyati tatas tad artham api na abhāva pramāṇa kalpanā yuktā iti 
[197,iii^1]	atha matam sarvasya aparidṛṣṭasya dṛśyamānāt anyatayā vyāptim na evam pratyakṣam sādhayati tat kutas tṛtīya rāśya bhāvaḥ pratyakṣatas eva syāt yatas abhāva prāmāṇya kalpanā vyarthā bhavet iti atas āha tasya tṛtīya rāśi tayā kalpyamānasya tatas dṛṣṭāt anya tayā vyāpti abhāve tena pratyakṣeṇa tatas arthāt sva viṣayasya avyavacchedāḥ dapṛthakkaraṇāt tad arthasya ca rāśi antara tvena kalpyamānasya sva viṣayāt avyavacchedāt apṛthak karaṇāt punar api bhāvasya sva viṣayasya apariccheda prasaṅgāt sa hi tad viṣayaḥ sakala para rūpa asaṃkīrṇa ātmā yadi tena ātmanā na paricchinnaḥ katham tena tasya paricchedaḥ 
[197,iii^2]	 tena ātmanā paricchede vā katham sarvasya tad anyatayā vyāpti asādhanam anyathā ekasya api tad anya tvam na syāt nimittasya samāna tvāt iti yatas evam tasmāt kvacid vastuni pramāṇam pratyakṣa ādikam pravṛttam tat vastu pratiniyatena ātmanā paricchinatti tatas anyat tad rūpa vikalam vyavacchinatti tad anyatvena vyavasthāpanāt tṛtīyasya ca tattva anyatva bahis bhūtasya prakārasya abhāvam sūcayati sarvasya anyatayā vyāpti sādhanāt tad viruddhasya vā sarva vastunaḥ dvaividhyasya sādhanāt iti 
[198,i^1]	evam ekasya pramāṇasya vyāpāraḥ eṣaḥ anantara uktaḥ iti tam eva upasaṃhṛtya sukha pratipattaye darśayan āha tathā hi kvacid vastuni pramāṇam pratyakṣa ādi pravṛttam tat eva vastu tad anyasmāt pārūpāt vyavacchinatti tatas pṛthakkaroti tad asaṃkīrṇa rūpa tayā pratipadyate paramārthataḥ tasya tad rūpa tvāt yathāvastu ca pratyakṣeṇa rūpa anukārāt kim iti para rūpāt vyavacchinatti tasya eva para rūpa vikalasya eka rūpasya paricchedāt tathā tat anyat eva ca tasmāt dṛśyamānāt anyat eva ca vyavacchinatti kutas tasmāt sva viṣayāt na kevalam sva viṣayam paratas vyavacchinatti param api sva viṣayāt iti 
[198,i^2]	kutas etat anyasya para rūpasya tatra kha ālambane aparicchedāt avaśyam eva aparicchinnasya paricchinnāt anya tvam bhavati yatas evam atas tat eva pramāṇam eka vastu paricchedakam prakāra antara abhāvam sādhayati na abhāva ākhyam kutas etat tasmim dṛśyamāne vastuni dṛṣṭa tad anya tvena tasya anyasya tatra aparicchidyamānasya anya tvam tad anya tvam dṛṣṭāt tad anya tvam dṛṣṭa tad anya tvam tena sarvasya tad vyatiriktasya vyavasthāpanena atad anyasya eva ca yat anyat na bhavati puras avasthitam sakala para bhāva vyāvṛttam tasya eva tattvena dṛśyamāna prakāra tayā vyavasthāpanāt iti 
[198,ii]	amum eva nyāyam anyatra api atidiśan āha etena kramākrama ādayaḥ ityādi etena anantara uktena nyāyena pratiniyata eka padārtha rūpa anukāriṇī buddhiḥ upajāyamānā tad viparīta rūpam sarvam sva viṣayāt vyavacchindatī dvairāśyam tṛtīya prakāra abhāvam ca sādhayati iti ye kecid anyonya vyaccheda rūpāḥ kramākrama nityān ityādayaḥ te vyākhyātāḥ tathā hi kāryasya kramam ananya sahāya tām pratiyati eva buddhiḥ tasya ākramam kārya antara sāhityam tatas pṛthakkaroti tatas krama ākrama tayā dvaita siddheḥ tṛtīyasya prakārasya sambhavaḥ nirastaḥ bhavati krama bhāva vyatirekiṇaḥ sarvasya kārya janmanaḥ tad anyatayā dvitīya prakāratayā avasthānāt evam udaya anantara dhvaṃsitā kṣaṇikatā ucyate iti pratīyatī vyavasthāpanā kālaḥ eva buddhiḥ tad viparīta rūpa tāyāḥ sva viṣayāt apākaraṇāt tatas anya tvena prakāra antare avasthāpanāt rāśi antara abhāvaḥ iti 
[199,i]	tat evam eka pramāṇa nibandha nāmasāṅkarya siddhim pratipādya upasaṃharan āha tat evam uktena nyāyena ekasya pratiniyata ātmanaḥ upalambhāt tasya upalabhyamānasya yaḥ tatas anyaḥ tad tulya yogya tā rūpaḥ tad viparītaḥ vā tad rūpa vikalaḥ tadā ātmanaḥ vyavacchedaḥ pṛthak karaṇam tasya upalabhyamānasya anupalabhyamāna svabhāvāt rūpa antareṇa pratibhāsanāt tathā tasya sva viṣayasya tad anya ātma tāyāḥ bhāva pradhāna tvāt nirddeśasya vyavacchedaḥ bhavati asāṅkaryam sidhyati 
[199,ii]	tat yadi etat aviśeṣeṇa anyasya sarvasya tat na abhāva siddhiḥ syāt iti atra abhimatam tadā siddha sādhanam yatas sarvam aviśeṣeṇa eva tad eka ākārayā budhyā tad rūpa vikalam sva viṣayāt avacchidyate sarvasya anya rūpasya tatra apratibhāsanāt atha tad deśa kālayoḥ abhāvaḥ sarvasya tad viparīta rūpasya vyavacchedaḥ abhimataḥ sa na yuktaḥ iti darśayati na tad deśa kālayoḥ yatra asau pratiniyata ātmā sakala trailokya vilakṣaṇaḥ padārthaḥ upalabhyate tatra sarvasya anyasya bhāvasya tad tulya yogya tā rūpasya itarasya vā vyavacchedaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ yena hi kāraṇena tad tulya yogya tā rūpasya tatra apratibhāsamānasya pratiṣedhaḥ tasmin sati tad eka rūpa niyatāyāḥ pratipatteḥ asaṃbhavāt tad abhāvanā antarīyikā sā bhāvantī tat pratiṣedham gamayati iti tad kāraṇam anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpte tad atulya yogya tā rūpe ca na sambhavati iti katham tad abhāvaḥ sidhyet 
[200,i]	etat eva upasaṃharan āha tasmāt atad ātmā ca sarvaḥ tad viparīta rūpaḥ tad eka ākārayā buddhyā prasādhitaḥ syāt tad deśa kālaḥ ca tasya pratibhāsamānasya yau deśa kālau tau yasya sa ca syāt kiṃvat rasa rūpa ādi vat iti na hi rūpa pratibhāsinā jñānena tad rūpa vikalasya rasasya sva viṣayāt pṛthakkaraṇe api tad asāṃkarya sādhane api tad deśa kālayoḥ abhāvaḥ sidhyati tatas ca katham sarvasya atulya yogyā avasthā asya api tatra abhāvaḥ syāt upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya iti viśeṣaṇam vā na ucyeta yatas evam tasmāt kvacid kadācid kasyacid abhāva siddhiḥ yathā uktāt eva anupalambhāt upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya tad tulya yogya tā rūpa upalambha ātmanaḥ ca iti evaṃrūpāt na tu sāmānyena yathā āhuḥ pare pramāṇa pañcakam yatra vastu rūpe na jāyate vastu sattā avabodha artham tatra abhāva pramāṇa tā iti 
[200,ii_200,iii]	na hi anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpte pramāṇa pañcaka apravṛttau api tad abhāvaḥ sidhyati sati api tasmin svabhāva ādi viprakarṣeṇa pramāṇa pañcaka apravṛtti sambhavāt iti tat evam prāsaṅgikam parisamāpayya yat uktam pareṇa saḥ eva anya bhāvaḥ tad viṣayā ca upalabdhiḥ tad abhāvasya kim na sādhanam iti tatra anya bhāvasya tad abhāvam prati liṅga tve niraste tad viṣayāyāḥ upalabdheḥ nirākurvan āha anya abhāva viṣaya ityādi yat punaruktam anya bhāva viṣaya upalabdhiḥ tad abhāvasya kin na sādhanam iti sā tad abhāvasya sādhika iṣṭā eva asmākam na tu liṅga tvena yathā uktavān asi kim kāraṇam yatas tatra api anya bhāva viṣayāyām upalabdha ava abhāvasya pṛthak anya bhāvāt sādhya tve kalpyamāne sambandha abhāvasya tad abhāvena tulya tvāt na hi tasyāḥ api anya bhāva rūpāyāḥ tad abhāvena kaścid ekārtha samavāya ādi rūpaḥ sambandhaḥ asti iti 
[200,iv^1]	apṛthak siddheḥ iti asya api tulya tām darśayan āha liṅga āvirbhāva ityādi yā iyam anya bhāva viṣayāḥ upalabdhiḥ lliṅgatayā ucyate tasyāḥ tad vivikta pradeśa ākārāyā avirbhāva kālaḥ eva janma kāle pratīti kālaḥ eva vā tad abhāva siddheḥ ca tathā hi tad pratibhāsa viviktānya bhāva pratibhāsa buddhi saṃvedanam eva tad abhāva saṃvedanam iti tat eva sādhayati na hi anyasya tad viviktasya bhāvam pratipadya pratipattā punar uttara kālam tad pratipatteḥ anya bhāva pratipatteḥ tad abhāvena anvaya vyatirekau prasādhya pratibandha sādhakena pramāṇena tad abhāvam pratipadyate kim tarhi tad anyam tad vivikta rūpam pratipadyamānaḥ eva tasya pratiyoginaḥ abhāvam pratipadyate tasya eva tad abhāva ātmaka tvāt 
[200,iv^2]	tathā hi sa ghaṭa pradeśa asaṃkīrṇa rūpasya kevala pradeśasya darśanam eva ghaṭa abhāva darśanam na hi ghaṭaḥ atra na asti ghaṭavān ayam na bhavati sa ghaṭāt anyaḥ iti artha bhedaḥ kaścid tatas sa ghaṭāt anyatayā kevala pradeśasya darśanam eva ghaṭa abhāva darśanam iti ghaṭaḥ atra na astī ti jñānam gṛhīta grāhitayā smṛtiḥ eva iti katham jñāyate iti ced darśana anantaram anvaya vyatireka sādhana lakṣaṇena vyavadhānena vinā idam ghaṭa viviktam pradeśavaḥ tu asti idam tu ghaṭavastu na asti iti pāścātyena vikalpa dvayena vyavasthāpanāt tatas na anvaya vyatireka anusaraṇam atra asti iti 
[201,i^1]	kiñca dṛṣṭānta asiddhe sva ātmani abhāva viṣaya upalabdhiḥ tad abhāvasya sādhanam tat eva vyatireka mukhena darśayati tat ca tasya ityādi iha api asti eva anvayaḥ iti ced āha na hi evam śakyam ityādi kasmāt na śakya darśayitum tad eka upalabdheḥ tasya ekasya ananya saṃsargiṇaḥ yā upalabdhiḥ viśeṣa rūpā tasyāḥ kvacid api anyatra abhāvāt atha tad vivikta upalabdhi sāmānyam hetuḥ ūcyate yatra yatra ghaṭa vivikta bhūta la upalabdhiḥ tatra tatra ghaṭa abhāvaḥ yathā pūrva anubhūte ghaṭa vivikte pradeśaḥ iti āha sāmānyena pradarśane kriyamāṇe dṛṣṭānte api pūrva anubhūta ghaṭa vivikte pradeśe ghaṭa abhāvasya prasādhakam pratyakṣa ādikam pramāṇa antaram anya bhāva viṣaya upalabdheḥ na asti kim tu sā eva tad anya bhāva upalabdhiḥ sādhya dharmasya tad abhāva lakṣaṇasya sādhikā sā ca yathā sādhya dharmiṇi tad abhāva siddhye dṛṣṭāntam apekṣate tathā dṛṣṭānte api 
[201,i^2]	tathā tatra api tat anyatra api iti anavasthā dṛṣṭāntānām iti anavasthāyām ca apratipattiḥ sarvatra tad abhāvasya yatas evam tasmāt na kutaścid liṅgāt tad anya bhāvāt tad upalabdheḥ vā tad abhāva siddhiḥ iti yadi tad anya bhāvaḥ tad abhāvam na sādhayati kim punar lliṅga tayā sādhayati iti atas āha saḥ anya bhāvaḥ pratyakṣa lakṣaṇena pratyakṣasya eva vivakṣita upalambhāt anya tvena anupalambha tvāt tad lakṣaṇena anupalambhena siddhaḥ sanna bhāva vyavahāram sādhayet karma stha kriyā apekṣāyām tad anya bhāvasya anupalabdhi rūpa tvāt kva punar asau abhāva vyavahāram sādhayet mūḍha pratipattau sādhyāyām yaḥ tu amūḍhaḥ viṣaya pratipattau viṣayiṇam smarati eva tasya abhāva vyavahāraḥ pratyakṣa nibandhanaḥ eva iti na tatra anupalabdheḥ liṅgatā iti sucarccitam eva anyatra iti iha alam prasaṅgena iti 
[202,i^1]	tat evam anupalabdheḥ aśeṣa vipratipatti nirākaraṇena sva rūpam avasthāpya prabheda nirddeśa artham āha sā iyam yathā uktā tridhā anupalabdhiḥ katham siddhe tad prasādhakena pramāṇena kārya kāraṇa bhāve sati kāraṇasya anupalabdhiḥ kīdṛśasya siddha abhāvasya tathā vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva siddhau satyām tad prasādhana pramāṇa balena eva siddhābhāvasya eva vyāpakasya na anyasya vyāpaka anupalabdheḥ eva asiddha tā prasaṅgāt yathā uktā svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ ca iti evam trividha anupalabdhiḥ katham punar kāraṇa vyāpa kayoḥ abhāva vyavahāraḥ sidhyati yatas tayoḥ siddha abhāva tā ucyate iti āha tatra kāraṇa vyāpakayoḥ api na kevalam yasya sākṣāt abhāva vyavahāraḥ sādhyate 
[202,i^2]	svabhāva anupalabdhau svabhāvasya asat vyavahārasya siddhiḥ anyasya tad viviktasya bhāva siddhiḥ yā sā eva asat vyavahāra siddhi hetu tvāt evam ucyate sa kāraṇa vyāpaka abhāvaḥ tathā asiddhaḥ anya bhāva siddhyā pratyakṣa rūpayā siddhaḥ abhāva vyavahāraḥ kārya vyāpyayoḥ pratiṣedhyayoḥ yadā anayoḥ virūpa viṣaya tayā sa viśeṣāṇām upalabdhiḥ na sidhyati tadā abhāvam abhāva vyavahāram vā sādhayati samuccaya arthaḥ vā śabdaḥ atha kim svabhāva anupalabdhau api abhāvaḥ liṅga tayā sādhyate iti āha svabhāva anupalabdhau tu ityādi abhāva vyavahāraḥ eva na abhāvaḥ api tasya pratyakṣa siddha tvāt 
[203,i^1]	atra parasya vacana avakāśam āśaṅkayā āha yadi tarhi kāraṇa vyāpakau siddhaḥ asat vyavahāraḥ yayoḥ tau santau kena tad anyasya kāraṇa vyāpaka viviktasya bhāvasya siddhiḥ yā pratyakṣa tmikā tad rūpayā anupalabdhyā anyasya kāryasya vyāpyasya vā abhāvam abhāva vyavahāram ca sādhayataḥ sā ca anya bhāva upalabdhiḥ tayoḥ kāraṇa vyāpakayoḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptau eva satyām asat vyavahārasya sādhikāḥ na anyathā iti evam iṣyamāṇe sati katham tayoḥ kāraṇa vyāpaka an upalabdhyoḥ parokṣe arthe viṣaye prayogaḥ 
[203,i^2]	yadā kārya svabhāva hetvoḥ vyatireka prayogaḥ kriyate yatra yatra agniḥ na asti tatra tatra dhūmaḥ api na asti tathā yatra yatra vṛkṣaḥ na asti kṣaṇikatā vā tatra tatra śiṃśapā na asti sattvam vā iti aśeṣa padārtha parigraheṇa vyatireka prayoge sati na hi tadā agni vṛkṣa vyatiriktāḥ sarve arthāḥ pratyakṣāḥ akṣaṇika tā vā tatas ca katham tad vivikta upalabdhi lakṣaṇa anupalabdhiḥ pratiyoginaḥ vā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tā siddhā tathā ca katham aśeṣa upasaṃhāreṇa vyāptyā kārya svabhāva hetvaḥ arvī atirekaḥ sidhyet tad asiddhau vā katham anayoḥ gamaka tvam tasmāt kvacid adarśana mātrāt eva vyatirekaḥ eṣṭavyaḥ kvacid ca darśana mātrāt anvayaḥ tathā ca pratibandha ghoṣaṇa anarthikā iti manyate paraḥ 
[203,ii^1]	siddhāntavādi āha na eva parokṣe arthe kāraṇa vyāpaka an upalabdhyoḥ prayogaḥ vyatireka upadarśana kāle pramāṇa tayā kāraṇasya vyāpakasya vā anupalabdhiḥ pramāṇa bhūtā na eva prayujyate kasmāt liṅgasya kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhi lakṣaṇasya tad abhāva lakṣaṇasya vā aniścayāt tad anupalabdhyoḥ sandeha rūpa tvāt tad abhāvasya ca sandigdha tvāt katham tarhi tadā anayoḥ prayogaḥ iṣyate iti āha kevalam ityādi kāraṇa vyāpakayoḥ hikārya kāraṇa bhāva prasādhakena pūrva uktena pramāṇena vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva sādhakena ca tad utpatti lakṣaṇe tādātmya lakṣaṇe ca sambandhe sādhite siddha sambandhayoḥ yadyabhāvaḥ yatra yatrā bhāvaḥ syāt parasya api kāryasya vyāpyasya vā avaśyam niyamena abhāvaḥ anyathā hetuka tva prasaṅgāt niḥsvabhāvatā prasaṅgāt ca 
[203,ii^2]	tad dvāreṇa pratibandha prasādhake pramāṇe smṛtiḥ katham nāma syāt iti etasya arthasya darśana artham ete kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhī prayujyete iti darśana adarśana balena tu sādhane yatra eva eka darśane paraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ adarśane vā na dṛṣṭaḥ tatra eva tasya bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ vā bhavatu sarvatra tu kasmāt bhavati na hi apratibaddha ātmanām gavāśu ādīnām kvacid tathā abhāva darśane api sarvatra tathā abhāvaḥ bhavati puruṣasya tu sarvadā kvacid eka bhāva abhāvayoḥ aparasya bhāva abhāva adarśanam yadṛcchā saṃvādaḥ sambhāvyeta asati pratibandhe tathā ca āha deśa ādi bheda adṛśyante bhinnāḥ dravyeṣu śaktayaḥ tatra eka dṛṣṭayā na anyatra yuktaḥ tad bhāva niścayaḥ iti 
[204,i]	tasmāt avaśyam pratibandhaḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ saḥ eva anvaya vyatireka prayogābhyām sucanīyaḥ na ca asau vyāptyā anvaya vyatireka upadarśanam antareṇa khyāpayitum śakyate iti yatra yatra iti sakala padārtha parigraheṇa khyāpyate pratibandhe hi pramāṇa siddhe satya vaśyam eva yatra yatra kāryam tatra tatra kāraṇam yatra yatra tad abhāvaḥ tatra tatra ca kāryasya api abhāvaḥ anyathā kāraṇam antareṇa kāryasya bhāve tasya ahetu tā eva syāt tatas ca nityam sattva ādi prasaṅgaḥ tathā yatra yatra yat svabhāvaḥ tatra tatra tad bhāvaḥ anyathā tasya nairātmyam eva syāt iti vyāptyā eva anvaya vyatireka upadarśane pratibandhaḥ khyāpayitum śakyate na anyathā iti prāk eva vistarataḥ vipañcitam 
[204,ii^1]	evam kārya svabhāva anupalabdhi lakṣaṇe eva pakṣa dharme tad sādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāvāt anvaya vi atireka sadbhāvaḥ na anyatra iti pratipādya upasaṃharan āha iti eṣaḥ eva svabhāva kārya anupalabdhi lakṣaṇaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ anvaya vyatirekavān pratibandha sadbhāvāt yataśva anvaya vyatirekavān pratibandha prasādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāvāt uktena nyāyena iti tasmāt tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ anvaya vyatireka niścayena eva tad aṃśa vyāpteḥ niścayāt yathoktam prāk tatas ca tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanāt tri lakṣaṇaḥ eva trirūpaḥ eva trividhaḥ eva hetuḥ gamakaḥ na anya lakṣaṇaḥ anyaḥ vā yathā ukta trairūpya sadbhāve rūpa antarasya vaiyarthyāt yathā ukta trairūpya abhāve ca rūpa antara kalpanāyām api avyabhicāra abhāvena āgamaka tvāt 
[204,ii^2]	kasmāt tri lakṣaṇaḥ eva trividhaḥ eva hetuḥ gamakaḥ na anya lakṣaṇaḥ anyaḥ vā iti darśayati sva sādhya dharma avyabhicārāt iti tri lakṣaṇasya eva sva sādhya dharma avyabhicārāt sva sādhya dharma avyabhicāraḥ eva ca gamaka tvam iti rūpa antara kalpanā vyarthā pratibandha nibandhana anvaya vyatireka apagame ca rūpa antara kalpanāyām api sva sādhya dharma avyabhicāra abhāvāt tat anena tridhā eva saḥ iti asya tri lakṣaṇaḥ eva sa hetuḥ avinā abhāvasya sva sādhya dharma avyabhicārasya niyamāt avaśyantayā sadbhāvāt pratibandha nimitta tad aṃśa vyāpti anabhyupagame ca rūpa antara kalpanāyām api hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare yathā ukta tri lakṣaṇāt apare rūpa antara yogi tayā vikalpyamānā hetvābhāsāḥ avinā abhāvasya sva sādhya dharma avyabhicārasya teṣu abhāvāt iti aparaḥ arthaḥ darśitaḥ iti 
[205,i^1]	yat uktam tri lakṣaṇaḥ eva hetuḥ na anya lakṣaṇaḥ iti tatra pareṣām vipratipattim darśayan āha ṣaṣ lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ iti apare naiyāyika mimāṃsaka ādayaḥ manyante kāni punar ṣaṣ rūpāṇi hetoḥ taiḥ iṣyaṃte iti āha trīṇi ca etāni pakṣa dharma anvaya vyatireka ākhyāni tathā ābādhita viṣaya tvam caturtham rūpam abādhitaḥ pramāṇena anirākṛtaḥ viṣayaḥ sādhya dharma lakṣaṇaḥ yasya sa tathā uktaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam aparam rūpam tathā vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvam rūpa antaram ekā saṃkhyā yasya hetu dravyasya tat eka saṃkhyam vivakṣitam eka saṃkhyam hetu dravyam āśraya tvena yasya hetu sāmānyasya tad vivakṣita eka saṃkhyam tad bhāvaḥ aparam rūpam 
[205,i^2]	yadi eka saṃkhyā vyāvacchinnāyām pratihetuḥ ahitāyām hetu vyaktau hetu tvam bhavati tadā gamaka tvam na tu pratihetu sahitāyām api dvi saṃkhyā yuktāyām iti yadi viruddha avyabhicārya param hetu antaram na upadarśyate iti yāvat tathā jñāta tvam ca jñāna viṣaya tvam ca na hi ajñātaḥ hetuḥ sva sattā mātreṇa gamakaḥ yuktaḥ iti tatra eteṣu rūpa antareṣu yat etabādhita viṣaya tvam nāma tat tāvat pratibandha nibandhana anvaya vyatireka ātmakā vinā abhau a sambhave sati tatas pṛthak anyat lakṣaṇam na bhavati 
[205,i^3]	tad ātmakam tu tat vacanena eva uktam iti na vaktavyam iti kasmāt pṛthak lakṣaṇam na bhavati bādhāyāḥ avinā abhāvasya ca virodhāt iti tathā hi sati api avinā abhāve yathā ukte bādhā sambhavam manyamānaiḥ abādhita viṣaya tvam rūpa antaram ucyate sā ca iyam tad sambhāvanā na sambhavati bādhāyāḥ avinā abhāvena virodhāt saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇāt tam eva virodham sādhayan āha avinā abhāvaḥ hi ityādi sati eva hi sādhya dharme bhāvaḥ hetoḥ avinābhāvaḥ ucyate pramāṇa bādhā tu tasmin asati yadi hi sati eva tasmin tad abhāva viṣayam pramāṇam pravarteta tadā asya bhrānta tvāt apramāṇa tā eva syāt iti kutas bādhā tatas sa hetuḥ tad lakṣaṇaḥ sādhya avinā bhāvī dharmiṇi syāt atra ca sādhya dharmaḥ katham na bhavet yatas bādha avakāśaḥ syāt tasmāt avinābhāvasya pramāṇa bādhāyāḥ ca saha anavasthānam avinā abhāvena upasthāpitasya dharmiṇi sādhya dharma bhāvasya pramāṇa bādha upasthāpitasya ca tad abhāvasya paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇa tayā virodhena ekatra dharmiṇī a sambhavāt iti 
[206,i]	tam eva virodham spaṣṭīkartum para upahāsa vyājena āha pratyakṣa anumāne hi ityādi sādhya dharmam hi bādhamāne pratyakṣa anumāne tam grīvāyām gṛhītvā dharmiṇaḥ sva āśrayāt niṣkāsayataḥ tasmin ca sādhya dharme sati eva tad avinā bhāvi tvāt hetuḥ bhavam stam sādhya dharmam niṣkāsyamānam gale gṛhītvā haṭhāt tatra eva dharmiṇī avasthāpayati iti param prakṛṣṭam bata bhāvānām sādhya dharma lakṣaṇānām asvāsthyam vartate tathā hi yantra dvaya niyantritānām nirucchāvasitayā maraṇam eva prāptam iti 
[207,i]	paraḥ bādhā vinā bhāvayoḥ viṣaya bhedāt avirodham darśayan āha anyatra sādhya dharmiṇam parihṛtya dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sādhya dharmeṇa avinābhāvī hetuḥ na punar sādhya dharmiṇī eva tatas kutas bādhā vinā bhāvayoḥ virodhaḥ anyatra bādhayā sādhya dharma abhāva sādhanāt anyatra ca hetunā tad bhāva sādhanāt tathā ca evaṃvidhe sati api avinā abhāve bādhā sambhavāt abādhita viṣaya tvasya rūpa antarasya sambhavaḥ iti 
[207,ii]	evaṃvidhāvinā abhāva upagame sati api abādhita viṣaya tva ādike rūpa antare hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare rūpa antara sambhavinaḥ iti āpāditām hetvābhāsa tām vivarītum para upahāsa pūrvakam āha tat kim ayam sādhya dharmī tapasvī varākaḥ śaṇḍham udvāhya tasmin sādhya dharma sādhana śakti vikalam hetum pariṇāyya sādhya dharma lakṣaṇam putram mṛgayate etat eva vyanakti yasya hetoḥ ddharmiṇī asati api sādhya dharme bhāvaḥ iṣyate sādhya dharmiṇaḥ anyatra āvinābhāva upagamāt tam tathāvidham sādhya dharmiṇī upadarśya katham dharmī sādhya dharmavān iti ucyate na hi ambhaḥ tu asya samudre lavaṇa tvena avinā abhāve api tad vyatirikte ambhasi lavaṇa tayā sādhya tvena iṣṭe ambhaḥ tu abhāve api lavaṇa tva siddhiḥ iti 
[207,iii]	parasya vacana avakāśam āśaṅkayā āha atas eva ityādi etat eva vivṛṇoti syāt etat bhavataḥ matam yatas eva hetuḥ anyathā api sādhya dharmam antareṇa api dharmiṇi bhavet ambhaḥ tu ādiṣu tathā adarśanāt sādhya dharmi parihāreṇa cāvinā abhāva upagamāt atas eva kāraṇāt pramāṇābhyām abādhita dharmāḥ dharmī iti ucyate yadi pratyakṣa anumānābhyām sādhya dharmiṇi hetoḥ viṣayaḥ sādhya dharmaḥ na bādhyate yathā ambhaḥ tu asya lavaṇa tvam tadā tasya gamaka tvam na anyathā iti tatas anyatra avinābhāva mātreṇa sādhya siddheḥ anabhyupagamāt na yathā uktaḥ doṣaḥ iti 
[208,i^1]	siddhāntavādi āha tat kim idānīm yadā hetoḥ dharmiṇya vinā bhāvita anabhyupagamāt sādhya siddheḥ abhāvāt tad siddhaye rūpa antaram abādhita viṣaya tvam ucyate tadā hetoḥ na kiñcid sāmarthyam kasmāt abādhayā eva hetum antareṇa api sādhya siddheḥ akiñcitkaraḥ eva hetuḥ tathā hi atra kalpanā dvayam bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttau sādhya abhāvaḥ niyataḥ vā syāt aniyataḥ vā tatra yadi pūrvaḥ vikalpaḥ tadā sādhya abhāvaḥ hi bādhaka pramāṇasya vṛttau niyataḥ tadā eva bhāvāt tad abhāve ca abhāvāt iti tasmāt abādhāyām bādhaka pramāṇa vṛtti abhāve tat niyatasya sādhya abhāvasya api abhāvāt sādhya siddhiḥ bhavati eva iti vyarthaḥ eva hetuḥ iti na upanyasanīyaḥ eva 
[208,i^2]	tatas kasya ābādhita viṣaya tvam rūpa antaram bhavet syāt matam mā bhud bādhaka pramāṇa vṛtti abhāve hetoḥ sāmarthyam yadā tu sādhyasya bādhakam pramāṇam dharmiṇi vartate tadā hetoḥ sādhya sādhane sāmarthyam bhaviṣyati iti atas āha bādhāyām api iti yadi bādhakam pramāṇam vartate tadā tena sādhya abhāvasya dharmiṇi sādhanāt punar brahmaṇā api tad bhāvasya kartum aśakyatvāt kim aṅga punar śaṭhena hetunā iti kutas sādhanasya hetoḥ sāmarthyam atas eva hi bhavadbhiḥ abādhita viṣaya tvam rūpa antaram ucyate iti 
[208,ii]	atha bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttau sādhya abhāvaḥ na niyataḥ tad abhāve api bhāvāt iti dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ iṣyate tadā api abādhāyāḥ sāmarthya virahaḥ iti darśayan āha aniyame bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttau sādhya abhāvasya iṣyamāṇe sati idam āpatitam na ca bādhakam pramāṇam syāt sādhya abhāvasya ca sambhavaḥ iti na sādhya sādhane sāmarthyam abādhāyāḥ satyām api tasyām sādhya abhāvasya sambhavāt iti tad yoginaḥ api hetvābhāsa tā eva iti 
[209,i_209,ii]	yat uktam abādhayā eva sādhya siddheḥ vyarthaḥ hetuḥ iti tatra anyathā artham abādhāyāḥ darśayan hetu sāmarthyam pratipādayan āha paraḥ na bādhāyāḥ abhāvaḥ mama ābādha abhimatā kim tarhi bādhāyāḥ anupalabdhiḥ sā ca tad anupalabdhiḥ puruṣasya śakti vaikalyāt kvacid deśa ādau bādhāyāḥ sambhave api syāt tatas bādhā anupalabdhi mātreṇa sādhya siddheḥ abhāvāt tad siddhaye avaśyam hetuḥ abhidhānīyaḥ iti sa hetu prayogasya viṣayaḥ tadā hi hetuḥ sva sādhyam sādhayan katham asamarthaḥ syāt iti siddhāntavādi āha kim nu vai hetuḥ bbādhāyāḥ yā upalabdhiḥ tasyāḥ vibheti na punar bbādhāyāḥ yena bādhām sambhavantīm api anādṛtya tad anupalabdhau satyām prayoktavyaḥ iṣṭaḥ bhavataḥ 
[209,iii^1]	kadācid paraḥ brūyāt kim kariṣyati vidyamānā api bādhā tapasvinī tad upalabdhiḥ eva rākṣasī tasmāt tatas eva hetoḥ bhayam tad abhāve hetuḥ prayoktavyaḥ eva iti atas āha sa tarhi ityādi evam tarhi parama arthena bādhā kim asti na asti iti etat anapekṣya bādhāyāḥ anupalabdhau satyām prayoktavyaḥ iti kā akvā pṛcchati kadācid paraḥ brūyāt uktam eva etat kim artham pṛcchyate iti āha kimartham prayujyate iti bādha anupalambhe api tad sambhave sādhya sādhana ayogāt iti abhiprāyaḥ paraḥ anavagata abhiprāyaḥ āha sādhya siddhi artham iti bādhaka pratyaya abhāve pramāṇi asya iṣṭa tvāt tatas sādhya siddhiḥ aviruddhā eva iti manyate 
[209,iii^2]	siddhānta vādī satyām bādhāyām tad anupalambhe api sādhya siddhim asambhāvayan pṛcchati sa kim kvacid ityādi kim punar asau hetuḥ satyām api bādhāyām sādhyam sādhayet iti sambhāvyate bhavatā yena asyāḥ bādhāyāḥ abhāva niścayam prati yatnaḥ na kriyate hetuḥ ca prayujyate iti evam etat iti ced tathā satyām api bādhāyām sādhya sādhana sāmartha upagame satya bādhita viṣaya tvam hetu lakṣaṇam na bhavati kim kāraṇam bādhāyām api satya ām asya hetoḥ sāmarthyāt sāmarthya upagamāt tat hi hetoḥ lakṣaṇam ucyate yena vinā sādhyam na sādhayet iti 
[210,i]	syāt matam anupalabhyamāna bādha tvam hetu lakṣaṇam parama arthena na ābādhita viṣaya tvam iti atas āha tathā ca ityādi evam hi sati bādhāyāḥ sadbhāva sambhave api tām abhyupagamya tad anupalambha mātreṇa hetoḥ prayogaḥ prāptaḥ yadi hi bādhām abhyupagamya hetu prayogaḥ na abhimataḥ syāt tadā anupalambha mātreṇa bādhāyam saṃśayāt satām api keṣāñcid kathañcid anupalambha sambhavāt saṃśayitasya hetu prayoge pravṛttiḥ eva na yujyeta tasmāt yaḥ yat saṃśaye api pravartate sa tasya bhāva pakṣam abhyupetya eva pravartate tathā ca yathā bādha anupalabdhau tām abhyupagamya hetuḥ prayujyate tathā tad upalabdhau api prayujyatām bādhāyāḥ sadbhāva abhyupagame sati tad upalambha anupalambhayoḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt iti na anupalabhyamāna bādha tvam api hetu lakṣaṇam yujyate iti kutas bādhaka pratyaya virahe api asati pratibandhe prāmāṇyasya sambhavaḥ iti 
[210,ii^1]	parasya vacana avakāśam āśaṅkayā āha na bādhāyām ityādi na eva hi bādhāyām saṃtyām hetoḥ sāmarthyam iṣyate tat katham tad upalambhe api prayogaḥ syāt siddhāntavādi āha yadi evam bādhāyām satyām hetuḥ asamarthaḥ yadi iṣyate tadā anirṇītaḥ bādhāyāḥ asaṃbhavaḥ yasya hetoḥ sa tathāvidhaḥ prayogam bādha anupalambha mātreṇa na arhati kim kāraṇam mā bhūt bādhāyāḥ sambhava pakṣe prayuktasya api hetoḥ sādhya siddhau asāmarthyam iti pūrva pakṣa vādī āha bādha anupalambhe sati bādhāyāḥ abhāvāt sat upalambhaka pratyaya abhāve satya vaśyam arthānām asattvāt hetoḥ sāmarthyam iti ced manyase siddhāntavādi āha kim upalambhaḥ bādhām ityādi 
[210,ii^2]	upalambhaḥ hi arthānām kāryam na ca kāryam kāraṇam vyāpnoti na hi aavaśyam kāraṇāni kāryavanti bhavanti pratibandha vaikalya sambhavāt tat katham avyāpakasya upalambhasya nivṛttau bādhāyāḥ nivṛttiḥ yatas hetoḥ bbādhāyāḥ sambhava kṛtam asāmarthyam na sambhavet iti etat ca paraiḥ apīṣyate eva pramāṇa tayā upagatasya api udaya kāle anupalabdha bādhasya kāla antareṇa bādhaka pratyaya utpāde satya prāmāṇya upagamāt atha avyāpakasya api upalambhasya nivṛttau bādhā nivartate nivartate hi mithyātvam doṣa ajñānāt ayatnataḥ 
[211,i_211,ii]	iti anena eva nyāyena jñāna nivṛttyā bādhā nivṛtteḥ iti āha ta thā api vyarthaḥ hetuḥ kutas bādha anupalambhāt eva hetu prayoga rahitāt sādhya siddheḥ kim kāraṇam anupalambhe bādhāyāḥ asambhavāt tathā hi yatra bādhāyāḥ anupalambhaḥ tatra paramārthataḥ eva sā na vidyate iti manyase yatra ca asau paramārthataḥ na asti tatra sādhya dharmasya abhāvaḥ api parama arthena eva na asti anyathā parama arthena bādhāyāḥ abhāva ayogāt tatas ca sādhya dharmasya abhāva abhāve sati bhāvaḥ iti bhavat matyā sādhya pratīteḥ vyarthatā hetoḥ iti atha mā bhūt yukti virodhaḥ iti na upalambha nivṛttau bādhā nivṛttiḥ iṣyate tatra āha upalambhasya nivṛttau api satyām bādhāyāḥ anivṛtta aviṣyamāṇāyām tad avastham heta urasa sāmarthyam yat avastham bādha upalambhaḥ iti hetoḥ aprayogaḥ iti kasya ābādhita viṣaya tvam rūpa antaram syāt 
[211,iii]	etat eva upasaṃharan āha tasmāt sva sādhyaḥ ityādi yatas evam vyāptyā hetoḥ sarvatra sādhyena avinā abhāva abhyupagame bahis vyāpta aviṣyamāṇāyām vaiyarthyam hetu prayogasya āpadyate tasmāt sva sādhya bhāva abhāvābhyām anyathā api svasādhya bhāve api abhavat na abhāve api ca bhavan hetuḥ dharmiṇi kiñcid sādhyam na bhāvayati na sādhayati na vibhāvayati tad viparītam na niṣedhayati iti tasya vidhi pratiṣedhau akurvataḥ upakṣepaḥ prayogaḥ na samarthaḥ iti avaśyam hetu prayogam icchatā sva sādhya avinābhāvaḥ sarvatra hetoḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ sa ca pratibandha nibandhanaḥ eṣa ca darśana adarśana mātra yattaḥ yathoktam prāk tasmin ca abhyupagate bādhāvinā bhāvayoḥ virodhaḥ siddhaḥ iti upasaṃharan āha tat naḥ ityādi yatas evam tena kāraṇena ābādhā rūpa antaram na bhavati 
[211,iv^1]	yadi nāma bādhāvinā abhāvayoḥ saha avasthāna abhāva āt avinā abhāve satyabādhā gamyate rūpa antaram tu kim iti na bhavati iti atas āha tad nāmaḥ ityādi tat hi tasmāt viśeṣaṇa antaram bhavet vastu sthityā lakṣaṇa kāraiḥ ca rūpa antara tvena upādānam arhati yasya viśeṣaṇasya bhāve api yasya aparasya abhāvaḥ syāt yatas sambhave vyabhicāre ca viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ na sambhavaḥ eva kevale udāharaṇam āha tat yathā ityādi sati api hi dharmi sambandhe śrāvaṇa tva ādeḥ sa pakṣe bhāvaḥ na asti sati api ca cākṣuṣa tva ādeḥ sa pakṣe bhāve sādhya dharmiṇi śabde sambandhaḥ na asti tatas anayoḥ sambhava vyabhicārayoḥ bhāvāt viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ lakṣaṇa antara tvena ca upādānam iha api evam bhaviṣyati iti ced āha na ca etat anantara uditam abādhāyāḥ avinā abhāve sati sambhavati 
[211,iv^2]	satya vinābhāve niyamena ābādhāyāḥ sambhavāt vyabhicāra abhāvāt kutas viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ kṣaṇa antara tvena ca upādānam arhati iti na hetoḥ sādhyāvinābhāvinaḥ viruddhasya ca sādhya viparyaya avinābhāvinaḥ viṣaye bādhā sambhavati uktena prakāreṇa viparyaye samyak hetuḥ eva aviṣaye tu prayogāt hetu ābhāsaḥ ucyate yatas evam iti tasmāt na tad abhāvaḥ bādhā virahaḥ pṛthak avinā bhāvāt anvayavi atireka ātmanaḥ anayoḥ hetu viruddhayoḥ lakṣaṇa antara tvena vācyaḥ vyabhicāra abhāvena rūpa antara tva ayogāt yatas ca āvinā abhāve sati bādhā na sambhavati virodhāt tasmāt hetoḥ yathā ukta lakṣaṇasya prayoge sati gamya arthāyāḥ api pratijñāyāḥ doṣāṇām pratyakṣa viruddha ādīnām sambhavaḥ na asti hetu lakṣaṇena eva teṣām nirasta tvāt tat katham bādhā virahaḥ hetoḥ rūpa antaram ucyate asambhavinām ca teṣām upavarṇanam niṣphalam iti ākūtam 
[212,i]	kevalāyāḥ prayoge asti sambhavaḥ iti ced āha na api ityādi hetu prayoge hi asati kevalā pratijñā eva na prayujyate hetu viṣaya tvena tad abhyupagamāt tatas ca śāstra kāraiḥ na pratijñā doṣāḥ pratyakṣa viruddha ādayaḥ vācyāḥ iti diṅnāga pādaiḥ tu sādhya asādhya viparyayeṇa vipratipatti darśanāt aprayoga arhasya api pakṣasya lakṣaṇa vidhāne nyāya prāptam eva apakṣa tvam nirākṛta padena pramāṇa viruddhasya ākhyānam na tu ati prasaktam pakṣa lakṣaṇam vyavacchinnam sandigdhasya eva sādhya tvāt pramāṇa bādhite sādhaka pramāṇa āvṛtteiḥ iti 
[213,i_213,ii]	tat evam abādhita viṣaya tvam nirākṛtya rūpa antaram nirākurvan āha etena avinā abhāve sati bādhāyāḥ asambhava darśanena eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā api viruddha avyabhicāri doṣa vipakṣeṇa ucyamānā pratyuktā pratyākhyātā paraḥ pṛcchati katham iti kena prakāreṇa yathā bādhāvinā abhāvayoḥ saha anavasthānam tathā pratihetu avinā abhāvayoḥ api yena eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā tadvat eva pratyākhyāyeta iti 
[213,iii]	siddhānta vādī sāmyam darśayan āha ekaḥ ityādi ekaḥ hi hetuḥ lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ sva sādhya avyabhicārī katham bhavati yadi sva sādhya bhāvaḥ eva bhavet anyathā tat lakṣaṇam avinābhāvaḥ nāma hīyeta yatra eva dharmiṇi sa tad lakṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ bhavati tatra eva dharmiṇi tasmāt anyaḥ api pratihetuḥ viruddhaḥ tena hetu lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ katham bhavati ekasya hetoḥ yat sādhyam tabda adhakasya tat viruddhasya aparasya dharmasya bhāvaḥ eva na abhāve bhāva ādavinā abhāvāt iti bādhayā samānam bādhā sambhavena samānaḥ pratihetuḥ iti tad nirāsena eva nirastaḥ iti 
[213,iv]	atra eva dūṣaṇa antaram abhidhātum vikalpayan āha api ca ityādi vastutas paramārthataḥ yasya pratihetuḥ na sambhavati kim asau samyak jñānasya viparyasya vā upanyasta sādhya viparīta jñānasya vā hetuḥ iṣṭaḥ yatas vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvam tad lakṣaṇam ucyate āhosvit yasya pratihetuḥ tad sādhya viparīta sādhakaḥ na pradarśitaḥ paramārthataḥ san api iti paraḥ doṣam apaśyan āha kiñca atas ityādi yadi nāma purvaḥ vikalpaḥ uttaraḥ vā tatas kaḥ doṣaḥ iti 
[214,i]	siddhāntavādi āha yadi asambhavan pratihetuḥ yasya sa samyak jñāna ādi hetuḥ iṣyate tadā alakṣaṇam etat vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvam kasmāt aśakyaḥ niścayaḥ yasya vastutas asambhavat pratihetutvasya sa tathā uktaḥ parama tāpekṣayā ca etat ucyate paraḥ hi darśana adarśanābhyām asati api pratibandhe avinā abhāvam icchati tatas tasya pratihetoḥ evaṃvidhasya sambhavaḥ asti sa ca anupalabhyamānaḥ api kadācid syāt iti vastutas tad abhāvaḥ niścīyate pratibandha nibandhanāvinā abhāva vādinām tu asmākam pratihetu asambhavaḥ su niścitaḥ eva na hi tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇe pratibandhe pramāṇataḥ siddhe tad nimitta avinā bhāvitayā ekena hetunā sva sādhye sādhite punar tatra eva dharmiṇi tad lakṣaṇasya tad viruddha artha sādhakasya pratihetoḥ sambhavaḥ śaṅkayate bhāvānām viruddha svabhāva dvaya ayogāt viruddha dharma adhyāsasya bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt viruddha dharma sādhaka sambhave ca tasya eva sva sādhya avinābhāvinaḥ prathamasya tatra pramāṇataḥ bhāva siddhaya yogāt iti 
[214,ii]	syāt matam yadi nāma prastutaḥ pratihetu asambhavaḥ asmābhiḥ niścetum aśakyaḥ tathā api asambhavat pratihetu tvam vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tva pratipāditam hetu lakṣaṇam kasmāt na bhavati iti āha na hi aniścita ātmanaḥ ityādi pratipādakaḥ yaḥ dharmaḥ hetoḥ tasya aniścita svabhāvasya yasmāt tad lakṣaṇa tvam pratipādaka dharma tā na bhavati yathā saṃdigdhasya pakṣa dharma tvasya iti pūrvakasya sādhanam na api sandhigdham lakṣaṇam yasya sa hetuḥ bhavati iti na kaścid hetuḥ bhavet iti hetu abhāvaḥ vai iti asya samarthanam tatas ca hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare iti atra api yojitam iti 
[214,iii]	syāt matam yasya pratiyogī dṛśyate tasya eva pratihetu bhāvāt ahetu tvam bhavatu yasya tu pratiyogī hetuḥ na dṛśyate sa vastutas eva asambhavat pratihetuḥ na hi tatra vastutas pratihetusambhavaḥ śaṅkayate bādhaka pratyayam antareṇa bādhā śaṅkāyāḥ ayogāt tat uktam bādhā jñāne tu anutpanne na āśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikāḥ iti 
[215,i^1]	atra āha tulye lakṣaṇe hi ityādi śaṅkayamāna pratihetunā tulyam lakṣaṇam darśana adarśana mātra nimitta avinā bhāva rūpam yasya tasmin dṛṣṭaḥ pratiyoginaḥ pratiheta urbbādhakasya sambhavaḥ sa yeṣām api tad tulya lakṣaṇānām pratiyogī na dṛśyate teṣu api śaṅkām pratihetu sambhava viṣayām utpādayati kim kāraṇam adṛṣṭa pratiyoginaḥ dṛṣṭa pratiyoginaḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt na hi tasya itareṇa kaścid viśeṣaḥ asti yatas tad sambhavaḥ na śaṅkayeta pruṣa śakti vaikalya ādinā tu tad adarśanam sambhāvyeta iti kim ucyate na āśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikāḥ iti atha viśeṣaḥ pratibandha lakṣaṇaḥ avinā abhāva niścāyakaḥ dṛṣṭa pratihetoḥ adṛṣṭa pratiyoginaḥ iṣyate yatas pratiyogi sambhava āśaṅkāḥ tam upaiti 
[215,i^2]	tadā sati vā viśeṣe sa viśeṣaḥ hetoḥ lakṣaṇam kim kāraṇam yatas tatas viśeṣāt hetuḥ ekāntena niścayena nirasta pratipakṣaḥ tathāvidhe dharmiṇi pratihetu asambhavāt sva sādhyam niścāyayati iti yaḥ tathāvidhaḥ na bhavati tad viśeṣa virahāt dṛṣṭa pratihetuḥ saḥ atad lakṣaṇaḥ na hetuḥ syāt tathā ca yadi nāma ahetau pratihetuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ hetoḥ kim āyātam yena tad nivṛttaye tatra eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā kriyate yathā ukta āvinā bhāva vacanena eva tad nivṛtteḥ iti āha tathā ca hetau tad viśeṣa yogini pratihetu asambhave sati vyarthāḥ niṣprayojanāḥ eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā iti yathā ukta viśeṣa aṅgīkarane tad lakṣaṇasya pratihetoḥ asambhavāt kasya eka saṃkhyā vivakṣayā vyavacchedaḥ kriyate yatas asya sārthaka tvam syāt iti 
[215,ii]	viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ ca hetvābhāsasya vyavaccheda artham eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā hetu lakṣaṇe kriyate vastutas asambhavat pratihetu tva siddhaye ca pratibandha lakṣaṇe viśeṣe hetā viṣyamāṇe viruddha avyabhicārī api hetvābhāsaḥ na bhavati tatas vyavacchedya abhāvāt kim eka saṃkhyā vivakṣayā iti darśayan āha atas pratibandha lakṣaṇa viśeṣa upagamāt viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ hetvābhāsasya yat lakṣaṇam tat hīyeta na sambhavet kim punar tad viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ lakṣaṇam iti āha sva lakṣaṇaḥ ityādi hetoḥ yat ātmīyam lakṣaṇam tad yuktayoḥ hetvoḥ ekatra dharmiṇi virodhena paraspara viruddha sādhya sādhaka tvena upanipāte sati viruddha avyabhicārī iti viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ lakṣaṇam na ca tat pratibandha aṅgīkaraṇe sati sambhavati na hi tādātmya tad utpattibhyām sva sādhya pratībandhavati ekatra hetau kvacid dharmiṇi saṃbhavati dvitīyaḥ tad lakṣaḥ tatra eva hetuḥ sambhavet bhāvānām viruddha svabhāva dvaya asambhavāt viruddha dharma adhyāsasya bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt tat avyabhicāriṇaḥ hetoḥ dvitīyasya tatra kutas sambhava avakāśaḥ iti 
[216,i^1]	nanu yadi tathavidhā viśeṣa sambhave sati viruddha avi abhicāri lakṣaṇam hīyate eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā vā vyarthā tathā api na eva hetu abhāva para saṅgaḥ tat kim uktam hetu abhāvaḥ vā iti atas āha na ca na eva tasya viśeṣasya pratibandha lakṣaṇasya yatas vastutas asambhavat pratihetu tvam niścīyate svarūpam tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇam nirddiśyate bhavadbhiḥ yathā asmābhiḥ nirdiṣṭam yat rūpam pratītya pratipadya pratiyoginaḥ ambhavā sambhavau utpaśyāmaḥ yatra sa viśeṣaḥ na asti tatra pratiyoginaḥ sambhavaḥ kalpitaḥ āgama āśraye anumāne yatra tu asti sa viśeṣaḥ vastu bala pravṛtte anumāne tatra pratiyoginaḥ asambhavaḥ iti 
[216,i^2]	yatas evam tasmāt na asti eva bhavatām sa viśeṣaḥ bhavadbhiḥ na jñāyate eva sa viśeṣaḥ iti tasmāt sarvatra yatra api pratiyogī na dṛśyate tatra api śaṅkayā pratiyogi viṣayayā bhavitavyam tām eva śaṅkām draḍhayan āha dṛṣṭa pratihetoḥ api ityādi yasya api hi pratihetuḥ dṛṣṭasya api prāk praityogi darśanāditareṇa sarva kālam adṛṣṭa pratiyoginā na kaścid viśeṣaḥ lakṣyate yad darśanāt jñāyeta atra pratiyogī sambhavati nyānyatra iti darśana adarśana mātra nibandhanayoḥ anvaya vyatirekayoḥ sarvatra samāna tvāt tathā api paścāt tatra pratiyogī dṛṣṭaḥ iti sarvatra tad tulya lakṣaṇe pratiyogi sadbhāva śaṅkā na nivartate iti 
[216,ii_217,i]	syāt matam yeṣu pratiyogī sambhavati teṣu aśyam eva kadācid asau upalabhyate yeṣu tu puruṣa āyuṣeṇa api na upalabhyate teṣu asau na asti eva tatas sa tathāvidhaḥ hetuḥ bhaviṣyati tat katham hetu abhāvaḥ asmākam iti atas āha na ca ityādi yeṣām api hi pratihetuḥ sambhavati teṣām api na eva sarvadā tasya pratihetaḥ rūpa labdhiḥ pratipattṝṇām na hi asarva darśinām upalabdhiḥ sarva bhāva sattām vyāpnoti pratibandha vaikalya sadbhāvāt nanu ca yatra sarvadā eva pratipattrā pratiyogī na dṛśyate tatra tad āśaṅkā katham kriyate tathā ca āha bādhā jñāne tu anutpanne na āśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikāḥ iti tathā aparam utprekṣeta hi yaḥ mohāt ajātam api bādhakam sa sarva vyavahāreṣu saṃśaya ātmā kṣayam vrajet iti 
[217,ii^1]	atas āha atiśayavatī tu ityādi tathā hi kasyacid eva pramātuḥ kuśa agrīya mateḥ atiśayavatī prajñā pratihetu utprekṣiṇī dṛṣṭā asmābhiḥ yathā veda prāmāṇya nirākartṛṣu hetuṣu saugataiḥ śiṣya paramparayā kumārila utpādāt prāc adṛṣṭa pratiyogiṣu upanyasteṣu tena eva prajñā atiśaya śālinā pratihetavaḥ utprekṣitāḥ tatas tad darśanāt yāvajjīvam adṛṣṭa pratihetuṣu api tad āśaṅkā na nivartate tatas katham āśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikā ucyate tulya lakṣaṇe hi iti ādikam api pratiyogi sambhava āśaṅkā kāraṇam uktam eva na ca pratiyogi sambhavam āśaṅkamānaḥ tad nimitta saṃbhavāt utprekṣeta hi iti ādi ākrośa mātreṇa nivartayitum śakyate 
[217,ii^2]	tena asya pratiyogi āśaṅkā apanoda kṣamam kiñcid kāraṇam abhidhānīyam yathā asmābhiḥ abhihitam svabhāva hetoḥ viparyeye bādhaka pramāṇa vaśāt tādātmya niścaye satya nvaya vyatirekayoḥ tatra nirṇayaḥ kārya hetau ca yathā ukta pratyakṣa anupalambhataḥ kārya kāraṇa siddheḥ ta niścayaḥ iti yatas evam sarvatra pratiyogi āśaṅkā na nivartate bhavat darśane tena kāraṇena aniścayaḥ pratiyoginaḥ sambhava asambhavayoḥ iha pratiyogī sambhavati iha tu na sambhavati iti evaṃrūpaḥ iti tasmāt vastutas asambhavat pratihetu tvam yat lakṣaṇam hetoḥ tasya aniścita tvāt eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā ādinām na kaścid hetuḥ syāt na hi aniścita lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ bhavati iti upasaṃhāraḥ iti 
[218,i^1]	tat evam kim yaḥ vastutas asambhavat pratihetuḥ sa samyak jñāna viparyaya hetuḥ iṣṭaḥ iti amum vikalpam nirākṛtya dvitīyam vikalpam nirācikīrṣuḥ āha atha apradarśita pratihetuḥ samyak jñāna viparya hetuḥ iṣṭaḥ iti sambandhaḥ ayam ca pakṣaḥ kila diṅnāga ācāryasya api abhimataḥ iti paraḥ upadarśayan āha yathā āha diṅnāga ācāryaḥ kim āha yadā tarhi ityādi śrāvaṇa tvasya hi na kathañcid vyavaccheda hetutvam iti diś nāga ācāryeṇa ukte pareṇa abhihitam yadā tarhi vaiyākaraṇaḥ śabda tvam sāmānya viśeṣam nityam abhyupagacchati tadā ayam śrāvaṇa tva lakṣaṇaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ hetuḥ eva syāt 
[218,i^2]	nityaḥ śabdaḥ śrāvaṇa tvāt śabda tva vat iti evam pareṇa ukte satya ācāryeṇa uktam yadi atra śabda ākhye dharmiṇī anitya tva hetum kṛtaka tva prayatna ān atarīyaka tva ādi lakṣaṇam kaścid vaiśeṣika ādiḥ na darśayet tadā ayama pradarśita pratihetuḥ hetuḥ eva bhavet iti tat evām ācārya pādaiḥ sākṣi tve datte bhujam utkṣipya śāstra kāraḥ pūtkurvan āha idam idānīm ityādi yadā hi ācāryasya api etat abhimatam iti kaiścid vyākhyāyate tat idam su mahat vyasanam āyātam gurubhiḥ abhihita tvāt aprakāśyam na hi gurūṇām doṣaḥ prakāśayitum yuktaḥ nyāyam anupālayadbhiḥ asaṃvaraṇīyam apracchādanīyam 
[218,i^3]	tat kim gurūn dūṣayāmaḥ uta nyāyam api upekṣāmahe iti ubhayam api aśakyam iti kaṣṭataram vyasanam katham nirvoḍhum śakyeta na kathaṃcid iti kaḥ punar atra doṣaḥ yena idam kaṣṭataram iti āha sa tāvat ayam śrāvaṇa tva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ vastūni śabda ādīni sva sādhyam tattvam nitya tvam tad prakṛtīni tad ātmakāni kṛtvā tad śrāvaṇa tvam pramāṇam yeṣām puruṣāṇām mīmāṃsaka vaiyākaraṇa ādīnām tān abhyudayena svargeṇa niḥśreyasena ca apavargeṇa yojayitvā tathā hi vastu tattvam bhāvayan yāvat kleśān prajahāti tāvat svargam āsādayati kleśān tu prajahat nirvāṇa parāyaṇaḥ bhavati 
[218,i^4]	atha āvā śabda nitya tva pratītau veda prāmāṇyāt tad vihita agnihotra anuṣṭhānāt svargaḥ vedānta niṣevaṇāt aparvak gaḥ punar uttara kālam pratibhāvatā prajñā jātīyena vaiśeṣika ādinā puruṣeṇa hetu antarasya pratihetoḥ nidarśanena yat asya nitya tva sādhana sāmarthyam pratihetu anupadarśane satya āsīt ttatad upadarśanena utkīlitam apanītam iti tāni vastūni nitya tva sampadaḥ pracyāvya tān ca tad pramāṇakān puruṣān svarga apavarga sampadaḥ pracyāvya śrāvaṇa tva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ śakti vaikalyāt paritrātum aśaktaḥ bhraṣṭa rājyaḥ iva rājā tapaḥ vanam gacchati svaiḥ eva duścaritaiḥ iti kim atra vayam brūmaḥ 
[219,i]	tat evam upahasya etasmin pakṣe doṣam upadarśayan āha puruṣa pratibhā ityādi yada hi apradarśita pratihetuḥ hetuḥ hetuḥ iṣyate tadā puruṣa pratibhā akṛtam sādhana tvam abhyupagatam bhavati tatas ca vastutas na kiñcid sādhanam asādhanam vā prāptam tathā hi yadā pratihetuḥ na upadarśyate tadā sādhanam yadā tu upadarśyate tadā na sādhanam iti puruṣa pratibhā akṛtam sādhana tvam āyātam iti 
[219,ii^1]	api ca apradarśita pratihetoḥ hetoḥ hetu tve aṅgi kriyamāṇe vikalpa dvayam kim paramārthataḥ hetuḥ tad dharma bhāvī uta atat dharma bhāvi iti tatra ādyam vikalpam adhikṛtya āha sa ca hetuḥ yaḥ asau prathamam upādīyate sa yadi svabhāvataḥ eva tasmin sādhya dharme sati eva bhavati iti evaṃśīlaḥ asmad upavarṇita pratibandha upagamāt yadi iṣyate tadā katham anyathā kriyeta hetu antareṇa ātad dharma bhāvī katham kriyeta na kathañcid kim kāraṇam 
[219,ii^2]	vastūnām hetu lakṣaṇānām yaḥ svabhāvaḥ satyam eva sādhya dharme bhavana ātmakaḥ a tad anyathā bhāvasya tad viparyayasya abhāvāt ubhayoḥ ca sva sādhya dharma avinābhāvi tve svabhāvataḥ eva dharmiṇī ekatra tayoḥ bhāve viruddhau ubhau svabhāvau ekasya syātām na ca ekasya viruddhau svabhāvau sambhavataḥ viruddha dharma adhyāsena tasya ekatva hāni prasaṅgāt atha dvitīyaḥ vikalpaḥ tadā atad dharma bhāvī ca asati api sādhya dharme bhavana śīlaḥ pratibandha anabhyupagamāt katham anyadā api apradarśita pratihetu avasthāyām api sādhanam kasyacid na eva tadā api sādhanam na kevalam pradarśita pratihetu avasthāyām iti 
[220,i]	upasaṃharan āha tasmāt svabhāvataḥ ityādi yatas evam bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ anyathā kartum na śakyate viruddha ubhaya svabhāvaḥ ca ekaḥ na sambhavati tasmāt paramārthataḥ svena svena sādhyena avinābhā vinoḥ yathā ukta lakṣaṇayoḥ kārya svabhāva hetvoḥ tad lakṣaṇasya kārya svabhāva lakṣaṇasya pratihetoḥ asambhavāt alakṣaṇam eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvam lakṣaṇam na bhavati kim kāraṇam iti āha vyavacchedya abhāvāt iti pratihetuḥ hi vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvasya vyavacchedyaḥ varṇyate sa ca pratihetuḥ sva lakṣaṇa yuktayoḥ kārya svabhāvayoḥ na bhavati eva iti katham tad hetu lakṣaṇam syāt iti tat evam anayoḥ dvayaḥ rūpayoḥ yaḥ sambhavaḥ yathā uktau inā abhā a asambhave sati iti rūpa antara upagame api hetvābhāsa tā eva iti hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare iti iti asya arthaḥ vivṛtaḥ iti 
[220,ii^1]	jñāta tva nirākaraṇāya āha jñānam punar ityādi avādhita viṣaya tvam vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvam ca kārya svabhāva hetvoḥ evā vina abhāve sati bādhā pratihetvoḥ a sambhavāt vyavacchedya abhāva tvena sati api liṅga dharma tve tad lakṣaṇam na bhavati iti uktam jñānam tu jñāta tvam tasya eva bhāva pratyayena abhidhānāt tathā hi jñāna śabda pravṛtti nimittam jñāta tvam ucyate tat ca jñānam eva tad utpāde sati jñātaḥ iti vyavahārāt na ca tat liṅgasya ātma rūpam iti katham liṅga lakṣaṇam bhaviṣyati 
[220,ii^2]	yadi api vikalpa pratibhāsī sāmānya ākāraḥ liṅga tayā avasthāpyate tathā api na jñānasya liṅga dharma tā na hi asau svatantraḥ eva liṅgam yat āha vikalpa bhedāna svatantrāṇām anvartha āśrayaṇāt tad kalpita viṣayāda artha pratipattau anartha pratilambhaḥ eva syāt iti tasmāt vāhya vastu upādānasya eva asya liṅgatā avasthā āpyate sādhya sādhana saṃkalpe vastu darśana hāneḥ sva lakṣaṇasya kvacid ananvayāt ca tad dharma tām eva tu anusmarantaḥ vikalpā nānā eka vyatirekān saṃdarśayantaḥ vastuni paramparayā pratibandhāt avisaṃvādakāḥ kārya ādi liṅga vyapadeśa nibandhanam ca iti ukta prāyam 
[221,i]	na ca tasya kārya ādeḥ ātma rūpam jñānam vikalpa avabhāsī ca sāmānya ākāraḥ na eva vikalpasya ātma bhūtaḥ tasya nīrūpasya vastu rūpa virodhāt tad rūpasya ca vikalpa pratibimba cakrasya sāmānya ātma tā virahāt yasmāt abādhyasya api bāhya tayā vyavasitasya ananuyāyinaḥ api anuyāyitayā sāmānya ātmaka tvam tathātve ca asya vikalpa rūpa tā kutas yat āha jñānāt avyatiriktam ca katham artha antaram vrajet tasmāt mithyā avabhāsaḥ ayam artheṣu eka ātma tā grahaḥ iti 
[221,ii]	na jñānasya liṅga dharma tā etat eva sādhayan āha kiṃrūpāt ityādi kimātmakāt hetoḥ anumeyaḥ arthaḥ jñātavyaḥ iti cintāyām prakṛtāyām pratipattuḥ puṃsaḥ yat avisaṃvādakam liṅgam tasya svarūpam abhidhīyate śāstra kāraiḥ yasya rūpasya darśana āt ayam pratipattā yatra tad rūpa sambhavaḥ tat sādhanam tad rūpa vikalam asādhanam iti pravibhāgena vyavasthāpya yat tatra sādhana tvena vyavasthāpitam tasya iṣṭa artha sannidhāna sampratyayāt pravṛttim avalambate tathā etasmin ca nyāye vyavasthite yat asya liṅgasya ātma rūpam tad lakṣaṇam bhavitum arhati pakṣa dharma ādi vat na tu yat para rūpam 
[221,iii]	syāt etat jñātasya liṅgasya sādhaka tvāt yuktā eva sādhya siddhi upayoginaḥ jñānasya liṅga lakṣaṇa tā iti atas āha pratipatti janmani ityādi yadi anumeya pratīti janmani upayujyate jñānam iti tanmātreṇa liṅgasya lakṣaṇam iṣyate tadā atiprasaṅgaḥ prāpnoti tam eva āha evam pratipatti janmani upayoga mātrāt liṅga lakṣaṇa tve prameyasya arthasya puruṣasya pramātuḥ ādi śabdāt saṃyoga samavāya ādīnām āloka manaskāra ādīnām liṅga lakṣaṇa tvam bhavet atra kāraṇam āha na hi teṣu api prameya ādiṣu asatsu liṅgini jñānam bhavati iti kṛtvā atra paraḥ aniṣṭam āpādayan āha niścita grahaṇam tarhi ityādi yadi para rūpa tvāt jñānam liṅga lakṣaṇam na bhavati tadā ca yat etat ācāryeṇa anumeye atha tad tulye sadbhāvaḥ na astitā asati niścite iti niścita grahaṇam kṛtam bhavataḥ ca abhimatam tat na kartavyayam tathā hi niścayaḥ hi liṅgasya para rūpam eva sa ced tad lakṣaṇam jñānam kim iti na iṣyate yatas niścayaḥ vijñānam eva tad viśeṣa tvāt asya iti 
[222,i]	siddhāntavādi āha na na kartavyam kintu kartavyam eva tasya niścita grahaṇasya liṅga rūpa pratipādanya artha tvāt tām eva anya artha tām darśayan āha sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ ityādi pare hi sa pakṣe darśana mātreṇa āsapakṣe ca adarśana mātrataḥ gamakam hetum icchanti teṣām na eva darśana mātreṇa sādhya siddhau samarthaḥ hetuḥ bhavati iti jñāpana artham niścita grahaṇam kṛtam yatas satoḥ vidyamānayoḥ api darśana adarśanayoḥ agamaka tvam hetoḥ dṛśyate sa śyāmaḥ tad putra tvāt iti ādau yatas evam tena kāraṇena sa pakṣe bhāvena vipakṣe sarvatra abhāva viśiṣṭena āsapakṣe ca sarvatra abhāvena sa pakṣe tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇa bhāva viśiṣṭena gamakaḥ hetuḥ iti asya arthasya jñāpana artham lakṣaṇa vākye niścita grahaṇam kṛtam boddhavyam etat uktam bhavati yau eva sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāvau pratibandha sādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā niścitau tābhyām eva hetuḥ gamakaḥ bhavati na tu yathā kathañcit darśana mātreṇa iti asya arthasya jñāpanāya niścita grahaṇam kṛtam iti 
[222,ii]	prakṛtam upasaṃharan āha tena ityādi yena viśiṣṭayoḥ bhāva abhāvayoḥ eva khyāpanāya niścita grahaṇam kṛtam na rūpa antara abhidhānāya anātma rūpasya ca lakṣaṇa tā na yujyate tena para rūpam liṅgasya lakṣaṇam na bhavati yatas tena jñāna ādinā para rūpeṇa liṅgasya na kaścid rūpa viśeṣaḥ abhidhīyate iti 
[223,i^1]	nanu ca pare api sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāvābhyām gamakam hetum icchanti darśana adarśane tu tayoḥ eva sādhake tat kim artham niścita grahaṇam iti atas āha tau hi ityādi yadi api pare bhāva abhāvābhyām eva gamakam hetum icchanti tathā api sa pakṣaḥ eva bhāvaḥ asapakṣe ca abhāvaḥ eva iti bhāva abhāvau darśana adarśana mātrataḥ vyavasthāpayanti na ca tatas tau tathāvidhau sidhyataḥ pratibandha vikalānām api arthānām kvacid bhāva abhāvayoḥ kathañcid darśana adarśana sambhavāt 
[223,i^2_223,ii]	tasmāt yau hetoḥ sa pakṣe eva bhāvaḥ asapakṣe ca abhāvaḥ eva iti evam ātmakau bhāva abhāvau tau tad bhāvasya sādhakam yat pramāṇam tādātmya tad utpatti sādhana viṣayam tat dhṛttyā vā uddhavyau kutas upāya antarasya abhāvāt tad anabhyupagame hi hetoḥ sa pakṣaḥ eva bhāvaḥ sarveṣām hetumatām bhāvānām sādhyena anugama darśane sati vipakṣe ca abhāvaḥ eva sādhya vikalānām sarva arthānām hetu viviktānām upalambhe sati syāt na ca etat asarva darśinaḥ sambhavati iti yatas upāya antaram na asti tena kāraṇena tayoḥ viśiṣṭayoḥ bhāva abhāvayoḥ pratipādanāya niścita śabdaḥ prayuktaḥ lakṣaṇe lakṣaṇa kāreṇa iti nanu ca bhāva abhāva vacana mātrāt eva pramāṇataḥ niścayaḥ labhyate anyathā tayoḥ eva sattā na prasidhyet iti atas āha yadi api ityādi 
[223,iii^1]	anumeye atha tad tulye sadbhāvaḥ na astitā asati iti anena eva sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāva vacana mātreṇā niścita grahaṇa nirapekṣeṇa tayoḥ bhāva abhāvayoḥ yat sādhanam pramāṇam tasya vṛttiḥ yadi api ākṣipyate katham punar niścita grahaṇam antareṇa bhāva abhāva vacana mātrataḥ tad dhṛtteḥ ākṣepaḥ iti āha anyathā yadi tad sādhana pramāṇa vṛttiḥ na ākṣipyeta tadā tayoḥ eva sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ eva bhāva abhāvayoḥ yā sattā sva rūpa vyavasthā tasyāḥ aprasiddheḥ kasmāt aprasiddhiḥ iti āha jñānasya upalabdheḥ yā sattā utpattiḥ tad nibandhana tvāt jñeyasya bhāva abhāva lakṣaṇasya sattā vyavasthāyāḥ svarūpa vyavasthiteḥ 
[223,iii^2]	na hi upalambham antareṇa svatas eva arthāḥ sidhyanti sarvasya sarva siddhi prasaṅgāt tasmāt idam evaṃrūpam na evaṃrūpam iti tad ākāra jñāna udayāt eva vyavasthāpyate yatas evam tasmāt sarvatra śāstre loke vā jñeya sattā vyavasthā eva niścita grahaṇam vinā api tad sādhanam tad sattā sādhanam pramāṇam ākarṣati ākṣipati iti kiñca para artha tvāt ca śāstra praṇayanasya tad sādhana pramāṇa vṛttiḥ ākṣipyate iti sambandhaḥ kīdṛśam punar tad śāstra praṇayanam yat para artha rūpa tayā sva vyavasthāpita jñeya sattā sādhanam pramāṇam ākṣipati 
[223,iii^3]	iti āha trirūpam liṅgam vaḥ saṃvādakam prāpakam vāñchitasya arthasya iti yadi nāma evaṃrūpam para artham śāstra praṇayanam tathā api katham tat sādhana pramāṇa vṛttim ākṣipati iti āha tad rūpam tasya liṅgasya trirūpasya rūpam svabhāvam śāstra uktam ye pratipattāraḥ na vidanti na teṣām tatas tri rūpāt liṅgāt śāstra uktāt vāñchite arthe pravṛttiḥ bhavati ajñātasya arthasya jñāpakasya sva sattā mātreṇa pravartaka tva abhāvāt yatas evam iti tasmāt para upalakṣaṇa tvāt eva pareṣām jñāpaka tvāt eva pravartake trirūpa liṅge jñānam siddham iti yadi api niścita grahaṇam atiricyate tathā api tau eva liṅgasya sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāvau viśiṣṭau śāstra uktau sa pakṣaḥ eva bhāvaḥ asapakṣe ca abhāvaḥ eva iti evaṃrūpau kecid naiyāyika prabhṛtayaḥ pare darśana adarśana mātreṇa ye darśana adarśane pratibandha sādhake na bhavataḥ tanmātreṇa vyavasthāpayanti yatas eva iti tasmāt teṣām vādinām niṣedha arthaḥ ayam lakṣaṇe niścita śabdaḥ prayuktaḥ ācāryeṇa asmābhiḥ ca abhyupagataḥ iti yadi tu para vipratipattiḥ na syāt tadā na eva asau prayujyeta iti 
[224,i]	kim iti punar ddarśana adarśanābhyām bhāva abhāva viṣayābhyām sa pakṣā sa pakṣayoḥ viśiṣṭau bhāva abhāvau anvaya vyatireka ātmakau neṣyete iti āha satoḥ api ityādi sati api kvacid sa pakṣe bhāva darśane hetoḥ kvacid ca āsapakṣe abhāva darśane sa śyāmaḥ tad putra tvāt iti ādau anvaya vyatirekayoḥ saṃśayāt tathā hi anvayaḥ nāma sarvatra sati eva sādhye hetoḥ bhāvaḥ vyāptyā ca asati sādhye hetoḥ abhāvaḥ vyatirekaḥ na ca kvacid sati sādhye hetoḥ bhāva darśane api tanmātreṇa tathā abhāvaḥ sarvatra bhavati apratibaddha svabhāvānām sahabhāva niyama abhāvāt tathā kvacid sādhya abhimatasya abhāve satyabhāva darśane api hetoḥ sarvatra tad abhāve avaśyam abhāvaḥ tad anāyat tasya tad nivṛttau niyamena nivṛtti abhāvāt tasmāt pratibandha prasādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā eva yathā uktau sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāvau sidhyataḥ na anyathā iti vipratipatti nirāsa artham eva niścita grahaṇam kṛtam iti upadarśayan āha tasmāt ityādi asmābhiḥ iti ācārya kṛte niścita grahaṇe anyatra asmākam abhimata tvāt asmābhiḥ iti āha 
[225,i]	tat evam vipratipatti nirāsa artham niścita grahaṇam asatyām tu vipratipattau tat na kartavyam eva iti pratipādya atas eva nyāyāt jñāta tvam rūpa antaram na bhavati iti darśayan āha yatas api ityādi pṛthak ataḥ iti pakṣa dharma tva ādeḥ trairūpyāt kutas tena evatraiḥ ūpya vacanena eva tad sādhana pramāṇa ākṣepataḥ avagata tvāt pratipanna tvāt iti kiṃvat upanaya artha vat pakṣa dharma tvāt iti yathā pakṣa dharma tva vacanena eva hetoḥ upanayasya arthaḥ avagataḥ tasya dharmiṇi hetoḥ sadbhāva pradarśana ātmaka tvāt pakṣa dharma vacanasya ca tad rūpa tvāt tatas pṛthak upanayaḥ rūpa antaram na bhavati tathā trairūpyāt jñānam tat vacanena eva avagata tvāt iti 
[225,ii]	atra paraḥ aniṣṭam āpādayan āha anvaya vyatirekayoḥ api ityādi yadi trairūpya vacanena eva sāmarthyāt jñānam labhyate iti tat tatas pṛthak na vaktavyam hantaḥ tarhi anvayāt pṛthak vyatirekaḥ na vaktavyaḥ vyatirekāt ca pṛthak anvayaḥ kim kāraṇam ekasya anvayasya vyatirekasya vā prayogāt ubhayasya gateḥ kṛtam ca tayoḥ pṛthak vacanam tathā jñāta tvasya api trairūpyāt gamyamānasya api pṛthak vacanam kartavyam iti 
[225,iii]	siddhāntavādi āha na hetoḥ ityādi na anvaya vyatirekayoḥ na pṛthaktvam kintu bhinna rūpa tā eva tathā hi anvayaḥ hetoḥ sa pakṣe bhāvaḥ ucyate vyatirekaḥ punar abhāvaḥ asapakṣe na ca tau parasparam ākṣipataḥ parasparam antarbhavataḥ vidhi pratiṣedha rūpayoḥ bhinna svabhāva tvāt na ca yaḥ yatas bhinna svabhāvaḥ sa tatra antarbhūtaḥ yuktaḥ nanu ca yadi anvaya vyatirekayoḥ bhinna rūpa tā katham tarhi trirūpam liṅgam ucyate na hi paraspara bhinnau ātmānau eva asya yujyete svabhāva bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt vastu bhedasya na eṣa doṣaḥ yatas yathā anvaya vyatirekau vyavasthā apyete tathā tayoḥ anantarbhāvaḥ ucyate na anyathā katham cetau vyavasthā apyete vyāvṛtti kṛtam bhedam upādāya tathā ca anayoḥ bhinna rūpa tā eva vyāvṛtti bhede api ca paramārthataḥ bhedaḥ na asti iti ekam liṅgam trirūpam iti ucyate iti 
[226,i]	katham tarhi prāk uktam na anayoḥ arthataḥ kaścid bhedaḥ anyatra prayoga bhedāt iti atas āha ekam vākyam ityādi anvaya mukhena vyatireka mukheṇa vā prayuktam ekam vākyam ubhayam anvayam vyatirekam ca bhinna lakṣaṇam eva gamayati iti ucyate asmabhiḥ na ekaḥ arthaḥ svabhāvaḥ dvitīyasya ucyate paraspara bhinnayoḥ eva eka vākya artha rūpa tvāt 
[226,ii]	atra paraḥ āha na tu tatra eva ityādi ayam abhiprāyaḥ lakṣaṇa vākya pratipāditau anvaya vyatirekau āśritya paraspara antarbhāvaḥ ca udyate sa ca vidyate eva tathā hi tatra eva bhāvaḥ iti atra lakṣaṇa vākye tad artha tayā tad abhāve abhāvaḥ gamyate atadbhāve avaśyam abhāvaḥ iti ca atra tad bhāve bhāvaḥ na hi asati pratibandhaḥ eka abhāve aparasya abhāvaḥ pratibandhaḥ ca tādātmya tad utpattibhyām tad bhāve bhāva rūpaḥ eva tatas ca ekena eva sa pakṣa āsa pakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāva pratipādakena prativiśiṣṭena lakṣaṇa vākyena ubhaya gateḥ dvitīya vacanam na kartavyam iti tathā ca eka vākya artha antarbhāvāt bhinna svabhāva tāpi anayoḥ durllabhā tatas ca yat uktam anvaya vyatirekayoḥ api tarhi na pṛthaktvam iti tat tad avastham eva iti 
[227,i]	siddhāntavādi āha vacanam etat tatra eva bhāvaḥ ityādi rūpam ubhayam ākṣipati pratipādayati kutas sāmarthyāt ubhaya pratipādana śakta tvāt katham iti ced āha ekasya api vākyasya kīdṛśasya niyama khyāpakasya sa pakṣaḥ eva bhāvaḥ asapakṣe ca abhāvaḥ eva iti sa avadhāraṇasya dvitīya ākṣepana antarīyaka tvāt dvitīya pratipādanana āntarīyaka tvāt na ca tāvatā eka vākya pratipādana mātreṇa ubhayoḥ eka svabhāva tā bhinna svabhāvānām api arthānām eka vākyena pratipādanāt ekena eva ca lakṣaṇa vākyena ubhaya gatau api yat pṛthak abhidhānam tat prayoga niyama artham sādharmya prayoge vaidharmya vacanam na kartavyam vaidharmya prayoge ca sādharmya vacanam iti na punar eka abhidhānena anavagatasya rūpa antarasya pratipādana artham na ca tathā trairūpya vacanena jñāna nibandhanena jñeya sattā vyavasthāyāḥ propalakṣaṇa arthena ca śāstra praṇayanena āśrita jñānasya eva trairūpyasya pratipādanāt labdhasya jñānasya punarvacane na kiñcid prayojanam asti iti na asya pṛthak vacanam yuktam iti 
[227,ii]	syāt matam kevalau api tarhi eka vākya artha anantarbhūtau para sparama abhinna svabhāvau bhaviṣyataḥ tatas eva evaka vākya artha antarbhāvāt iti atas āha na punar kevalau eka vākya artha anapekṣau tad antar bhāva mātreṇa sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāvau parasparam ākṣipataḥ antarbhavataḥ bhinna rūpāṇām api arthānām eka vākya antar bhāva darśanāt nanu ca niyamavantau api bhāva abhāvau kevalau eva tayoḥ paraspara ākṣepe kevalayoḥ api tad prasaṅgaḥ iti atas āha niyamavantau ca sa avadhāraṇa vākya pratipāditau na kevalau kintu sahitau eva kutas niyamasya sa avadhāraṇasya vākyasya ubhaya rūpa tvāt bhāva abhāva pratipādana ātmaka tvāt 
[227,iii]	tat evam sa avadhāraṇena vākyena na eva kevalaḥ anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vā abhidhīyate tad antar bhāvāt tu dvitīya gatiḥ kintu paraspara antarbhūtau eva sahitau ekena vākyena abhidhīyete iti pratipādya upasaṃharan āha tasmāt tatra eva sa pakṣaḥ eva bhāvaḥ iti anena vākyena na sa pakṣe bhāvaḥ eva ucyate kim tarhi asapakṣe abhāvaḥ api tathā ca itareṇa api asa pakṣe abhāvaḥ eva iti vacanena na abhāvaḥ eva kevalaḥ ucyate kintu sa pakṣe bhāvaḥ api yena kevala vacanena bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ vā tad ātmaka tayā dvitīyam ākṣipet yatas anayoḥ pṛthak vacanam na syāt tasmāt yadā anvaya vyatirekau bhava abhāvau abhipretau tadā tau bhinna rūpau eva iti katham tayoḥ na pṛthaktvam atha niyamavatā vākyena abhihitau tadā eka vākyāt eva ubhaya gateḥ pṛthak vacanam na kartavyam eva tat tu kṛtam na apratipanna pratipattaye kintu prayoga niyama artham iti uktam etat iti 
[228,i^1]	syāt matam yathā anvaya vyatirekau bhāva abhāva lakṣaṇau na paraspara ātmakau tatas ca tayoḥ parasparataḥ rūpa antara tvam evam para upalakṣaṇa śāstra pratipāditāt trailakṣaṇyāt bhidyate eva jñānam na tatra antarbhatam tatas rūpa antaram bhaviṣyati iti atas āha na evam yathā anvaya vyatirekau bhāva abhāva lakṣaṇau parasparam anantarbhūtau na tathā jñānam para upalakṣaṇa śāstra pratipādite trailakṣaṇye anantarbhūtam kutas para upalakṣaṇāt pare upalakṣyante upalakṣaṇam trairūpya viṣayām pratītim kāryante yena śāstreṇa tatas yat trailakṣaṇyam pratīyate āgṛhīta jñānam tasmāt avyatirekādāgṛhīta jñāne trailakṣaṇye antarbhāvāt iti yāvat iti tasmāt na lakṣaṇa antaram trairūpyāt iti 
[228,i^2_229,ii]	tat ayam atra samudāya arthaḥ yadi jñāta tvam jñāna śabda pravṛtti nimittam uktena prakāreṇa jñānam eva ucyate tadā tad liṃgasya anātma bhūtam iti na tad lakṣaṇam atha api jñāna apekṣaḥ karma bhāvaḥ jñāta tvam ucyate tadā api jñeya sattā vyavasthāyāḥ jñāna sattā nibandhana tvāt trairūpya vyavasthā eva tad sattā vyavasthāpakam jñānam ākṣipati tatas tad apekṣaḥ api karma bhāvaḥ anukta siddhaḥ iti na tat vacanam pṛthak kartavyam tathā para upalakṣaṇa artha śāstra pratipādita agṛhīta jñānāt trailakṣaṇyāt avyatirekāt iti tat evam abādhita viṣaya tva ādikam rūpa trayam nirākṛtya nigamayan āha tasmāt na hetuḥ ṣaṣ lakṣaṇaḥ kim tarhi trailakṣaṇyaḥ eva iti imam kṣata aśeṣa kutarka mārgam muni īśarāt dhāntanaya pradīpam vitatya puṇyam yat upārjitam tat parām viśuddhim jagataḥ vidheyāt hetu binduṭīkā samāptā 
[229,iii_229,v]	 mā yatataḥ imā yā tad rūpā vala tribhuvanasya hitāya śasvat narasya setoḥ do tathāgata matasya nivodhayitrī mārgasira vādi ravau maṃgalam mahā śrīḥ na guroḥ upadeśam agrahīt bubudhe vastu tatas dhīḥ yatate sma na tasya vṛddhaye na parispanditum api apārayat jīva ātmakam cāndramasam ca tejaḥ kṛta āspadam tasya tai t tat eva śaktā thā paratra citrā hi viśva prakṛti nāḥ he rohiṇī ramaṇa sarva kalāniketa tārāpate rajani nātha sudhā nidhāna kādambarī rasa guṇeṣu ni va mā ātmānam arpita śarīram anusmara indoḥ śrī brahmāṇa gacche pam abhaya kumārasya hetu bindu tarkaḥ
